40001001	Jisos Kraist wey dem born for David and Abraham famili, na em stori bi dis.
40001002	Abraham born Izik, Izik kon born Jakop. Na Jakop born Juda and en brodas,
40001003	Juda born Perez and Zera (wey en mama bi Tamar), Perez born Hezron and Hezron kon born Ram,
40001004	Ram na Amminadab papa, Amminadab born Nahshon, Nahshon kon born Salmon,
40001005	Salmon born Boaz (wey Rahab bi en mama), na Boaz bi Obed papa (wey Rut bi en mama), Obed kon born Jesse,
40001006	Jesse born David wey bi Izrel pipol king. David born Solomon (wey Uria wife bi en mama),
40001007	Solomon born Rehoboam, Rehoboam naim bi Abija papa and Abija kon born Asa,
40001008	Asa born Jehoshaphat, Jehoshaphat kon born Joram, Joram born Uzzia,
40001009	Uzzia born Jotham, Jotham kon born Ahaz, wey born Hezekia,
40001010	Hezekia born Manasse, Manasse naim bi Amon papa and Amon kon born Josia.
40001011	Josia born Jeconia and en brodas for di taim wey dem kari Izrel pipol go bi slave for Babylon.
40001012	Afta dem kari Izrel pipol go Babylon, Jeconia kon born Shealtiel, Shealtiel kon bi Zerubabel papa,
40001013	Zerubabel born Abiud, Abiud naim bi Eliakim papa, Eliakim kon born Azor,
40001014	Azor born Zadok, Zadok naim bi Achim papa, Achim kon born Eliud,
40001015	Eliud born Eleazar wey bi Matthan papa, Matthan kon born Jakop,
40001016	Jakop born Josef wey bi Mary husban, dis Mary naim bi Jisos Kraist mama.
40001017	So, from Abraham go rish David taim, na fourteen generashon dey and from David taim go rish wen dem kari Izrel pipol go Babylon, na fourteen tu and from dat taim go rish wen dem born Jisos Kraist, na fourteen generashon e bi.
40001018	Dis na haw dem born Jisos Kraist. Wen Mary en mama don redi to mari Josef, bifor dem bigin slip togeda, Mary kon si sey e don get bele wit Holi Spirit pawa.
40001019	Josef wey won mari am, na pesin wey dey fear God wel-wel and bikos e nor won disgrace am, e kon tink for en maind sey e nor go mari Mary again.
40001020	As e dey tink haw e go liv am, God angel show ensef to am for dream kon tel am sey, "Josef, David pikin, mak yu nor fear to mari Mary, bikos di pikin wey dey en bele, na Holi Spirit gi-am.
40001021	"E go born boy and yu go kol am Jisos Kraist, bikos e go save en pipol from dia sin."
40001022	Dis tins go hapun as God profet tok:
40001023	"Si! Di wuman wey neva slip wit man bifor go get bele and e go born boy and dem go kol am, 'Emmanuel' wey min, 'God dey wit us.'"
40001024	Wen Josef wak-up, e kon du wetin God angel tel am. So, e kon mari Mary,
40001025	bot e nor slip wit am ontil Mary born di pikin. Den e kon name am, Jisos Kraist.
40002001	Afta dem born Jisos Kraist for Betlehem wey dey Judea, for di taim wey Herod bi king, som wise men from east, kon go Jerusalem
40002002	dey ask, "Wer di Ju king wey dem jos born dey? Wi si di star wey tok abaut am, so wi kom woship am."
40002003	Wetin dem tok so, ves King Herod and Jerusalem pipol.
40002004	So, di king gada all di prist oga dem and di pipol wey sabi di law, kon ask dem, "Wer una tink sey dem go for born Kraist?"
40002005	Dem kon ansa, "Na for Betlehem, wey dey Judea, jos as Profet Isaia rite sey:
40002006	'Betlehem pipol, una wey smol pas for all di pipol wey dey rule Juda, na from among una di pesin wey go lid all my pipol for Izrel, go from kom.'"
40002007	Den Herod kon kol di wise men go kona, mak dem for tel am wen dem si di star.
40002008	E kon sey, "Mak una go luk for di pikin wel-wel. Wen una don si-am, mak una kom tel mi, so dat mi tu, go-go woship am.”
40002009	Wen di king tok finish, di wise men kon dey go and di star wey dem si bifor, kon dey lid dem ontil e stop on-top di haus wer di pikin dey.
40002010	Wen dem si di star, dem kon dey hapi.
40002011	Dem enta di haus, si di pikin wit en mama kon nil dan woship am. Den dem opun dia bag kon gi-am som gifts wey bi, gold, frankincence and myrrh.
40002012	Bikos God warn dem for dream mak dem nor go bak go mit Herod, dem kon pas anoda road go dia haus.
40002013	Wen di wise men don go, God angel kon tel Josef for dream, "Get up, kari di pikin and en mama run go Egypt, mak una stay der ontil I go tel yu wetin una go du, bikos Herod won kil di pikin."
40002014	Dat same nite, Josef wak-up, kari di pikin and en mama kon run go Egypt.
40002015	Dem stay der til Herod die. Dis tin mak wetin God profet tok hapun sey, "I kol my pikin komot from Egypt."
40002016	Wen Herod si sey di wise men disiv am, e ves wel-wel, so e send sojas mak dem go kil all di boys wey don rish tu years kom dan, bikos e don rish tu years wen di wise men kom mit am sey, dem si di star.
40002017	Dis won mak wetin Profet Jeremia tok hapun sey,
40002018	"Pipol hear krai and shaut for Rama. Rashel dey krai for en pikin dem wey don die and nortin wey pipol tok fit mak en heart strong."
40002019	Afta Herod die, God angel apier to Josef for dream wen e stil dey Egypt,
40002020	kon tel am, "Mak yu get up, kari di pikin and en mama go Izrel, bikos di pesin wey won kil-am, don die."
40002021	So, e kari di pikin and en mama go bak to Izrel.
40002022	Bot wen e hear sey Arkelaus dey rule for Judea, afta Herod en papa don die, Josef kon fear to go der. Afta God don warn am for dream, e kon go Galili.
40002023	Wen e rish Nazaret, e kon stay der. Dis won mak wetin Profet Jeremia tok hapun sey, "Dem go sey Jisos Kraist, na Nazaret e from kom."
40003001	For dat taim, Jon di Baptist dey prish insaid desert for Judea sey,
40003002	"Mak una turn from sin kom mit God, bikos God Kindom don near."
40003003	Na dis Jon Profet Isaia tok abaut sey, "Won pesin dey shaut insaid desert sey, 'Mak una mak God road strate.'"
40003004	Jon wear klot wey dem yuz camel hair mak, e yuz leda belt tie waist and na locust and honi for bush, e dey chop.
40003005	Pipol from Jerusalem, Judea and all di tawn wey dey near Jordan kon dey run go mit am
40003006	and e kon baptaiz dem insaid Jordan Riva, afta dem konfes dia sins.
40003007	Bot wen e si meni Farisi and Sadusi pipol dey kom mak e baptaiz dem, e kon tel dem, "Una, snake shildren! Hu warn una abaut God jojment wey dey kom?
40003008	"Naw, mak una du wetin go show sey una don turn from sin kom mit God,
40003009	mak una nor tink sey una don fri bikos una sey, 'Abraham na awa papa.' Mak I tel una, God fit turn all dis stone to Abraham shildren!
40003010	"Naw sef, dem don put di axe for di tri botom and eni tri wey nor bear beta frut, dem go kut am trow insaid fire.
40003011	"I dey baptaiz una wit wota mak una for turn from sin kom mit God, bot di pesin wey go kom afta, strong pas mi. I nor big rish to luz di rope wey dey en shu, na-im go baptaiz una wit Holi Spirit and fire.
40003012	"Di fan wey e go tak blow kanda from corn dey en hand and e go burn di dirti for fire wey nor dey kwensh."
40003013	Jisos kom from Galili mak Jon for baptaiz am for Jordan Riva.
40003014	Bot Jon won kon stop am sey, "Na yu sopoz baptaiz mi, insted yu kom mit mi mak I baptaiz yu?"
40003015	Jisos ansa, "Mak e bi so naw, e beta mak wi du evritin wey God wont." So, Jon kon baptaiz am.
40003016	As Jisos dey kom out from di wota afta Jon don baptaiz am, hevun opun and Jon kon si God Spirit wey bi laik dove, stay on-top Jisos head.
40003017	Naim won vois from hevun kon sey, "Dis na My pikin wey I luv and e dey mak bele swit mi."
40004001	Di Holi Spirit tak Jisos go insaid desert mak devol for tempt am.
40004002	Afta Jisos don fast for forti days and forti nites, e kon dey hungri.
40004003	Den devol kon mit am sey, "If yu bi God pikin, komand dis stone mak e turn to bread."
40004004	Jisos kon ansa, "God wod sey, 'Nor bi onli fud man go tak sovaiv, bot na wit evri wod wey God tok.'"
40004005	Den, devol show Jisos di tawn wey dey holi, kon mak am stand on-top di place wey high pas for di Tempol
40004006	and e tel Jisos, "If yu rili bi God pikin, jump go dan, bikos dem rite for God wod sey, 'God go komand en angels mak dem du evritin for yu and dem go kash yu mak yor leg nor nak stone.'"
40004007	Jisos ansa am, "God wod sey, 'Mak yu nor trai God wey bi yor Oga.'"
40004008	Den devol tak Jisos go won mountin wey high wel-wel, kon show am all di kindom for dis wold and all di beta tins insaid am.
40004009	Devol kon tel am, "I go giv yu all dis tins, if yu go fal for groun woship mi."
40004010	Jisos ansa, "Komot here, devol! Bikos dem rite for God wod sey, 'Na onli God wi sopoz to serv and woship.'"
40004011	So, devol kon liv Jisos and God angels kon bigin help am.
40004012	Wen Jisos hear sey dem don put Jon insaid prizin, e kon go bak to Galili.
40004013	From der, Jisos komot from Nazaret go Kapanum wey near di sea, wer Zebulun and Naphtali pipol dey stay,
40004014	so dat wetin Profet Isaia tok, go hapun:
40004015	"Zebulun and Naphtali, di place wer riva for kros Jordan go Galili, wer pipol wey nor bi Ju dey stay,
40004016	una wey dey daknes, don si big lite and una wey don nearli die, don get life."
40004017	From dat taim, Jisos bigin prish sey, "Mak una turn from sin kom mit God, bikos God Kindom don kom mit una."
40004018	As Jisos dey waka for Galili wotasaid, e si tu brodas: Saimon wey dem dey kol Pita and Andru en broda, dem dey trow net insaid di riva dey kash fish.
40004019	Jisos kon tel dem, "Mak una folo mi and I go mak una kash pipol."
40004020	At wons, dem liv dia net kon folo Jisos.
40004021	As Jisos komot from der, e kon si tu brodas, James and Jon, wit Zebedi dia papa, dey ripair net insaid dia boat. Den Jisos kol di brodas.
40004022	Kwik-kwik dem run liv dia papa insaid di boat, kon folo Jisos.
40004023	Jisos kon dey waka for Galili dey tish insaid dia sinagog. E prish abaut God Kindom and dey heal pipol wey get difren-difren diziz and siknes.
40004024	So di news abaut Jisos kon spread go evriwer for Syria. Dem kon bring pipol wey nor wel, wey nor fit waka, pipol wey devol dey wori and di pipol wey dim on dey insaid dem, kom mit am and e heal all of dem.
40004025	Meni pipol from Galili, Dekapolis, Jerusalem, Judea and pipol wey dey stay near Jordan Riva, kon folo am.
40005001	Wen Jisos si di pipol, e kon klimb go di mountin top and en disaipols folo am. Afta e sidan,
40005002	e kon bigin tish dem sey;
40005003	"God go bless una wey dey poor for spirit, na una go get hevun.
40005004	"God go bless una wey dey mourn, bikos e go mak una hapi.
40005005	"God go bless una wey nor dey kari bodi up, una go enjoy en promis for dis wold.
40005006	"God go bless una wey dey laik to du gud tins, e go giv una evritin wey una wont.
40005007	"God go bless una wey dey sori for pipol, una go risiv mesi.
40005008	"God go bless una wey get pure heart, na una go si God.
40005009	"God go bless una wey dey mak peace, pipol go kol una God shildren.
40005010	"God go bless una wey dey sofa bikos una dey du wetin dey rite, na una go enjoy God Kindom for hevun.
40005011	"God go bless una wey pipol dey kos, dey sofa and lai for una head bikos of mi.
40005012	"Mak una hapi and mak bele swit una, bikos na big tin dey wait una for hevun. Mak una rimemba sey, na so di profets wey kom bifor una, sofa tu."
40005013	"Na una bi salt for dis eart. Bot if salt nor get taste; haw e go bi for pipol mout? E beta mak dem trowey-am and mak pipol mash-am.
40005014	"Na una bi lite for dis wold and tawn wey dey on-top mountin, nor dey hide.
40005015	"Pesin nor dey lite lamp kon kova am wit bazin, insted e go put am for wer evribodi wey dey insaid di haus go si-am.
40005016	"Laik dat tu, mak yor lite shine wel-wel for wer pipol dey, so dat dem go si di gud tins wey yu dey du, wey go mak dem praiz yor Papa wey dey hevun."
40005017	"Mak una nor tink sey I kom spoil Mosis Law and di tins wey di profets tish. Nor bi so, misef kom obey dem.
40005018	"I tel una tru wod, bifor dis wold go end, evritin wey dey insaid di Law, ivun di smol-smol won, go hapun.
40005019	"So enibodi wey nor du wetin God komand and dey tish odas to du as e dey du, naim go smol pas for God Kindom. Bot pesin wey obey God and tish odas to du wetin di Law tok, na big pesin e go bi for God Kindom.
40005020	"I tel yu di trut, if di gud wey yu du, nor beta pas wetin di Farisi and di pipol wey dey tish di Law du, yu nor go fit enta God Kindom."
40005021	"Yu hear as God tel awa papa dem bifor-bifor sey, 'Nor kil and enibodi wey kil, God go joj am.'
40005022	"Bot I tel una, enibodi wey ves for en broda, God go joj am tu. Enibodi wey kos en broda, go face di konsol and enibodi wey kol pesin, 'Mumu', go-go hell fire.
40005023	"If yu tak gift go altar and yu kon rimemba sey yor broda get bad bele for yu,
40005024	mak yu liv di gift for di altar, first go setol wit yor broda, den yu go fit kom bak kon giv yor gift.
40005025	"Kwik setol wit hu dey akiuz yu bifor una rish kourt, if not, e go giv yu to di joj and di warda go trow yu insaid prizin.
40005026	"I tel una di trut, yu nor go komot from dat trobol ontil yu pay all di moni!"
40005027	"Yu hear wey pipol sey, 'Mak yu nor slip wit hu yu nor mari.'
40005028	"Bot I dey tel una naw sey, 'Enibodi wey luk wuman kon get di maind to slip wit am, don alredi komit sin for en heart.'
40005029	"If yor rite eye go mak yu sin, mak yu plok am komot. E beta sey won part for yor bodi nor dey, dan sey all yor bodi enta hell fire.
40005030	"If yor rite hand go mak yu du bad tin, mak yu kut am trowey! E beta sey won part for yor bodi nor dey, dan sey all yor bodi enta hell fire."
40005031	"Pipol dey sey, 'Enibodi wey driv en wife, must gi-am paper sey e nor won mari am again.'
40005032	"Bot I dey tel una naw sey, enibodi wey driv en wife komot from marage, wey nor bi sey di wuman slip wit anoda man, don mak di wuman komit adultri and eni man wey mari di wuman, don komit adultri tu."
40005033	"Again, yu don hear sey dem tel pipol bifor-bifor sey, 'Mak yu nor break yor promis, bot du wetin yu promis God.'
40005034	"Bot I dey tel una naw sey, mak una nor eva yuz hevun swear at all, bikos na God throne e bi,
40005035	or wit eart, bikos naim God dey put en leg, or yuz Jerusalem, bikos na di big king tawn e bi.
40005036	"Nor ivun yuz yor head swear, bikos yu nor fit mak won singol hair white or blak.
40005037	"Wen yu sey, 'Yes,' mak yu min am and wen yu sey 'No,' mak yu min am tu. Eni oda tin wey yu tok pas dis, na devol e from kom."
40005038	"Una hear sey, 'Enitin enibodi du una, mak una du-am bak.'
40005039	"Bot I tel una, mak una nor fite, if enibodi slap yor face, turn di oda side gi-am tu.
40005040	"If enibodi drag yor shirt wit yu, mak yu gi-am yor koat join.
40005041	"And if enibodi fos yu waka won mile, mak yu folo am waka tu mile.
40005042	"Giv pipol enitin wey dem ask from yu and nor driv enibodi wey kom boro somtin from yu."
40005043	"Una hear sey, 'Mak una luv una nebor and hate una enemi.'
40005044	"Bot I tel una naw sey, 'Mak una luv una enemis and pray for pipol wey dey sofa una,
40005045	so dat una go bi laik una Papa for hevun wey dey alow sun to shine and rain to fal on-top bad and gud pipol.
40005046	"If una luv onli di pipol wey luv una, wetin una go gain?Na so bad pipol dey du tu, abi nor bi so?
40005047	"If una dey grit onli una brodas, una nor beta pas odas, bikos pipol wey nor no God stil dey du laik dat, abi nor bi so?
40005048	"So mak una dey pafet as una Papa wey dey for hevun, pafet."
40006001	"Mak una nor dey du gud bikos una wont mak pipol si una; if una du so, God nor go pay una for di gud wey una du .
40006002	"Enitiam una giv somtin to pipol, mak una nor show unasef as pritendas dey du for dia sinagog and road, so dat oda pipol go praiz dem. I tel una tru wod, dem don alredi get dia riwod.
40006003	"Bot wen una dey giv, mak una nor let una left hand no wetin una rite hand giv.
40006004	"So dat una gift, go dey sikrit and una Papa wey dey si for sikrit, go riwod una for pipol present."
40006005	"Enitiam wey una dey pray, mak una nor du laik pipol wey dey pritend, wey laik to dey stand pray insaid sinagog and for road, so dat pipol go si dem. I tel una tru wod, dem don alredi get dia riwod.
40006006	"Bot wen una dey pray, mak una go insaid room, klose di door and pray to una Papa for sikrit. And una Papa wey dey si for sikrit, go riwod una for pipol present.
40006007	"Wen una dey pray, mak una nor tok won wod meni taims as pipol wey dey serv juju dey du, bikos dem tink sey dia juju go hear dem wen dia tok plenti.
40006008	"Mak una nor bi laik dem. Una Papa no wetin una nid bifor una bigin ask am.
40006009	"So mak una pray laik dis: 'Awa Papa wey dey for hevun, wi praiz yor name,
40006010	mak yor Kindom kom, mak wetin yu wont, hapun for dis wold as e bi for hevun.
40006011	'Giv us di fud wey wi go chop evriday,
40006012	forgiv us all di bad-bad tins wey wi don du, as wi sef dey forgiv odas di bad tins wey dem du us.
40006013	'Nor alow us enta temtashon bot mak yu save us from bad tins.'
40006014	"If una forgiv oda pipol di bad tins wey dem du una, una Papa wey dey for hevun go forgiv una tu.
40006015	"Bot if una nor forgiv odas, una Papa sef nor go forgiv una."
40006016	"Wen una dey fast, mak una nor skwiz una face laik pipol wey dey pritend, so dat pipol go si sey dem dey fast. I tel una tru wod, dem don alredi get dia ful riwod.
40006017	"Bot wen una dey fast, mak una wosh and rub pomade for una face,
40006018	so dat odas nor go no sey una dey fast, bot onli una Papa wey dey for sikrit go no. And una Papa wey dey si for sikrit, go riwod una for pipol present."
40006019	"Mak una nor jos gada propati for dis wold, bikos ant go chop dem or dem go rust, or tif fit enta insaid di haus tif dem.
40006020	"Bot mak una gada beta tins for unasef for hevun, wer ant nor go fit chop dem and dem nor go rust and tif nor go fit enta,
40006021	bikos, wer una properti dey, na der una heart go dey tu.
40006022	"Na eye bi di lite for pesin bodi. If pesin eye dey okay, lite go ful en bodi.
40006023	"Bot if pesin eye blind, den daknes go ful en bodi. If di lite wey dey insaid una na daknes, di daknes big wel-wel!
40006024	"Nobodi go fit serv tu oga, e go hate won kon luv di oda won, or e go serv won wit all en heart and nor respet di oda won. Nobodi go fit serv God and moni for di same taim.
40006025	"So I tel una, mak una nor wori abaut una life, wetin una go chop or drink and wetin una go wear for bodi. Life nor big pas fud? Abi bodi nor beta pas klot?
40006026	"Mak una luk di birds wey dey flai for skai, dem nor dey plant or put enitin wey dem gada insaid store, bot una Papa for hevun dey fid dem. Una nor beta pas dem?
40006027	"Hu among una wey dey wori go fit add won hour join en life?
40006028	"Why una dey wori abaut klot wey una go wear? Mak una tink haw flawa dey grow for field; dem nor dey wok or mak klot wey dem dey wear.
40006029	"I tel una tru wod, ivun Solomon, upon all di moni wey e get, e nor wear klot wey fine rish di wons wey dis flawa dem dey wear!
40006030	"If God mak gras fine laik dis, gras wey una go si today and tumoro dem go trow am for fire, E nor go dress una pas dem? Una fate smol wel-wel o-o.
40006031	"So mak una nor wori kon dey sey, 'Wetin wi go chop' or 'Wetin wi go drink?' or 'Wetin wi go wear?'
40006032	"Na dis kaind tins pipol wey nor no God dey porshu and una Papa for hevun no sey una nid dem.
40006033	"Bot mak una first du di gud tins wey God wont and evri oda tin go bi una own.
40006034	"So mak una nor wori abaut tumoro, bikos tumoro get en own wahala. Today trobol don du."
40007001	"Mak una nor dey joj pipol enihaw, so dat God nor go joj una.
40007002	"Bikos, na as una joj, na so God go tak joj una and as una du oda pipol, na so dem go du una tu.
40007003	"Why yu dey si di smol dirti wey dey yor broda eye, bot yu nor dey si di big wud wey dey for yor own eye?
40007004	"Haw yu won tak tel yor broda sey, 'Mak I rimov di dirti wey dey yor eye, wen big wud dey yor own?'
40007005	"Yu wey dey pritend, first rimov di big wud wey dey yor eye, den yu go fit si di smol dirti for yor broda own.
40007006	"Mak una nor giv dog wetin bi God own or trow yor gold giv pig, bikos dem go mash am wit leg, turn face yu, den kon tear yu to pieces.
40007007	"Wen yu ask for somtin, God go giv am to yu; wen yu luk for somtin, yu go si-am and wen yu knok, di door go opun for yu.
40007008	"Enibodi wey ask for somtin, go get-am; enibodi wey dey faind somtin, go si wetin e dey faind and pesin wey knok door, dem go opun for am.
40007009	"E get eni of una wey en pikin ask am for bread and e kon gi-am stone?
40007010	"Or if di pikin ask for fish, yu go gi-am snake?
40007011	"If yu wey bad fit giv yor pikin gud tin, yu tink sey God wey dey hevun nor go giv beta tin to pipol wey ask am?
40007012	"Bikos of dis, mak yu trit pipol as yu wont mak dem trit yu, bikos na so dem rite am for di Profets and for Mosis law.
40007013	"Mak yu pas di smol gate enta, bikos di gate wey pipol go pas go sofa, wide wel-wel and meni pipol dey waka enta.
40007014	"Bot di gate wey pipol dey pas enta life, smol wel-wel and e hard to enta and na onli few pipol go fit si-am.
40007015	"Mak yu shine yor eye, bikos lai-lia profets go kom laik ship, bot for insaid dia heart, dem bi wiked anima wey dey kil.
40007016	"Yu go no dem wit wetin dem dey du. Pipol nor dey gada grape or fig from shuku-shuku.
40007017	"So tu, evri gud tri go bear gud frut, bot bad tri, go bear bad frut.
40007018	"Gud tri nor go fit bear bad frut and bad tri nor go fit bear gud frut.
40007019	"Eni tri wey nor bear gud frut, dem go kut-am dan kon trow am insaid fire.
40007020	"So, yu go no di lai-lia profets wit wetin dem dey du."
40007021	"Nor bi evribodi wey dey kol God, 'Oga, Oga, go enta God Kindom, bot na onli di pipol wey dey du wetin my Papa for hevun wont.

40013001	Dat same day, Jisos komot from di haus go sidan for Galili wotasaid.
40013002	Meni pipol gada round am, so e enta won boat and all di pipol stand for groun near di wota.

40013004	"As e dey plant, som seed fal for road and bird kon chop dem.

40013021	bot di sid nor get root, bikos di wod wey e hear nor strong for en heart, so wen trobol kom, e nor go fit bear-am.

40014001	Dat taim, Herod wey dey rule hear abaut Jisos,

40018001	Dat taim, di disaipols kon ask Jisos, "Na hu big pas for God Kindom?"

40018014	"Na laik dis tu yor Papa for hevun nor wont mak eni of en shildren loss."

40018019	"Again, I tel una tru wod, if tu of una for dis wold gri and pray for enitin, my Papa for hevun go du-am for una.

40018023	"God Kindom bi laik wen won king won no haw en savants dey manage en biznes.
40018024	"As di king dey shek di account, dem kon bring won savant, wey dey hol ten tazon koins kom.

40018029	"Di savant wey e seize for trot kon fal for groun dey beg am, 'Mak yu dey patient wit mi, I go pay yu yor moni.'
40018030	"Bot e nor gri. Insted e kari am go put for prizin, ontil e go pay wetin e hol.

40019001	Wen Jisos tok finish, e kon komot from Galili go Judea aria for di oda side for Jordan Riva.

40020001	"God Kindom bi laik wen pesin komot for earli mornin go hire pipol wey go wok for en farm.
40020002	"Afta en and di wokas don agri haw mush dem go get for dia wok, e kon send dem go wok for en farm.
40020003	"Wen nain o' klok rish for mornin, e kon si pipol wey nor get wok stand for market.
40020004	"E kon tel dem, 'Mak una go wok for my farm, I go pay una wel.'

40020006	"Wen faiv o' klok for evenin don nearli rish, e si som pipol wey nor get wok and e kon ask dem, 'Why una nor dey wok and today don nearli finish?'

41003010	Jisos kon heal meni pipol, so all di pipol wey nor wel kon dey push ish oda, so dat dem go fit tosh am.
41003011	And enitaim evil spirit wey dey insaid som pipol bodi si Jisos, dem go fal for en front dey shaut, "Yu bi God Pikin."
41003012	Bot Jisos kon warn dem wel-wel mak dem nor let pipol no hu e bi.

41003016	Na di twef wey e shuz bi dis: Saimon wey e kol Pita,

41003020	Jisos go haus and plenti pipol kon gada am sotey en and en disaipols nor fit chop.
41003021	Wen Jisos famili hear wetin dey hapun, dem kon go hol am, bikos pipol dey sey, "E don dey krase."

41003023	So Jisos kon tok to di pipol for parabol sey: "Haw Satan go fit tak driv Satan komot?
41003024	"Eni kindom wer pipol dey fite ish oda, nor go fit stand.
41003025	"And eni famili wey dey fite demsef, go skata.
41003026	"So, if Satan kindom divide against ensef, e nor go fit stand and en end don rish.
41003027	"Nobodi go fit enta strong man haus tif en propati, unles e first tie di strong man, bifor e go fit tif en tins.
41003028	"I tel una tru wod, God go forgiv pipol di sins wey dem komit and all di bad wod wey dem tok.
41003029	"Bot enibodi wey tok bad wod against di Holi Spirit, God nor go eva forgiv am, bikos e don komit sin wey go last foreva."
41003030	Jisos tok so, bikos som pipol sey, "Evil spirit dey insaid am."
41003031	Jisos mama and en brodas kom mit am. Dem stand for outsaid kon send pesin go kol am.
41003032	Di pipol wey sidan near Jisos kon tel am, "Yor mama and yor brodas dey outsaid, dem won si yu."
41003033	Bot Jisos ansa dem, "Hu bi my mama and my brodas?"
41003034	Den e kon luk di pipol wey sidan roun am, tel dem, "Na my mama and my brodas bi dis pipol!
41003035	"Bikos enibodi wey du wetin God wont, na-im bi my broda, sista and mama."
41004001	Again, Jisos kon bigin tish pipol for di wotasaid. Since pipol wey gada roun am meni, e kon enta boat dey tish di pipol as dem sidan for groun near di wota.
41004002	E kon tish dem meni tins for parabol sey:
41004003	"Mak una Listin! Won farma go plant sid for en farm.
41004004	"As e dey plant, som sid fal for road and birds kom chop dem.
41004005	"Odas fal for wer stones and sand dey. Dem kwik grow kom out, bikos gud soil nor dey der.
41004006	"Wen sun kom out, e burn di plant, bikos dem nor get deep root, dem kon die.
41004007	"Odas fal for wer shuku-shuku dey and wen dem grow kom out, di shuku-shuku, shuk dem die.
41004008	"Bot odas fal for beta groun. Dem grow wel kon bear oda sids, som bear rish tati, som sisti and som ondred."
41004009	Jisos kon sey, "Enibodi wey get ear, mak e hear wetin I dey tok!"
41004010	Wen Jisos dey alone, pipol wey dey wit am and en twef disaipols kon ask am abaut di parabol.
41004011	E kon tel dem, "God don show una di kindom sikrit. Bot doz wey dey outsaid God Kindom, na parabol e bi for dem,
41004012	so dat dem go dey luk, bot dem nor go si, dem go dey hear, bot dem nor go undastand and dem nor go fit turn from dia sin kom mit God mak E forgiv dem."
41004013	Jisos kon ask dem, "Una nor undastand dis parabol? Den haw una go tak undastand eni oda parabol?
41004014	"Na God wod di farma dey plant.
41004015	"Som pipol bi laik di sid wey fal for road: enitaim dem hear God wod, Satan go kom tif-am from dem kwik-kwik.
41004016	"Som bi laik di sids wey fal for wer stones and sand dey: as dem hear God wod, dem go risiv am wit hapines,
41004017	and bikos dem nor get root and patient, wen trobol or wahala kom bikos of di wod, dem go forget God wod.
41004018	"Odas bi laik di sids wey fal for wer shuku-shuku ful: dem hear di wod,
41004019	bot trobol for life, big eye for moni and di way dem dey run folo oda tins, go kon blok di wod and e nor go bear enitin for dia life.
41004020	"Bot di wons wey fal for beta groun, na doz wey hear di wod kon risiv am and bear meni fruts, som bear rish tati, som sisti and som ondred."
41004021	Jisos stil ask dem, "Pipol dey hide lamp for unda basket? Nor bi on-top di place wer dem dey kip lamp, dem sopoz put am?
41004022	"E nor get wetin pipol hide wey God nor go show and e nor get wetin dey for sikrit naw, wey nor go kom out for opun.
41004023	"If enibodi get ear, mak e hear wetin I dey tok!"
41004024	Jisos kon tel dem, "Mak una dey kareful for wetin una dey hear, bikos na wetin yu yuz tak measure giv oda pipol, na-im God go tak measure for yu tu and E go add join am.
41004025	"Bikos enibodi wey get, God go gi-am more, bot enibodi wey nor get, ivun di smol won wey e get, God go tak am from am."
41004026	Jisos kon sey, "God Kindom bi laik pesin wey skata sid for groun.
41004027	"Di pesin go dey slip and dey wak-up day and nite, di sid kon grow kom out, ivun doh di man nor no haw e hapun.
41004028	"As plant dey grow from groun, di bodi go first kom out, den di head go bear frut and sid go kom out from insaid.
41004029	"Wen e ripe, di farma go kut am, bikos di taim to plok wetin e plant, don rish."
41004030	Jisos kon ask dem, "Wetin wi go tak kompare God Kindom? Wish parabol wi go fit yuz tak show as e bi?
41004031	"E bi laik mustard sid wey bi di sid wey smol pas for di wold, wey pesin plant for groun.
41004032	"Afta dem don plant am, e go grow kon big pas all di oda plants and en bransh go big and birds go land kon build dia nest for der."
41004033	Na wit meni parabol laik dis won, Jisos tak prish God wod to dem, so dat dem go fit undastand.
41004034	E nor get wetin e tel dem wey e nor yuz parabol. Bot wen onli en and di disaipols dey, e dey explain evritin giv dem.
41004035	Wen evenin rish dat day, Jisos kon tel en disaipols, "Mak wi kros go di oda side for di riva."

41004037	Den, strong briz kon dey blow and wota dey enta di boat, so di boat kon dey won sink.

41004039	So Jisos get up kon komand di briz, den e tel di riva, "Mak yu kwayet!" Di briz stop and evriwer kon kwayet at wons.
41004040	Den Jisos tel dem, "Why una dey fear? Una stil nor get fate?"
41004041	Fear kash dem wel-wel and dem kon dey ask ish oda, "Hu dis man bi sef? Ivun briz and riva dey obey am!"
41005001	So Jisos and en disaipols kon kros go di oda side for di riva for Gerasenes aria.
41005002	As Jisos jos dey kom dan from di boat, won man wey get evil spirit kon kom out from di beria groun, run kom mit am.
41005003	Na insaid beria groun di man dey stay and nobodi dey fit tie am, ivun wit chain.
41005004	Bikos dem don tie en hand and leg meni taims wit chain and handkoff, bot e kut dem trowey. Nobodi strong rish to hol am.
41005005	Evriday and nite for di beria groun near wer mountin dey, e dey shaut, dey yuz stone dey kut en bodi.

41005020	So di man kon go, bigin tok for di hol vilage abaut wetin God du for am and evribodi wey hear am, sopraiz wel-wel.

41005026	Dis wuman don sofa wel-wel for meni doktor hand and e don spend all di moni wey e get, bot insted of am to wel, di siknes kon dey wos more-more.
41005027	Wen e hear abaut Jisos, e waka go wer Jisos dey kon manage tosh en klot.
41005028	Bikos e tok for en maind sey, "If I go fit tosh en klot, I go wel."
41005029	At wons, di blood kon stop and e feel am for en bodi sey e don wel.
41005030	Na wons, Jisos no sey pawa komot for en bodi. E kon turn roun ask di pipol, "Hu tosh my klot?"

41005034	So Jisos tel am, "My pikin, yor fate don mak yu wel. Mak peace folo yu and mak yu wel finish."

41005036	Jisos nor listin to dem, bot e kon tel di man, "Mak yu nor fear, bot mak yu jos biliv."
41005037	Jisos nor let enibodi folo am esept Pita, James and Jon, wey bi James broda.
41005038	Dem kon rish Jairus haus kon si plenti pipol dey mak nois, dey krai.

41006001	Jisos kon komot for dat place go en home tawn wit en disaipols.

41006020	Herod dey fear Jon wel-wel, so e dey protet am, bikos e no sey Jon na holi man wey dey du wetin God laik. Enitaim Herod hear Jon dey prish, en maind go dey wori am, bot e stil dey laik to listin to am.

41007001	Di Farisi pipol and som law tishas, wey kom from Jerusalem gada for wer Jisos dey.
41007002	Dem kon si sey Jisos disaipols dey chop bread wen dem neva wosh dia hand.

41007004	And wen dem kom bak from market, dem nor dey chop unles dem first wosh dia hand. Dem stil dey folo meni oda tradishons, laik to wosh cup, ketol and chair wey dem dey sidan put chop.)
41007005	Di Farisi pipol and di law tishas kon ask Jisos, "Why yor disaipols nor dey du akordin to awa tradishon, bot insted dem dey chop wit dirti hand?"
41007006	Jisos ansa dem, "Di tin wey Isaia profesai abaut una, na tru, bikos una dey pritend, as dem rite for God wod, 'Dis pipol dey praiz Mi wit dia mout, bot dia heart dey far from Mi.
41007007	'Dem dey woship Mi for nor-tin, dey tish sey mak pipol obey humanbin law.
41007008	'Dem nor dey respet God law, bot dem dey obey humanbin law.'"
41007009	Jisos stil tel dem, "Una rejet God komandment, so dat una go fit kip una own.
41007010	"Bikos Mosis sey, 'Mak yu respet yor papa and mama' and 'Enibodi wey kos en papa or mama, dem must kil-am.'
41007011	"Bot if enibodi tel en papa and mama sey, 'Di moni wey I sopoz giv yu, I don giv God,'

41007015	"Nor bi wetin enta insaid pesin bodi go mak am dirti for God eye, insted na wetin kom out from en mout, dey mak am dirti.
41007016	"Enibodi wey get ear, mak e hear wetin I dey tok."
41007017	Wen Jisos liv di pipol enta haus, en disaipols kon ask am abaut di parabol.
41007018	E kon tel dem, "Na so una fool rish? Una nor no sey enitin wey from outsaid enta pesin bele nor go fit mak am dirti for God eye?
41007019	"Bikos nor bi di pesin heart e dey enta, na en bele and e go shit am komot. (Dis won min sey all fud dey klin.)"
41007020	Jisos kon sey, "Wetin kom out from insaid pesin, naim dey mak am dirti.
41007021	"Bikos to slip wit hu yu nor mari, to tif, to kil pesin,
41007022	to slip wit anoda pesin husban or wife, longtrot, evil tins, to disiv pesin, to dey misbihav, jelosi, to spoil anoda pesin, to kari bodi up and to du foolish tins, na from insaid pesin heart all dis bad-bad tins dey from kom.

41007024	Afta Jisos komot from der, e kon go di aria wey dem dey kol Tyre. Wen e enta won haus, e nor wont mak enibodi no sey e dey der, bot e nor fit hide.

41012001	Jisos kon tok to dem wit parabol: "Won man plant grape for en farm. E fence am roun, dig wer dem go dey press di wine put, den kon build big haus wey gaid go dey stay. E haya am giv tenants wey go dey kare for di place kon travol go far.
41012002	"Wen havest taim rish, e send won of en savant go mit di tenants mak dem gi-am en own share for di havest.
41012003	"Bot di tenants seize di savant, beat am kon send am go bak wit empti hand.
41012004	"Di man stil send anoda savant go mit dem. Dem nak en head kon beat am enihaw.
41012005	"E send anoda won again, dem kon kil-am. Na so dem beat and kil oda savants wey e send tu.
41012006	"Di man get won pikin wey e luv wel-wel and na dis won rimain for am to send. At last, e kon send am go mit dem dey tok for en maind sey, 'As dis won bi my pikin, dem go respet am.'
41012007	"Bot wen di tenants si-am dey kom, dem kon sey, 'Na di owna pikin dey kom so. Mak wi kil-am, so dat wi go get all di propati for awasef.'
41012008	"So dem seize am, kil-am kon trow en bodi outsaid di farm.
41012009	"Na wetin una tink sey di farm owna go du? E go distroi doz tenant kon giv di farm to oda pipol.
41012010	"Una neva read God wod wey sey, 'Di stone wey di buildas rejet, don turn to di main stone?'
41012011	"Dis na wetin God du and e gud for awa eye wel-wel.'"
41012012	Naw, dem won kon arres am, bot dem dey fear di pipol, bikos dem no sey Jisos tok dis parabol against dem. So dem kon waka liv am.
41012013	Dem send som Farisi and Herod pipol, mak dem faind way to kash Jisos wit wetin e go tok.
41012014	Wen dem mit am, dem kon ask am, "Tisha, wi no sey yu dey tok trut, yu nor dey du wayo and yu dey tish di trut abaut God way. E gud mak wi dey pay tax giv Caesar, abi mak wi nor pay?"
41012015	Bot Jisos no dia wayo, so e tel dem, "Why una dey test mi? Mak una bring won koin mak I si."
41012016	So dem bring won koin and Jisos ask dem, "Wish pesin face and name dey di moni so?" Dem ansa, "Na Caesar own."
41012017	Jisos tel dem, "Mak una giv Caesar di tins wey bi Caesar own and mak una giv God di tins wey bi God own." Dem sopraiz wel-wel for wetin Jisos tok.
41012018	Di Sadusi pipol (wey nor biliv sey pipol go wak-up from deat) kom mit Jisos tel am,
41012019	"Tisha, Mosis rite giv us sey: 'If man broda die and en wife nor born for am, en broda must mari di wuman, mak dem for born shildren for di broda wey don die.'
41012020	"E get sevun brodas. Di first won mari and wen e die, e nor get shildren.
41012021	"Di sekon won kon mari di wuman and e nor stil get pikin bifor e die and na so e hapun for di ted won.
41012022	"No won for di sevun brodas wey mari di wuman get pikin. At last, di wuman tu kon die.
41012023	"For di taim wey pipol go wak-up from deat, na wish pesin wife di wuman go kon bi, as e bi sey all di sevun brodas mari am?"
41012024	Jisos ansa dem, "Una nor no sey una dey disiv unasef, bikos una nor no God wod and en pawa.
41012025	"Wen pipol wak-up from deat, dem nor go mari again, insted dem go bi laik angels for hevun.
41012026	"Naw, for di mata abaut pipol wey go wak-up, una neva read for di book wey Mosis rite abaut di bush wey fire dey burn and haw God tel Mosis, 'Na Mi bi Abraham, Izik and Jakob God'?
41012027	"God nor bi God for di pipol wey don die, bot na for di pipol wey dey alaif. Na big mistak una dey mak so!"
41012028	So, won man wey sabi di law kon dey hear dem dey argue. Wen e si sey Jisos dey ansa dem wel, e kon ask am, "Wish komandment big pas?"
41012029	Jisos ansa am, "Na dis bi di komandment wey big pas: 'Mak una listin, Izrel pipol, di Oga, awa God na won e bi.
41012030	'Mak una luv God una Oga wit all una heart, soul and all una pawa.'
41012031	"Di sekon won na, 'Mak una luv una nebor as una luv unasef.' E nor get eni komandment wey big pas dis tu."
41012032	Di man wey dey tish di law kon tel Jisos, "Na tru, Tisha. Yu dey koret for wetin yu tok, na onli God bi Oga and no oda god dey apart from am.
41012033	"To luv God wit all awa heart, maind and pawa and to luv awa nebor as awasef big pas all di sakrifais and ofrins wey pesin fit giv God."
41012034	Wen Jisos si sey di man tink wel bifor e ansa, e kon tel di man, "Yu nor dey far from God Kindom." From dat taim, nobodi get di maind to ask am eni kweshon again.
41012035	As Jisos dey tish for di Tempol varanda, e kon sey, "Why e bi sey di law tishas dey sey Kraist na David pikin?
41012036	"Di Holi Spirit pawa mak David tok sey, 'God tel my Oga, sidan for my rite hand ontil I go put yor enimis unda yor leg.'
41012037	"If David ensef kol Kraist, 'Oga,' haw Kraist go kon tak bi en pikin again?" Di pipol wey gada kon dey listin to am wit hapines.
41012038	Wen Jisos dey tish, e kon sey, 'Mak una dey kareful abaut di pipol wey sabi di law. Dem laik to dey waka abaut wit long klot and dem laik loud gritin for market,
41012039	di chair wey beta pas for sinagog and high tabol for parti, na der dem dey laik sidan put.
41012040	"Wuman wey en husban don die, dem dey kolet en propati and dem dey pray long praya mak pipol for si dem. Na dia ponishment go wos pas."
41012041	Den, Jisos sidan face di ofrin box, dey luk as pipol dey put moni insaid. Meni rish pipol kon dey put plenti moni insaid.
41012042	Won poor wuman wey e husban don die kon kom, put tu koins wey nor rish won penni for insaid di box.
41012043	Jisos kon kol en disaipols sey, "I tel una tru wod, dis poor wuman wey e husban don die put moni wey pas di oda pipol own.
41012044	"Bikos di oda pipol giv dia ofrin from di plenti moni wey dem get, bot dis wuman, as e poor rish, put evritin wey e get for life."
41013001	As Jisos dey komot from di Tempol varanda, won of en disaipol kon sey. "Tisha, si dis fain-fain stone wey dem tak build dis haus!"
41013002	Jisos kon ansa, "Una dey si all dis big haus? Dem nor go ivun liv won stone on-top anoda. All of dem go skata!"
41013003	As Jisos sidan for Mount Olives wey face di Tempol, Pita, James, Jon and Andru kom mit am wen odas nor dey and dem kon sey,
41013004	"Mak yu tel us wish taim dis tins go hapun and wetin go bi di sign to show sey di taim for dis tins to hapun, don rish?"
41013005	Jisos ansa dem, "Mak una tak kare, so dat nobodi go disiv una.
41013006	"Meni pipol go kom wit my name sey dem bi Jisos and dem go disiv meni pipol.
41013007	"Wen una hear abaut war wey dey hapun and rumor sey war won hapun, mak una nor fear. All dis tins must hapun, bot di end for di wold neva rish.
41013008	"Difren kontris and kindoms go fite ish oda. Eartquake and hunga go dey for meni place. Bot wen di wahala won start, e go bi laik wen wuman won born.

41013010	"Bifor di wold go end, pipol must first prish di gospol for evri kontri for dis wold.
41013011	"Wen dem arres una kari go kourt, mak una nor wori abaut wetin una go tok. God go giv una wetin to tok for dat taim, bikos nor bi una go tok, bot na di Holi Spirit go du-am.
41013012	"Broda go betray en broda mak dem kil-am. Papa go sel en pikin giv dem tu. Shildren go betray dia papa and mama and dem go kil dem.
41013013	"Evribodi go hate una bikos of my name. Bot di pesin wey go fit bear rish end, go dey save."
41013014	"Wen una si wetin nor sopoz hapun dey hapun for di Holi Place (mak di pesin wey dey read, no wetin dis wod min), den doz wey dey Judea, must run go mountin.
41013015	"Mak di pesin wey dey on-top haus nor kom dan or go insaid en haus go kolet enitin.

41013019	"Bikos wen dis tins go dey hapun, di kaind sofa wey go dey, neva dey since wen God kreate dis wold and dat kaind sofa, nor go dey again.
41013020	"If God nor kut doz days short, nobodi go save. Bot bikos of di pipol wey God don shuz, E don mak doz days short.
41013021	"Dat taim, if enibodi tel una, 'Luk! Mak una si Jisos for here!' or 'Si-am for der!', mak una nor biliv dem.
41013022	"Bikos fake kraists and profets go kom and dem go du signs and mirakols wey bi laik majik to disiv pipol. If to sey e posibol, dem go disiv di pipol wey God don shuz.
41013023	"Mak una tak kare! I don tel una evritin bifor di taim go rish."
41013024	"Bot for dat taim, afta di sofa, di sun go dak and di moon nor go shine again.
41013025	"Di stars go fal from hevun and di pawa wey dey hol di skai, go shake.
41013026	"Den evribodi go si Man Pikin dey kom from insaid kloud wit strong pawa and glori.
41013027	"Den, God go send en angels go gada di pipol wey E don shuz from di for kona for di wold go rish hevun."
41013028	"Mak una learn wetin dis fig tri parabol min: Wen en bransh don dey soft and en leaf dey fal komot, mak una no sey dry season don near.
41013029	"So wen unasef si dis tins dey hapun, mak una no sey di taim wey Man Pikin go kom, don near.
41013030	"I tel una tru wod, di pipol for dis taim nor go die finish bifor all dis tins go hapun.
41013031	"Hevun and eart go vanish, bot my wod go dey foreva."
41013032	"Di day or di taim wen dis tins go hapun, nobodi no am, ivun angels for hevun nor no and God Pikin sef nor no tu. Na onli di Papa, for hevun no am.
41013033	"Mak una dey wosh and shine una eye, bikos una nor no wen di taim go rish.
41013034	"E go bi laik wen man dey travol go far. E liv en haus mak en savant luk am, giv dem wok to du kon tel di gateman mak e wosh en haus.
41013035	"So mak una shine una eye, bikos una nor no wen di haus owna go kom bak- weda na for evenin, nite, mornin or wen day don break.
41013036	"If not, e go fit kom bak wen una nor espet and e go mit una dey slip.
41013037	"Wetin I dey tel una so, I dey tel evribodi. So mak una shine una eye!"
41014001	Tu days bifor Passova and di Bread wey nor get yist Fist, di prist oga dem and di law tishas kon dey faind as dem go tak arres Jisos, mak dem for kil-am.

41014003	Wen Jisos dey Betani for Saimon haus (wey get leprosi bifor), e sidan wit dem to chop, naim won wuman bring oil insaid alabasta box kom, di oil dear wel-wel and dey sent fine. Afta e don opun di kontena, e pour di oil for Jisos head.

41015001	For earli mornin afta dem don plan wetin dem go du Jisos, di prist oga dem wit di law tishas and di Sanhedrin, tie am kon tak am go mit Pilate.

41015021	Di sojas kon fos Saimon, won man from Syrene, wey jos dey enta di tawn, mak e kari Jisos kros. (Di man na Alexander and Rufus papa.)

41015029	Pipol wey dey waka pas kon dey shake dia head and dey tok bad abaut am sey, "Eehen! Yu wey sey, yu go fit distroi di Tempol kon build am again for tiri days.

41015031	Ivun di prist oga dem and di law tishas dey laff Jisos for wer dem sidan, dey sey, "E save oda pipol, bot e nor fit save ensef!
41015032	"Kraist, wey sey e bi Izrel king, mak e kom dan from di kros naw mak wi si-am, so dat wi go biliv!" Doz wey dem nail for kros wit am kon dey kos am tu.
41015033	Wen twef o' klok for aftanoon rish, daknes kon kova di kontri ontil tiri o' klok for aftanoon.
41015034	Aroun tiri o' klok, Jisos kon shaut sey, "Eloi! Eloi! Lama Sabaktani?" Wey min, "My God! My God! Wetin mak Yu abandon mi?"
41015035	Wen som pipol wey stand near der hear wetin e tok, dem kon sey, "Listin. E dey kol Elija!"
41015036	Den won pesin run kom wit foam kon soak am insaid bita wine, den e put am for stik giv Jisos mak e drink, den e kon sey, "Mak una liv am! Mak wi si weda Elija go kom save am."
41015037	Bot Jisos shaut again, den e kon die.
41015038	So di kurtain for di Tempol kon tear into tu from top go rish botom.
41015039	Wen di soja wey stand for Jisos front si haw e tak die, e kon sey, "Tru-tru dis man na God Pikin!"
41015040	Som wimen dey der dey luk from far. Dem bi Mary Magdalene, Mary wey bi Joses, James and Salome mama.
41015041	For di taim wen Jisos dey Galili, dis wimen dey folo and help am. Meni oda wimen wey folo am kom from Jerusalem, dey der tu.
41015042	Wen evenin don rish for di day bifor di Sabat,
41015043	Josef wey kom from Arimatia, wey bi Ju kansol memba, wey dey wait for God Kindom and pipol dey respet am wel-wel, go mit Pilate kon ask for Jisos bodi.
41015044	Pilate sopraiz sey Jisos don die. So e kol di soja kon ask am weda e don tey wen Jisos die.

41015047	Mary Magdalene and Mary wey bi Joses mama dey luk and dem si wer dem bere Jisos put.
41016001	Wen Sabat Day don pas, Mary Magdalene, Mary wey bi James and Salome mama kon buy spices wey dey sent wel-wel, mak dem go rub am for Jisos bodi, mak e nor for smel.
41016002	For earli mornin on Sunday, as sun jos dey kom out, dem kon go di place wey dem bere Jisos put.
41016003	Dem kon dey ask ish oda as dem dey go sey, "Hu go help us rol di stone komot from di grave mout?"
41016004	Bot wen dem luk, dem si sey, dem don alredi rol di stone komot.
41016005	As dem enta, dem si won man wey wear white klot sidan for di rite side and fear kon kash dem.
41016006	Bot e tel dem, "Mak una nor fear. Una dey faind Jisos wey kom from Nazaret, wey dem kil. God don raiz-am from deat! E nor dey here again. Mak una luk di place wey dem put am bifor.
41016007	"Mak una go tel en disaipols and Pita sey, Jisos don go Galili go wait for dem. Una go si-am for der, as e tel una bifor."
41016008	Dem kom out kon run from di grave side, bikos dem sopraiz and fear kon kash dem. Dem nor fit tel enibodi enitin, bikos dem stil dey fear.
41016009	[For earli mornin on Sunday, afta Jisos don wak-up, e first apier to Mary Magdalene wey e driv sevun dimon komot for en bodi.
41016010	For wer di pipol wey dey folo Jisos dey mourn and krai dey, Mary Magdalene kon go tel dem wetin hapun.

41016013	Dem go bak go tel di res pipol, bot di pipol nor stil biliv dem.
41016014	Den Jisos kon apier to di ilevun disaipols wen dem dey chop. E kon shaut giv dem, since dem nor biliv, bikos of dia strong heart.
41016015	Jisos komand dem sey, "Mak una enta evriwer for di wold go prish di gospol giv evribodi.
41016016	"Enibodi wey biliv and dem baptize am, God go save am, bot enibodi wey nor biliv, God go kondem am.

41016018	dem go fit hol snake and if dem drink poison, e nor go du dem enitin; dem go put dia hand for sik pipol bodi and di pipol go wel."

42001008	E kom rish Zekaraya famili turn to du prist wok for di Tempol

42001011	God angel apier to Zekaraya for di alta side wer dem dey burn insent.

42001015	bikos God go yuz am wel-wel. E nor go drink wine or strong drink, bot di Holi Spirit go dey insaid am, ivun bifor dem go born am.

42001017	"E go first kom wit Elija spirit and pawa, bifor di Oga ensef go kom. E go mak papa setol wit dia shildren and pipol wey nor dey obey God bifor, e go mak dem obey am naw, so dat dem go dey redi to mit am for hevun."
42001018	Zekaraya ask di angel, "Haw I go tak no sey wetin yu tok so go hapun? Bikos mi and my wife don old wel-wel."

42001023	Wen en taim to wok insaid di Tempol finish, e kon go haus.

42002036	Won profetess dey, wey en name bi Anna, Fanuel dota, wey kom from Asher famili. E don old wel-wel and e mari en husban for sevun years, bifor di man die.

42003001	Tiberius Caesar don dey rule for fiftin years wen Pontius Pilate bi govnor for Judea and Herod dey rule Galili, en broda Filip dey rule Iturea and Trakonitis aria and Lysanias dey rule Abilene.
42003002	For dat taim, na Annas and Kaifas bi di High Prists. So God kon tok to Jon, wey bi Zekaraya pikin, for insaid desert.
42003003	Jon kon go all di aria wey dey roun Jordan Riva dey prish sey mak pipol turn from dia sin kom mit God and mak dem baptaiz, so dat God go forgiv dem.
42003004	As Profet Isaia tok for di book wey e rite sey, "Won vois dey shaut for insaid desert sey: 'Priper di way for di Oga and mak en road strate.
42003005	"Evri place wey low, God go mak am high and evri place wey high, God go mak am low, ben-ben road go strate, di road wey bad, go gud
42003006	and evribodi for dis wold go si God savashon.'"
42003007	So Jon tel di pipol wey kom mak e for baptaiz dem sey, "Una wey bi snake shildren! Hu warn una mak una run komot from God ponishment wey dey kom?
42003008	"Naw, mak una bear frut wey go show sey una don rili turn from sin kom mit God, mak una nor start to sey, 'Abraham na awa papa.' Bikos God fit tak dis stones wey dey for groun tak mak pikin for Abraham!
42003009	"Ivun naw sef, di axe don redi to kut di tri wey nor dey bear beta frut, dem go kut am dan kon trow am insaid fire."
42003010	So di pipol kon ask am, "Wetin wi go du naw?"
42003011	Jon ansa dem, "Di pesin wey get tu klot must giv won to pesin wey nor get at-all and di pesin wey get fud must share wit pesin wey nor get."
42003012	Tax koletors tu waka kom mak Jon for baptaiz dem and dem kon ask am, "Tisha, wetin wi go du?"
42003013	Jon tel dem, "Mak una nor kolet moni pas di won wey di law tok."
42003014	Den som sojas kon stil ask am, "Wot of us? Wetin wi go du?" E tel dem, "Mak una nor yuz fos kolet moni from enibodi hand or lai for enibodi head and mak una salari, rish una."
42003015	All di pipol kon dey wonda weda Jon, naim bi di Mezaya wey dem dey wait for.
42003016	Jon ansa dem, "Na ordinari wota I tak dey baptaiz una, bot di pesin wey big pas mi, dey kom, I nor rish hu go luz di rope wey dey en shu. E go baptaiz una wit di Holi Spirit and fire.
42003017	"E hol shovel for hand to havest di corn kip for en store, bot e go burn di corn kanda wit fire wey nor dey kwensh."
42003018	Na so Jon prish di Gud News for di pipol.
42003019	Bot wen Jon tel Herod wey bi govnor sey, God dey ves wit am, bikos of en broda wife, Herodias, wey e mari and all di bad-bad tins wey e du,
42003020	Herod tak all dis join di vesnashon wey e get for Jon, so e kon lock am for prizin.
42003021	So wen all di pipol don baptaiz, Jisos ensef kon baptaiz tu. Wen e dey pray, hevun opun,
42003022	di Holi Spirit kon kom dan for en head laik dove. Den won vois tok from hevun sey, "Yu bi my Pikin wey I luv wel-wel and yu dey mak bele swit mi."
42003023	Jisos start en ministri wen e bi tati years. Evribodi no am as Josef pikin, wey Heli born.
42003024	Heli na Mattat pikin, wey Levi born. Levi na Melchi pikin, wey bi Jannai pikin and na Josef bi Jannai papa.
42003025	Josef na Mattatias pikin wey bi Amos pikin, wey bi Nahum pikin, wey bi Esli pikin, wey bi Naggai pikin.

42004001	Di Holi Spirit enta Jisos bodi kon kari am from Jordan Riva go insaid widanes.
42004002	For der, devol kon tempt am for forti days. Dat taim, Jisos dey fast, so e nor chop fud, bot afta e fast finish, e kon dey hungri.
42004003	Devol kon tel am, "If na tru sey yu bi God Pikin, mak yu komand dis stone mak e turn to fud."
42004004	Den Jisos ansa, "God wod sey, 'Nor bi onli fud man sopoz to chop for dis wold, bot na evri wod wey God tok.'"
42004005	Den devol tak Jisos go on-top won mountin kon show am all di kindom wey dey dis wold.
42004006	den e tel am, "I go giv yu all dis place and all di onor wey folo am as yor kindom, bikos dem don giv am to mi and I fit gi-am to enibodi wey I wont.
42004007	"So, if yu bow dan woship mi, I go giv yu evritin."
42004008	Jisos ansa, "God wod sey, 'Na onli God yu must woship and serv.'"
42004009	Den devol tak Jisos go Jerusalem kon mak am stand on-top di place wer high pas for di Tempol kon tel am, "If yu rili bi God Pikin, mak yu jump go dan,
42004010	bikos God wod sey, 'God go tel en angels mak dem gaid yu'
42004011	and, 'Dem go kari yu for dia hand, so dat yu nor go yuz yor leg nak stone.'"
42004012	Jisos ansa am, "God wod sey, 'Mak yu nor test God wey bi yor Oga.'"
42004013	So wen devol don tempt Jisos finish, e kon liv am ontil anoda taim.
42004014	As di Holi Spirit pawa ful Jisos bodi, e kon go bak to Galili and en stori bigin spread for di hol aria.
42004015	E bigin tish for dia sinagog and evribodi kon dey praiz God.
42004016	Afta, Jisos go Nazaret wer e for grow up, e enta di sinagog for Sabat Day as e dey always du and e kon get up mak e read.
42004017	Dem gi-am di book wey Profet Isaia rite. Jisos kon opun am rish di place wey dem rite sey,
42004018	"God Spirit dey my bodi, bikos E don anoint mi mak I prish Gud News giv poor pipol. E send mi mak I prish fridom giv pipol wey dey prizin and mak blind pipol for si. E stil sey mak I fri doz wey dem dey opres
42004019	and mak I annouce sey di taim wen God won save en pipol, don rish."
42004020	Jisos klose di book kon gi-am bak to di pesin wey dey hol am, den e go sidan. So evribodi wey dey di sinagog kon dey luk am.
42004021	Den Jisos tel dem, "Today, di tins wey dem rite for God wod for wer I read, don hapun, jos as una hear am wen I dey read am."
42004022	Evribodi dey tok gud abaut Jisos, dem sopraiz for di swit-swit wod wey kom out from en mout. So dem kon ask, "Dis nor bi Josef pikin?"
42004023	Jisos tel dem, "I no sey una go kwote proverb for mi sey, 'Doktor, mak yu kior yorsef!' And una go sey, 'For here wey bi yor home-tawn, wi won mak yu du wetin wi hear sey yu du for Kapanum.'"
42004024	Jisos stil sey, "Mak I tel una tru wod, profet nor dey get respet for en home-tawn.
42004025	"Bot I tel una di trut, wimen wey dia husban don die meni for Izrel for Elija taim, wen God stop rain for tiri and haf years and beta hunga kon dey evriwer.
42004026	"Bot God nor send Elija go mit eni of doz wimen, esept won wuman wey en husban die for Zarepat insaid Sidon.
42004027	"Pipol wey get leprosi meni for Izrel for profet Elisha taim, bot God nor heal eni won esept Naaman, wey kom from Syria."
42004028	Wen dem hear dis tins, all di pipol for di sinagog kon dey ves.
42004029	Dem push Jisos komot from di tawn kon tak am go di hil wey dia tawn dey on-top, mak dem for trow am dan.
42004030	Bot Jisos pas dia senta, waka komot.
42004031	So Jisos kon go Kapanum, wey dey Galili and e bigin tish pipol for Sabat Day.
42004032	Dem sopraiz wel-wel for en tishin, bikos e dey tok wit autoriti.
42004033	Insaid di sinagog, won man wey evil spirit dey en bodi kon dey shaut,
42004034	"Abeg, mak yu liv us alone, Jisos wey kom from Nazaret! Yu don kom distroi us? I no hu yu bi, yu bi God savant wey holi."
42004035	Bot Jisos tel am: "Mak yu shut up! Yu dimon, komot for en bodi." Di dimon trow di man for groun for dia front kon komot for en bodi, bot di man nor wound.
42004036	Di pipol sopraiz kon dey ask ish oda, "Wetin dey hapun so? Dis man dey yuz God pawa tak komand dimon and dem dey obey am!"
42004037	So di news abaut Jisos kon spread enta di hol aria for Galili.
42004038	Afta Jisos komot for di sinagog, e enta Saimon haus. Saimon wife mama get fiva and dem kon beg Jisos make e heal am.
42004039	So Jisos stand near di wuman kon komand di fiva komot for en bodi. Kwik-kwik, di wuman get up, bigin kare for Jisos and di odas wey dey di haus.
42004040	As day dey dak, evribodi wey get pipol wey nor wel kon bring dem kom mit Jisos. E tosh dem for head and dem kon wel.
42004041	Dimons dey shaut dey komot from meni pipol bodi, dey sey, "Yu bi God Pikin!" Bot Jisos warn dem mak dem nor tok, bikos dem no sey, naim bi di Mezaya.
42004042	Wen day break, Jisos komot go won place wer nobodi dey. Bot pipol faind am rish der and dem kon dey trai to hol am mak e nor for liv dem.
42004043	Bot Jisos tel dem, "I must prish dis Gud News abaut God Kindom giv pipol wey dey oda tawns, bikos na wetin God send mi kom du, bi dat."

42005001	Jisos stand near Genesaret and pipol gada mak dem for hear God wod.
42005002	E si tu kenu for di wotasaid, bot di fishamen wey get dem, don kom dan dey wosh dia net.
42005003	E enta insaid won kenu wey bi Saimon Pita own kon tel am mak e push di kenu enta wota smol. Den Jisos kon sidan dey tish di pipol from di kenu.
42005004	Wen e don tok finish, e kon tel Saimon, "Push di kenu go wer deep pas for di wota, mak una for fit kash fish."
42005005	Saimon ansa, "Oga, wi dey here from nite til day-break and wi nor kash enitin. Bot as yu tok, wi go put awa net insaid wota."
42005006	So, dem trow dia net insaid wota and dem kash meni fish sotey dia net kon start to tear.
42005007	So, dem kon du sign giv di oda pipol wey dey folo dem wok, mak dem kom help dem. Wen dem put all di fish insaid di tu kenu, di kenu dem kon dey won sink.
42005008	Wen Saimon si wetin hapun, e kon nil dan for Jisos front dey sey, "Abeg, nor near mi Oga, bikos I bi sina."

42005011	So wen dem don push dia kenu rish groun for di wotasaid, dem liv evritin kon folo Jisos.

42005013	So Jisos tosh di man kon sey, "I laik to du-am. 'Oya! Mak yor bodi klin naw!'" At wons, di leprosi komot for di man bodi.

42005015	Bot di news abaut Jisos kon spread pas bifor and meni pipol kom mit am mak dem for fit hear en wod and mak e for heal dem.
42005016	Bot Jisos komot go pray for widanes, wer pipol nor dey.
42005017	Won day, wen Jisos dey tish, som Farisi pipol and di law tishas kon kom from all di vilage wey dey Galili, Judea and Jerusalem, dem sidan near Jisos and God pawa dey wit am to heal pipol.
42005018	Som men kari won man for bed wey nor fit waka, kom. Dem kon dey trai to kari am enta di haus kom mit Jisos,
42005019	bot bikos pipol meni, dem nor fit kari am pas, so dem kon opun di zink for di haus top, drop di man wit di bed smol-smol, til e rish Jisos front for di pipol senta.
42005020	Wen Jisos si haw dia fate big rish, e kon tel di man, "My frend, I forgiv yu all yor sins."
42005021	So di law tishas and di Farisi pipol kon dey tink for dia maind sey, "Hu bi dis man wey dey shalenge God laik dis? Hu fit forgiv sin esept God?"
42005022	Jisos no wetin dem dey tink, so e ask dem, "Why una dey tink laik dis sef?
42005023	"Wish won eazi to tok? 'I forgiv yu yor sin?' or 'Get up mak yu waka?'
42005024	"Bot mak una for no sey Man Pikin get pawa for dis wold to forgiv sin, e kon tel di man wey nor fit waka, 'I tel yu, get up, kari yor bed mak yu dey go haus.'"
42005025	At wons, di man kon get up for dia present, kari di bed wey e laidan put bifor kon dey praiz God as e dey go haus.

42005028	Levi get up, liv evritin kon folo am.

42005031	Jisos ansa dem, "Pipol wey wel nor nid doktor, na onli doz wey nor wel, nid am.

42005034	So Jisos ansa dem, "Yu espet sey mak pipol wey kom marage dey hungri wen di man wey dey mari dey der?
42005035	Bot taim go rish wen di man wey dey mari nor go dey wit dem, dat taim, dem go fast."
42005036	E stil tel dem won parabol: "Nobodi dey tear new klot tak pash old won. If e du laik dat, e go fit spoil di new klot and di new klot pisis nor go mash di old won.
42005037	"And nobodi dey pour new wine insaid old wine bag. If e du laik dat, di new wine go tear di bag, di wine go trowey and di bag go skata.
42005038	"Insted, pipol sopoz pour new wine insaid new wine bag.
42005039	"Nobodi go laik to drink new wine afta e don drink old wine. Bikos e go sey, 'Na di old wine beta pas.'"

42006024	"Bot kos dey una head, una wey get moni wel-wel naw, bikos una don alredi get una riwod.

42006031	"Mak una du for pipol as una wont mak dem du for una.

42006033	"And if una du gud for onli doz wey dey du gud for una, wetin go mak God bless una? Ivun sinas dey du di same tin tu.
42006034	"And if una borow pesin moni wen una no sey e go fit pay una bak, wetin go mak God bless una? Sinas sef dey borow moni giv sinas, so dat dem go pay dem bak dia koret moni.
42006035	"Bot mak una luv una enimis kon du gud and mak una nor espet enitin bak wen una borow enibodi somtin. Na dis go mak God pay una bak and una go bi en shildren, bikos God ensef dey du gud for wiked pipol and doz wey nor dey sey tank yu.
42006036	"So, mak una dey show mesi, jos as una Papa dey show mesi.
42006037	Mak una nor joj oda pipol, so dat God nor go joj una. Mak una nor kondem odas, so dat God nor go kondem una. Mak una forgiv odas and God go forgiv una.
42006038	"Mak una giv pipol wey nor get and God go giv una wetin rili big, E go pack am wel-wel and di tins go ova ful. God go pour all dis tins for una life. Bot na as una tak giv odas, na so God go tak giv una tu."

42006042	"Haw yu go tak tel yor broda sey, 'Broda, mak I rimov di dirti wey dey yor eye, bot yu nor dey si di wud wey dey yor own eye? Yu wey dey pritend, mak yu first komot di wud for yor eye, den yu go si wel to fit rimov yor broda own.'

42006044	bikos na frut wey tri bear, naim pipol dey tak no di kaind tri wey e bi. Pipol nor dey plok fig or grape from shuku-shuku tri.

42006046	"Why una dey kol mi, 'Oga' and una nor dey du wetin I tel una?

42007033	"Wen Jon di Baptist kom, e nor chop fud or drink wine, bot una sey, 'E get dimon!'

42007035	"Bot doz wey get wisdom, no sey evritin abaut am, na trut."
42007036	Won Farisi kon invait Jisos kom chop for en haus, so Jisos enta di Farisi haus kon sidan.
42007037	Den, wen won wuman from dat tawn wey bi sina hear sey Jisos dey chop for di Farisi haus, e kon bring won fine oil botol, wey dey sent wel-wel, kom.
42007038	E nil dan for Jisos front dey krai and e kon dey wet Jisos leg wit di tears from en eye. E klin Jisos leg wit en hair kon kiss dem, den e pour di oil put.
42007039	Wen di Farisi wey invait Jisos si wetin dey hapun, e kon tok for en maind sey, "If dis man na profet tru-tru, e for no sey dis wuman wey dey tosh am so, na sina e bi."
42007040	Jisos kon tel di Farisi, "Saimon, e get wetin I won tel yu." Saimon kon sey, "Tisha, I dey listin."
42007041	"E get won man wey get tu savant wey dey hol am moni, won dey hol am faiv tazon and di oda won, faiv ondred.
42007042	"Wen tu of dem nor fit pay di moni bak, e kon sey mak dem forget abaut di moni. Afta dat, wish of dem go laik di man pas?"
42007043	Saimon ansa, "Na di won wey en moni big pas." Jisos kon tel am, "Wetin yu tok, koret."
42007044	Den Jisos luk di wuman kon ask Saimon, 'Yu dey si dis wuman? I enta yor haus, yu nor giv mi wota wosh leg, bot di wuman don wosh my leg wit en tears kon tak en hair klin am.
42007045	"Wen I enta yor haus, yu nor kiss or grit mi as awa tradishon bi, bot since I enta, dis wuman neva stop to kiss my leg.
42007046	"Yu nor pour oil for my head, bot dis wuman don anoint my leg wit oil wey dey sent wel-wel.
42007047	"Mak I tel yu, I don forgiv dis wuman en meni sins, so en luv don big wel-wel, bot di pesin wey dem forgiv smol sin, en luv go smol."
42007048	Den Jisos tel di wuman, "I forgiv yu all yor sins."
42007049	Bot di pipol wey sidan dey chop wit Jisos kon dey tel ish oda, "Hu bi dis man wey dey forgiv sin?"
42007050	So, Jisos tel di wuman, "Yor fate don save yu; mak peace folo yu go."
42008001	Afta som taim, Jisos kon travol go all di tawn and vilage dey prish di Gud News abaut God Kindom. Di twef apostols
42008002	and som wimen wey Jisos driv evil spirit and difren siknes komot for dia bodi, go wit am: Mary (wey dem dey kol Magdalene), wey Jisos driv sevun dimon komot for en bodi,
42008003	Joanna, Shuza wife (wey bi managa for Herod haus), Susanna and meni oda wimen wey dey yuz dia own moni sopot Jisos and en disaipols.
42008004	Meni pipol gada roun Jisos and som stil dey kom from difren place, so e kon tel dem dis parabol:
42008005	"Won man go plant sid for en farm. As e dey plant, som fal for road, pipol mash dem pas and birds kon chop dem.
42008006	"Som wey fal for wer stones dey kon grow and die, bikos wota nor dey dat groun.
42008007	"Odas fal for wer shuku-shuku dey and wen dem grow, di shuku-shuku grow tu, kon shuk dem die.
42008008	"Bot di wons wey fal for beta groun, grow kon bear pas ondred sid." Den Jisos sey, "Enibodi wey get ear, mak e hear!"
42008009	Den en disaipols ask am wetin di parabol min.
42008010	Jisos ansa dem, "Una get di shanse to no God Kindom sikrit, bot dis oda pipol, na onli parabol dem go tak hear am, so dat as dem dey luk, dem nor go si and as dem hear, dem nor go undastand.
42008011	"Na wetin di parabol min bi dis: Di sid na God wod.
42008012	"Di won wey fal for road, na di pipol wey hear God wod, bot devol kon tif am from dia heart, so dat dem nor go biliv and God nor go save dem.
42008013	"Di won wey fal for wer stones dey, na di pipol wey hear God wod kon risiv am wit hapines, bot dem nor get root. Dem biliv smol, bot wen wahala kom, dem nor biliv again.
42008014	"Di sid wey fal for shuku-shuku, na di pipol wey hear God wod, bot wahala, plenti propati and jolli-jolli for dis wold kon shuk dem, so di frut nor ivun ripe.
42008015	"Bot di sid wey fal for beta groun, na di pipol wey hear God wod, hol am wit beta maind, dey obey God and bear wahala, so dem kon bear plenti frut."
42008016	"Pesin nor go lite kandol kon tak bucket kova am or hide am unda bed, bot e go put am for wer pipol go si-am wen dem enta di haus.
42008017	"Bikos e nor get wetin pipol hide naw, wey God nor go bring out and wetin dey sikrit naw, God go bring am out for wer lite dey.
42008018	"So mak una listin wel-wel, bikos pesin wey get, God go gi-am more, bot pesin wey nor get, ivun di smol won wey e tink sey e get, God go tak am from en hand."
42008019	Jisos mama and en brodas kom mit am, bot dem nor fit go near am, bikos pipol plenti for der.
42008020	So pipol tel am, "Yor mama and brodas dey outsaid, dem won si yu."

42008022	Won day, Jisos and en disaipols enta kenu, den e tel dem, "Mak wi kros go di oda side for di riva." So dem kon go.
42008023	As dia kenu dey move for di wota, Jisos dey slip den strong briz start to dey blow and dem kon dey fear, bikos wota dey enta di kenu.
42008024	Dem kon tel Jisos, "Oga! Oga! Na die wi dey so!" Jisos get up, kon komand di briz mak e stop and di wota wey rof bifor, stop and evriwer kon kwayet.
42008025	Den Jisos ask dem, "Wer una fate dey?" Bot dem dey fear and sopraiz dey tel ish oda, "Wish kaind man bi dis sef? Ivun briz and wota dey obey am!"
42008026	Dem kon rish Gerasenes aria wey face Galili.
42008027	As Jisos kom dan from di kenu, won man wey get dimon wey dey di tawn kom mit am. E don tey wen dis man stop to wear klot or stay insaid haus, bot e dey stay for beria groun.
42008028	Wen e si Jisos, e fal for en front kon shaut, "Mak yu liv mi! Jisos, God Pikin, I beg yu, nor ponish mi!"

42008033	Di dimons komot for di man bodi go enta di pigs and all of dem kon rush enta di riva go die.

42008035	So di pipol run kom si wetin dey hapun and dem mit Jisos for der. Di man wey Jisos driv dimon komot for en bodi, don wel and e wear klot sidan near Jisos leg, so fear kon kash di pipol.
42008036	Pipol wey si wetin hapun, tel di tawn pipol haw Jisos heal di man wey get dimon bifor.

42008042	bikos e onli dota wey don rish twef years, dey die. As Jisos dey go di man haus, pipol kon dey waka jam am enihaw bikos dem plenti.
42008043	Won wuman dey among dem wey don dey mestrate for twef years naw, bikos nobodi fit heal am.

42011001	Won day Jisos dey pray for won place. Wen e pray finish, won of en disaipols kon tel am, "Oga! Mak yu tish us haw to pray, jos as Jon tish en disaipols.
42011002	So Jisos kon tel dem, "Wen una dey pray, mak una sey: 'Awa Papa wey dey for hevun, wi grit Yu, Mak yor kindom kom.
42011003	'Giv us di bread wey wi go chop today,
42011004	Mak Yu forgiv us awa sins, as wi dey forgiv doz wey du us bad. Nor let us enta temtashon.'"

42011007	"Den yor frend kon ansa from insaid haus, 'Mak yu nor disturb mi. I don lock my door and mi and my shildren dey slip. I nor go fit get up giv yu enitin naw.'

42011009	"So, I tel yu tru wod: Mak yu ask and God go giv yu, faind and yu go si wetin yu dey luk for, mak yu nok and di door go opun for yu.
42011010	"Bikos pesin wey ask, go get, pesin wey faind, go si wetin e dey faind and di pesin wey nok, di door go opun for am.
42011011	"Wish of una wey bi papa go giv en pikin snake, if e ask for fish?
42011012	"Or if di pikin ask for egg, una go gi-am skorpion?

42011014	Won day, Jisos kon driv dimon wey dey mak pesin nor fit tok komot for won man bodi. Wen di dimon don komot, di man bigin tok and di pipol sopraiz wel-wel.
42011015	Bot som of dem sey, "Belzibub wey bi dimon oga, na en pawa Jisos dey yuz tak driv dimons."

42011018	"So, if Satan kindom divide, haw en kindom go tak last? I dey ask una dis tin, bikos una dey sey na Belzibub pawa I tak dey driv dimons.
42011019	"If na Belzibub pawa I tak dey driv dimons, den na wish pawa una pikin dem dey yuz? So, na una pikin go joj una.
42011020	"Bot if na God pawa I tak dey driv dimon komot, naim bi sey God Kindom don rish wer una dey.

42011022	"Bot wen pesin wey get pawa pas am atak and win am, di pesin go kari all di tins wey di man tak dey protet ensef kon divide di propati wey rimain.

42011025	"Wen e kom bak kon si sey dem swip evriwer klin, arange am and nobodi dey stay der.

42011033	"Nobodi dey lite lamp put for unda basket or for wer pipol nor go fit si-am, bot dem go put am for wer pipol go si-am wen dem enta di haus.
42011034	"Na eye bi di lamp wey bodi get. If yor eye wel, lite go ful yor hol bodi, bot wen yor eye nor wel, na daknes go ful yor bodi.
42011035	"So mak sure sey wetin dey insaid yu, na lite, nor bi daknes.
42011036	"If lite ful yor bodi and daknes nor dey insaid at-all, e go shine wel-wel laik wen lamp dey shine for yor face."
42011037	As Jisos dey tok, won Farisi kol am kom en haus kon chop, so Jisos go sidan for wer dem go for chop.

42011042	"Kos dey una head! Una wey bi Farisi pipol! Una dey giv God won out of evri ten tins wey una get! "Bot una dey forget pipol wey nor get.

42011044	"Kos dey una head! Una bi laik grave wey pipol dey mash pas and dem nor no sey na grave."

42011046	Bot Jisos ansa am, "Kos dey una head! Una wey sabi di law wel-wel! Una kari heavi load put for pipol bak and una nor won ivun tak hand tosh di load!

42011052	"Kos dey una head! Una wey no di law wel-wel! Una don sieze di key wey dey mak pipol no di trut! Since una nor gri enta, una nor wont mak oda pipol enta tu."

42012001	Plenti pipol gada aroun Jisos kon dey waka jam won anoda, so Jisos kon tel en disaipols, "Mak una shine una eye wel-wel, bikos of di Farisi pipol wey dey pritend.

42012028	"If God dey dress grass, wey dey today and pipol go kut am trow for fire tomoro, dat God nor go fit kare for una? Una fate smol wel-wel-o-o!
42012029	"Mak una nor dey wori abaut wetin una go chop or drink.

42012053	"Papa go dey against en son and son go dey against en papa, mama go dey against en dota and dota go dey against en mama, husban-mama go dey against en pikin wife and wife go dey against en husban-mama."

42014001	For won Sabat day, wen Jisos go chop for won Farisi oga haus, di pipol kon dey luk am,

42015001	Enitaim Jisos dey prish, tax koletors and sinas dey kom listin to am.

42020001	Won day wen Jisos dey tish pipol for di Tempol, di prist oga dem and di law tishas kon mit am,
42020002	dey sey, "Mak yu tel us, na wish pawa yu tak dey du dis tins? Na hu giv yu di pawa sef?"
42020003	Jisos ansa dem, "Mak I stil ask una won kweshon and mak una ansa mi.
42020004	Jon baptism kom from hevun, abi na from pipol?"
42020005	Dem kon dey tok wit ish oda sey, "If wi sey na from hevun, e go sey, 'Den why una nor biliv am?'

42020029	"E get won famlili wey get sevun brodas. Di first won mari, bot dem nor born bifor di man die.
42020030	"Den di sekon won kon mari di wuman,
42020031	den di ted won, ontil numba sevun die tu, bot di wuman nor stil born for eni of dem.

42021001	For insaid di Tempol, Jisos kon si rish pipol dey put dia moni for ofrin box.
