42023033	Wen dem rish di place wey dem dey kol, "Di Skul," dem kon nail Jisos for kros wit di tu tif, won for en left and di oda for en rite side.
42023034	(Den Jisos kon sey, "Papa, mak Yu forgiv dem, bikos dem nor no wetin dem dey du.") So, di sojas kon gambol to no hu go tak Jisos klot.
42023035	Di pipol stil stand der dey luk, bot dia ledas dey laff Jisos sey, "E save oda pipol. Mak e save ensef if e bi di Mezaya wey God shuz!"
42023036	Di sojas stil dey laff Jisos and dem kon gi-am wine wey don sawa mak e drink,
42023037	den sey, "If yu bi di Ju pipol king, mak yu save yorsef!"
42023038	Dem kon rite on-top en kros sey, "Dis na, 'Ju Pipol King.'"
42023039	Won of di tif dey shaut for Jisos, "Nor bi yu bi di Mezaya? Mak yu save yorsef and us naw!"
42023040	Bot di oda tif kon shaut for di first tif, "Yu nor dey fear God as e bi sey na di same ponishment wi dey sofa?
42023041	"Na dis ponishment fit us, bikos na wetin wi du naim mak dem dey ponish us so. Bot dis man nor du eni bad tin."
42023042	Den e kon tel Jisos, "Wen yu rish yur kindom, mak yu rimemba mi!"
42023043	Jisos ansa am, "I tel yu di trut, today yu go dey wit mi for paradaiz."
42023044	By naw, twef o' klok don nearli rish for aftanun and daknes kon kova di hol kontri ontil tiri o' klok for dat aftanun,
42023045	bikos sun stop to shine. Di Tempol kurtain kon tear into tu.
42023046	So, Jisos shaut, "Papa, I put my spirit for yor hand!" Afta e tok finish, e kon die.
42023047	Wen di soja oga si wetin hapun, e kon praiz God sey, "Tru-tru, dis man na gud pesin!"
42023048	So wen all di pipol wey gada dey luk si wetin hapun, dem kon dey krai go dia haus.
42023049	And evribodi wey no Jisos bifor, stand for far and di wimen wey folo Jisos kom from Galili, si di tins wey hapun.
42023050	E get won man for di kansol, wey bi Josef and e kom from Arimatia wey dey Judea. E bi beta pesin wey dey du wetin God laik and e dey wait for di taim wen God Kindom go kom.
42023051	(E nor gri wit di oda kansol membas wit dia plan and for wetin dem du so.)
42023052	E go mit Pilate kon ask for Jisos dead bodi.
42023053	Den e kari di bodi from di kros, wrap am wit linen klot kon put am for di grave wey e dig insaid rock and dem neva bere enibodi for der bifor.
42023054	Dat day na Friday wen dem dey redi for Sabat serimoni.
42023055	Di wimen wey folo Jisos from Galili kon folo Josef go si di grave. So dem put Jisos bodi insaid.
42023056	Den di wimen go haus go priper beta perfume. Bot for Sabat Day, dem kon res as Mosis law tok.
42024001	For earli mornin for di first day for di wik, di wimen kari di perfume wey dem priper go di grave wer dem bere Jisos put.
42024002	Dem kon si sey dem don rol di stone komot from di grave mout,
42024003	bot wen dem enta insaid, dem nor si Jisos bodi for der.
42024004	As dem dey konfuz bikos of dis tin, dem kon si tu men wey dia klot dey shine laik lite and dem stand for kona.
42024005	Fear kash di wimen and dem kon face groun. Bot di men tel dem, "Why una dey faind pesin wey dey aliaf for wer dead bodi dey?
42024006	"E nor dey here again, God don wak-am! Una rimemba wetin e tel una wen e dey Galili sey,
42024007	'Dem must sel Man Pikin giv wiked pipol and dem go kil-am trowey and for di ted day, e go wak-up.'"
42024008	Den di wimen kon rimemba wetin Jisos tel dem,
42024009	so dem komot from di grave kon go tel di ilevun apostols and di res pipol wetin hapun.
42024010	Na Mary Magdalene, Joana, Mary wey bi James mama and di oda wimen wey dey wit dem, na dem tel di apostols all dis tins.
42024011	Bot dia wod nor min enitin to di apostols, so dem nor biliv di wimen.
42024012	Bot Pita kon get-up, run go di grave. E ben-dan luk insaid and e si onli di klot, den e kon go haus dey wonda wetin hapun.
42024013	Dat day, tu Jisos disaipols dey waka go won vilage wey dem dey kol Emmaus, wey nor tu far from Jerusalem.
42024014	Dem dey tok to ish oda abaut di tins wey hapun.
42024015	As dem dey tok, Jisos kon bigin waka wit dem,
42024016	(bot Jisos nor let dem no hu e bi.)
42024017	Den Jisos kon ask dem, "Na wetin mak una dey tok laik dis for road?" Dem kon stand for won place, dey sopraiz for am.
42024018	Den won of dem, wey en name bi Kleopas, kon ask am, "Na onli yu bi strenja for Jerusalem wey nor no di tins wey dey hapun since?"
42024019	Jisos ansa dem,"Wish tins?" Dem ansa, "Di tins abaut Jisos wey kom from Nazaret, won man wey wetin e dey tok and du show sey en na God profet
42024020	and haw awa prist oga dem and di pipol wey dey rule us kil-am trowey.
42024021	"Bot wi bin hope sey naim go fri Izrel and dis tins don hapun for tiri days naw.
42024022	"Som wimen wey dey wit us kon ivun sopraiz us. Dem go wer dem bere am put dis mornin
42024023	and dem nor si en bodi for der. Dem kom bak dey tok sey dem si angels wey tel dem sey Jisos dey alaif.
42024024	"Den som pipol wey dey wit us kon go di grave and dem si evritin as di wimen tok, bot dem nor si Jisos."
42024025	So Jisos tel dem, "Una nor get sense and una nor dey kwik biliv wetin all di profets tok.
42024026	"Dem nor tok sey di Mezaya go must sofa all dis tins and den e go enta en glori?"
42024027	Den e kon yuz wetin Mosis and all di profets rite tak tel dem wetin God tok abaut am for en wod.
42024028	As dem near di vilage wey dem dey go, Jisos kon du laik sey e won waka go front,
42024029	bot dem kon tel am, "Mak yu stay wit us, bikos evenin don nearli rish and day go soon dak." So Jisos enta di vilage kon folo dem stay.
42024030	E sidan for wer dem dey chop, tak bread, bless am kon divide am giv dem.
42024031	At wons dia eye opun and dem kon no am. Den e vanish from dia front.
42024032	Dem kon tel ish oda, "No wonda e bi laik sey fire dey burn insaid awa heart wen e dey tok wit us for road abaut God!"
42024033	So dem get up at wons go bak to Jerusalem. Dem kon si di ilevun apostols and di oda pipol wey dey wit dem
42024034	kon tel dem, "Jisos don rili wak-up and e don apier to Saimon!"
42024035	Den dem kon tok wetin hapun for road and haw dem tak no Jisos wen e divide di bread.
42024036	As dem stil dey tok, Jisos kon stand wit dem, tel dem, "Mak peace dey wit una."
42024037	Bot dem shok and fear kash dem, bikos dem tink sey na spirit dem dey si.
42024038	Den Jisos kon sey, "Why una dey fear and nor biliv?
42024039	"Mak una luk my hand and leg and mak una tosh mi: spirit nor get flesh and bone as una si sey I get."
42024040	Wen Jisos don tok dis won, e kon show dem en hand and leg.
42024041	And as dem neva stil biliv (bikos of dia hapines) and stil dey sopraiz, Jisos ask dem, "Una get enitin to chop for here?"
42024042	So dem kon gi-am fish wey dem don kook,
42024043	e kon tak am chop for dia front.
42024044	Den Jisos tel dem, "Na di wod wey I tel una wen I stil dey wit una bi dis, evritin wey dem rite abaut mi for Mosis law, di profets books and Psalm, must hapun."
42024045	Den e opun dia maind so dat dem go fit undastand God wod
42024046	kon tel dem, "Na wetin dem rite bi dis, 'Di Mezaya go sofa and e go wak-up from deat for di ted day
42024047	and dem go yuz en name prish giv pipol mak dem for turn from dia sin kom mit God and di prishin go start from Jerusalem.
42024048	"Una bi witnes for dis tins.
42024049	"I dey send wetin my Papa promis kom mit una. So mak una stay for dis tawn ontil pawa go kom from hevun kon kova una."
42024050	Den Jisos tak dem go Betani kon lift en hand and bless dem.
42024051	As e dey bless dem, God kon kari-am go hevun.
42024052	So, dem woship am kon go bak to Jerusalem dey hapi wel-wel
42024053	and dem kon dey go di Tempol evritaim, dey praiz God.
43001001	From wen taim bigin naim di Wod dey and di Wod dey wit God and na God ensef bi di Wod.
43001002	Di Wod dey wit God from wen taim bigin.
43001003	Naim mak evritin and if to sey E nor mak dem, dem nor for dey dis wold at-all.
43001004	Na insaid am life dey and na dat life bi di lite wey pipol get.
43001005	Di lite dey shine insaid daknes, bot daknes nor gri wit am.
43001006	E get won man wey en name bi Jon, wey God send kom dis wold.
43001007	E kom bear witnes for di lite, mak evribodi for fit get di shanse to biliv wetin God tok tru en wod.
43001008	Nor bi Jon ensef bi di lite, bot e kom tel pipol abaut Jisos wey bi di lite.
43001009	Na Jisos bi di tru lite wey go shine for evribodi for dis wold.
43001010	E kom insaid di wold wey ensef mak, bot di pipol nor no am.
43001011	E kom mit en own pipol, bot dem nor wont am.
43001012	Bot evribodi wey risiv and biliv en name, e go giv dem di rite to bi God pikin.
43001013	Dem go bi God shildren, nor bi as dia mama and papa tak born dem from bele, or bikos sombodi mak dem so, bot bikos God ensef mak dem en own shildren.
43001014	Den di Wod kon shange to pesin and e stay wit us for dis wold. Wi si en glori wey show sey, naim bi di onli pikin wey get koret favor and trut, wey God send kom mit us.
43001015	Jon kon bigin shaut sey, "Dis na di pesin wey I tel una abaut sey, 'Di pesin wey go kom afta mi, big pas mi, bikos e dey bifor mi.'"
43001016	Evribodi for dis wold don risiv plenti gud tins from am.
43001017	Na tru Mosis God giv us di law, bot God giv us favor and trut, tru Jisos Kraist.
43001018	Nobodi don fit si God face bifor. Bot Jisos, wey bi God ensef, wey en and en Papa bi tait frend, na-im kom show us haw God bi.
43001019	Di Ju oga dem send prists and Levi pipol mak dem go ask Jon sey, "Hu yu bi sef?"
43001020	E ansa dem, "I nor dey lai, bikos nor bi mi bi di Kraist."
43001021	Den dem ask am, "So, na hu yu bi? Abi yu bi Elija?" E kon sey, "No, I nor bi Elija." Dem kon ask am again, "Yu bi di profet?" E ansa, "No-o-o!"
43001022	Again, dem ask am, "Hu yu bi sef? Mak yu tel us, so dat wi go no wetin to tel di pipol wey send us. Hu yu sey yu bi?"
43001023	Jon kon sey, "Na mi bi dat vois wey dey shaut insaid widanes sey, 'Mak una mak di road wey pipol go pas go mit God strate wel-wel', as Profet Isaia tok bifor.'"
43001024	(Na di Farisi pipol send dis pipol go mit Jon).
43001025	Dem kon ask Jon sey, "Why yu dey baptize pipol, if yu nor bi di Kraist or Elija or di Profet?"
43001026	Jon kon tel dem, "I dey baptize pipol wit wota, bot among una, won pesin dey wey una nor no.
43001027	"E go kom afta mi. I nor rish to luz di rope wey dey en shu."
43001028	All dis tins hapun for Betani wer pipol dey kros Jordan Riva kom mit Jon, mak e baptize dem.
43001029	Wen day break, Jon si Jisos dey waka kom mit am, den Jon sey, "Mak una luk! Dis na di Ship wey God send kom die, mak God for forgiv us awa sins".
43001030	Na dis pesin I tel una sey, "Afta mi, won man wey big pas mi go kom, bikos e dey bifor mi.
43001031	"Misef nor no am bifor, bot I dey baptize pipol wit wota, so dat God go show Izrel pipol hu Jisos bi."
43001032	Den Jon bear witnes sey, "I si God Spirit wey kom dan laik dove from hevun kon stay for Jisos head.
43001033	"I nor no am bifor, bot di pesin wey send mi kom baptize wit wota tel mi sey, 'Di pesin wey yu go si God Spirit kom stay on-top en head, na-im go baptize pipol wit Holi Spirit.'
43001034	"I don si-am and I bear witnes sey, 'Dis man na di pesin wey God shuz.'"
43001035	Wen day break, Jon wit en tu disaipol stand for outsaid.
43001036	Dem kon dey luk Jisos wen e dey waka pas, den Jon kon sey, "Mak una luk! Na dat pesin bi God Ship."
43001037	Wen Jon tu disaipols hear wetin e tok, dem kon folo Jisos.
43001038	Jisos luk bak kon si di disaipols dey folo am. Den e ask dem, "Wetin una wont?" Dem ansa am, "Oga, (wey min Tisha) wer yu dey stay?"
43001039	Jisos ansa dem, "Mak una kom si-am." So dem go si di place wey e dey stay kon stay wit am dat day. Dat taim na abaut for o' klok for aftanun.
43001040	Andru, Saimon Pita broda, na won of di disaipols wey hear wetin Jon tok and wey folo Jisos.
43001041	E first go faind en broda Saimon kon tel am, "Wi don si di Mezaya", (wey min Kraist).
43001042	Andru kon bring Saimon kom mit Jisos. Wen Jisos si-am, e kon tel am, "Yu bi Saimon, Jon pikin, na Sefas (wey min Pita) pipol go dey kol yu from today go."
43001043	Wen day break, Jisos kon plan to go Galili. Wen e si Fillip, e tel am, "Mak yu folo mi."
43001044	Fillip na from Betsaida, wey bi Andru and Pita home-tawn.
43001045	Wen Fillip si Nataniel, e tel am, "Wi don si di pesin wey Mosis and di profets rite abaut for dia book sey, 'En name na Jisos, wey en home-tawn bi Nazaret and na Josef pikin e bi.'"
43001046	Nataniel kon sey, "Beta tin go fit kom out from Nazaret?" Fillip ansa am, "Mak yu kom si."
43001047	Wen Jisos si Nataniel dey waka kom mit am, e kon sey, "Mak una luk! Dis na beta pesin wey kom from Izrel, wayo nor dey en bele."
43001048	Nataniel kon ask am, "Haw yu tak no mi." Jisos ansa, "Bifor Fillip kol yu wen yu dey unda di tri, I don si yu."
43001049	Nataniel sey, "Tisha, tru-tru, yu bi God Pikin and na yu bi Izrel king."
43001050	Jisos kon tel am, "Bikos I tel yu sey I si yu unda di fig tri, yu biliv wetin I tok? Bikos yu biliv, yu go si wetin big pas dis won."
43001051	Den e kon sey, "Wetin I dey tel una na tru wod, una go si hevun opun and God angels go dey waka up-and-dan on-top God Pikin."
43002001	Wen tiri days don pas, Mary, wey bi Jisos mama, go won marage for Kana, wey dey for Galili.
43002002	Dem invait Jisos and en disaipol for di marage tu.
43002003	Wen wine finish, Jisos mama kon tel am, "Dia wine don finish."
43002004	Jisos ansa am, "Mama, why yu dey tel mi dis? My taim neva rish."
43002005	So en mama kon tel di savants sey, "Enitin wey e tel una, mak una du-am."
43002006	For dat place, sis big wota pot dey and ish won fit kontain abaut twenti to tati gallon for wota, wey di Ju pipol dey yuz wosh leg as dia tradishon tok.
43002007	Jisos kon tel di savants, "Mak una ful di pots wit wota." So dem kon ful all di pot wit wota.
43002008	Jisos tel dem, "Mak una tak som wota from di pot go giv di chairman for di parti." So, dem kon du as e tok.
43002009	Wen di chairman taste di wota wey don turn to wine, bikos e nor no haw e hapun (bot di savants wey draw di wota no), e kon kol di man wey dey mari tel am sey,
43002010	"Wen pesin dey du parti, na beta wine e dey first serv pipol, den wen di pipol don drink taya, naim e dey serv cheap wine. Bot yu kon kip di gud wine ontil di parti don won finish."
43002011	Dis na di first mirakol wey Jisos du and e hapun for Kana wey dey Galili. Dis na haw e show en onor, so en disaipols kon biliv am.
43002012	Den Jisos wit en mama, brodas and en disaipols kon go Kapanum. Dem kon stay der for som days.
43002013	By dis taim, di Ju Passova Fist don near wel-wel, so Jisos kon go Jerusalem.
43002014	E si di pipol dey sel melu, ship and dove insaid di Tempol yard, e stil si pipol wey dey shange moni, sidan near dia tabol.
43002015	E yuz koboko wey e mak, tak driv dem wit dia ship and melu komot from di Tempol yard. E trowey di tabol wey di pipol dey tak shange moni and dia moni kon skata.
43002016	E kon tel di pipol wey dey sel dove, "Mak una kari all dis tins komot for here. Mak una nor turn my Papa haus to market."
43002017	Den en disaipols kon rimemba as den rite for Psalm Book sey, "Di luv wey e get for en Papa haus dey burn for en heart laik fire."
43002018	Di Ju oga dem kon ask am, "As yu dey du all dis tins, na wish sign yu go show us mak wi for fit biliv yu?"
43002019	Jisos ansa dem, "Ivun if una distroi dis Tempol, for tiri days taim, I go build am again."
43002020	Den di Ju oga dem tel am, "Na forti-sis years dem tak build dis Tempol and yu dey sey yu go fit build am for tiri days?"
43002021	Bot na di Tempol for Jisos bodi naim e dey tok abaut.
43002022	So wen Jisos don wak-up from deat, en disaipols kon rimemba sey, e tok so bifor. Den dem kon biliv wetin dem rite for God wod and wetin Jisos tel dem.
43002023	Jisos dey for Jerusalem by di taim wey dem dey du di Passova Fist. For der, meni pipol kon biliv am, bikos dem si di mirakols wey e du.
43002024	Bot Jisos nor gri opun en maind giv di pipol, bikos e no dem wel-wel.
43002025	E nor nid enibodi to tok abaut am, bikos e no wetin dey insaid pipol bele, so e nor fit trust dem.
43003001	E get won man wey bi Farisi, en name na Nikodimos and e bi memba for di konsol wey dey rule Ju pipol.
43003002	E hide go mit Jisos for nite kon tel am, "Tisha, wi no sey yu bi di pesin wey God send kon mit us, bikos nobodi fit du di mirakols wey yu dey du, unles God dey wit am."
43003003	Jisos tel am, "Mak I tel yu tru wod, unles dem born pesin di sekon taim, e nor go fit si God kindom."
43003004	Den Nikodimos kon ask am, "Haw dem go fit tak born pesin wey don old for di sekon taim? Abi di pesin go enta en mama bele mak di mama born am again? E fit hapun laik dat?"
43003005	Jisos ansa am, "I tel yu di trut, unles God born pesin wit wota and en Spirit, di pesin nor go fit enta God kindom.
43003006	"Wetin flesh born, na flesh e bi, bot wetin God Spirit born, na spirit e bi.
43003007	"So, mak yu nor konfuz bikos I tok sey, 'God go born yu for di sekon taim.'
43003008	"Wen briz dey blow, e dey go eniwer e wont, yu dey hear di sound wey e dey mak, bot yu nor fit no wer e dey kom from or wer e dey go. Na so e bi wit evribodi wey God Spirit born."
43003009	Nikodimos kon ask am, "Haw dis tins go fit hapun?"
43003010	Jisos ansa, "Yu bi tisha for Izrel, yet yu nor fit undastand dis tins?
43003011	"Mak I tel yu di trut, wi dey tok wetin wi sabi and dey bear witnes for wetin wi don si wit awa eyes, bot una nor gri asept wetin wi tok.
43003012	"Naw, if I dey tel una abaut di tins wey dey for dis wold and una nor fit biliv wetin I tok, haw una go fit tak biliv mi, if I bigin dey tel una abaut di tins wey dey for hevun?
43003013	"Nobodi don go hevun bifor, esept Man Pikin wey kom dan from hevun and e go-go bak der.
43003014	"Yu si, as Mosis kari di snake go up wen dem dey insaid desert, na so tu dem go kari Man Pikin up,
43003015	so dat enibodi wey go biliv am, go get life wey nor dey end.
43003016	"Bikos God luv di pipol wey dey dis wold wel-wel, E kon send di onli pikin wey E get to us, so dat enibodi wey biliv am, nor go die, bot e go get life wey nor dey end.
43003017	"God nor send en pikin kom kondem di pipol wey dey insaid di wold, bot mak e kom save dem.
43003018	"Enibodi wey biliv am, God nor go kondem am. Bot di pesin wey nor biliv am, God don kondem am alredi, bikos di pesin nor biliv God Pikin name.
43003019	"Na dis bi di rizin why God go joj di wold, bikos lite don kom insaid di wold, bot pipol laik to stay for daknes insted of lite, bikos dem dey du tins wey nor gud.
43003020	"Yu si, evribodi wey dey du bad tin dey hate lite and dem nor go gri kom out for wer lite dey, mak pipol nor for si di bad tins wey dem dey du.
43003021	"Bot di pesin wey dey du gud tins, dey kom out for lite, so dat pipol go si di tins wey e dey du, bikos na as God wont, naim e dey du.’’
43003022	Leta, Jisos and en disaipols go Judea aria and dem kon stay der for som taim dey baptize pipol.
43003023	Jon dey baptize for Aenon, won tawn wey near Salim, bikos plenti wota dey der and pipol dey kom mit am mak e baptize dem.
43003024	(For dis taim, dem neva put Jon for prizin).

43003027	Jon ansa dem, "Nobodi go fit get enitin unles God wey dey hevun, gi-am."
43003028	Unasef go fit bear witnes sey, I tok sey I nor bi di Kraist, bot God send mi kom, bifor Kraist go kom.
43003029	"Di pesin wey won mari new wife naim bi di bridegroom. En frend, wey bi di bestman, dey listin to am. E go dey hapi wel-wel wen e hear di bridegroom dey tok. Na dis dey mak mi hapi and my joy don ful.
43003030	"Pipol must no Kraist pas as dem no mi.

43003032	"Bot di pesin wey kom from hevun dey tok abaut wetin e si and hear for hevun, bot pipol nor gri listin to am.

43004001	Jisos kon no sey di Farisi pipol don hear sey e dey baptize plenti pipol pas Jon and di pipol dey folo am,
43004002	(aldo nor bi Jisos ensef dey baptize pipol, bot na en disaipols dey du-am).
43004003	Jisos kon komot for Judea dey go Galili.
43004004	For am to rish der, e go must pas tru Samaria.
43004005	E kon rish won tawn for Samaria wey dem dey kol Sykar, wey near di land wey Jakop giv Josef, wey bi en pikin.
43004006	Jakop wel dey der tu. Dat aftanun, bikos Jisos don taya to waka, e kon sidan near di wel.
43004007	So won wuman for di tawn kom draw wota for di wel. Jisos tel am, "Abeg giv mi wota mak I drink".

43004009	Den di wuman kon tel Jisos, "Haw yu wey bi Ju kon dey ask mi wey bi Samaria pesin, sey, "Mak I giv yu wota drink?'" (E tok dis won bikos Ju and Samaria pipol nor dey agri at-all.)
43004010	Jisos ansa am, "If yu no wetin God gift bi and di pesin wey dey ask yu for wota so, yu for ask am and e go giv yu di wota wey dey mak pesin liv foreva."
43004011	Di wuman ask am, "Oga, yu nor get bucket and di wel deep wel-wel, wer yu go fit get dat kaind wota?"
43004012	"Yu big pas awa gran papa Jakop wey giv us dis wel, wer en famili and animas dey drink from?"
43004013	Jisos ansa, "Pesin wey drink from dis wota go always dey hungri for wota.
43004014	"Bot enibodi wey go drink from di wota wey I go gi-am, nor go hungri for wota again, bikos di wota wey I go gi-am, go turn to riva wey nor dey dry insaid en bele and di wota go gi-am life wey nor dey end."
43004015	Di wuman kon tel am, "Oga, giv mi dis wota, so dat I nor go hungri for wota or kom here kon draw wota again."
43004016	Jisos tel am, "Go kol yor husban, mak tu of una kom mit mi."
43004017	Di wuman ansa, "I nor get husban." Den Jisos kon tel am, "Yu tok tru wen yu sey 'I nor get husban.'
43004018	"Bikos yu don mari faiv husban bifor and di man wey yu dey stay wit naw, nor bi yor ril husban. Na tru yu tok."
43004019	Di wuman kon tel am, "Oga, I si sey yu bi profet wey dey tok wetin go hapun.
43004020	"Awa papa dem serv God for dis mountin, bot una kon tok sey, di place wey pipol sopoz to woship God, na Jerusalem e dey."
43004021	Jisos kon sey, "Wuman, mak u biliv mi, di taim dey kom, wen pipol go woship God for eniwer dem dey, nor bi onli for dis mountin or for Jerusalem.
43004022	"Una dey serv wetin una nor no, bot wi dey serv wetin wi no, bikos na Ju pipol, naim God first kol to ensef.
43004023	"Bot di taim dey kom and e don ivun rish, wen di pipol wey won rili serv God, go serv am for di tru way, wey God Spirit go show dem.
43004024	"God na Spirit and di pipol wey won serv am, must serv am for di tru way wey God Spirit go show dem."
43004025	Di wuman ansa, "I no sey di Mezaya (di won wey dem dey kol Kraist), wey go save evribodi, go kom and enitaim wen e kom, e go tel us evritin."
43004026	Jisos kon tel am, "Na mi wey dey tok to yu so, bi di Mezaya."
43004027	Wen Jisos dey tok to di wuman, en disaipols kon kom bak. Dem sopraiz sey e dey tok wit won wuman, bot dem nor fit ask am, "Wetin e wont?" or "Why e dey tok to di wuman?"
43004028	By dis taim, di wuman don liv en pot wey e tak kom draw wota kon run go insaid di tawn go tel pipol sey,
43004029	"Mak una kon si won man wey tel mi all di tins wey I don du. Dis man nor bi di Mezaya so?"
43004030	So di pipol kom out for di tawn go mit Jisos.
43004031	By dis taim, di disaipols kon beg am, "Tisha, mak yu chop somtin naw."
43004032	E tel dem, "I get fud wey I go chop wey una nor no abaut."
43004033	Di disaipols kon dey ask demsef, "Abi sombodi don bring somtin for am to chop wen wi nor dey here?"
43004034	Jisos kon tel dem, "My fud na to du wetin my Papa tok and mak I finish di wok wey E send mi.
43004035	"Nor bi una dey tok sey, 'Na for monts rimain bifor dem go plok frut wey dem plant for farm?' Mak una luk roun and una go si sey frut don ripe rish to plok.
43004036	"God go riword di pesin wey plok plenti frut from wetin odas plant and e go get life wey nor dey end. So, di pesin wey plant and di pesin wey plok wetin dem plant, go hapi togeda.
43004037	"Dis won show sey, di tin wey pipol dey tok sey, 'Won pesin plant and anoda pesin plok di friut', na tru wod.
43004038	"I send una go plok wetin una nor plant, oda pipol don sofa plant dem, bot una kon enjoy wetin dem sofa for."
43004039	By dis taim, meni pipol from Samaria tawn kon biliv am, bikos of di tins wey di wuman tok, "E tel mi all di tins wey I don du."
43004040	Wen Samaria pipol kom mit am, dem kon dey beg am sey, mak e stay wit dem. So e kon stay der for tu days,
43004041	and bikos of wetin e tok, meni pipol kon biliv am.
43004042	Den dem kon tel di wuman, "Nor bi wetin yu tel us mak us biliv, bot bikos wi don tak awa own ear hear and wi don no sey, dis pesin tru-tru, na-im go save all di pipol wey dey dis wold."
43004043	Wen tu days pas, Jisos komot from der go Galili.
43004044	(Bikos Jisos don tok am sey, "Pesin wey bi profet nor dey get respet for en home-tawn").
43004045	Wen e rish Galili, di pipol wey dey der kon welkom am, bikos dem don si all di tins wey e du for Jerusalem for di taim wen dem dey du Passova Fist.
43004046	Again, e go Kana wey dey Galili, for wer e first turn wota to wine. For Kapanum, won soja-man wey dey wok for di king palise dey der and en pikin wey nor wel.
43004047	Wen e hear sey Jisos don kom bak to Galili, e go mit am kon beg am sey mak e kom heal en pikin wey won die.
43004048	So Jisos ask am, "If una nor si signs and wondas una nor go biliv mi?"
43004049	Di man ansa, "Oga, abeg mak yu kom bifor my pikin go die."
43004050	Jisos kon tel am, "Mak yu go haus, yor pikin nor go die." Di man biliv wetin Jisos tel am, so e kon komot go en haus.
43004051	Wen e don near haus, en savants kon mit, tel am sey, "Yor pikin don wel, e nor die."
43004052	So, e ask dem di taim wen di pikin bigin dey beta. Dem kon tel am, "Na yestaday for won o' klok for aftanun naim e wel."
43004053	Bikos of wetin dem tok, di pikin papa kon rimemba sey dat na di taim wen Jisos tel am sey, "Yor pikin nor go die." Bikos of dis, di man and evribodi wey dey en haus kon biliv Jisos.
43004054	Dis na di sekon mirakol wey Jisos du for Galili, afta e kom bak from Judea.
43005001	Jisos kon go won fist wey dem dey du for Jerusalem.
43005002	Won pool dey der wey near di Ship Gate, di name na Betsaida for Aramaic language. Na faiv roads pipol tak dey enta insaid.
43005003	Pipol wey nor wel, wey blind and wey nor fit waka dey laidan for di difren roads.
43005004	From taim-to-taim, won angel dey kom shake di wota and enibodi wey first enta di wota afta di angel don shake am, go wel.
43005005	Won man dey der wey nor fit waka for tati-ate years.
43005006	Wen Jisos si-am laidan for der, e kon no sey di man neva fit waka for long taim. So, Jisos kon ask am, "Yu won waka?"
43005007	Di man ansa am, "Oga, I nor get enibodi wey go put mi insaid di pool wen di wota dey shake. Enitaim I dey trai to enta di wota, anoda pesin go kwik enta bifor I rish der."
43005008	Jisos tel am, "Mak yu get up! Kari yor mat mak yu bigin waka."
43005009	At wons, di man get up, kari en mat kon bigin waka. (Dat day na Sabat).
43005010	Den di Ju oga dem kon tel di man wey dey waka naw sey, "Today na Sabat, yu nor sopoz to kari yor mat dey waka."
43005011	Naim e ansa dem, "Di man wey mak mi wel, tel mi sey, 'Mak I kari my mat and mak I bigin waka.'"
43005012	Dem kon ask am, "Hu bi di man wey sey, 'Mak yu kari yor mat, mak yu dey waka?'"
43005013	Bot di man nor no hu e bi, bikos Jisos don komot der and plenti pipol dey for dat place.
43005014	Afta dis, Jisos kon si di man insaid di Tempol. So e kon tel am, "Luk, yu don wel naw, mak yu nor komit sin again, oda-wise, di tin wey bad pas wetin du yu bifor, go hapun to yu."
43005015	Di man kon go tel di Ju oga dem sey, "Na Jisos bi di pesin wey mak mi wel."
43005016	Bikos Jisos dey du all dis tins for Sabat Day, di Ju oga dem kon dey mak trobol wit am.
43005017	So e tel dem, "My Papa dey wok evritaim and na so mi tu dey wok."
43005018	Bikos of dis, di Ju oga dem kon dey trai to kil-am, bikos dem sey e dey break di Sabat law and e dey kol God en papa, laik sey en and God na mate.
43005019	Naim Jisos ansa dem, "Mak I tel una tru wod, di Pikin nor fit du enitin wit en own maind, esept di tins wey e si en Papa dey du. And na enitin wey e si en Papa dey du, naim e dey du tu.
43005020	"Bikos di Papa get strong luv for en pikin, e dey always show am evritin wey e dey du and e go show am plenti tins wey pas dis won and una go sopraiz.
43005021	"As di Papa get pawa to tak wak pesin wey don die, na so tu di pikin get pawa to giv life to enibodi wey en won giv.
43005022	Di Papa nor dey joj enibodi, bot e don giv en pikin pawa to joj evribodi,
43005023	so dat evribodi go bow dan for di pikin as dem dey bow dan for di Papa. If enibodi nor bow show respet for di pikin, e nor go get di maind to respet di Papa wey send di pikin kom.
43005024	"I tel una tru wod, di pesin wey tak wetin I tok and biliv sey na di Papa send mi, go get life wey nor dey end and e nor go enta hell fire, bot e go get life wey nor dey end.
43005025	"I tel una tru wod, di taim dey kom and e don ivun rish groun naw, wen doz wey don die go hear Man Pikin vois and wen dem hear am, dem go wak-up and dem nor go die again.
43005026	"Bikos as di Papa get life for insaid am, na so e giv en pikin life tu.
43005027	"Di Papa don giv en pikin di pawa to joj pipol.
43005028	"So, mak dis wod nor sopraiz una, bikos di taim dey kom, wen all doz wey dey insaid grave go hear di pikin vois,
43005029	and di angels go kon seprate di pipol wey du gud tins, mak dem enta life wey nor dey end, bot God go kondem di pipol dem wey dey du bad tins.
43005030	"I nor go fit du enitin wit my own pawa, bot na wetin I dey hear from my Papa, naim I dey yuz tak joj. Eni jojment wey I giv, na tru won, bikos I nor dey du my own tin, bot I onli dey du as my Papa send mi.
43005031	"If I tok abaut mysef, e fit bi sey wetin I tok nor bi tru",
43005032	bikos anoda pesin dey wey go tok abaut mi and I no sey wetin e tok abaut mi, na tru.
43005033	"Una don send mesage go mit Jon and e don tel una tru wod.
43005034	"(I nor dey trust wetin pipol tok, bot I dey tel una dis wod mak God for save una.)
43005035	Jon lite shine wel-wel for smol taim and una hapi wen una si en lite."
43005036	Bot I get pesin wey go bear witnes abaut mi wey big pas Jon, bikos di wok wey my Papa giv mi mak I du, naim I dey du so; so di wok dey bear witnes sey, na my Papa send mi.
43005037	And my Papa wey send mi, en ensef don bear witnes abaut mi. Una neva hear my Papa vois or si-am bifor.
43005038	En wod neva stil dey insaid una, bikos una nor biliv sey na-im send mi.
43005039	Una dey read God wod wel-wel, bikos una biliv sey na wetin una read go giv una life wey nor dey end and na dis same wod dey tok abaut mi,
43005040	bot una nor redi to kom mit mi, so dat una go get life wey nor dey end.
43005041	"I nor laik mak pipol dey praiz mi,
43005042	bikos I no sey, una nor luv God for insaid una heart.
43005043	"I kom wit my Papa name and una nor gri asept mi, bot if anoda pesin kom wit en own name, una go asept am.
43005044	"Haw una go fit biliv wen una dey praiz ish oda and una nor kare for di praiz wey onli God fit giv.
43005045	"Mak una nor tink sey I go akiuz una bifor my Papa. Di tin wey go stand against una na di law wey Mosis rite, wey una dey put hope for.
43005046	"If una biliv wetin Mosis rite for di law, una sopoz to biliv mi tu, bikos na mi e rite abaut.
43005047	"Bot if una nor biliv wetin Mosis rite, haw una go tak biliv wetin I dey tel una naw?"
43006001	Wen Jisos don tok finish, e kon kros go Tiberias wey dey di oda side for Galili wotasaid.
43006002	Plenti pipol kon dey folo am, bikos dem si wen e heal sik pipol.
43006003	Jisos kon komot for der go di mountin side kon sidan der wit en disaipols.
43006004	(Dat taim, Passova Fist don rish.)
43006005	And wen Jisos luk up, e si plenti pipol dey kom mit am. Den e kon ask Filip, "Na wer wi go fit si bread buy wey all dis pipol go chop?
43006006	Jisos tok dis won mak e for si wetin Filip go du, bikos en ensef no wetin e won du.
43006007	Filip ansa, "Ivun if wi buy bread wey rish tu ondred silva koins and if dem share am smol-smol, e nor go rish evribodi chop.".
43006008	Anoda disaipol wey en name bi Andru, wey bi Saimon Pita broda kon tel Jisos sey,
43006009	"Won boy dey here wey get faiv bread and tu fish, bot dis won nor go rish dis plenti pipol chop beleful?"
43006010	Jisos ansa, "Tel all di pipol mak dem sidan (as plenti grass dey di place wey dem go fit sidan put). Di men wey sidan, rish faiv tazon.
43006011	Jisos tak di bread kon tank God. Den e divide am giv di pipol wey sidan. E du di same tin wit di fish. All of dem chop as dem wont, kon beleful wel-wel.
43006012	Wen evribodi don beleful, Jisos kon tel en disaipols, "Mak una gada wetin rimain, mak enitin nor waste."
43006013	Wen dem gada wetin dem chop rimain for di faiv bread, e ful twef basket.
43006014	So wen di pipol si di mirakol wey Jisos du, dem kon dey tok among demsef sey, "Tru-tru, dis man na di profet wey God send kom dis wold."
43006015	Since Jisos no sey dem go won tak am by fos go mak am dia king, e kon komot go on-top di mountin alone.
43006016	Wen evenin rish, en disaipols kon go wotasaid go wait am,
43006017	dem enta won kenu, kros go Kapanum (by dis taim, evriwer don dey dak and Jisos neva kom mit dem.)
43006018	Den strong briz bigin blow and di riva kon dey ruff wel-wel.
43006019	Wen dem don padol di kenu go rish abaut tiri or for miles, dem si Jisos dey waka on-top di wota dey kom near dem. Fear kon kash dem wel-wel.
43006020	Jisos kon tel dem, "Na mi, mak una nor fear."
43006021	As dem dey trai mak e enta insaid di kenu, dem kon si sey di kenu don rish wer dem dey go.
43006022	Wen day don break, di pipol wey dey di oda side for di riva no sey na onli won smol kenu dey der. Dem stil no sey Jisos enta di kenu wit dem.
43006023	So som kenu wey kom from Tiberias kon rish di wotasaid near di place wey dem for chop bread, afta Jisos don pray.
43006024	So wen di pipol si sey Jisos and en disaipols nor dey der, dem enta di kenu kon go luk for Jisos for anoda tawn wey dem dey kol Kapanum.
43006025	Wen dem si Jisos for di oda side for di riva, dem ask am, "Tisha, wish taim yu kom here?"
43006026	Jisos ansa dem, "Mak I tel una tru wod, na bikos of di bread wey una chop naim mak una dey faind mi, nor bi bikos of di mirakols wey una si.
43006027	"Mak una nor wok for fud wey nor dey last, bot for fud wey go giv una life wey nor dey end and dat kaind fud, na onli Man Pikin go fit giv una, bikos na-im God send kom."
43006028	Dem kon ask am, "Wetin wi go du to mak God hapi wit us?"
43006029	Jisos ansa, "God wont sey mak una biliv di pesin wey E send."
43006030	Dem stil ask Jisos, "Wish kaind mirakol yu go du mak wi si, mak wi for biliv yu?
43006031	"Awa gran papa dem chop manna for widanes as dem rite for God wod sey, 'God giv dem bread from hevun to chop.'"
43006032	Den Jisos kon tel dem, "Mak I tel una tru wod, nor bi Mosis giv una bread from hevun, bot God, wey bi my Papa, na-im giv una di tru bread from hevun.
43006033	God bread na di pesin wey kom dan from hevun kon giv beta life to di pipol wey dey dis wold."
43006034	So dem tel am, "Oga, from naw go, mak yu giv us dis bread."
43006035	Jisos kon tel dem, Na mi bi di bread wey dey giv life. Pesin wey kom mit mi nor go hungri lia-lai and di pesin wey biliv mi, nor go hungri for wota again.
43006036	As I don tel una, una dey si mi, bot una nor biliv.
43006037	"Enibodi wey my Papa giv mi, go kom mit mi and wen e kom, I nor go eva driv am.
43006038	"Nor bi to du wetin I wont mak mi kom dan from hevun, bot na to du wetin my Papa wont.
43006039	"Wetin my Papa wey send mi wont, na mak I nor luz enibodi wey e giv mi, bot mak I for tak dem go up for di last day.
43006040	"Wetin my Papa wont bi sey, enibodi wey biliv en pikin, go get life wey nor dey end and I go wak-am up for di last day."
43006041	Den di Ju pipol bigin ves and komplian abaut Jisos, bikos e tok sey, "Na mi bi di bread wey kom dan from hevun."
43006042	Den dem kon sey, "Dis Jisos sef nor bi Josef pikin, wey wi no en papa and mama? Na haw e kon dey tok sey, 'I kom dan from hevun?'"
43006043	Jisos ansa, "Mak una nor komplain abaut mi to won anoda.
43006044	"Nobodi go fit kom mit mi wit en own pawa, unles my Papa wey send mi draw am kom mit mi and I go tak am go up for di last day.
43006045	"Na so di profets rite sey, 'God go tish evribodi.' Enibodi wey hear wetin my Papa tok, go kom mit mi.
43006046	(Nor bi sey enibodi don si di Papa bifor, esept mi wey kom from hevun).
43006047	"I dey tel una tru wod, enibodi wey biliv mi, don get life wey nor dey end.
43006048	"Na mi bi di bread wey dey giv pesin life.
43006049	"Una gran-gran papa dem chop manna for widanes, bot dem stil die.
43006050	"Dis na di bread wey kom from hevun, so dat enibodi wey chop am, go get life wey nor dey end.
43006051	"Na mi bi di bread wey kom dan from hevun. Enibodi wey chop dis bread go liv foreva. Na my flesh bi di bread wey I go giv di pipol wey dey for dis wold."
43006052	Den di Ju pipol wey dey ves wit Jisos kon bigin dey argue wit won anoda dey sey, "Haw dis man go giv us en flesh mak wi chop?"
43006053	Jisos tel dem, "I dey tel una tru wod, unles una chop Man Pikin flesh and drink en blood, una nor go get life for insaid una.
43006054	"Di pesin wey go chop my flesh and drink my blood, don get life wey nor dey end and I go tak am up for di last day.
43006055	"My flesh na di ril fud and my blood na di koret drink.
43006056	Di pesin wey chop my flesh and drink my blood, go stay insaid mi and I go dey insaid am tu.
43006057	"Na my Papa wey dey for hevun send mi and as I dey for dis life bikos of am, na so di pesin wey chop my flesh go get life, bikos of mi.
43006058	"Dis na di bread wey kom dan from hevun, e nor bi laik di bread wey una gran papa dem chop and afta, dem stil die. Di pesin wey go chop dis bread nor go eva die, bot e go liv foreva."
43006059	Jisos tok dis tins wen e dey tish dem for insaid di Tempol for Kapanum.
43006060	Wen Jisos meni disaipols hear wetin e tok, dem kon sey, "Dis tin wey Jisos dey tok so hard wel-wel-o-o! Na hu go fit undastand dem?"
43006061	Wen Jisos no sey en disaipols dey komplain abaut wetin e tok, e kon ask dem, "Wetin I tok so dey mak una ves tu?
43006062	"Wetin go hapun if una si Man Pikin go bak to hevun wer e dey bifor?
43006063	"Na di Spirit go fit giv pesin life; humanbin pawa nor fit du-am. All dis wod wey I dey tel una so, dem bi Spirit and dem dey giv pesin life.
43006064	"Bot som of una nor biliv." (From biginin, Jisos don no di pipol wey nor go biliv and di pesin wey go sel am giv en enemi.)
43006065	So Jisos kon sey, "Na bikos of dis I tel una sey, nobodi go fit kom mit mi wit en own pawa, unles my Papa let am kom."
43006066	Afta dis, Jisos meni disaipols kon stop to folo am.
43006067	Den Jisos kon ask en twef disaipols, "Una won go tu?"
43006068	Den Saimon Pita ansa am, "Oga, na hu wi go kon go mit? Na yu get di wod wey dey giv pipol di life wey nor dey end.
43006069	"Wi don biliv and no sey, 'Na yu bi di Holi Won wey God send kom mit us.'"
43006070	Jisos kon ansa, "Nor bi twef of una I shuz? Bot won pesin among una na devol pikin."
43006071	(E tok dis won abaut Judas, wey bi Saimon Iskarot pikin, bikos na dis Judas, wey bi won of en twef disaipols, naim go sel am giv en enemi.)
43007001	Afta, Jisos kon travol go evriwer for Galili. Den e komot for Judea, bikos di Ju oga dem won kil-am.
43007002	Di taim kon rish wen Ju pipol dey du dia fist wey dem dey kol Tabanakol Fist.
43007003	Jisos brodas kon dey tel am, "Komot for here go Judea, mak yor disaipols si di mirakols wey yu dey du.
43007004	"Bikos enibodi wey wont mak pipol sabi hu e bi, nor go du enitin for kona. Since yu dey du dis tins, e gud sey mak yu show yorsef to evribodi."
43007005	(Ivun en brodas nor biliv wetin Jisos dey du.)
43007006	Jisos ansa dem, "Taim neva rish for mi to go, bot una fit go enitaim una laik.
43007007	"Pipol laik una, bot dem nor laik mi, bikos I dey tel dem sey wetin dem dey du nor gud.
43007008	"Mak una go di fist, I nor go-go, bikos my taim neva rish."
43007009	Afta e don tok finish, e kon stay for Galili.
43007010	Bot wen en brodas don go di fist, Jisos kon go der tu, bot e nor let enibodi no sey e dey der.
43007011	Di Ju oga dem kon dey ask pipol, "Wer e dey?"
43007012	Dem kon dey tok among demsef. Som sey, "Jisos na gud pesin", bot odas sey, "E dey play pipol wayo."
43007013	Bot nobodi fit tok out, bikos dem dey fear di Ju oga dem.
43007014	Wen di fist don rish haf, Jisos enta di Tempol kon dey tish.
43007015	Di Ju oga dem sopraiz and dem kon dey sey, "Haw e tak no dis tins wey e dey tish so, as e bi sey e nor go school at-all?"
43007016	Jisos ansa dem, "Wetin I dey tish nor bi my own, bot na di Pesin wey send mi, na-im giv mi.
43007017	"Enibodi wey redi to du wetin God wont, di pesin go no weda wetin I dey tish na from God or na my own.
43007018	"Enibodi wey dey tok wit en own pawa, go wont mak pipol praiz am, bot di pesin wey won onor hu send am, naim dey du wetin koret and sin nor dey insaid am.
43007019	"Mosis nor giv una di law? Bot una nor gri obey am. Why e bi sey una won kil mi sef?"
43007020	Di pipol ansa Jisos, "Dimon don enta yor bodi! Hu won kil yu?"
43007021	Den Jisos ansa, "Na won mirakol wey I du so, mak una dey sopraiz?
43007022	"Na tru sey Mosis tel una to sekonsaiz una son, (nor bi Mosis start am, na from Abraham taim e start) and una dey sekonsaiz una son for Sabat Day.
43007023	"Since una dey sekonsaiz for Sabat so dat una nor go break Mosis law, why una dey ves wit mi, bikos I heal dis sik man for Sabat Day?
43007024	"Mak una nor dey joj pesin, bikos of wetin una si wit una eye, bot mak una giv koret jojment as e sopoz to bi."
43007025	Som pipol wey dey stay for Jerusalem kon dey sey, "Dis nor bi di man wey dem won kil?
43007026	"Naim dey here dey tok for publik so and dem nor fit tel am enitin. Abi di oga dem don gri sey naim bi di Kraist?
43007027	"Wi sef no di place wer dis man from kom and wi no sey enitaim wey Kraist go kom, nobodi go fit no wer e go kom from."
43007028	As Jisos dey tish for di Tempol, e kon shaut sey, "Una no mi and di place wey I from kom, nor bi my pawa I tak kom, na God wey send mi naim bi di koret Pesin. Bot una nor no am.
43007029	"Bot I no am wel-wel, bikos na from am, I kom and naim send mi."
43007030	Dem kon trai to kash Jisos, bot nobodi fit tosh am, bikos en taim neva rish.
43007031	Meni pipol for der biliv am kon sey, "Enitaim di pesin wey bi di Kraist kom, e go fit du mirakol wey pas wetin dis won dey du so?"
43007032	Wen di Farisi pipol hear pipol dey tok abaut Jisos, dia oga and di prists kon send sojas go arres am.
43007033	Jisos kon tel dem, "I go onli stay wit una for smol taim and afta, I go-go mit di Pesin wey send mi.
43007034	"Una go dey luk for mi, bot una nor go si mi and una nor go fit kom mit mi for wer I dey."
43007035	Den di Ju oga dem kon dey ask ish oda, "Wer e won go wey wi nor go fit si-am, abi e won go tish Ju pipol wey dey stay wit Greek pipol?
43007036	"Wetin e min wen e tok sey, 'Una go luk for mi, bot una nor go si mi and wer I dey, una nor go fit kom der?'"
43007037	For di last day for di fist, wey bi di biggest day, Jisos stand kon shaut, "If wota dey hungri enibodi, mak e kom mit mi.
43007038	"Di pesin wey biliv mi and wetin I tok, mak e kom drink, jos as God wod sey, 'Plenti wota wey dey giv life, go flow from insaid en bele.'"
43007039	(E tok dis tin abaut di Spirit wey di pipol wey biliv am go get, bikos by dis taim, God neva giv en Spirit to pipol, bikos E neva onor Jisos Kraist.)
43007040	Wen pipol hear wetin e tok, som of dem kon sey, "Tru-tru, dis man naim bi di Profet!"
43007041	Som stil sey, "Na-im bi di Kraist", bot odas sey, "Na lai, Kraist nor fit kom from Galili.
43007042	"Abi God wod nor sey, 'Kraist go kom from David famili wey dey Betlehem, di vilage wey David from kom?'"
43007043	So di pipol kon divide bikos of Jisos.
43007044	Som of dem kon dey trai to kash am, bot nobodi fit tak hand tosh am.
43007045	Wen di sojas go bak, di prist oga dem and Farisi pipol kon ask dem, "Why una nor kash Jisos kom?"
43007046	Di sojas ansa, "Wi neva si enibodi wey tok laik dis man bifor!"
43007047	Den di Farisi pipol kon ask di sojas, "Abi, e don disiv una tu?
43007048	"Abi eni of us wey bi Farisi pipol or prists don biliv Jisos?
43007049	"Kos dey dis pipol head, bikos dem nor no di law."
43007050	Den won man wey en name bi Nikodimos, wey don first go mit Jisos and wey bi won of di big oga dem kon sey,
43007051	"Awa law nor dey kondem pesin unles wi don hear wetin di pesin tok or si wetin e dey du, abi nor bi so?"
43007052	Dem kon ask am, "Abi na Galili yu tu from kom? If yu luk wel, yu go si sey no profet go fit kom from Galili."
43007053	Afta dis, evribodi bigin go en haus.
43008001	Den Jisos waka enta Mount Olives.
43008002	For earli mornin, e enta di Tempol. Plenti pipol gada for der and e kon sidan dey tish dem.
43008003	Di pipol wey sabi di law and di Farisi pipol kon bring won wuman wey dem kash, sey e slip wit man wey nor bi en husban. Dem kon mak am stand for dia front,
43008004	den dem tel Jisos, "Tisha, wi kash dis wuman wen e dey slip wit won man wey nor bi en husban.
43008005	"Mosis law sey, 'Mak dem stone dis kaind wuman til e die.' Wetin yu get to tok for dis mata?"
43008006	(Dem ask am dis kweshon to set trap for am, mak dem for fit kash am). Bot Jisos bend dan kon tak en finga dey rite somtin for groun.
43008007	Wen dem kontinu to dey wori am, e kon get up tel dem, "Eni of una wey neva komit sin bifor, mak e bi di first pesin to stone dis wuman."
43008008	E kon bend dan again bigin rite for groun.
43008009	Wen dem hear wetin e tok, dem kon dey komot for der won by won. Na di old pipol first start to komot, til e kon rimain onli Jisos and di wuman wey stand for en front.
43008010	Den Jisos stand-up kon ask am, "Wuman, wer di pipol wey bring yu? Nobodi rimain to kondem yu?"
43008011	Di wuman ansa, "Oga, nobodi rimain." Den Jisos tel am, "Mi tu nor go kondem yu. Bot from naw go, mak yu nor sin again."
43008012	Den Jisos kon sey, "Na mi bi di lite wey dey di wold, enibodi wey folo mi, nor go waka for daknes lai-lai, bot e go get di lite wey go gi-am life."
43008013	Di Farisi pipol kon dey argue wit am dey sey, "Yu dey tok abaut yorsef and wetin yu tok, nor bi tru".
43008014	Jisos ansa dem, "Ivun if I dey tok abaut mysef, wetin I dey tok na tru, bikos I no wer I from kom and wer I dey go. Bot una nor no wer I from kom or wer I dey go.
43008015	"Una dey joj pesin wit wetin una si wit una eye, bot I nor dey joj pipol laik dat.
43008016	"Bot, if I sey pesin du bad, di tins wey I si and tok abaut, na tru, as e bi sey nor bi onli mi dey tok am. Na mi and my Papa wey send mi, dey tok am togeda.
43008017	"God wod sey, 'Wetin tu pipol bear witnes abaut, na tru.'
43008018	"I dey bear witnes abaut mysef and my Papa wey send mi, dey bear witnes abaut mi tu."
43008019	Dem kon bigin kweshon am, "Hu bi yor Papa sef?" Jisos ansa dem, "Una nor no mi or my Papa, if to sey una no mi, una for no my Papa tu."
43008020	Jisos dey tok to dem near di box wer dem dey put ofrin moni, wey dey insaid di Tempol. Nobodi fit kash am, bikos en taim neva rish.
43008021	Den Jisos kon tel dem again, "I dey go and una go luk for mi, bot una go die insaid una sin. Wer I dey go, una nor go fit kom der."
43008022	So di Ju oga dem kon dey ask, "Abi e won go kil ensef? As e dey tok sey, 'Wer I dey go, una nor go fit kom der?'"
43008023	Jisos ansa dem, "Na groun una from kom, bot mi, na hevun I from kom. Una kom from dis wold, bot I nor kom from dis wold.
43008024	"Na dis mak mi sey una go die insaid una sin. Unles una biliv sey, 'Na mi bi di pesin wey I tok sey I bi', una go die insaid una sin."
43008025	Den dem ask am, "Hu yu bi sef?" Jisos ansa, "Na wetin I tel una from di biginin.
43008026	"I get plenti tins to tok abaut wetin una dey du, bot my Papa wey send mi, nor dey lai and na wetin E tel mi I dey tel pipol wey dey dis wold."
43008027	(Bot dem nor undastand sey e dey tok abaut en Papa for hevun).
43008028	Den Jisos sey, "Wen una don kari mi put for kros, una go no hu I bi. I nor jos dey du enitin wey I laik, bot I dey always du wetin my Papa tel mi.
43008029	"And di Pesin wey send mi dey wit mi. E nor dey liv mi, bikos I dey always dey du di tins wey E wont."
43008030	As e dey tok, meni pipol kon biliv am.
43008031	Jisos kon tel di pipol wey kom from Judea wey biliv am, "If una obey wetin I dey tish una, den una go bi my disaipols
43008032	and una go no di trut and di trut go fri una."
43008033	Dem tel am, "All of us na Abraham pikin, wi neva bi slave to enibodi bifor. Why yu dey sey, wi go dey fri?"
43008034	Jisos kon ansa dem, "Na tru wod I dey tel una, enibodi wey dey komit sin, na sin bi di masta wey dey rule am.
43008035	"Pesin wey bi slave nor dey stay for insaid dat famili foreva, bot pesin wey bi pikin for di famili, naim dey stay foreva.
43008036	"So wen Man Pikin fri una, una don dey fri bi dat.
43008037	"I no sey una kom from Abraham famili, bot una won kil mi bikos una nor won hear wetin I dey tok.
43008038	"Na wetin I si wen I dey wit my Papa, naim I dey tel una, so mak una dey du di tins wey una hear from my Papa."
43008039	Dem tel am, "Abraham naim bi awa papa." Den Jisos ansa dem, "If una bi Abraham pikin, una for dey du di tins wey Abraham du.
43008040	"Bot una won kil mi, bikos I tel una di ril trut wey I hear from God. Abraham nor du wetin una dey du so -o-o.
43008041	"Una dey du di tins wey una papa du." Dem kon tel Jisos, "Awa papa nor born us for outsaid marage. Na God ensef bi di papa wey wi get."
43008042	Den Jisos ansa, "If to sey na God bi una Papa, una for laik mi, bikos I kom from God and as I dey so, I nor kom du my own tins, bikos na-im send mi.
43008043	"Na bikos una nor won asept wetin I dey tish, naim mak una nor fit undastand wetin I dey tok.
43008044	"Na devol bi una papa and na di tin wey una papa wont, naim una dey du. E dey kil pipol from di biginin and e nor dey sopot wetin gud, as e nor get eni gud tin insaid am. Enitaim e dey tok, na di lai wey dey insaid am, na-im e dey tok, e bi lai-lai pesin, bikos naim bi lai-lai papa.
43008045	"Na bikos I dey tel una tru wod, naim mak una nor gri biliv mi.
43008046	"Eni of una go fit show sey I komit sin? Since I dey tel una tru wod, why una nor won biliv mi?
43008047	"Di pesin wey bi God pikin, dey listin and du wetin dem rite for God wod. Una nor dey listin and una nor dey du wetin dem rite for God wod, bikos una nor bi God Pikin."
43008048	So di pipol kon sey, "E bi laik sey yu bi Samaria pesin and dimon dey insaid yu."
43008049	Jisos kon tel dem, "I nor get dimon. I dey respet my Papa, bot una nor gri respet mi.
43008050	"I nor wont mak una praiz mi, bot God, di Won wey dey hevun, na-im wi sopoz praiz and E go joj evribodi for di koret way.
43008051	"I dey tel una tru wod, if enibodi folo wetin I dey tish, e nor go die again."
43008052	Den di pipol kon sey, "E-hen! Wi don no naw sey dimon dey insaid yu. Abraham and di profets don die, yu kon dey tel us sey, 'Enibodi wey folo wetin I dey tish nor go die.'
43008053	"Yu big pas awa papa Abraham and all di profets wey don die? Hu yu tink sey yu bi sef?"
43008054	Jisos ansa, "If I dey praiz mysef, my praiz na yeye won. Di pesin wey dey praiz mi na my Papa, wey una dey sey, 'Na-im bi awa God.'
43008055	"Una nor no am, bot I no am and if I sey I nor no am, I dey lai laik una. I no am and I dey folo wetin e dey tok.
43008056	"Una papa Abraham hapi wel-wel wen e hear sey I dey kom. E si-am and e hapi wel-wel."
43008057	Den di pipol ask am, "Yu neva old rish fifti years and yu sey yu don si Abraham?"
43008058	Jisos ansa dem, "Na tru wod I dey tel una so, bifor dem born Abraham, I don alredi dey!"
43008059	Den, dem kon dey pick stone to stone am, bot Jisos hide kon komot from di Tempol aria.
43009001	Wen Jisos dey waka pas, e kon si won man wey blind from di taim wey en mama born am.
43009002	Naim en disaipols ask am, "Tisha, na wish pesin sin, wey mak dis man blind since di taim en mama born am? Na di man or na en papa and mama?"
43009003	Jisos ansa dem, "Nor bi di man or en papa and mama sin, bot e blind since dem born am, bikos God won yuz dis won show en pawa wit wetin go hapun to am.
43009004	"I must du di wok for di Pesin wey send mi bifor day go dak, bikos nite dey kom wen nobodi go fit wok.
43009005	"As far as I dey insaid dis wold, na mi bi di lite for di wold.
43009006	Afta e tok finish, e spit for groun kon tak di san-san wey e spit put tak rub di blind man eye.
43009007	Den e tel am, "Mak yu go wosh yor face insaid di pond wey dem dey kol Siloam (dis name min 'Send'). So di blind man kon go wosh en face as Jisos tel am. As e dey kom bak, e kon bigin si.
43009008	Den en nebors and oda pipol wey dey si-am dey beg bifor, kon dey ask sey, "Dis nor bi di man wey dey sidan dey beg for moni?"
43009009	Som pipol ansa, "Na-im o-o!" Odas tok sey, "Nor bi en, bot e luk laik am." Di man ensef kon sey, "Na mi bi di pesin."
43009010	Dem ask am, "Wetin hapun wey mak yu bigin si?"
43009011	E kon ansa dem, "Na di man wey dem dey kol Jisos tak san-san wey e spit put rub my eye. Den e tel mi sey, 'Mak yu go Siloam go wosh yor face.' Afta I go wosh my face for di pond, I kon bigin si."'
43009012	Naim dem ask am, "Wer di man dey?" E kon ansa dem, "I nor no-o-o."
43009013	Dem kon tak di man wey blind bifor go mit di Farisi pipol.
43009014	(bikos na for Sabat Day Jisos spit for san-san tak rub di blind man eye).
43009015	Naim di Farisi pipol ask am again, "Haw yu tak bigin si?" E kon ansa dem, "E tak di san-san wey e spit put rub my eye and afta I don wosh my face, I kon bigin si."
43009016	Som Farisi pipol kon sey, "Nor bi God send dis man, bikos e nor sopoz to du eni wok for Sabat Day." Bot odas sey, "Haw pesin wey dey komit sin go fit du dis kaind mirakol?" Dis argument kon mak di pipol divide.
43009017	Dem kon ask di man wey blind bifor sey, "Wetin yu tink abaut di man wey mak yu dey si?" Di man ansa, "Na profet e bi."
43009018	Di Ju oga dem nor gri biliv sey, tru-tru di man blind bifor, so dem kon kol en papa and mama.
43009019	Dem kon ask dem, "Na una pikin bi dis? Na tru sey e blind wen una born am? Haw e kon tak dey si naw?"
43009020	So en papa and mama ansa, "Wi no sey dis na awa pikin and e blind wen wi born am.
43009021	"Bot wi nor no haw e tak bigin si or ivun hu opun en eye. Mak una ask am, e don big rish to tok for ensef."
43009022	(En papa and mama tok laik dis, bikos dem dey fear di Ju oga dem wey don tok sey, "Enibodi wey tok sey na Jisos bi di Kraist, dem go driv am komot from di sinagog."
43009023	Na dis won mak en papa and mama sey, "Mak dem ask am, bikos e don big rish to tok for ensef)".
43009024	So dem kol di man again kon tel am, "Mak yu promis bifor God sey yu go tok di trut, bikos wi no sey di man na sina."
43009025	E kon ansa dem, "Weda na sina e bi, I nor no! Bot wetin I no bi sey, bifor I blind, bot naw, I don dey si."
43009026	So dem ask am again, "Wetin e du? Haw e tak mak yu dey si sef?"
43009027	E kon ansa dem, "I don tel una bifor, bot una nor gri. Why una won hear am again? Abi, una won bi en disaipols tu?"
43009028	Dem shaut for di man kon sey, "Na yu bi en disaipol. Wi bi Mosis disaipols.
43009029	"Wi no sey God tok to Mosis, bot wi nor no wer dis man from kom."
43009030	Di man kon sey, "I sopraiz for una o-o. Una nor no wer e from kom, bot na-im opun my eye!
43009031	"Wi no sey God nor dey listin to enibodi wey dey sin, bot if pesin dey du wetin God tok, God go hear en praya.
43009032	"Wi neva hear bifor sey, enibodi don fit mak pesin wey blind si.
43009033	'If God nor send dis man, e nor go fit du dis kaind tin."
43009034	Dem kon tel di man, "Na for insaid sin dem born yu, yu tink sey yu go fit tish us enitin?" So dem driv am komot from di place.
43009035	Wen Jisos hear sey dem don driv di man komot, e go luk for am kon ask am, "Yu biliv hu Man Pikin bi?"
43009036	Di man kon sey, "Oga, tel mi hu e bi, mak I for fit biliv am?"
43009037	Jisos ansa am, "Na-im dey here dey tok to yu so."
43009038	Di man kon sey, "Oga, I biliv." Den e nil dan kon woship Jisos.
43009039	Jisos tel am, "I kon joj pipol for di wold, so dat di pipol wey nor dey si, go bigin si and doz wey tink sey dem dey si, dia eye go blind."
43009040	Wen di Farisi pipol wey dey der hear wetin Jisos tok, dem kon ask am, "Yu tink sey wi sef blind?"
43009041	Jisos ansa dem, "If una gri sey una blind, God nor go kondem una bikos of una sin, bot as una tok sey una dey si so, una sin dey for una head."
43010001	"Na tru wod I dey tel una, pesin wey nor pas door enta di place wey dem dey kip ship, bot klimb pas anoda side enta di place, na big tif.
43010002	"Di pesin wey pas di door enta, na-im bi di shepad wey dey gaid di ship.
43010003	"Di gateman go opun di door for am and en ship go hear en vois wen e kol dia name and e go lid dem kom out.
43010004	"Wen e don bring all en ship kom out, e go-go dia front and di ship go folo am, bikos dem no en vois.
43010005	"Dem nor go gri folo stranja, bot dem go run from am, bikos dem nor no di stranja vois."
43010006	Jisos tel dem dis parabol, bot dem nor undastand wetin e tok.
43010007	So Jisos kon tel dem again, "I dey tel una tru wod. Na mi bi di door wey di ship go must pas enta.
43010008	"All di pipol wey kom bifor mi, na big tif dem bi and di ship nor go gri listin to dem.
43010009	"Na mi bi di door, enibodi wey enta tru mi, God go save am. E go-go insaid and out and e go si beta grass chop.
43010010	"Di tin wey tif dey du, na to tif, kil and distroi pipol, bot mi, I kom so dat pipol go get life, di kaind life wey ful wel-wel.
43010011	"Na mi bi di gud shepad. Di gud shepad redi to die for di ship.
43010012	"Di pesin wey dem haya nor bi di shepad and bikos nor bi en get di ship, e go run wen e si lion dey kom, so di lion go skata di ship, kon kil di won wey e kash.
43010013	"Bikos di pesin nor kare for di ship, naim go mak am run liv dem.
43010014	"Na mi bi di gud shepad, I no di ship wey bi my own and dem no mi tu.
43010015	bikos my Papa no mi and I no am, naim mak mi redi to die for di ship.
43010016	"I get oda ship wey nor dey here. I must gada dem tu and dem go listin to my vois, all of dem go dey togeda and na won shepad go lid dem.
43010017	"Na dis bi di rizin wey mak my Papa laik mi, bikos I redi to sakrifais my life, so dat I go fit tak am bak again.
43010018	"Nobodi go fit tak my life from mi, bot na mi go put am dan by mysef and I get di pawa to tak am bak again. Dis na wetin God komand mi to du."
43010019	Anoda big kworel kon hapun bitwin di Ju pipol bikos of wetin Jisos tok.
43010020	Meni of dem kon dey sey, "Dimon dey insaid am and en head nor koret. Why una dey listin to am sef?"
43010021	Odas kon sey, "Di pesin wey get dimon nor go fit tok laik dis. No dimon fit mak blind pesin si."
43010022	Di taim for di Dedikeshon Fist for Jerusalem kon rish.
43010023	Dat na di taim wey rain dey fal (and kold dey strong wel-wel) and Jisos kon dey waka insaid di varanda wer Solomon for dey tak briz, wey dey insaid di Tempol yard.
43010024	Di Ju oga dem gada roun Jisos, kon ask am, "Haw long yu go mak us dey wait? If na yu bi di Kraist, mak yu tel us."
43010025	Jisos ansa dem, "I don tel una and una nor biliv. Di tin wey I tak my Papa name dey du, dey bear witnes for mi.
43010026	"Bot una nor biliv mi bikos una nor bi my ship.
43010027	"My ship dey hear my vois and I no dem and dem dey folo mi.
43010028	"I don giv dem life wey nor dey end and dem nor go eva die. Nobodi go fit tak dem komot from my hand.
43010029	"My Papa wey giv dem to mi big pas evribodi and nobodi go fit tak dem komot from my Papa hand,
43010030	bikos mi and my Papa, na won."
43010031	Di Ju oga dem kon pick stone again, to tak stone am.
43010032	So Jisos tel dem, "I don du meni gud tins wey una si from my Papa, wish won mak una won stone mi so?"
43010033	Di Ju oga dem kon ansa, "Wi nor won stone yu bikos of di gud tins, bot na bikos yu wey bi ordinari pesin, dey mak mout sey, yu bi God."
43010034	Jisos kon ansa dem, "Una law nor tok sey, I sey, 'Una bi gods?'
43010035	"If dem kol di pipol wey God send en wod go mit, sey, 'Dem bi gods' and God wod nor go eva shange,
43010036	'Why una dey tel di pesin wey God shuz for ensef and wey E send kom dis wold, "Yu dey tok against God", bikos I sey, "I bi God Pikin?'"
43010037	"If I nor du di tins wey my Papa send mi, mak una nor biliv mi.
43010038	"Bot if I dey du dem, ivun if una nor biliv mi, mak una biliv di tins wey I dey du, so dat una go no and undastand sey, I dey insaid my Papa and my Papa dey insaid mi tu."

43010040	Jisos go bak kon kros Jordan Riva, wer Jon for baptize pipol and e kon stay for der.

43011001	Won man wey en name bi Lazarus wey nor wel. En wit Mary and Marta, en sistas kom from Betani.
43011002	Dis Mary naim pour perfume for Jisos leg, kon klin dem wit en hair.
43011003	So di sistas kon send mesage go mit Jisos sey, Oga, yor frend wey yu luv wel-wel wey nor wel.
43011004	Wen Jisos hear di mesage, e kon sey, "Dis siknes nor go kil Lazarus. E go mak God and en pikin get onor."
43011005	(E klear sey Jisos luv Marta, Mary and Lazarus wel-wel.)
43011006	Afta e don hear sey Lazarus nor wel, e stay wer e dey for anoda tu days.
43011007	Den e kon tel en disaipols, "Mak wi go bak to Judea."
43011008	Bot en disaipols kon ask, 'Tisha, nor bi di place wer di Ju pipol won for kil us yu sey mak wi go again so?
43011009	Jisos ansa, "Evriday get twef hours wey lite dey tak shine, so pipol nor dey fear to waka, bikos dem dey si wel-wel, as e bi sey lite dey.
43011010	Bot pesin wey waka for nite, go fit fal, bikos e nor get lite to si road."
43011011	Den Jisos tel dem, "Awa frend Lazarus dey slip, bot I won go wak-am up."
43011012	Di disaipols sey, "Oga, if e jos dey slip, den e go wak-up."
43011013	(Dem tink sey, wetin Jisos min bi sey, Lazarus jos dey slip, bot wetin e min bi sey, Lazarus don die.)
43011014	So e kon tel dem sey, "Lazarus don die.
43011015	"I hapi sey I nor dey der, so dat una go get anoda shanse to biliv mi. Mak una kom mak wi go si-am."
43011016	So Tomas, (wey bi Twins) kon tel di oda disaipol, "Mak wi folo am go, so dat wi go die wit am."
43011017	Wen Jisos rish Betani, dem kon tel am sey e don rish for days wey dem bere Lazarus.
43011018	(Betani na abaut tu miles from Jerusalem,
43011019	and from der, meni Ju pipol kon salot Mary and Marta, bikos of dia broda wey die.)
43011020	So wen Marta hear sey Jisos dey kom, e kon waka go mit am, bot Mary sidan for haus.
43011021	Marta kon tel Jisos, "Oga, if to sey yu dey here, my broda for nor die."
43011022	Bot I no sey, "God go giv yu enitin wey yu ask am."
43011023	So Jisos tel am, "Yor broda go wak-up again."
43011024	Den Marta sey, I no sey e go wak-up again for di resureshon day."
43011025	Jisos ansa am, "Na mi bi di resureshon and na mi dey giv life. Enibodi wey biliv mi go get life ivun if e don die,
43011026	and di pesin wey biliv mi for dis life, nor go eva die. Marta, yu biliv wetin I tok so?"
43011027	Marta kon ansa, "Yes! Oga, I biliv sey yu bi Kraist, God Pikin, wey kom dis wold."
43011028	Den Marta go mit Mary, en sista, kon tok for en ear sey, "Di tisha dey here and e won si yu."
43011029	Wen Mary hear wetin e tok, e kon get up go mit Jisos.
43011030	Jisos stil dey outsaid di vilage wen Marta go mit am.
43011031	Di pipol wey kom salot Mary kon si haw e waka komot kwik-kwik, dem tink sey na Lazarus grave e for dey go krai, so dem folo am.
43011032	Wen Mary si Jisos, e fal for en front kon sey, "Oga, if to sey yu dey here, my broda nor for die."
43011033	Jisos kon si as Mary and di oda pipol dey krai. So e sori for dem and di tin pain am wel-wel.
43011034	E kon ask dem, "Wer una bere am?" Den dem tel am, "Oga, kom mak wi show yu."
43011035	Jisos kon krai.
43011036	Di pipol wey kom salot dem kon sey, "Jisos luv dis man wel-wel o-o."
43011037	Bot som of dem sey, "Dis man wey mak blind man si, e nor fit du mak Lazarus nor for die?"
43011038	Jisos kon sori for dem again, den e waka go di grave. (Dis grave na big hol insaid rock wey dem tak big stone kova).
43011039	Jisos kon sey, "Mak una rimov di stone." Marta wey bi Lazarus sista kon sey, Oga, by dis taim e go don dey smel, bikos e don rish for days wey dem bere am."
43011040	Jisos tel am, "I nor tel yu bifor sey, 'Yu go si God pawa, if yu biliv mi?'"
43011041	So, dem kon rol di stone komot from di grave mout. Den Jisos luk hevun, kon sey, "Papa, I tank yu sey Yu dey always hear mi and dey du di tins wey I ask from Yu."
43011042	I no sey Yu dey always hear mi, bot I dey tok laik dis, bikos of di pipol wey stand here naw, so dat dem go biliv sey na Yu send mi."
43011043	Wen e don tok dis finish, e kon shaut, "Lazarus, kom out!"
43011044	Den Lazarus kon kom out, bot di klot wey dem tak bere am stil kova en bodi. So, Jisos tel dem, "Mak una luz di klot komot for en bodi, mak e dey go."
43011045	Den meni of di Ju pipol wey folo Mary go di gravside biliv Jisos, wen dem si wetin hapun.

43011047	Den di prist oga dem and Farisi pipol kon kol di kansol memba dem togeda, ask dem, "Wetin wi go du, since di man dey du plenti mirakols?
43011048	"If wi let am kontinu laik dis, evribodi go biliv am and di Roman govnor go kom tak di place wey wi dey woship and awa kontri."
43011049	Den won of dem wey en name bi Kaifas, wey bi di High Prist dat year, kon sey, "Una bi fool wey nor undastand wetin dey hapun.
43011050	"Una nor no sey e beta mak won man die for evribodi, dan sey mak evribodi for dis kontri die?"
43011051	(Dis man tok laik dis, bikos naim bi di High Prist dat year. E tok tru sey, Jisos go die for di hol Ju pipol, bot e nor no wetin e tok,
43011052	and nor bi for onli di Ju pipol, bot mak all God shildren, wey dey di wold for gada togeda.)

43011054	Bikos of dis, Jisos nor kon dey waka for Judea as e dey du bifor, bot en and en disaipols kon go stay for di tawn wey dem dey kol Efraim, wey near desert.

43011057	(By dis taim, di prist oga dem and di Farisi pipol don giv orda sey, enibodi wey no wer Jisos dey, mak e kon tok, so dat dem go-go kash am).
43012001	Sis days bifor Passova Fist rish, Jisos go Betani, wer Lazarus, di pesin wey e wak-up from deat, dey stay.
43012002	So dem kon du parti for Jisos dat evenin. Marta kon dey serv dem fud and Lazarus dey among di pipol wey sidan for tabol wit Jisos.
43012003	Mary tak perfume wey dear wel-wel, wey plenti rish quota galon kon pour am for Jisos tu leg. Den e yuz en hair tak klin dem. (Di perfume sent kon ful evriwer for insaid di haus).

43012006	(Judas tok laik dis, nor bi sey e kare for poor pipol, bot bikos na tif e bi. As e bi sey naim dey kip di moni, e dey tif from am.)
43012007	Den Jisos ansa, "Mak yu nor trobol di wuman, e du dis tin dey wait di day wen dem go bere mi.

43012010	Di prist oga dem kon plan to kil Lazarus tu,
43012011	bikos naim mak plenti Ju pipol for Jerusalem, biliv Jisos.

43012014	Jisos si won smol donkey and e kon sidan put, jos as God wod sey,
43012015	"Pipol wey dey Zion, mak una nor fear; mak una si una king sidan on-top donkey dey kom!"

43012020	Som Greek pipol go woship God for di fist for Jerusalem.
43012021	Dem kon mit Filip wey kom from Betsaida for Galili kon tel am, "Oga, wi go laik to si Jisos."
43012022	Filip tel Andru, den dem kon go tel Jisos.
43012023	Jisos tel dem, "Di taim don kom wen God go onor en own pikin.
43012024	"I tel una tru wod, if won corn sid fal for groun and e nor die, e nor go grow, bot if e die, e go grow kon bear plenti sid.
43012025	"Enibodi wey luv en life for dis wold, go luz am, bot di pesin wey nor luv en life for dis wold, go get life wey nor dey end.
43012026	"Enibodi wey redi to serv mi, go must folo mi and wer I dey, na der my savant go dey tu. Enibodi wey serv mi, my Papa go onor am.
43012027	"My heart heavi wel-wel. Wetin I go tok? 'Papa, mak yu save mi from dis tin wey won hapun'? No! Na dis tin mak mi kom dis wold.
43012028	"Papa, mak yu onor yor name." Den won vois tok from hevun sey, "I don onor am bifor and I go onor am again."

43012031	Di taim to joj di pipol for dis wold don rish and God go driv Satan, wey dey kontrol dis wold komot.
43012032	Bot as for mi, if una kari mi go up for kros, I go draw evribodi kom mit mi."

43012035	Jisos ansa dem, "My lite nor go dey wit una tey. Naw wen di lite dey, mak una tak am waka, so dat daknes nor go kova una. Bikos di pesin wey dey waka for daknes, nor dey si wer e dey go.
43012036	"As una get di lite naw, mak una biliv am, so dat una go bi lite shildren. Wen Jisos don tok dis tin finish, e kon komot der go hide.
43012037	Aldoh Jisos don du meni mirakol for dia front, dem nor stil biliv am.
43012038	Dis mak wetin Profet Isaia tok hapun, wen e sey, "Oga, wish pipol don biliv wetin wi tok and hu God don show en pawa?"
43012039	As di pipol nor fit biliv, naim mak Isaia tok anoda wod sey,
43012040	"God don blind dia eye and mak dia heart strong laik stone, so dat dem nor go si wit dia eye and undastand wit dia heart, so dem nor go fit kom mit mi, mak I for heal dem."
