43012042	Meni pipol and meni Ju oga kon biliv Jisos, bot bikos of di Farisi pipol, doz wey biliv nor fit tok for publik abaut Jisos Kraist, so dat dem nor go driv dem komot for di sinagog.
43012043	Bikos Ju pipol laik mak pipol dey praiz dem pas wetin God tink abaut dem.
43012044	Jisos kon shaut sey, "Di pesin wey biliv mi, nor bi mi e biliv, bot na my Papa wey send mi.
43012045	"And di pesin wey si mi, don si God wey send mi.
43012046	"I kom as lite for dis wold, so dat enibodi wey go biliv mi nor go waka insaid daknes.
43012047	"Enibodi wey hear wetin I tok and nor obey am, nor bi mi go joj am, bikos I nor kom joj di wold, bot I kom save pipol for di wold.
43012048	"Enibodi wey rejet mi and nor du wetin I tok, God go yuz dis my wod joj am for di last day.
43012049	"Bikos nor bi my pawa I tak dey tok, bot na my Papa wey send mi dey tel mi wetin I dey tok.
43012050	"I no sey enitin wey God komand, dey giv life wey nor dey end, so I dey tok wetin E send mi."
43013001	Bifor dem du di Passova Fist, Jisos no sey en taim don rish wen e go komot for dis wold go mit en Papa. Bikos e luv di pipol wey dey di wold, e kon show dem haw en luv for dem strong rish.
43013002	Bifor dem start to chop evenin fud, devol don alredi enta Judas Iskarot maind, wey bi Saimon pikin, sey, mak e sel Jisos giv en enemi.
43013003	Bikos Jisos no sey en Papa don gi-am pawa to kontrol evritin and as e bi sey e kom from God and e dey go bak go mit am,
43013004	e kon stand-up for wer dem dey chop, rimov en big koat kon tie towel for en waist.
43013005	E kon pour wota for basin, bigin dey wosh en disaipols leg and dey dry dem wit di towel wey dey en waist.
43013006	Wen e rish Saimon Pita turn, Pita kon tel am, "Oga, yu won wosh my leg?"
43013007	Jisos ansa, "Yu nor go fit undastand wetin I dey du naw, bot yu go undastand am leta."
43013008	Pita kon tel am, "I nor go gri mak yu wosh my leg!" Den Jisos ansa, "If I nor wosh yor leg, mi and yu nor go get enitin togeda again."
43013009	So Saimon Pita tel am, "Oga, mak yu nor wosh onli my leg, bot mak yu wosh my hand and head tu!"
43013010	Jisos ansa, "Di pesin wey don baff, onli nid to wosh en leg, bikos e don dey klin. Una dey klin, bot nor bi all of una."
43013011	(Bikos Jisos no di pesin wey go sel am, naim mak am sey, "Nor bi all of una dey klin.")
43013012	So wen Jisos don wosh dia leg finish, e kon wear en big koat bak. Den e go sidan for di tabol kon ask dem, "Una undastand wetin I du for una so?
43013013	"Una dey kol mi 'Tisha' and 'Oga', una koret, bikos na so I bi.
43013014	"So, if mi, wey bi una oga and tisha, wosh una leg, e gud mak una wosh ish oda leg tu.
43013015	"I don giv una ezampol wey una go folo. So mak una du for ish oda as I don du for una."
43013016	"Mak I tel una tru wod, savant nor dey big pas en oga, jos as di pesin wey bi mesenga nor dey big pas di oga wey send am.
43013017	"Since una no wetin I dey tok, God go bless una, if una du dem."
43013018	"Wetin I dey tok so nor konsan all of una, bikos I no di pipol wey I shuz. Dis show sey God wod na tru, sey, 'Di pesin wey folo mi chop don turn to my enemi.'
43013019	"I don tel una bifor e go hapun, so dat wen e hapun, una go biliv sey na mi bi Kraist.
43013020	"I dey tel una tru wod, enibodi wey risiv di pesin wey I send, don risiv mi and enibodi wey risiv mi, don risiv God wey send mi kom."
43013021	Wen e don tok dis tin finish, en heart kon heavi wel-wel, den e sey, "I dey tel una tru wod, won of una go sel mi giv my enemi."
43013022	Di disaipols luk ish oda kon dey wori and tink for dia maind sey, "Wish pesin e dey tok abaut?"
43013023	Jon, di disaipol wey Jisos luv wel-wel, sidan for en rite hand wen dem dey chop.
43013024	So, Saimon Pita kon yuz eye tel am sey mak e ask Jisos wish pesin e dey tok abaut.
43013025	Den Jon bend en head near Jisos chest kon ask am, "Oga, hu yu dey tok abaut?"
43013026	Jisos ansa, "Na di pesin wey I go giv dis bread afta I don shuk-am insaid di pot." Den e shuk di bread insaid di pot kon gi-am to Judas Iskarot, wey bi Saimon pikin.
43013027	Afta Judas tak di bread, devol enta en maind. Jisos kon tel am, "Di tin wey yu won du, mak yu go du-am kwik-kwik."
43013028	(None of dem wey sidan for di tabol undastand why Jisos tok to Judas laik dat.
43013029	Som of dem tink sey, since na Judas dey kip di moni, Jisos tel am sey mak e go buy wetin dem go yuz for di fist or mak e giv poor pipol moni).
43013030	Wen Judas don tak di bread, e huri komot for di place. (By dis taim, day don dak.)
43013031	Wen e don komot, Jisos kon sey, "Naw, di taim don rish wen God go onor en pikin and en pikin go onor am tu.
43013032	"Wen di pikin don onor God, God sef go onor am bak.
43013033	"My shildren, na smol taim rimain wey I go dey wit una. Leta, una go dey faind mi and as I tel di Ju oga dem bifor sey, 'Wer I dey go una nor go fit kom der', na di same wod I dey tel una naw.
43013034	"I dey giv una new komand: Una must luv ish oda, as I luv una,
43013035	so dat evribodi go no sey una bi my disaipols, if una luv ish oda."
43013036	Saimon Pita kon tel am, "Oga, wer yu dey go?" Jisos ansa, "Una nor go fit folo mi go di place wey I dey go naw, bot una go kom mit mi for der leta."
43013037	Pita ask am, "Oga, why wi nor go fit folo yu naw? I redi to die bikos of yu!"
43013038	Jisos ansa am, "Yu rili redi to die for mi? Mak I tel yu tru wod, bifor fawo go du 'Kukuruku' dis nite, yu go tok tiri taims sey, yu no mi."
43014001	"Mak una nor let enitin wori una maind. Since una biliv God, mak una stil biliv mi.
43014002	"Meni rooms dey for my Papa haus and I dey go priper place for una to stay, if nor bi so, I for tel una.
43014003	"Wen I don finish, I go kom tak una, so dat una go stay wit mi for wer I dey.
43014004	"And una go no di place wey I dey go and haw una go tak rish der."
43014005	Tomas kon ask am, "Oga, wi nor no wer yu dey go, haw wi go tak no road?"
43014006	Jisos ansa am, "Na mi bi di road, di trut and life. Nobodi go fit go mit my Papa, unles e pas tru mi.
43014007	"Bot since una don no mi, una go no my Papa tu. Naw wey una don no am, una don si-am."
43014008	Filip kon sey, "Oga, show us yor Papa and wi go dey okay."
43014009	Jisos ansa am, "So Filip, I don dey wit una all dis taim and yu stil nor no mi? Di pesin wey don si mi, don si my Papa! Why yu kon dey sey, 'Show us yor Papa?'
43014010	"Yu nor biliv sey mi and my Papa na di same? As e dey insaid mi, na so I dey insaid am. Di wod wey I dey tel una so, I nor dey tok am wit my own pawa, bot na my Papa wey dey insaid mi, dey du all dis mirakol tru mi.
43014011	"Mak una biliv sey I dey insaid my Papa and my Papa dey insaid mi, bot if una nor fit biliv mi, mak una biliv bikos of di mirakols wey I dey du.
43014012	"I tel una tru wod, di pesin wey biliv mi, go du di kaind mirakol wey I dey du and e go ivun du di wons wey big pas dem, bikos I dey go mit my Papa.
43014013	"And enitin wey una yuz my name ask, I go du-am, so dat pipol go onor di Papa bikos of en pikin.
43014014	"If una ask enitin wit my name, I go du-am for una.
43014015	"If una luv mi, una go du wetin I tok.
43014016	"Den I go ask my Papa and E go send una anoda Pesin wey go help and stay wit una foreva.
43014017	"Naim bi di Spirit wey dey tok trut, wey pipol for dis wold nor go fit risiv, bikos dem nor fit si-am or no am, bot una no am, bikos e dey stay insaid una.
43014018	"I nor go liv una laik pikin wey nor get papa and mama, bikos I go kom mit una again.
43014019	"Afta somtaim, di pipol for dis wold nor go si mi, bot una go si mi and bikos I dey alaif, una go dey alaif tu.
43014020	"Dat taim, una go no sey I dey insaid my Papa and una dey insaid mi, as I dey insaid una.
43014021	"Enibodi wey hear and du wetin I tok, luv mi. Di pesin wey luv mi, mi and my Papa go luv am tu and I go show am hu I bi."
43014022	Judas (dis nor bi Judas Iskarot) kon sey, "Oga, why yu won show yorsef giv us and yu nor won show oda pipol for di wold?"
43014023	Jisos ansa am, "Enibodi wey luv mi, go du wetin I tok and my Papa go luv am, wi go kon mit and stay wit am.
43014024	"Di pesin wey nor luv mi, nor go du wetin I tok. Wetin una dey hear so nor bi my wod, bot na my Papa own.
43014025	"I don dey tel una all dis tins since I dey wit una.
43014026	"Bot di pesin wey go help una na di Holi Spirit, wey my Papa go send kom for my name. E go tish una evritin and e go help una rimemba evritin wey I don tel una.
43014027	"Mak una maind res, bikos na my peace I giv una. My peace difren from di won wey di wold dey giv. Mak una nor fear or alow enitin wori una maind.
43014028	"Una rimemba wen I tel una sey, 'I dey komot and I go kom bak kon mit una?' If una luv mi, una go hapi wen I tok sey, 'I dey go mit my Papa', bikos my Papa big pas mi.
43014029	"I don tel una naw bifor e hapun, so dat wen e hapun, una go biliv mi.
43014030	"I nor go tok tu mush naw, bikos di devol wey dey rule dis wold, dey kom and e nor get pawa for my bodi.
43014031	"Since I dey du wetin my Papa tel mi, di wold go no sey I luv my Papa. So mak una get up mak wi dey go."
43015001	"Na mi bi di koret vine and na my Papa bi di gardina.
43015002	"E dey kut evri bransh wey nor dey bear frut for my bodi komot and e dey ripair evri bransh for my bodi wey dey bear frut, so dat e go bear more frut.
43015003	"Una dey klin alredi, bikos of di wod wey I tel una.
43015004	"Mak una dey insaid mi, so dat I go dey insaid una tu. As di bransh nor fit bear frut wit en own pawa, unles e dey insaid di vine plant, na so una nor go fit bear frut, unles una dey insaid mi.
43015005	"Na mi bi di vine and na una bi di bransh dem. Di pesin wey stay insaid mi and I stay insaid am, go bear plenti frut, bikos witout mi, una nor go fit du enitin.
43015006	"Enibodi wey nor stay insaid mi, go dry and pipol go gada en bransh dem, trow dem insaid fire kon burn dem.
43015007	"If una stay insaid mi and my wod dey insaid una, enitin wey una ask, I go du-am for una.
43015008	"My Papa go get big onor if una bear plenti frut, wey go show sey una bi my disaipols.
43015009	"As my Papa luv mi, na so I luv una tu, so mak una liv di kaind life wey go let mi fit luv una more-more.
43015010	"If una du wetin I tok, I go luv una, jos as I dey obey wetin my Papa tok and E luv mi.
43015011	"I don tel una all dis tins, so dat my joy go dey insaid una and una joy go ful wel-wel.
43015012	"Dis na di komand wey I giv una sey, 'Mak una luv ish oda di way I luv una.'
43015013	"E nor get luv wey big rish di won wey mak pesin die for en frend.
43015014	"Una go bi my frend if una du wetin I tok.
43015015	"I nor go kol una savant again, bikos savant nor dey undastand wetin en oga dey du, bot I dey kol una my frend, bikos I don show una evritin wey I hear from my Papa.
43015016	"Nor bi una shuz mi, bot na mi shuz una. Bikos of dat, I don giv una pawa to bear frut wey go last, so dat my papa go giv una enitin wey una ask am for my name.
43015017	"Wetin I dey tel una bi sey, 'Mak una luv ish oda.'"
43015018	"If pipol for dis wold hate una, mak una rimemba sey na mi dem first hate.
43015019	"If una bi frend wit di pipol for dis wold, dem go luv una as dia own pipol. Bot una nor bi dia frend, bikos I don shuz una from di wold, naim mak dem nor laik una.
43015020	"Mak una rimemba wetin I tel una, 'Savant nor dey big pas en oga.' If dem sofa mi, den dem go sofa una tu. If to sey dem obey my wod, dem go obey una own tu.
43015021	"Since dem nor no di Pesin wey send mi kom, dem go du all dis tins to una bikos of my name.
43015022	"If to sey I nor kom tok to dem, dem for nor dey guilti for dia sin. Bot naw, dem nor get eni eskius for dia sin.
43015023	"Di pesin wey hate mi, hate my Papa tu.
43015024	"If to sey dem nor si di mirakol wey I du, wey nobodi don du bifor, dem nor for dey guilti for dia sin. Bot afta dem don si di mirakols, dem stil hate mi and my Papa.
43015025	"All dis tins hapun, so dat wetin God law tok, go bi tru sey, 'Dem nor get rizin to tak hate mi.'
43015026	"Bot wen di tru Spirit wey I go send from my Papa to help una don kom, e go tok abaut mi.
43015027	"And unasef go tok abaut mi, bikos una dey wit mi from di biginin."
43016001	"I dey tel una all dis tins, so dat nobodi go fit disiv una.
43016002	"Dem go driv una komot for di sinagog and di taim dey kom wen di pesin wey go kil una, go tink sey e dey du God wok.
43016003	"Dem go du all dis tins, bikos dem nor no mi and my Papa.
43016004	"Bot I tel una all dis tins, so dat wen di taim rish, una go rimemba sey I tel una abaut dem bifor. I jos dey tel una all dis tins, bikos I dey wit una since.
43016005	"Naw, I dey go mit di Pesin wey send mi kom, bot una dey ask mi, 'Wer yu dey go?'
43016006	"Bot una nor hapi as I dey tel una all dis tins.
43016007	"I tel una tru wod, na for una own gud naim mak mi won go, bikos if I nor go, di Pesin wey go help una nor go kom, bot if I go, I go send am kom mit una.
43016008	"Wen e kom, e go show pipol for dis wold wetin sin, God raitiousnes and God jojment, bi.
43016009	"Di Spirit go show dem sey dem dey wrong abaut sin, bikos dem nor biliv mi.
43016010	"Dem dey wrong abaut God raitiousnes, bikos I dey go mit my Papa and dem nor go si mi again.
43016011	"And dem dey wrong abaut jojment, bikos God don kondem di pesin wey dey rule dis wold.
43016012	"I get plenti tins wey I won tel una, bot una nor go fit bear dem naw.
43016013	"Bot wen God Spirit kom, e go show una di trut. E nor go tok wetin dey en maind, bot e go tok wetin e hear from God and wetin go hapun afta I don go.
43016014	"E go dey giv mi glori wen e dey tel una di tins wey e dey hear from mi.
43016015	"Evritin wey my Papa get, na my own, naim mak mi tok sey di Spirit go tel una wetin e dey hear from mi.
43016016	"Taim go soon kom wen una nor go si mi, bot afta som taim, una go si mi."
43016017	Den som of di disaipol kon dey ask ish oda, "Wetin e min wen e sey, 'Taim go soon kom wen una nor go si mi, bot afta som taim, una go si mi bikos I dey go mit my Papa?'"
43016018	Som of dem stil sey, "Wetin e get for maind wen e sey, 'Taim go soon kom?' Wi nor undastand wetin e dey tok."
43016019	Jisos si sey dem won ask am abaut wetin e tel dem, naim e ask dem, "Una dey ask ish oda wetin I min wen I sey, 'Taim go soon kom wen una nor go si mi, bot afta som taim, una go si mi?'
43016020	"I tel una tru wod, una go krai and mourn, bot di wold go dey hapi; una go dey sad wel-wel, bot una sadnes go turn to hapines.
43016021	"Wen wuman won born pikin, e dey sofa strong pain, bikos en taim to born don rish, bot wen e don born, e go hapi and e nor go rimemba di pain again, bikos e go si sey e don born pikin.
43016022	"Na so e bi to una naw, bikos una heart dey heavi, bot I go si una again and for dat taim, una go dey hapi and nobodi go fit tak di hapines from una.
43016023	"By dat taim, una nor go ask mi enitin again. I tel una tru wod sey, enitin wey una ask my Papa wit my name, E go giv una.
43016024	"Bifor naw, una neva tak my name ask for enitin. Naw mak una yuz my name ask for enitin wey una wont and una go get-am, so dat una joy go ful wel-wel.
43016025	"Since I dey yuz parabol tok to una; bot di taim dey kom wen I nor go yuz parabol again, bot I go tel una abaut my Papa for di way wey una go undastand.
43016026	"By dat taim, una go fit ask enitin wit my name and God go du-am for una.
43016027	"My Papa luv una, bikos una luv mi and biliv sey na-im send mi.
43016028	"Na my Papa send mi kom dis wold, bot naw, I dey go bak go mit am."
43016029	En disaipols kon sey, "Yu si, na naw yu dey tok for di way wey wi undastand and nor bi wit parabol.
43016030	"Naw wi no sey yu no evritin and yu nor nid enibodi to ask yu eni kweshon. Bikos of dis, wi biliv sey na God send yu kom."
43016031	Jisos kon tel dem, "So una don biliv naw?
43016032	"Luk, di taim dey kom and e don ivun rish, wen una go skata and evribodi go-go en own way and I go stay alone. Bot I nor dey alone, bikos my Papa dey wit mi.
43016033	"I don tel una all dis tins, so dat my peace go stay wit una. Wahala ful insaid di wold and sofa dey tu, bot mak una heart dey strong, bikos I don alredi win di wold."
43017001	Wen Jisos don tok all dis tins finish, e luk up go hevun kon sey, "My Papa, di taim don kom wen Yu go giv glori to yor pikin, so dat yor pikin go giv Yu glori tu.
43017002	"Jos as Yu don giv mi pawa ova all di pipol for di wold, na so tu I go giv life wey nor dey end to evribodi wey Yu giv mi.
43017003	"Life wey nor dey end, dis na wetin e min, 'Na mak pipol no yu wey bi di onli tru God and Jisos Kraist, wey Yu send.'
43017004	"I don giv Yu glori for dis wold and I don finish di wok wey Yu send mi.
43017005	"And naw, Papa onor mi, mak Yu draw mi near Yu, jos as wi dey bifor di wold start."
43017006	"I don mak di pipol wey Yu giv mi for dis wold no yor name. Na yor own dem bi bifor Yu giv dem to mi and dem don obey yor wod.
43017007	"Naw, dem don no sey evritin wey Yu giv mi kom from Yu,
43017008	bikos I don tel dem di mesage wey Yu giv mi. Dem don asept wetin I tel dem and dem no and biliv sey na Yu send mi.
43017009	"I dey pray for di pipol wey Yu giv mi, bikos dem bi yor own, bot I nor dey pray for di oda pipol wey dey insaid di wold.
43017010	"Evritin wey I get, na yor own and evritin wey Yu get, na my own and dem don onor mi.
43017011	"I nor go dey di wold again, bot dem go stil dey insaid di wold, since I won kom mit Yu. Holi Papa, mak yor name protet di pipol wey Yu giv mi, so dat dem go bi won, jos as mi and Yu na won.
43017012	"Wen I dey wit dem, I kip dem wit yor name. No won loss, esept di won wey yor wod sey e go perish.
43017013	"Since I dey kom mit Yu, I dey tok all dis tins for di wold, so dat dia joy go ful wel-wel.
43017014	"I don giv dem yor wod and bikos of dat, di pipol for wold hate dem, since dem nor bilong to di wold, as misef nor bilong to di wold.
43017015	"I nor sey mak Yu rimov dem from di wold, bot mak Yu protet dem from di devol.
43017016	"Dem nor bilong to di wold, jos as misef nor bilong to di wold.
43017017	"Mak Yu protet dem wit di trut, bikos na yor wod bi di trut.
43017018	"Jos as Yu send mi kom insaid dis wold, na so tu I send dem go insaid di wold.
43017019	"I don seprate mysef from di wold for dia sake, so dat dem go fit seprate diasef from di wold tu."
43017020	"I nor dey pray for dem alone, bot I also dey pray for oda pipol wey go biliv mi tru di wod wey dem go tok abaut mi.
43017021	"Papa, I dey pray, so dat all of dem go get won maind, jos as mi and Yu bi won. I stil dey pray mak dem dey wit us, so dat di wold go biliv sey na Yu send mi.
43017022	"I don giv dem di onor wey Yu giv mi, so dat dem go bi won jos as wi bi won:
43017023	"I dey wit dem and Yu dey wit mi, so dat dem go rili bi won, jos as wi bi won and di wold go no sey na Yu send mi and Yu luv dem, as Yu luv mi.
43017024	"Papa, I wont mak di pipol wey Yu giv mi stay wit mi for wer I dey, so dat dem go si di glori wey Yu giv mi, bikos Yu luv mi bifor Yu mak di wold.
43017025	"Holi Papa, ivun if di pipol for di wold nor no Yu, I no Yu and dis wons no sey na Yu send mi.
43017026	"I don help dem no yor name and I go dey trai to mak oda pipol no am tu, so dat di luv wey Yu get for mi, go dey wit dem, as I dey wit dem.
43018001	Afta e don tok finish, Jisos and en disaipols komot kros go Kidron Vali kon enta won big farm.
43018002	(Judas, wey sel Jisos, no di place, bikos Jisos don go der wit en disaipols meni taims).
43018003	So Judas kon eskot meni soja, som Tempol polish and Farisi pipol enta di farm. Dem hol lamp, tosh and som hol sword and stick for hand.
43018004	Bikos Jisos no evritin wey go hapun to am, e kon ask dem, "Hu una dey faind?"
43018005	Dem ansa am, "Na Jisos wey kom from Nazaret." E kon tel dem, "Na mi bi di pesin." (Judas wey sel am, stand der wit dem).
43018006	So wen Jisos don tel dem sey, "Na mi bi di pesin", dem dress go bak kon fal for groun.
43018007	Den Jisos ask dem again, "Hu una sey una dey faind?" Dem ansa, "Na Jisos wey kom from Nazaret."
43018008	Jisos kon sey, "I don tel una sey na mi bi di pesin. Since na mi una dey faind, mak una alow dis men go."
43018009	(E tok dis wod mak e bi sey wetin dem rite for God wod na tru, "I nor loss enibodi wey Yu giv mi.")
43018010	Den Saimon Pita bring en sword out kon kut di High Prist savant rite ear komot. (Di savant name na Malkus).
43018011	Jisos kon tel Pita, "Mak yu put yor sword bak for wer e dey bifor! Yu nor no sey I go drink from di sofa cup wey my Papa giv mi?"
43018012	Den di sojas wit dia oga and di Ju oga dem tak Jisos kon tie-am wit rope.
43018013	Dem tak am go mit Annas, Kaifas fada-en-law, wey bi di High Prist for dat year.
43018014	(Dis na di Kaifas wey advise di Ju oga dem sey, "E gud mak won man die for evribodi").
43018015	Saimon Pita wit anoda disaipol kon folo dem as dem dey tak Jisos go mit Annas. (Di oda disaipol no di High Prist wel-wel, so e folo Jisos enta insaid di High Prist kompoun).
43018016	Bot Saimon Pita stand outsaid di kompoun near di door. Den di oda disaipol wey no di High Prist kom out tok to di savant girl wey dey gaid di gate and e kon alow Pita enta insaid.
43018017	Di girl wey dey di gate kon ask Pita, "Yu nor bi won of dis man disaipol?" At wons, Pita kon ansa, "I nor bi won of dem."
43018018	For dis taim, all di savant and gaids gada roun shakol fire wey dem mak to warm demsef, bikos kold strong wel-wel. Pita folo dem stand der dey warm ensef tu.
43018019	As dem dey der, di High Prist bigin dey ask Jisos kweshon abaut en disaipols and wetin e tish.
43018020	Jisos kon ansa am, "Na for publik I tok wetin I tish. Na insaid sinagog and Tempol wer all di Ju pipol dey gada, na der I for dey tish. I nor tok enitin for sikrit.
43018021	"Why yu dey ask mi? Mak yu ask di pipol wey hear mi. Dem no wetin I tok."
43018022	Afta Jisos don tok finish, won of di High Prist savant, wey stand near am slap am for face kon ask am, "Na di High Prist yu dey tok to laik dis?"
43018023	Den Jisos sey, "If wetin I tok nor koret, mak yu tel mi, bot if e koret, why yu slap mi?"
43018024	Den Annas kon send am as dem stil tie am wit rope, go mit Kaifas, wey bi di High Prist.
43018025	As Saimon Pita stand for insaid di kompoun dey warm ensef, dem kon ask am, "Yu tu nor bi won of en disaipol?" Pita denai sey, "I nor dey among dem."
43018026	Won High Prist savant, wey bi di same famili wit di man wey Pita tak sword kut en ear kon sey, "I nor si yu wit am for insaid di farm?"
43018027	Pita denai again for dia front and fawo kon du "Kukuruku."
43018028	Den, dem tak Jisos komot from Kaifas place go di Roman Govnor palise. (By dis taim, mornin don rish). Dem nor gri enta insaid di govnor haus, mak dem nor for dirti as dia tradishon tok, so dat dem go fit chop di Passova fud.
43018029	So Pilate kom mit dem for outsaid kon ask dem, "Wetin una sey dis man du?"
43018030	Dem ansa, "If to sey dis man nor bi krimina, wi nor for bring am kom mit yu."
43018031	Den Pilate tel dem, "Mak una go joj am as una law tok." Di Ju Oga dem kon sey, "Awa law nor giv us pawa to kil enibodi."
43018032	(Dis tin hapun to show sey wetin Jisos tok abaut haw e go die, na tru).
43018033	So Pilate go insaid en haus for di palise, kon kol Jisos ask am, "Na yu bi di Ju pipol king?"
43018034	Jisos ansa am, "Na from yor maind yu ask dis kweshon, abi pipol don tel yu abaut mi?"
43018035	Pilate ansa am, "Yu no sey I nor bi Ju, abi? Na yor pipol and prist oga dem bring yu kom mit mi. Wetin yu du sef?"
43018036	Jisos ansa, "My kindom nor dey dis wold. If to sey my kindom dey dis wold, my savants for fite mak I nor for kom mit di Ju oga dem. Bot as e bi so, my kindom nor dey here."
43018037	Den Pilate ask am, "So yu bi king?" Jisos ansa, "Na yu tok so and yu dey koret sey, I bi king." Na dis mak dem born mi and naim mak mi kom dis wold kon tok di trut. Enibodi wey wont hear di trut, go listin to wetin I dey tok."
43018038	Pilate stil ask am, "Wetin bi di trut?" Den e go outsaid again go mit di Ju oga dem kon tel dem, "I nor si eni bad tin wey dis man du o-o.
43018039	"Bot as una kustom sey mak I fri won prizina for una for Passova, una wont mak I fri Jisos, wey bi di Ju king?"
43018040	Den, dem kon dey shaut, "Wi nor wont dis man, na Barabas wi wont." (Na krimina dis Barabas bi).
43019001	Den Pilate kon sey mak dem flog Jisos wit koboko.
43019002	Den di sojas go kut tri bransh wey get shuku-shuku mak krawn put for en head and dem kon wear am klot wey dear wel-wel.
43019003	Dem kon dey laff am, dey tak am mak ye-ye, dey sey, "Mak una kon si di Ju pipol king." Dem slap am for face meni taims.
43019004	Pilate kom out again kon tel di Ju oga dem sey, "I won bring am kom out for una, to let una no sey I nor si enitin bad wey e du."
43019005	So Jisos kom outsaid, wit di shuku-shuku krawn for en head and di fine klot wey dem gi-am wear. Den Pilate kon sey, "Na di man bi dis!"
43019006	Wen di prist oga dem and di Tempol polish dem si-am, dem kon dey shaut, "Nail am for kros! Nail am for kros!" Den Pilate sey, "Mak onli una go nail am. Bot as for mi, I nor si eni bad tin wey e du."
43019007	Di Ju oga dem ansa, "Wi get law and di law sey, e sopoz to die, bikos e sey en na God Pikin."
43019008	Wen Pilate hear wetin dem tok, fear kon kash am wel-wel.
43019009	So e enta di haus bak kon ask Jisos, "Na wer yu from kom sef?" Bot Jisos nor ansa am.
43019010	So Pilate kon sey, "Yu nor won tok to mi? Yu nor no sey I get pawa to fri or kil yu?"
43019011	Jisos ansa, "Yu nor get pawa at-all for my life, esept God gi-am to yu. So, na di pipol wey bring mi kom mit yu, na dia sin big pas yor own."
43019012	From dat taim, Pilate kon bigin faind way to fri Jisos, bot di Ju oga dem kon dey shaut, "If yu fri dis man, yu nor bi Caesar frend. Enibodi wey sey en bi king, na Caesar enimi e bi."
43019013	Wen Pilate hear wetin dem tok, e bring Jisos kom out kon sidan for di chair for wer e dey joj kase, (dem dey kol di chair, 'Di Stone Pavement', bot na Gabata dem dey kol am for Aramaic language.)
43019014	(Dat taim na aftanun for di day wen dem dey priper for Passova Fist). So, Pilate kon tel di Ju oga dem, "Mak una luk, na una king bi dis!"
43019015	Den, dem kon bigin dey shaut, "Kil am trowey! Kil am trowey! Mak yu kil-am!" Pilate kon ask dem, "Una wont mak I nail una king for kros?" Di High Prist dem kon sey, "Di onli king wey wi get na Caesar."
43019016	So Pilate kon gi-am to dem mak dem go kil-am. Den dem kon tak Jisos komot for der.
43019017	As Jisos kari en kros dey go, e kon rish di place wey dem dey kol "Di Skul" (na Golgota dem dey kol di place for Aramaic language.)
43019018	For der, dem kon nail Jisos for kros. Dem stil nail tu oda pipol for kros, won for en rite and di oda for en left.
43019019	Pilate kon rite for sign-board wey dem nail on-top Jisos kros, wey sey, "Dis na Jisos wey kom from Nazaret, wey bi di Ju pipol king."
43019020	Since di place wer dem kil Jisos near tawn, meni of di Ju pipol wey dey for Jerusalem kom read di sign-board, bikos dem rite am for tiri language wey bi Aramaic, Latin and Greek.
43019021	Den di chief prists kon tel Pilate, "Mak yu nor rite sey, dis na Ju pipol king", bot rite sey, dis man sey, 'I bi Ju pipol king.'"
43019022	Bot Pilate ansa dem, "Wetin I don rite finish, na so e go bi."
43019023	Wen di sojas don nail Jisos for kros, dem tear en klot and dem for kon divide am. Bot dem liv di fine koat (bikos e nor get wer dem join am, since dem weave-am from top go rish botom).
43019024	So di sojas tel ish oda sey, "Mak wi nor tear am, bot mak wi gambol to si hu go tak am. Dis tin hapun to show sey, wetin dem rite for God wod na tru sey, "Dem go divide my klot, afta dem don gambol for am".
43019025	By dis taim, di onli pipol wey stand near di kros wer dem nail Jisos, na-im mama; en aunti, Mary wey bi Klopas wife and Mary Magdalin.
43019026	So wen Jisos si en mama and Jon, di disaipol wey e luv wel-wel stand for der, e kon tel en mama, "Mama, luk, dis na yor pikin."
43019027	Den e tel di disaipol, "Mak yu luk, dis na yor mama." From dat taim, di disaipol kon tak Jisos mama go en own haus.
43019028	Wen Jisos si sey evritin don finish, e kon sey, "Wota dey hungri mi", (dis show sey wetin God tok, rili hapun).
43019029	Di sojas soak sponge insaid wine wey bita, wey dey won kontena for der kon put am for di bransh of won plant wey dem dey kol hyssop kon stresh am put for Jisos mout.
43019030	Wen e don taste di wine, Jisos kon sey, "Evritin don finish." Den e bend en head dan, kon die.
43019031	Dis tin hapun for di day wen dem dey priper for di Passova Fist and bikos dem nor wont mak di dead bodi dem stay for kros for Sabat Day, (bikos dat Sabat Day na special won for dem), di Ju oga dem kon tel Pilate mak dem break dia leg, to mak sure sey dem don die, so dat dem go fit bring dia dead bodi kom dan.
43019032	So di sojas break di oda tu pipol leg wey dem kil wit Jisos.
43019033	Bot wen dem rish di kros wey Jisos dey and si sey e don die, dem nor kon break en leg.
43019034	Bot won soja kon tak spear shuk di kona of en bele, den blood and wota kon dey rush kom out.
43019035	All dis stori na tru, (bikos na di pesin wey si dem hapun, naim tok abaut dem and wetin e tok na tru), so dat una go fit biliv.
43019036	All dis tin hapun to show sey, wetin dem rite for God wod na tru sey, "Dem nor go break won singol bone for en bodi."
43019037	And God wod stil sey, "Dem go stand dey sopraiz as dem dey luk di pesin wey dem shuk en bodi."
43019038	Afta dis taim, Josef wey kom from Arimatia, wey bi Jisos sikrit disaipol, (bikos e dey fear di oda Ju oga dem), kon ask Pilate mak e alow am kari Jisos dead bodi komot for der. Pilate gri for am and e go kari Jisos bodi komot.
43019039	Nikodimos, di man wey hide go si Jisos for nite, kon folo Josef. E kari perfume wey heavi rish sevunti-faiv pounds, wey dem tak myrrh and aloe spice mak.
43019040	Den dem pour di perfume for Jisos bodi kon rap am wit linen klot akordin to di way Ju pipol dey priper dead bodi for beria.
43019041	Won garden dey near di place wer dem kil Jisos and won new grave wey dem neva bere enibodi put bifor, dey insaid di garden.
43019042	Since dat day na di day wey Ju pipol dey priper for di Passova Fist and bikos di new grave dey near der, dem kon bere Jisos insaid di grave.
43020001	For di first day for di wik, wen day neva break wel, Mary Magdalin kon go wer di grave dey. E si sey dem don rimov di stone wey dem tak kova di grave mout.
43020002	Den e run go mit Saimon Pita and Jon kon tel dem, "Sombodi don kari Jisos bodi komot from di grave and wi nor no wer dem put am."
43020003	So Pita and Jon kon go wer di grave dey.
43020004	Di tu of dem kon dey run togeda, bot Jon run pas Pita kon first am rish di grave.
43020005	E nor enta insaid di grave, bot e bend dan kon si di linen klot wey dem tak wrap Jisos bodi for groun insaid di grave.
43020006	Wen Saimon Pita rish der, e enta insaid di grave kon si di linen klot for groun tu.
43020007	Bot di smol klot wey dey for Jisos head nor dey for di same place wer di oda klot dey, e dey on en own for won kona.
43020008	Den Jon kon enta insaid and wetin e si kon mak am biliv.
43020009	(Bikos dem undastand God wod wey sey, Jisos go wak-up afta e die).
43020010	So di tu disaipol kon go bak to dia haus.
43020011	Bot Mary stand for outsaid di grave dey krai. As e stil dey krai, e kon bend dan luk insaid di grave.
43020012	Den e si tu angel wey wear white klot sidan for wer dem put Jisos bodi. Won dey for wer di head dey and di oda dey for wer di leg dey.
43020013	Dem kon ask am, "Wuman, why yu dey krai?" Mary ansa, "Dem don kari my oga komot and I nor no wer dem kari am go."
43020014	Afta e tok finish, e turn roun kon si Jisos stand for der, bot e nor no sey na Jisos bi dat.
43020015	Jisos tel am, "Wuman, why yu dey krai? Na hu yu dey faind?" Bikos Mary tink sey naim bi di gardina, e kon sey, "Oga, if na yu kari am komot, mak yu tel mi wer yu kari am go, so dat I go-go kari am."
43020016	Den Jisos kon kol am, "Mary". So, Mary turn roun face am kon kol am for Hebrew language, "Raboni" (wey min Tisha).
43020017	Jisos ansa am, "Mak yu neva tosh mi, bikos I neva go mit my Papa for hevun. Go mit my brodas, tel dem sey, "I dey go hevun go mit my Papa, wey bi yor Papa tu, my God, wey bi yor God tu."
43020018	Den Mary Magdalin go mit di disaipols for wer dem dey kon tel dem, "I don si di Oga!" Den e tel dem wetin Jisos tel am.
43020019	Dat evenin, for di first day for di wik, en disaipols kon gada togeda. Dem lock di door for di haus wey dem dey, bikos dem dey fear di Ju oga dem. Jisos stand among dem kon sey, "Mak peace dey wit una."
43020020	Wen e don tok finish, e show dem en hand and di kona of en bele wey dem tak spear shuk. Den di disaipols kon hapi wel-wel, wen dem si Jisos.
43020021	Den Jisos tel dem again, "Mak peace dey wit una. As my Papa send mi, na so I send una tu."
43020022	Wen e tok finish, e breat for dia bodi kon sey, "Mak una risiv di Holi Spirit.
43020023	"If una forgiv enibodi en sin, God go forgiv am, bot if una nor forgiv enibodi en sin, God nor go forgiv am."
43020024	For dis taim, Tomas (wey bi twins), won of di twef disaipols, nor dey der wen Jisos show ensef to dem.
43020025	Di oda disaipols kon tel am, "Wi don si Jisos." Bot e ansa dem, "Unles I si en tu hand wey dem nail kon put my finga insaid di hol wey di nail mak and shuk my hand insaid di hol wey dey en bele, I nor go eva biliv una."
43020026	Afta ate days, wen all di disaipols gada again insaid di haus and Tomas dey der wit dem dis taim, aldo dem lock all di doors, Jisos show ensef stand among dem sey, "Mak peace dey wit una."
43020027	Den e tel Tomas, "Put yor finga for my hand, mak yu tosh am. Stresh yor hand put insaid di kona for my bele. Mak yu nor dey doubt again, bot mak yu biliv."
43020028	Tomas kon ansa am, "O! My Oga and my God."
43020029	Den Jisos tel am, "So yu biliv naw, bikos yu don si mi? God go bless pipol wey neva tak eye si mi, bot dem biliv mi."
43020030	Jisos du meni mirakols wen e dey wit en disaipols wey dem nor rite for dis book.
43020031	Bot dis tins wey dem rite so, na mak una for biliv sey na Jisos bi di Kraist and naim bi Man Pikin and if una biliv am, una go get life tru en name.
43021001	Afta dis, Jisos show ensef again to en disaipols near Tiberias Sea. Dis na haw e du-am.
43021002	Saimon Pita and Tomas (wey bi twins), wit Nataniel (wey en tawn bi Kana for Galili), wit Zebedi pikin and tu oda Jisos disaipols, kon gada togeda.
43021003	Saimon Pita kon tel dem, "I dey go kash fish." Dem sey, "Wi tu go folo yu go." Den dem komot go enta won kenu. Bot dat nite dem nor kash eni fish.
43021004	Wen day break, Jisos stand for di wotasaid, bot di disaipols nor no sey naim dey der.
43021005	Jisos kon ask dem, "My shildren, una kash eni fish?" Dem ansa, "No o-o."
43021006	E kon tel dem, "Mak una trow una net go di rite side for di kenu and una go kash som fish." Wen dem don trow dia net insaid di riva, dem nor fit draw am komot from di wota, bikos di fish wey dem kash, plenti wel-wel.
43021007	Den, Jon, di disaipol wey Jisos luv kon tel Pita, "Dis man na Jisos o-o." Wen Saimon Pita hear sey di man na Jisos, e kon kwik-kwik tie en klot wel (bikos e nor wear enitin unda), den e kon jump insaid di riva.
43021008	By dis taim, di oda disaipols dey insaid di kenu dey pul di net wit di plenti fish go rish groun for di wotasaid (bikos wer dem dey, na abaut won ondred yard from di wotasaid).
43021009	Wen dem don kom dan from di kenu, dem kon si shakol fire wit fish and som bread on-top am.
43021010	Jisos tel dem, "Mak una bring som of di fish wey una kash kom."
43021011	Den Saimon Pita enta di kenu kon pul di net kom groun. Di net kash plenti big-big fish wey rish won ondred and fifti-tiri and di net nor tear.
43021012	Jisos kon tel dem, "Mak una kom chop." Bot dem nor fit ask am, "Hu yu bi"? bikos dem biliv sey na Jisos e bi.
43021013	Den Jisos kon giv dem bread and fish.
43021014	Dis mak am di ted taim wen Jisos show ensef to en disaipols, afta e don kom out from grave.
43021015	Wen dem don chop finish, Jisos kon ask Saimon Pita, "Saimon, Jon pikin, yu luv mi pas all dis tins?" E ansa, "Yes, Oga! Yu no sey I luv yu". Jisos kon tel am, "Mak yu fid my ship."
43021016	Jisos ask am again, "Saimon, Jon pikin, yu rili tink sey yu luv mi?" Pita ansa, "Yes, oga! Yu no sey I luv yu." Jisos kon tel am, "Mak yu kare for my ship."
43021017	Jisos ask am di ted taim, "Saimon, Jon pikin, yu sure sey yu luv mi so?" Pita heart kon heavi, bikos e pain am wel-wel, as Jisos ask am di same kweshon tiri taims, "Yu sure sey yu luv mi so?" Den Pita kon sey, "Oga, yu no evritin, yu no sey I rili luv yu." So, Jisos kon sey, "Mak yu fid my ship.
43021018	"I tel yu tru wod, wen yu dey smol, yu dey du as yu laik, dey dress as yu laik and dey go eniwer wey yu wont, bot wen yu go kon old, yu go spread yor hand and oda pipol go help yu tie yor klot and kari yu go wer yu nor won go."
43021019	(Jisos tok dis to show haw Pita go die, so dat God go get onor). Afta Jisos tok finish, e kon tel Pita, "Mak yu folo mi."
43021020	Wen Pita turn roun, e kon si Jon, (di disaipol wey Jisos luv wel-wel), dey folo dem. (Dis na di disaipol wey bend en head near Jisos chest wen dem dey chop kon ask am, "Oga, hu bi di pesin wey go sel yu giv yor enemi?")
43021021	Wen Pita si-am, e kon ask Jisos, "Oga, wot abaut dis man?"
43021022	Jisos ansa am, "Mak yu maind yor own biznes. If I wont sey mak e stay ontil I kom bak, wish won konsan yu insaid? Mak yu yorsef folo mi."
43021023	Den di rumor kon dey spread among di brodas and sistas sey, di disaipol nor go die. Bot Jisos nor rili tel Pita sey di oda disaipol nor go die, bot e tok sey, "If I wont sey mak e stay ontil I kom bak, wish won konsan yu insaid?"
43021024	Na dis bi di disaipol wey bear witnes abaut all dis tins and wey rite dem and wi no sey wetin e rite, na tru.
43021025	Jisos du meni oda tins wey dem nor rite dan. If to sey dem rite all of dem, di wold nor go get space wey go kontain all di books, wer dem rite dem put.
44001001	My frend Teofilos, for di book wey I first rite giv yu, I tok abaut all di tins wey Jisos Kraist start to dey du and tish,
44001002	ontil di day wen God kon kari am go hevun, afta e giv orda to di apostols, wey e shuz wit di Holi Spirit.
44001003	Na di same apostols e show ensef meni taim sey, e stil dey alaif, afta di sofa wey e sofa. Dem si-am for forti days and e tel dem abaut God kindom.
44001004	Den wen e folo dem sidan dey tok, e kon komand dem sey, "Mak una nor liv Jerusalem, bot mak una wait for di tin wey my Papa promis wey I don tel una bifor.
44001005	"Jon dey baptaiz wit wota, bot e nor go tey wen God go baptaiz una wit en Holi Spirit (wey go kontrol una life foreva)".
44001006	So wen dem gada, dem kon start to ask Jisos Kraist, "Oga! Na naw yu go start to rule Izrel?"
44001007	Jisos ansa dem, "Di taim wey God plan nor konsan una,
44001008	bot una go get pawa wen di Holi Spirit don enta una life and una go tel pipol abaut mi for Jerusalem, for evriwer for Judea and Samaria go rish all di far place wey dey dis wold."
44001009	So afta e don tok wit dem, God kon kari am up ontil kloud kova am and dem nor fit si-am again.
44001010	As dem stil dey luk up as e dey go, tu men wey wear white klot stand near dem
44001011	kon sey, "Galili pipol, na wetin mak una stand der dey luk hevun laik dat? Dis Jisos Kraist wey God don kari go hevun today, go stil kom bak di same way wey una si-am dey go hevun."
44001012	So dem waka go bak to Jerusalem from Mount Olives (wey dey near Jerusalem and di place wey dem waka so, far pas haw di law dey alow pipol waka for Sabat Day).
44001013	Wen dem enta Jerusalem, dem kon go di room for upstair wer dem dey stay. Pita and Jon; James and Andru; Filip and Tomas; Batlomi and Matiu; James wey bi Afius pikin, Saimon wey dem dey kol Zilot and Judas wey bi James pikin, na all of dem gada for der.

44001016	"My brodas, di wod wey di Holi Spirit yuz David tok abaut Judas, wey show road to di pipol wey arres Jisos Kraist, must hapun,
44001017	bikos e dey awa grup bifor and e dey folo us du di wok."
44001018	(Dis Judas buy won land wit di moni wey e kolet for di wiked tin wey e du and na der e hang ensef til en bele burst and all en intestine kon skata kom out,
44001019	sotey all di pipol for Jerusalem hear di stori and naim mak dem dey kol di place for dia language, 'Akeldama, wey min, Blood Land). '
44001020	"For Psalm book, God wod sey, 'Mak en haus empti, mak nobodi stay der again and mak anoda pesin tak en place. '
44001021	"So, mak won pesin from di men wey dey folo us since di taim wey Oga Jisos Kraist dey wit us,
44001022	from wen dem baptaiz am, ontil e go up liv us, mak e kon join us tel pipol di trut sey, Jisos Kraist don raiz-up from grave."
44001023	So dem shuz tu men, won na Josef wey dem dey kol Basabas (bot oda pipol dey kol am Justus) and di oda won, na Matias.
44001024	Den dem kon pray, "Oga Jisos Kraist, na yu no wetin dey insaid evribodi maind. Mak yu show us di pesin wey yu wont among dis tu pipol,
44001025	so dat e go tak Apostol Judas, wey kil ensef, place."

44002001	Wen Pentecost Day rish, di disaipols kon gada for won place.
44002002	At wons, won kaind nois wey bi laik heavi briz kom from hevun kon ful di hol haus wer dem sidan.
44002003	Dem kon si smol-smol fire wey bi laik kando lite dey fal kom from hevun on-top dia head, won-by-won.
44002004	Den di Holi Spirit enta dia bodi and as di Spirit giv dem pawa, dem kon start to tok for difren language.

44002015	dis men neva drink enitin as una tink, bikos na jos nain o' klok for mornin and e tu earli to drink.

44002018	"For dat taim, I go giv my Spirit to all di pipol wey dey serv mi and dem go dey profesai.

44002027	bikos I no sey God nor go alow mi stay for grave or mak my bodi rotin for groun.

44003001	Won day, Pita and Jon dey go di Tempol go pray for tiri o' klok for aftanun.
44003002	Som pipol dey always kari won man, wey nor fit waka since en mama born am, kom di Tempol domot wey dem dey kol, "Beautiful Gate", so dat e go dey beg for moni from pipol, wey dey enta insaid di Tempol.
44003003	As di man si Pita and Jon wen dem won enta di Tempol, e kon dey beg dem for moni,
44003004	bot dem luk am strate for eye kon sey, "Mak yu luk us!"

44003006	Pita kon tel am, "I nor get silva or gold to giv yu: bot na wetin I get, I go giv yu. Wit Jisos Kraist name wey kom from Nazaret, stand-up mak yu bigin waka!"

44003013	"Na Abraham, Izik, Jakop and awa gran-gran papa dem God, naim kari en savant Jisos Kraist go up, di won wey una rejet kon gi-am to Pilate mak e joj am, ivun wen e won fri am.

44004001	As Pita and Jon stil dey tok, di prists, di Tempol gaid oga and di Sadusi pipol waka kon mit dem.

44005001	Won man wey dem dey kol Ananias wit en wife Safaira kon sel dia land.
44005002	Dem kon gri sey dem go kip som of di moni for demsef. So Ananias tak di rimainin moni go giv di apostols.
44005003	Bot Pita tel am, "Ananias, why yu alow Satan enta yor heart and yu kon dey lai giv di Holi Spirit? Why yu kip som of di moni wey una sel di land, for unasef?
44005004	"Bifor una sel di land, nor bi una own propati? Naw wen una sel am finish di moni nor stil bi una own to spend as una laik? Wetin mak una get dis kaind maind? Dis lai wey yu tok so, nor bi pesin yu du-am to, bot na God!"
44005005	Wen Ananias hear di wod wey Pita tok, e fal for groun at wons kon die. Dis tin mak fear kash evribodi wey hear wetin hapun.
44005006	So di young men wey dey der tak rapa kova en bodi kon kari am go bere.
44005007	Wen tiri hours don pas, en wife, Safaira waka kom, bot e nor no wetin don hapun to en husban.
44005008	Den Pita ask am, "Madam, tel mi di trut. Na dis bi di price wey una sel di land? Safaira ansa, 'Yes, na-im.'"
44005009	So Pita tel am, "Wetin mak yu and yor husban decide to trai God Spirit laik dis? Luk! Na di pipol wey go bere yor husban dey kom so and dem go kari yu go bere tu!"
44005010	At wons, di wuman fal for groun kon die for Pita front. So wen di young men enta insaid di haus kon si sey di wuman don die, dem kari am go bere near wer dem bere en husban put.
44005011	Fear kash pipol for di shosh and odas wey hear wetin hapun.
44005012	Na dis kaind mirakol and wonda God du tru di apostols for di pipol front and dem kon dey mit for Solomon Porsh.
44005013	Fear nor let enibodi wey nor dey among dem go join dem enihaw and e kon mak all di pipol dey respet dem wel-wel.
44005014	Bot plenti men and wimen wey biliv Jisos Kraist kon join dem,
44005015	sotey dem ivun dey kari sik pipol put for bed and mat for road, so dat as Pita dey pas, en shadow go heal dem.
44005016	Dem bring sik pipol and doz wey get evil spirit from all di tawns and vilage wey near Jerusalem and God heal all of dem.
44005017	Bot jelosi kon ful di High Prist and di Sadusi pipol maind,
44005018	so dem kon arres di apostols put for prizin.
44005019	Bot for dat nite, God angel opun di prizin door kon bring dem kom out and tel dem,
44005020	"Mak una go stand for di Tempol varanda bigin prish God wod wey dey giv pipol life."
44005021	Afta dem hear dis, dem enta di Tempol varanda for mornin kon start to dey tish di pipol. Den di prist oga dem and di pipol wey dey folo am kon kol di Sanhedrin, wey bi di big kansol for Izrel pipol. Dem kon send pipol go di prizin mak dem go bring di apostols kom, bikos dem won joj dia kase.
44005022	Bot di savant wey dem send go, nor si dem for di prizin, so dem go bak go ripot sey,
44005023	"Wi si sey dem lock di prizin wel and all di sojas stand for di front, bot wen wi opun di gate, wi luk insaid, bot wi nor si enibodi."
44005024	So wen di soja oga wey dey di Tempol and di prist oga dem hear dis tin, dem kon sopraiz wel-wel kon dey wonda wetin hapun to di apostols.
44005025	Na dat taim won pesin kon tel dem sey, "Si o-o, di men wey una put for prizin dey for di Tempol varanda dey tish pipol!"
44005026	So di soja oga wey dey di Tempol kon eskot di savant go bring di apostols, bot dem nor yuz fos, bikos dem dey fear sey di pipol wey gada der, fit stone dem.
44005027	Wen dem don bring dem insaid, dem kon sey mak dem stand for di kansol front and di prist oga dem kon dey kweshon dem.
44005028	E ask dem, "Wi komand una sey mak una nor tish pipol abaut dis name, bot si naw, di hol Jerusalem don ful wit di tins wey una dey tish. Una won put dis man blood for awa head?"
44005029	Bot Pita and di apostols ansa, "Wi go must obey God insted of humanbin"
44005030	"Di God wey awa gran-gran papa dem serv naim raiz-up Jisos Kraist wey una hang for tri.
44005031	"Bot God don promote am sey mak e sidan for en rite hand kon gi-am big posishon as Oga and di Pesin wey go save di wold, so dat Izrel shildren go turn from dia sin kom mit God mak e forgiv dem.
44005032	"All of us no sey dis tin na tru and di Holi Spirit wey God don giv to pipol wey dey obey am, dey stil bear witnes sey, dis tin na tru."
44005033	Wen di prist oga dem hear dis tin, dem kon ves wel-wel and won kil di apostols.
44005034	Den won Farisi wey dem dey kol, Gamaliel, wey dey tish di law and wey di pipol dey respet wel-wel kon stand-up tok, "Mak una send dis men go outsaid first."
44005035	Den e kon tok to di kansol, "Una Izrel oga, mak una tink wel bifor una du enitin to dis men.
44005036	"Bikos na so Teudas stil kom up bifor, dey tok sey en na pesin wey dey impotant and na abaut for ondred pipol folo am. Wen dem kil-am, all di pipol wey dey folo am skata and evritin kon end.
44005037	"Afta am, Judas wey kom from Galili kom out wen dem dey du census. E push pipol to join am opoz wetin dem dey du. Dem stil kil-am and all di pipol wey dey folo am skata tu.
44005038	"Naim mak I sey for dis mata so, mak una rimov una hand and liv all dis men alone, bikos if all di tins wey dem dey plan and du, na from dia maind, dem nor go succeed,
44005039	bot if na from God, una nor go fit stop dem, esept una won fite God."
44005040	So dem bring di apostols kom bak kon tel dia savant mak dem flog dem. Afta dem riliz dem, dem kon warn dem sey mak dem nor yuz Jisos Kraist name tak prish again.
44005041	So di apostols komot from der dey hapi wel-wel sey God don giv dem di shanse to sofa, bikos of Jisos Kraist.
44005042	So evriday for di Tempol kompond and from haus to haus, dem kontinu to dey tish and prish di Gud News sey, "Jisos Kraist naim bi di Mezaya."
44006001	As taim dey go, wen di disaipols don plenti, di Ju pipol wey dey tok wit Greek language kon dey kworel wit di oda kontri men wey dey tok Hebrew. Dem kon dey komplain sey, "Wen dem dey share fud, di Hebrew men dey sofa wimen wey dia husban don die."
44006002	So di twef apostols gada evribodi kon sey, "E nor gud mak wi liv God wod wey wi dey prish kon put hand for fud mata.
44006003	"So mak una luk roun kon shuz among una, sevun men wey una no sey dey bihav wel, di Holi Spirit dey yuz wel-wel and wey get sense, so dat dem go du dis wok for us.
44006004	"So dat wi go fit put awa maind for praya, as wi dey prish God wod."
44006005	Evribodi laik wetin di apostols tok, so dem kon shuz won man wey en name na Steven, bikos di Holi Spirit dey yuz am wel-wel. Di odas wey dem shuz, na Filip, Prokorus, Nikanor, Timon, Parmenas and Nikolas wey kom from Antiok and e dey serv God laik Ju pipol.
44006006	Dem kon show dem to di apostols. Di apostols put hand for dia head kon pray for dem.
44006007	Na so God wod start to spread and di disaipols wey dey Jerusalem kon plenti wel-wel. And meni prists kon biliv Jisos Kraist.
44006008	God bless Steven wel-wel kon gi-am pawa to tak du meni wondas and mirakols among di pipol.
44006009	Bot som men kon dey argue wit am. Dis men dey woship God for won place wey dem dey kol "Di Freedmen Sinagog." Som of dem kom from Alexandria, Syrene, Silicia and Asia.
44006010	Bot dis pipol nor fit stand di wisdom and pawa wey Steven tak dey tok.
44006011	So, dem kon bribe som men mak dem lai sey, "Wi hear wen dis man tok tins wey dey against Mosis and God law."
44006012	Dem lai for Steven head, so di pipol, di eldas and di oga dem for di law kon hate am. So dem arres Steven kon kari am go di kansol.
44006013	Dem bring pipol kon lai sey, "E don tey wey dis man dey tok bad-bad tins abaut Mosis law and dis Tempol.
44006014	"Wi hear wen e dey tok sey Jisos Kraist wey kom from Nazaret go skata dis place and e go shange all di tradishon wey Mosis giv us."
44006015	Evribodi wey dey di kansol dey luk Steven kon si sey en face dey shine laik angel own.
44007001	Di prist oga dem kon ask Steven, "All dis tins wey dem tok abaut yu so, na tru?"
44007002	Steven ansa, "My brodas and fadas, mak una listin to wetin I won tok so. Na wen Abraham, awa gran-gran papa dem dey for Mesopotamia, bifor e go stay for Haran, naim God wey get pawa, apier to am
44007003	kon tel am sey, "Mak yu liv yor kontri and yor pipol kon go di land wey I go show yu.
44007004	"So Abraham liv Kaldian kontri kon go stay for Haran. Afta en papa die, God kon tel am mak e stay for dis land wey una dey naw.
44007005	"Dat taim, God neva giv am eni part for di land and e neva born eni pikin, bot God promis am sey E go gi-am di land and en and en shildren go stay der foreva.
44007006	"God tel am, 'Di shildren wey yu go born go bi strenja for anoda kontri and di pipol for dat kontri go sofa dem kon yuz dem as slave for for ondred years.'
44007007	"Bot God sey, 'I go ponish di pipol wey go yuz dem as slave and afta all dis tins, dem go komot for der kon woship mi for dis place.'
44007008	"So God mak kovenant wit Abraham tru sekonsishon. Abraham kon born Izik and sekonsaiz am afta ate days. Izik born Jakop and Jakop born di twef brodas, wey bi awa gran-gran papa dem.
44007009	"Jakop shildren wey bi awa gran-gran papa dem, bikos dem dey jelos Josef dia broda, dem kon sel am as slave go Egypt, bot God dey wit am
44007010	kon save am from all en wahala and from Fero wey bi Egypt king, E gi-am favor wit wisdom and Fero kon mak am oga for di hol Egypt and ova evritin wey e get.
44007011	"Hunga kon dey for di hol Egypt and Kanan and awa gran-gran papa dem nor si fud chop.
44007012	"So wen Jakop hear sey fud dey for Egypt, e kon send awa gran-gran papa dem go shek if na tru.
44007013	"Afta dem don go tu taims, Josef show ensef giv en brodas and Fero kon no Josef famili.
44007014	"Josef send mesage go giv en papa Jakop sey mak en and all di pipol wey dey wit am kom Egypt and dem bi sevunti-faiv wey go.
44007015	"So Jakop and awa gran-gran papa dem go Eygpt and dem die for der.
44007016	"Dia bone dey der til dem kari dem go bere for Shekem for di grave wey Abraham buy from Hamor shildren.
44007017	"Bot as taim dey near wen God go fulfil di promis wey e mak wit Abraham; Izrel pipol kon dey meni insaid Egypt,
44007018	til anoda Fero wey nor no Josef kon dey rule.
44007019	"E disiv and sofa awa pipol sotey e fos dem to liv dia shildren mak dem die.
44007020	"Na dat taim dem born Mosis and God kon laik am wel-wel. Mosis stay for en papa haus for onli tiri monts
44007021	and wen dem trowey am for riva, Fero dota kon tak and train am as en own pikin.
44007022	"So dem tish Mosis all di wise tins wey Egypt pipol dey du and e kon get wisdom for haw e dey tok and wetin e dey du.
44007023	"Bot wen forti years don rish, e kon tink am sey e gud mak e go visit en own Izrel pipol.
44007024	"Wen e si won man from Egypt dey opres won Izrel pesin, Mosis kon difend and kil di Egypt man.
44007025	"E tink sey en own pipol go undastand sey God won yuz am tak save dem, bot dem nor undastand.
44007026	"Di next day, Mosis si tu Izrel men dey fite and e won trai setol dem. So e tel dem, 'My pipol, una bi brodas, why una kon dey fite unasef laik dis?'
44007027	"Bot di man wey dey opres en broda kon sey, 'Hu giv yu pawa to rule and joj us?
44007028	'Hope yu nor won kil mi di way yu kil dat Egypt man yestiday?'
44007029	"Wen di man tok laik dis, Mosis run go Midian, anoda land wer e stay as strenja kon born tu boys for der.
44007030	"Afta forti years don pas, won angel apier to am for insaid desert for Mount Sinai, wer won bush for dey burn.
44007031	"As Mosis si dis tins, e sopraiz wel-wel and wen e waka near mak e si-am wel, e hear God vois wey sey,
44007032	'Na mi bi di God wey yor gran-gran papa Abraham, Izik and Jakop dey woship.' Mosis start to shake and fear nor let am luk tu mush.
44007033	"Bot God tel am, 'Mak yu pul yor shu komot from yor leg, bikos di place wey yu stand so, na Holi Groun.
44007034	'I don si as my pipol dey sofa for Egypt and I don hear as dem dey krai, so I don kon save dem. Mak yu kom, bikos I won send yu go Egypt bak. '
44007035	"Dis Mosis wey dem rejet and ask sey, 'Hu mak yu awa oga and joj', naim God kon send mak e bi oga and savior tru di angel wey apier to am for bush.
44007036	"Na dis Mosis lid dem komot from Egypt. E stil du plenti mirakols for Egypt, di Red Sea and insaid di widanes for forti years.
44007037	"Na dis Mosis tel Izrel pipol sey, 'Na from among una God promis sey, E go raiz-up won profet wey go lid una. '
44007038	"Na dis same man dey wit di pipol for widanes, wit di angel wey tok to am for Mount Sinai, wit awa gran-gran papa dem and e kon risiv God wod for una.
44007039	"Bot una papa nor gri obey am. Insted, dem nor ansa am, bot dem shange dia maind sey dem won go Egypt bak.
44007040	"Dem kon tel Aaron, 'Mak yu du juju for us wey go lid us bikos, wi nor no wetin don hapun to Mosis!'
44007041	"So dem mak image wey bi laik melu, sakrifias gi-am kon bigin serv di melu wey dem tak dia own hand mak.
44007042	"God liv dem mak dem woship stars to mak wetin Profet Amos tok, hapun sey, 'Izrel pipol, una tink sey na mi una dey serv wen una dey sakrifais anima for insaid widanes for forti years? '
44007043	'Na bikos of di haus wey una build for "Molech and Refan", wey bi una god and juju wey una dey woship, naim mak mi send una go bi slave for Babylon. '
44007044	"God giv di tabanako to awa gran-gran papa dem, di haus wer dem go for woship am, jos as E sey mak Mosis build am.
44007045	"Afta, awa gran-gran papa dem kari di tabanako wey God giv dem wit Joshua kon driv all di oda tribes and tak dia land til di taim wey David bigin rule Izrel.
44007046	"God favor David wel-wel and e sey e go build haus for God
44007047	bot na Solomon en pikin kon build am.
44007048	"Wi no sey God nor dey stay for haus wey humanbin build, jos as di profet tok,
44007049	'Hevun na my chair and na di eart I dey put my leg, so wish kaind haus una go fit build for mi or wish kaind place I go stay?
44007050	'Nor bi mi mak all dis tins by mysef?'
44007051	"Si haw una stuborn! Jos as una gran-gran papa dem bi, na so una stil bi tu, bikos una don mak una heart strong to disobey God!
44007052	"E get eni profet wey una gran-gran papa dem nor kil? Dem ivun kil di mesenja wey tok bifor sey, 'Di Raitious Man go kom and una go gi-am to wiked pipol and dem go kil-am.
44007053	"Na una risiv God law wey E send tru en angels, bot una nor obey am."
44007054	As di kansol membas hear all di tins wey Steven tok, dem kon dey ves wel-wel.
44007055	Bot Steven, wey God dey yuz wel-wel, luk strate go hevun kon si God glori and Jisos Kraist wey stand for God rite hand.
44007056	Naim e shaut, "Luk! I si hevun wey opun and I si Jisos Kraist, God Pikin, stand for en rite hand."
44007057	Bot di pipol klose dia ear bigin shaut and all of dem kon rush am.
44007058	Wen dem don drag am go outsaid for di Tempol, dem kon start to dey stone am, den dem kon pul all dia klot giv won man wey dem dey kol Sol, mak e hol.
44007059	As dem dey stone Steven, e kon pray, "Oga, Jisos Kraist, mak yu risiv my spirit."
44007060	So e fal for groun kon shaut, "My Papa, abeg, mak Yu nor kount dis sin against dem." Wen e tok so finish, e kon die.
44008001	Sol hapi wen dem dey kil Steven. Na from dat day trobol start for di shosh wey dey Jerusalem and all di bilivas kon skata go Judea and Samaria, bot na onli di apostols nor run.
44008002	Som men wey dey holi, kari Steven go bere, afta dem don mourn am.
44008003	Bot Sol trai to distroi di shosh; e dey go from haus to haus dey arres men and wimen put for prizin.
44008004	So di pipol wey skata kon dey go from place to place dey prish di gospol.
44008005	Filip travol go Samaria main tawn kon dey prish abaut di Mezaya giv dem.
44008006	Di pipol wey gada, put dia maind for wetin Filip dey tok, bikos dem don hear and si all di mirakols wey e du.
44008007	Wiked spirit dey shaut and dey komot from pipol bodi as dem hear God wod and God heal meni pipol wey nor fit waka.
44008008	So all di pipol wey dey di tawn kon dey hapi wel-wel, bikos of wetin dey hapun.
44008009	E get won strong man for di tawn wey dem dey kol Saimon and e dey du magic wey dey mak Samaria pipol sopraiz.
44008010	Evribodi, both smol pikin and big pipol, dey biliv wetin e dey du and dem biliv sey, "Na God gi-am pawa!"
44008011	Dem dey listin to am bikos, e don tey wen e dey yuz magic tak dey du wondas.
44008012	Bot wen dem biliv di Gud News wey Filip prish abaut God Kindom and abaut Jisos Kraist, dem kon baptaiz di pipol wey biliv.
44008013	Ivun Saimon sef biliv and afta dem don baptaiz am, e kon dey waka wit Filip, bikos all di mirakols wey God dey du tru Filip, dey sopraiz am.
44008014	Wen di apostols wey dey Jerusalem hear sey Samaria pipol don risiv God wod, dem kon send Pita and Jon go mit dem,
44008015	so dat dem go pray for di pipol, mak dem for risiv di Holi Spirit.
44008016	Bikos for dat taim, dem neva risiv di Holi Spirit. Na onli Jisos name dem tak baptaiz dem.
44008017	Pita and Jon put hand for di pipol head and dem kon risiv di Holi Spirit.
44008018	Wen Saimon si sey pipol dey risiv di Holi Spirit as di apostols put hand for dia head, e kon giv di apostols moni
44008019	kon sey, "Abeg, mak una giv mi dis pawa mak I for fit put my hand for pipol head mak dem for risiv di Holi Spirit tu."
44008020	Bot Pita ansa am, "Mak yu and yor moni go die! Yu tink sey yu fit buy God gift wit moni?
44008021	"Yu nor get share for insaid dis tin wey God dey giv, bikos God don si sey na bad tin yu won tak am du.
44008022	"So mak yu turn from sin kom mit God and from di bad tins wey dey yor maind and pray mak God forgiv yu.
44008023	"Bikos I si sey na long-trot and bad bele dey wori yu and sin stil ful yor maind."
44008024	Saimon kon ansa, "Mak yu pray to God for mi, so dat di tin wey yu tok so, nor go hapun to mi."
44008025	Afta Pita and Jon don tel dia stori and prish God wod finish, dem kon go bak to Jerusalem, dey prish God wod for insaid Samaria, as dem dey go.
44008026	God angel kon tel Filip, "Get up mak yu waka for di desert road wey dem dey pas from Jerusalem go Gaza."
44008027	So Filip kon dey waka dey go wer di angel tel am. As e dey go, e mit won unok wey kom from Ethiopia, e bi ofisa for Kandace, Ethiopia queen and na-im dey kip dia moni. E kon woship God for Jerusalem
44008028	and e dey go haus bak. E sidan for en horse dey read di book wey Profet Isaia rite.
44008029	Naim di Holi Spirit tel Filip, "Mak yu waka go mit di man."
44008030	So Filip run go mit am kon hear am dey read wetin Profet Isaia rite. So e kon ask di man, "Yu undastand wetin yu dey read so."
44008031	Di man ansa, "Haw I won tak undastand, unles pesin tish mi!" E kon tel Filip sey mak e kom sidan wit am.
44008032	Na di place wey e dey read for God wod bi dis, "Dem lid am laik ship go kil and as ship pikin dey kwayet wen dem dey shave-am, na so tu e nor opun en mout.
44008033	"Dem disgrace am kon tak pawa from en hand. Nobodi go fit tok abaut en shildren or en gran shildren, bikos dem kil-am wen e stil dey young."
44008034	So di man ask Filip, "Abeg tel mi, na hu dis profet dey tok abaut? Na ensef, abi na anoda pesin?"
44008035	Filip kon start to prish di Gud News abaut Jisos Kraist giv di man from di place wey e dey read.
44008036	As dem dey go, dem kon rish wer wota dey, naim di man sey, "Si, wota dey here! Wetin go mak mi nor baptaiz naw?"
44008037	Filip ansa, "If yu biliv, I go baptaiz yu." Di man kon sey, "I biliv sey Jisos Kraist na God Pikin."
44008038	So e tel di driva mak e stop, Filip wit am waka go wer di wota dey and e kon baptaiz am.
44008039	Wen dem kom out from di wota, God Spirit kari Filip komot from der and di man nor si-am again, bot e kon dey hapi as e dey go.
44008040	Filip si ensef for Azotus and as e dey waka pas for di aria, e kon dey prish di Gud News for all di tawns til e rish Sizeria.
44009001	As all dis tins dey hapun, Sol stil dey tel di disaipols sey e go kil dem. E go mit di High Prist
44009002	kon tak pamishon to tak go Damaskus, so dat if e si enibodi wey dey folo Jisos Kraist wey bi di Way, weda na man or wuman, e go arres dem kom Jerusalem.
44009003	As e dey go, won lite from hevun kon shine roun wer e dey.
44009004	E fal for groun kon hear won vois wey kol en name, "Sol, Sol, wetin mak yu dey ponish mi?"
44009005	So e ansa, "Oga, na hu dey tok so?" Di vois ansa am, "I bi Jisos Kraist wey yu dey ponish!
44009006	"Naw, mak yu get up go insaid di tawn and dem go tel yu wetin yu go du."
44009007	Di men wey dey folo am travol, sopraiz dey luk, bikos dem hear vois dey tok, bot dem nor si enibodi.
44009008	So Sol get up from groun, en eye opun, bot e nor dey si. En frends hol en hand kon eskot am enta Damaskus.
44009009	E nor si at-all for tiri days and for dat taim, e nor chop or drink enitin.
44009010	Dat taim, e get won disaipol for Damaskus and en name na Ananias. God kol am for insaid vishon, "Ananias", e kon ansa, "Na mi bi dis, Oga."
44009011	God kon tel am, "Get-up mak yu go di strit wey dem dey kol 'Strate' and wen yu rish Judas haus wey dey der, mak yu luk for won man, en name na Sol and e kom from Tarsus. You go mit am dey pray for der.
44009012	"I don show am for vishon sey won man wey dem dey kol Ananias go kom mit am and e go put hand for en head, pray for am, mak e for fit si again."
44009013	Bot Ananias ansa, "Oga, meni pipol don tel mi abaut dis man and all di wiked tins wey e don du to yor pipol for Jerusalem.
44009014	"E ivun kolet leta from di prist oga dem, wey e go tak kash and trow pipol wey biliv yu, for prizin."

44009016	"Tru-tru I go show am haw e go sofa, bikos of my name."

44009018	At wons, somtin wey bi laik fish scale fal komot from Sol eye and e kon dey si. E get up and dem kon baptaiz am.
44009019	Afta e chop finish, en bodi kon strong again.
44009020	At wons, e kon start to dey prish for di sinagog sey Jisos Kraist na God Pikin.
44009021	Evribodi wey hear am kon dey sopraiz dey ask demsef sey, "Dis nor bi di man wey dey kil pipol wey biliv Jisos Kraist? Wi tink sey e kom here kon arres pipol kari go giv di prist oga dem."
44009022	Bot Sol stil dey prish wit pawa. E dey show sey na Jisos Kraist bi di Mezaya and di Ju pipol wey dey for Damaskus, nor fit ansa am.
44009023	Afta som days, di Ju pipol kon dey plan to kil-am,
44009024	bot Sol hear wetin dem dey plan. Som pipol dey wosh for di tawn gate day and nite mak dem for fit kil-am wen dem si-am.
44009025	Bot won nite, di pipol wey dey folo Sol kon put am for basket, drop am dan smol-smol from won smol window wey dey near di tawn fence.
44009026	Wen e rish Jerusalem, e kon trai to join di disaipols, bot dem dey fear am, bikos dem nor biliv sey e don bi Jisos Kraist disaipol.
44009027	So Banabas tak Sol go mit di apostols, den e tel dem haw Sol tak si Jisos Kraist for vishon wen e dey go Damaskus and haw e bigin dey prish wit boldnes abaut Jisos Kraist.
44009028	Sol stay and waka wit dem for Jerusalem and e dey tok wit boldnes abaut Jisos Kraist.
44009029	E bigin dey tok and argue wit di Ju pipol wey dey speak Greek, bot som pipol kon dey trai to kil-am.
44009030	Wen di brodas no abaut wetin dem dey plan, dem kon tak am go Sizeria and from der, dem send am go Tarsus.
44009031	Dat taim, di shosh wey dey Judea, Galili and Samaria get res and dis kon mak dem strong as dem dey stay togeda, dey woship God wit all dia heart and as di Holi Spirit dey tok to dem. So pipol wey dey di shosh kon dey plenti more-more.
44009032	Pita dey travol from won place go anoda and e stil go wer di bilivas dey for Lydda.
44009033	E kon mit won man for der, en name na Aeneas wey nor fit waka since wen e bi ate years.
44009034	Pita kon tel am, "Aeneas, Jisos Kraist, wey bi di Mezaya, won heal yu naw. So mak yu stand-up, kari yor bed!" At wons, e get up kon kari en bed.
44009035	All di pipol wey dey Lydda and Sharon si wetin hapun and dem kon bigin folo Jisos Kraist.
44009036	Won wuman dey for Jopa wey bi Jisos Kraist disaipol and en name na Tabita (wey min Dorkas for Greek language). E dey du gud tins and dey help poor pipol.
44009037	E sik and e kon die. Wen di pipol don wosh en dead bodi, dem kon kari am put for won room for upstair.
44009038	Bikos Lydda dey near Jopa, so wen di disaipols hear sey Pita dey der, dem kon send tu men go kol am sey, "Mak yu kom mit us at wons."
44009039	So Pita get up folo dem and wen e rish der, dem kon tak am go di room for up. All di wimen wey dia husban don die stand near Pita dey krai and dey show am all di dress wey Dorkas mak for dem, wen e dey wit dem.
44009040	Bot Pita driv all of dem go outsaid, den e nil dan kon pray. E turn face di dead bodi kon sey, "Tabita, get up!" Naim di wuman opun en eye and wen e si Pita, e kon sidan.
44009041	Pita kon hol en hand stand-up. Den e kol di bilivas and all di wimen wey dia husban don die and e kon giv di wuman to dem.
44009042	Wen evribodi for Jopa hear dis tin wey hapun, meni of dem kon biliv Jisos Kraist.
44009043	Pita kon stay for Jopa for meni days wit won man wey dem dey kol Saimon, wey dey du leatha wok.
44010001	Won man wey en name bi Konilios dey stay for Sizeria and e bi ofisa for Itali armi.
44010002	E dey holi and en and en famili dey woship God. E dey help di pipol wel-wel and dey pray to God evritaim.
44010003	Won day, aroun tiri o' klok for aftanun, e kon si vishon and God angel kol am, "Konilios."
44010004	Fear kash am as e dey luk di angel, so e ansa, "Oga, Wetin yu wont?" Di angel tel am, "God don hear yor praya and si all di gud tins wey yu dey du for poor pipol.
44010005	"So, send som men go Jopa mak dem go kol won man wey en name bi Saimon Pita.
44010006	"Di man dey stay wit Saimon wey dey du leatha wok and di haus dey near di sea."
44010007	Wen di angel don go, Konilios kon kol tu of en haus boys wit won soja wey dey serv am
44010008	and wen e don tel dem evritin wey hapun, e kon send dem go Jopa.
44010009	For aftanun for di next day, as di men dey near di tawn, Pita kon go di haus top go pray,
44010010	afta som taim, e kon dey hungri, bot di fud neva redi. As e dey wait, e kon si vishon.
44010011	E si sey hevun opun and somtin wey bi laik tray, wey dem hol for en for kona kon dey kom dan smol-smol.
44010012	Difren-difren animas wey get for legs and di wons wey dey krip for groun and difren birds dey insaid di tray.
44010013	Den won vois tel am, "Pita, get up, kil mak yu chop."
44010014	Bot Pita ansa, "Oga, I nor go fit, bikos yu no sey since dem born mi, I neva chop enitin wey get blood or wey nor klin."
44010015	Bot di vois tel am, "Wetin God don mak klin, mak yu nor forbid am."
44010016	Dis tin hapun tiri taims and di tray kon go bak to hevun.
44010017	As Pita stil dey wonda wetin di vishon min, di men wey Konilios send kon rish Saimon haus.
44010018	Dem ask if enibodi wey bi Saimon Pita dey di haus.
44010019	As Pita stil dey tink abaut di vishon, di Holi Spirit kon tel am, "Luk!, tiri men dey faind yu.
44010020	"Mak yu get up go mit dem and mak yu folo dem, bikos na Mi send dem kom."
44010021	So Pita go dan go mit di men kon sey, "Na mi bi di pesin wey una dey luk for. Wetin bring una kom?"
44010022	Dem ansa, "Konilios, di armi ofisa, wey dey du gud tins and dey woship God wel-wel, wey all di Ju pipol dey respet, na-im send us kom. Won angel komand am sey mak e invait yu kom prish giv am."
44010023	So Pita sey mak dem enta haus and e welkom dem wel-wel. Di next day, e kon folo dem go and som brodas for Jopa, folo am go tu.
44010024	Afta dem don travol for won ful day, dem kon rish Sizeria. Konilios don gada all en famili and frends dey wait for dem.
44010025	So as Pita enta di kompound, Konilios nil dan for en front kon dey woship am.
44010026	Bot Pita hol am kon sey, "Stand up, bikos I bi ordinari humanbin laik yu."
44010027	As Pita stil dey folo am dey tok wen e enta di haus, e kon si sey meni pipol gada dey wait am.
44010028	E kon tel dem, "Una no sey di law nor alow us, wey bi Ju pipol, to visit Gentai pipol or folo dem du enitin, bot God don show mi sey mak I nor sey enibodi nor dey klin.
44010029	"Na dis mak wen una send pipol kom kol mi, I nor sey 'No'. So mak una tel mi, 'Why una kol mi?'"
44010030	Konilios ansa, "For days ago, for dis kaind taim for aftanun, as I dey pray for my haus, won man wey en dress dey shine kon stand for my front.
44010031	"E kon sey, 'Konilios, God don hear yor praya and E don rimemba all di gud tins wey yu dey du.
44010032	'So mak yu send pipol go Jopa go kol Saimon, wey dem dey kol Pita. E dey stay as visitor wit Saimon wey dey du leatha wok, wey e haus dey near di sea.'
44010033	"So, I kon send pipol go kol yu and yu du wel as yu kom. Na wi bi dis for God front, wi redi to hear wetin E sey mak yu tel us."
44010034	Den Pita tel dem, "Naw, I don undastand sey God nor dey opres enibodi,
44010035	bot for evri tribe, di pesin wey fear am and dey du wetin gud, na dat pesin, E dey laik.
44010036	"Una no di mesage wey E send to Izrel pipol, wen E tok abaut di Gud News wey dey giv peace, tru Jisos Kraist, di ril Oga.
44010037	"Una no wetin hapun from Galili go rish Judea afta Jon prish sey,
44010038	Jisos Kraist wey kom from Nazaret, na-im God giv di Holi Spirit and pawa. Haw e kon du gud for evriwer kon heal pipol wey devol dey opres, bikos God dey wit am.
44010039	"All of us si di tins wey e du for Judea and Jerusalem. Dem hang am for tri kon kil-am,
44010040	bot God raiz-am for di ted day kon alow pipol si-am.
44010041	"Nor bi evribodi si-am, bot na di wons wey God don shuz, wey folo am chop and drink afta e don wak-up from deat.
44010042	"E kon komand us mak wi prish and warn pipol sey, na en ensef bi di Pesin wey God shuz mak e joj pipol wey dey alaif and di wons wey don die.
44010043	"All di profets tok abaut am sey, 'Evribodi wey biliv am, tru en name, God go forgiv dem.'"
44010044	As Pita stil dey tok, di Holi Spirit kon enta insaid all di pipol wey dey hear di mesage.
44010045	Di bilivas wey bi Ju wey folo Pita go Jopa kon sopraiz wel-wel sey Gentai pipol tu, fit risiv di Holi Spirit,
44010046	bikos dem dey hear wey dem dey yuz difren-difren language tak dey praiz God. Den Pita sey,
44010047	"Enibodi go fit sey mak wi nor baptaiz all dis pipol wey don risiv di Holi Spirit, jos laik di res of us?"
44010048	So e sey mak dem baptaiz dem for Jisos Kraist name. Den di pipol sey mak e stay wit dem for som days.
44011001	Di apostols and di brodas wey dey Judea kon hear sey Gentai pipol tu don risiv God wod.
44011002	So wen Pita rish Jerusalem, di bilivas wey bi Ju kon bigin argue wit am sey,
44011003	"Yu go chop wit pipol wey dem nor sekonsaiz."
44011004	Bot Pita tel dem evritin wey hapun. E kon sey,
44011005	"As I dey pray for Jopa I kon si vishon. For insaid di vishon, I si somtin wey bi laik tray dey kom dan smol-smol from hevun, dem hol am for for kona and e kon stop for my front.
44011006	"As I luk insaid, I kon si animas wey get for leg, bush meat, di wons wey dey krip and difren-difren birds.
44011007	"I stil hear won vois wey tel mi sey, 'Get up Pita, kil som, mak yu chop.'
44011008	"Bot I ansa, 'Oga, I nor fit, bikos since dem born mi, I neva chop enitin wey nor dey klin.'
44011009	"Bot di vois from hevun kon tel mi again, 'Wetin God don mak klin, mak yu nor forbid am!'
44011010	"Dis tin hapun tiri taims, den di tray kon go hevun bak.
44011011	"Na dat same taim tiri men wey dem send kom mit mi from Sizeria kon rish di haus wer wi dey stay.
44011012	"Di Holi Spirit kon tel mi sey mak I folo dem go. Sis brodas for Jopa folo mi go tu and wi kon enta di man haus.
44011013	"Di man tel us haw e si angel wey stand for en haus kon tel am, 'Send pipol go Jopa go kol Saimon wey dem dey kol Pita.
44011014	'Wen e kom, e go giv yu di mesage wey God go yuz tak save yu and yor famili.'
44011015	"And wen I start to tok, di Holi Spirit kon enta dem, jos as e enta us for di first taim.
44011016	"So I kon rimemba wetin di Oga don yuz en own mout tel us bifor sey, 'Jon yuz wota baptaiz pipol, bot God go baptaiz una wit di Holi Spirit.'
44011017	"So my pipol, if God fit giv doz Gentai pipol di same gift wey E giv us afta wi biliv Jisos Kraist, hu I bi to stop God?"
44011018	Wen dem hear wetin Pita tok, dem nor argue wit am again, so dem kon start to praiz God. Den dem sey, "Naim bi sey God don giv Gentai pipol di shanse to tak turn from sin kom mit am, so dat dem go get di life wey nor dey end."
44011019	All di pipol wey skata komot from Jerusalem di taim wey dem kil Steven kon travol go far place laik Fonicia, Syprus and Antiok, dey prish giv onli Ju pipol.
44011020	Bot som of dem wey kom from Syprus and Syrene kon go Antiok dey tok to di Greek pipol abaut di Gud News wey konsan Jisos Kraist.
44011021	God pawa dey wit dem and meni pipol wey biliv kon bigin dey folo Jisos Kraist.
44011022	Wen di pipol for di shosh wey dey Jerusalem hear di news, dem kon send Banabas go Antiok.
44011023	Wen e rish der kon si haw God don bless di pipol, e hapi wel-wel kon enkorage dem sey mak dem kontinu to woship God wit all dia heart.
44011024	Banabas na beta pesin, di Holi Spirit dey insaid am and e get fate wel-wel, so meni pipol kon bigin folo Jisos Kraist.
44011025	Banabas komot from der go faind Sol for Tarsus
44011026	and wen e si-am, e kon tak am go Antiok. Banabas and Sol stay der for one year dey tish di pipol wey dey di shosh and na for der dem for first kol di disaipols, "Kristens."
44011027	For di same taim, som profets kon go Jerusalem from Antiok.
44011028	Won of dem wey en name bi Agabush, get up and di Holi Spirit kon put wod for en mout sey, "Heavi hunga go hapun for di hol wold." Dis tin hapun di taim wen Klaudios dey rule.
44011029	So di disaipols, evribodi akodin to haw e fit du rish, kon sey dem go send moni go giv di brodas wey dey Judea.
44011030	Afta dem don kontribute, dem kon send Banabas and Sol go giv di eldas di moni wey dem gada.
44012001	For dat taim, King Herod kash som pipol wey dey go shosh kon sey e go kil dem.
44012002	E kil James, wey bi Jon broda, wit sword.
44012003	Wen e si sey di Ju pipol hapi wit wetin e du, e kon arres Pita tu. (Dis tin hapun for di taim wey dem dey du di bread wey nor get yist fist.)
44012004	Wen e don kash Pita put for prizin, e put for sojas for for difren grups, mak dem gaid am. Herod plan na to bring Pita out mak e joj am for di hol tawn front wen Passova don finish.
44012005	So as Pita dey prizin, di pipol wey dey di shosh dey pray to God for am, day and nite.
44012006	Bot for di nite bifor dem go joj am, dem tie Pita wit tu chains and e slip for tu sojas senta. Oda sojas stil dey di prizin front, dey gaid am.
44012007	God angel apier and lite kon shine for di prizin. Di angel wak Pita kon tel am, "Get up kwik-kwik!" At wons, di chains fal komot from Pita hand.
44012008	Di angel sey, "Wear yor klot and yor sandal." So Pita du wetin di angel tel am. Den di angel sey, "Wear yor koat mak yu folo mi."
44012009	Pita folo am go outsaid. E biliv sey wetin dey hapun so na tru, e tink sey na dream e dey dream.
44012010	Afta, en and di angel kon pas di first and di sekon sojas grup, den dem kon rish di iron gate wey go di tawn. Di gate opun by ensef and dem go outsaid kon waka pas won smol strit, den di angel kon liv am for der.
44012011	Wen Pita si sey all dis tins wey dey hapun, nor bi dream, e kon sey, "Naw I no sey, 'Tru-tru, God send en angel kon save mi from Herod hand and from all di tins wey di Ju pipol tink sey go hapun."
44012012	Wen Pita eye don klear, e kon waka face Mary haus wey bi Jon Mark mama, wer meni pipol gada dey pray for am.
44012013	Wen e nok di door, Rhoda, won savant girl, kon ansa.
44012014	Wen di girl hear Pita vois, e kon dey hapi sotey e nor rimemba to opun di door, bot e run go tel dem sey Pita dey for outsaid.
44012015	Dem ansa di girl, "Yu nor no wetin yu dey tok!" Bot di girl stil dey sey na Pita, so dem kon sey, "E go bi en spirit!"
44012016	Bot Pita stil dey nok and wen dem opun di door si-am, dem kon sopraiz.
44012017	E yuz en hand tak tel dem mak dem kwayet and e kon tel dem haw God tak fri am from prizin. E tel dem, "Mak una tel James and all di brodas dis stori," den e liv dem kon go anoda place.
44012018	Wen day break, di sojas wey dey gaid Pita sopraiz wel-wel and fear kash dem wen dem nor si-am again.
44012019	Wen Herod send pipol go faind am and dem nor si-am, e kweshon di sojas wey dey gaid Pita kon komand sey mak dem kil all of dem. Den Herod komot from Judea go Sizeria go stay.
44012020	Herod kon dey ves wel-wel for Tyre and Sidon pipol. So dem gada go si-am. Bot dem kon first beg Blastus wey bi di king ofisa, mak e help dem beg am, bikos na di king kontri dey suppli fud giv dia kontri.
44012021	Wen di day wey dem gri to mit am don rish, Herod kon wear en king dress and e kon sidan for en throne dey folo dem tok.
44012022	Bot as e dey tok, di pipol wey gada kon dey shaut, "Na god dey tok so-o, nor bi man!"
44012023	At wons God angel kon nak Herod fal for groun, bikos e nor giv God glori and plenti worm kon chop en bodi til e die.
44012024	Bot God wod kontinu to dey spread.
44012025	Banabas and Sol kon go bak to Jerusalem wen dem don finish dia wok and dem tak Jon Mark folo bodi.
44013001	Dis na di profets and tishas wey dey di shosh for Antiok: Banabas, Saimon wey dem dey kol Niger, Lucius wey kom from Syrene, Manaen (wey bi Herod di Tetrak frend from smol pikin) and Sol.
44013002	As dem dey fast and woship God, di Holi Spirit kon tel dem, "Mak una seprate Banabas and Sol for di wok wey I want mak dem du."
44013003	Afta dem don fast and pray finish, dem pray for Banabas and Sol kon send dem go.
44013004	So Banabas and Sol wey di Holi Spirit send kon go Seleucia and from der, dem enta ship go Syprus.
44013005	Wen dem rish Salamis, dem kon dey prish God wod for di Ju sinagog, (Jon dey der dey help dem.)
44013006	Wen dem don kros di hol Island go rish Pafos, dem kon si won magician wey bi Ju and na wayo profet. En name na Bar-Jisos,
