44013007	e dey wit Sergius Paulus, wey bi Roman ofisa and e no book wel-wel. Di ofisa invait Banabas and Sol kom en haus, bikos e won hear God wod.
44013008	Bot "Elymas" wey bi magician, (bikos na wetin en name min bi dat) kon dey opoz dem, so dat di Roman ofisa nor go biliv wetin dem dey prish.
44013009	Bot Sol (wey dem dey kol Pol) wey get di Holi Spirit, luk Elymas for face
44013010	kon tel am, "Yu devol pikin wey nor laik gud tin, na so-so wayo and bad tins yu sabi du, yu nor go stop to dey opoz God?
44013011	"Naw, God don raiz en hand against yu. Yor eye go blind and yu nor go fit si for somtaim!" At wons, e eye jos blind and daknes kova en face and e kon dey tak hand faind pipol mak dem show am road.
44013012	So wen di Roman ofisa si wetin hapun, e kon biliv, bikos e sopraiz wel-wel for wetin dem tish abaut Jisos Kraist.
44013013	Pol and di pipol wey folo am kon travol from Pafos go rish Perga wey dey for Pamfilia, bot Jon Mark liv dem kon go bak to Jerusalem.
44013014	Wen dem komot for Perga, dem rish Antiok for Pisidia for Sabat Day kon enta di sinagog go sidan.
44013015	Afta dem don read from di law and di profets book, di oga for di sinagog kon send mesage go mit dem sey, "Awa brodas, if una get eni mesage to tak enkorage di pipol, mak una kon tok naw."
44013016	So, Pol stand-up raiz en hand kon sey, "Izrel and Gentai pipol wey dey fear God, mak una hear wetin I won tok:
44013017	"Na from Izrel pipol God shuz awa gran-gran papa dem and E kon mak dem great for di taim wey dem stay for Egypt as strenja and E kari dem komot from Egypt wit en own hand.
44013018	"For forti years, E stay wit dem for insaid widanes.
44013019	"Afta E don destroi sevun tribes for Kanan, E kon dash en pipol di land.
44013020	"All dis tins hapun for for ondred and fifti years. Afta dis, E kon giv dem profet wey go joj dem, ontil Profet Samuel taim rish.
44013021	"Di pipol kon ask for king and God giv dem Sol, wey bi Kish pikin, wey kom from Benjamin tribe and e rule dem for forti years.
44013022	"Afta God rimov am, E kon mak David dia king. Na dis man God tok abaut sey, 'I don si David, Jesse pikin, di man wey I laik wel-wel and e go du evritin wey I wont.'
44013023	"Na from dis man famili God giv Izrel, Jisos Kraist, di savior wey E promis dem bifor.
44013024	"Bifor Jisos kom, Jon don prish to all Izrel pipol sey mak dem turn from sin kom mit God and mak e baptaiz dem.
44013025	"Bot as Jon dey finish en wok, e kon tok meni taims sey, 'Wetin una tink sey I bi? Nor bi mi bi di Mezaya. Mak una si, sombodi dey kom afta mi. I nor rish to rimov shu from en leg!'
44013026	"So my brodas, wey bi Abraham shildren and una wey bi Gentai pipol wey dey fear God, na di mesage abaut haw God go tak save pipol, naim wi kom tel una so.
44013027	"Bikos di pipol wey dey stay for Jerusalem and all di rulas nor no am, so dem kon yuz wetin dem dey read for Sabat, wey di profets tok, tak kil-am.
44013028	"Dem nor si enitin wey go mak dem kondem am, bot dem stil tel Pilate mak e kil-am.
44013029	"Wen dem don du evritin wey Bibol tok abaut am, dem bring am dan from di kros kon put am for grave.
44013030	"Bot God raiz-am from deat
44013031	and for meni days, e apier to di pipol wey dey folo am from Galili go rish Jerusalem. Na dis pipol kon dey bear witnes sey, dis tins na tru.
44013032	"And wi dey tel una di Gud News abaut dis tins wey God promis awa gran-gran papa dem.
44013033	"E don du wetin E promis us and dia shildren, wen E raiz Jisos Kraist, as dem rite am for Psalm sey, 'Yu bi my Son and today, I don bi yor Papa.'
44013034	"Bot bikos E don raiz Jisos Kraist from deat mak e nor for rotin, God kon sey: 'I go giv yu di holi promis wey una fit trust, wey I promis David.'
44013035	"E stil tok for anoda Psalm sey, 'Yu nor go alow yor Pikin wey dey holi, mak e rotin.'
44013036	"Bikos David, afta e don du wetin God send am kon du among en pipol, e kon die and dem bere am wit en gran-gran papa dem and e rotin,
44013037	bot di pesin wey God raiz-up, nor rotin.
44013038	"So my pipol, mak una no sey, na tru dis Pesin wi dey prish sey, 'God go forgiv una.'
44013039	"Tru am, evribodi wey biliv, go dey fri from evritin wey Mosis law nor fit fri dem from.
44013040	"So mak una mak sure sey wetin di profets tok for groun, nor hapun to una:
44013041	"Una wey dey laff; mak una hear, una go sopraiz til una die! Bikos I go du somtin for una taim, somtin wey una nor go biliv ivun if dem tel una."
44013042	As Pol and Banabas dey komot, di pipol kon dey beg dem mak dem stil kon tok abaut all dis tins for di next Sabat Day.
44013043	Wen di mitin for di sinagog don finish, meni Ju and Gentai pipol wey dey fear God kon folo Pol and Banabas, dey enkorage dem sey, mak dem kontinu for di grace wey God giv dem.
44013044	Di next Sabat Day, nearli evribodi for di tawn gada mak dem for hear God wod.
44013045	Bot wen di Ju pipol si as di pipol plenti rish, jelosi kon ful dia maind, so dem start to opoz wetin Pol dey tok kon dey kos am.
44013046	Pol and Banabas kon yuz boldnes tak ansa dem, "E gud sey na una wi first prish God wod giv. Bot since una rejet am and una nor redi to get life wey nor dey end, wi go-go prish giv Gentai pipol.
44013047	"Bikos dis na wetin God don alredi komand us sey: 'I don shuz una to bi lite for Gentai pipol, mak una bring salvashon kom dis wold.'"
44013048	Wen di Gentai pipol hear wetin e tok, dem start to hapi kon dey tank God for en wod and evribodi wey God don shuz to get life wey nor dey end, kon biliv.
44013049	So God wod kon dey spread roun di hol kontri.
44013050	Bot di Ju pipol tok bad tins abaut Pol and Banabas giv all di big wimen wey dey fear God and di big-big men for di tawn, so dem sofa dem and driv dem komot from di aria.
44013051	So wen dem don shake di land san-san wey dey dia leg komot, dem kon go Ikonium.
44013052	So di disaipols begin hapi and di Holi Spirit kon ful dia life.
44014001	For Ikonium, Pol and Banabas go insaid di Ju sinagog and dem prish sotey meni Ju and Greek pipol kon biliv God wod.
44014002	Bot di Ju pipol wey nor gri biliv, gada di Gentai pipol kon spoil dia maind against Pol and Banabas.
44014003	Di apostols stay der tey wel-wel and dem tok wit boldnes abaut God, wey show sey dia mesage abaut en gudnes na tru, bikos E kon giv dem pawa to du meni mirakols and wondas.
44014004	Bot di pipol wey dey di tawn kon divide; som dey di Ju side and som dey di apostol side.
44014005	Wen di Gentai and di Ju pipol (wit di oga dem wey dey rule dem) kon trai to sofa and stone di disaipols,
44014006	Pol and Banabas kon no abaut am, so dem kon run go Lystra and Derbe wey dey for Lycaonia and all di aria wey dey near der
44014007	and dem kontinu to dey prish for der.
44014008	For Lystra, dem mit won man wey nor fit waka since wen dem born am.
44014009	Di man dey listin to Pol as e dey tok. Wen Pol kon luk am for eye kon si sey e get fate wey go fit heal am,
44014010	e tel am, "Stand up." Di man kon jump up and e bigin waka.
44014011	Wen di pipol si wetin Pol du, dem kon shaut for Lycaonian language sey, "Awa gods don turn to humanbin kom mit us."
44014012	Dem start to kol Banabas, "Zeus" and Pol, "Hermes", bikos na Pol dey lid dem.
44014013	Di prist wey dey woship di god wey dem dey kol Zeus wey en shrine dey outsaid di tawn kon bring melu and flawas kom di tawn gate; so dat en and all di pipol go sakrifais giv di apostols.
44014014	Wen Banabas and Pol hear abaut di tin wey di pipol won du, dem shaut, tear dia klot kon run go mit di pipol sey,
44014015	"Why una won du dis kaind tin? Wi tu na humanbin laik una! Wi kon tel una di Gud News, wey go mak una turn from sin kom mit God, wey mak hevun, eart, sea and all di tins wey dey insaid dem.
44014016	"Bifor-bifor, E let difren tribes dey du as dem laik,
44014017	bot E nor stop to du gud for una, E dey giv una rain from hevun and fud from groun, so dat una go chop and bele go swit una."
44014018	Upon all dis tins wey Pol and Banabas tok, dem nor fit stop di pipol mak dem nor du di sakrifias.
44014019	Bot afta som Ju pipol wey kom from Antiok and Ikonium don win di pipol maind, dem kon stone Pol, drag am komot from di tawn, bikos dem tink sey e don die.
44014020	And as di disaipols gada roun am, e get up kon waka go bak to di tawn. Di next day, en and Banabas kon komot go Derbe.
44014021	Afta dem don prish God wod for dat tawn and meni pipol don turn from sin kom mit God, dem kon go bak to Lystra, Ikonium and Antiok.
44014022	Dem enkorage di disaipols sey mak dem get heart and mak dem kontinu to dey biliv sey, "Wi go must sofa wel-wel for pipol hand, bifor wi go fit enta God Kindom."
44014023	Wen dem don shuz eldas wey go lid di bilivas for di difren-difren shosh, dem kon pray and fast sey, mak God protet dem.
44014024	Dem kon liv Pisidia go Pamfilia
44014025	and wen dem don prish for Perga, dem kon go Attalia.
44014026	From der, dem enta ship go Antiok, wer dem for first pray for dem, for di wok wey dem jos finish naw.
44014027	Wen dem rish Antiok, dem gada di pipol kon tel dem all di tins wey God yuz dem du and haw E opun road for Gentai pipol to biliv.
44014028	So dem stay der for somtaim wit di bilivas.
44015001	Som men kom from Judea kon dey tish di brodas sey, "Unles dem sekonsaiz una di way Mosis tok for di law, una nor go fit get salvashon."
44015002	Wen Pol and Banabas don argue wit di pipol wel-wel, di shosh pipol kon send Pol and Banabas wit som oda pipol go Jerusalem go mit di apostols and di eldas, so dat dem go ask dem abaut di mata.
44015003	So di shosh send dem go and as dem dey go, dem pas Fonicia and Samaria kon tel pipol wey dem mit for der haw Gentai pipol tak turn from dia sin kom mit God and di stori mak all di brodas wey hear am, hapi wel-wel.
44015004	Wen dem rish Jerusalem, di hol shosh wit di apostols and di eldas kon welkom dem, den dem tel dem evritin wey God don yuz dem du.
44015005	Bot som Farisi wey don biliv Kraist stand-up kon sey, "E gud mak wi tel Gentai pipol mak dem sekonsaiz and du evritin wey Mosis law tok."
44015006	Di apostols and di eldas kon hol mitin to tok abaut di mata.
44015007	Afta dem don argue wel-wel abaut di mata, Pita kon stand-up sey, "My brodas, una no sey bifor-bifor, na mi God shuz mak e go prish giv Gentai pipol mak dem hear and biliv en wod.
44015008	"And God, wey no wetin dey insaid pipol maind, don show ensef to dem wen E giv dem di Holi Spirit, jos as E giv us
44015009	and E nor du wayo bitwin wi and dem bikos, E mak dia heart klin by fate.
44015010	"So why una won kon trai God? Load wey wi and awa gran-gran papa dem nor fit kari, why una dey put am for dis disaipols head?
44015011	"Wi biliv sey God save us tru grace wey kom from Jisos Kraist, jos as E du for dis Gentai pipol tu."
44015012	Evribodi wey dey for der kon kwayet dey hear wetin Banabas and Pol dey tok and dem tel dem abaut di mirakols and wondas wey God yuz dem du among Gentai pipol.
44015013	Afta dem don tok finish, James ansa, "Awa brodas, mak una hear wetin I won tok.
44015014	"Simeon don tel us haw God first shuz som pipol from Gentai wey go dey tok abaut am.
44015015	"Dis tins gri wit wetin di profets tok bifor sey:
44015016	'Afta all dis tins, I go kom bak and I go build David haus wey don fal; I go build am wit all di sand wey skata for groun and e go strong again,
44015017	so evribodi go kom mit God, plus Gentai pipol wey I don kol to bi my pipol.' God wey mak all dis tins, na so E tok
44015018	and E no sey na so e go bi.'
44015019	"So, I go sey mak wi nor mak tins hard for Gentai pipol wey jos start to serv God,
44015020	bot insted, mak wi rite leta go giv dem sey, mak dem nor chop fud wey dem sakrifias giv juju and mak dem nor slip wit hu dem nor mari, anima wey dem kil and di blood nor tosh groun, mak dem nor chop or drink en blood.
44015021	"Bikos na since awa gran-gran papa dem taim dem don dey prish Mosis law for di sinagog for evri Sabat Day."
44015022	So di apostols, eldas and di hol shosh kon gri sey dem go send som men folo Pol and Banabas go Antiok. Den shuz Judas, wey dem dey kol Basabas and Silas and dem bi ledas among di brodas.
44015023	Na wetin dem rite for di leta, bi dis, "From di apostols and eldas wey bi una brodas, to all di brodas and sistas wey bi Gentai wey dey Antiok, Syria and Silicia. Wi grit una o-o!
44015024	"Wi hear sey som pipol kom mit una sey dem kom from us, ivun doh wi nor send dem. Dem dey konfuz and tel una wetin go disturb una maind.
44015025	"So all of us kon gri sey mak wi shuz pipol wey go folo Banabas and Pol, wey bi awa frend, kom mit una.
44015026	"Dis men dey risk dia life, bikos of awa Oga Jisos Kraist name.
44015027	"So wi send Judas and Silas wey go tel una all this tins by demsef.
44015028	"Bikos wi and di Holi Spirit nor won put heavi load for una head, so na dis smol advise wi dey giv una:
44015029	'Wi advise sey mak una forbid meat and blood wey dem don sakrifias giv juju and eni anima wey una kil wey en blood nor tosh groun. And mak una nor slip wit hu una nor mari.' If una forbid all dis tins, una go du wel!"
44015030	So wen dem don send dem go, dem kon go Antiok and afta dem gada evribodi, dem kon giv dem di leta.
44015031	Bikos of wetin dem rite put for di leta, all di pipol hapi wen dem read am out.
44015032	Bot Judas and Silas, wey bi profet, enkorage di pipol and wetin dem tok kon mak di pipol heart strong.
44015033	Afta dem don stay der tey smol, di brodas kon send dem bak wit peace to di pipol wey send dem kom.
44015034	Bot Silas sey e go stil stay der for somtaim.
44015035	Pol, Banabas and odas kon stil stay for Antiok dey tish and prish God wod.
44015036	Afta som days, Pol kon tel Banabas, "Mak wi go bak go visit di brodas for all di tawn wey wi for prish God wod, so dat wi go no haw dem dey."
44015037	Banabas won kon kari Jon Mark folo bodi,
44015038	bot Pol sey mak dem nor kari am, bikos na so e tak liv dem for Pamfilia bifor and e nor folo dem du di wok.
44015039	Dis mata kon kause serious kworel, sotey dem kon seprate. Banabas tak Mark folo bodi and dem kon enta ship go Syprus,
44015040	bot Pol shuz Silas and dem go mit di brodas and sistas kon pray mak God bless dem.
44015041	Pol pas tru Syria and Silicia dey enkorage di pipol wey dey di shosh dem for der.
44016001	Pol kon stil go Derbe and Lystra. Won disaipol wey dem dey kol Timoti dey der. En mama na Ju wey biliv Kraist, bot en papa, na Greek.
44016002	Di brodas wey dey Lystra and Ikonium dey tok gud abaut am.
44016003	Pol wont mak Timoti folo am, so e sekonsaiz am, bikos di Ju pipol wey dey for di aria, no sey en papa na Greek.
44016004	As dem dey go from tawn to tawn, dem kon dey pas di mesage wey di apostols and eldas for Jerusalem send to all di Gentai pipol wey biliv Kraist sey, mak dem obey.
44016005	So di pipol for di shosh dey strong more-more for fate and dem kon dey plenti evriday.
44016006	Dem pas tru Frigia and Galatia aria, bikos di Holi Spirit warn dem sey mak dem nor prish di mesage for Asia.
44016007	Wen dem rish Mysia, dem kon trai to enta insaid Bitinia, bot Jisos Kraist Spirit nor alow dem enta,
44016008	naim dem pas tru Mysia kon face Troas.
44016009	Pol si dis vishon for nite: Won man wey kom from Masidonia stand dey beg am sey, "Mak yu kom help us for Masidonia!"
44016010	Wen Pol si dis vishon finish, wi kon trai to go Masidonia. Wi kon biliv sey God don kol us mak wi go prish di Gud News to di pipol wey dey der.
44016011	Wi travol for wota from Troas and awa ship kon from der go Samotrace and di next day, wi go Neapolis
44016012	and from der, to Filipai wey bi numba won tawn for Masidonia, wey Rome dey rule. Wi stay for dis tawn for som days.
44016013	Wen Sabat Day rish, wi komot from di tawn go di wotasaid, wer wi tink sey wi go si wer dem for dey pray, naim wi sidan kon start to dey tok to di wimen wey gada for der.
44016014	E get won wuman wey dey listin to us, en name na Lydia and e kom from Tiatira. E dey fear God wel-wel and dey sel purpol klot. God opun en heart to biliv evritin wey Pol tok.
44016015	Afta en and en famili don baptize, e kon beg us sey, "If una don asept mi as pesin wey biliv Kraist, mak una kon stay for my haus." So e beg us ontil wi gri.
44016016	Won day, as wi dey go di place wer dem for dey pray, won slave girl wey get spirit wey dey mak am si vishon, kon si us. Di girl oga dey yuz am mak plenti moni, enitaim e tel pipol wetin go hapun.
44016017	Di girl kon dey folo mi and Pol for bak kon dey shaut sey, "Dis pipol na God savants -o-o, dem dey prish to una abaut haw una go tak dey save."
44016018	E kontinu to dey shaut laik dis for meni days. So di tin ves Pol wel-wel, naim e turn face di girl kon tel di spirit, "I komand yu wit Jisos Kraist name, komot for dis girl bodi!" At wons, di spirit komot from di girl bodi.
44016019	Bot wen di pipol wey get di girl si sey wetin dem tak dey mak moni done go, dem seize Pol and Silas kon drag dem go mit di tawn oga dem for di market senta.
44016020	Den dem drag dem go mit di joj dem kon sey, "All dis men dey kause wahala for dis tawn. Dem bi Ju
44016021	and dem dey tish law wey nor bi awa own, since wi bi Rome pipol."
44016022	All di pipol wey gada for der kon join put mout against dem and di joj dem kon giv orda sey, mak dem rimov Pol and Silas klot komot for dia bodi and flog dem wit heavi stick.
44016023	Afta dem don flog dem wel-wel, dem put dem for prizin kon tel di warda mak e gaid dem wel-wel.
44016024	Bikos of dis strong orda, di warda put dem for insaid-insaid di prizin kon hook dia leg wit big-big chains..
44016025	Wen mid nite rish, Pol and Silas kon dey pray and sing song giv God and all di pipol wey dey di prizin dey listin to dem.
44016026	At wons, di groun start to shake, sotey all di wall and pilas wey dey di prizin kon dey shake tu. Na wons di door opun and di chains wey dem tak hook di pipol wey dey di prizin, kon luz.
44016027	Wen di warda wak-up kon si sey all di doors for di prizin opun, e bring en sword kom out, won kon kil ensef, bikos e tink sey all di prizinas don run.
44016028	Bot Pol kon shaut, "Mak yu nor kil yorsef, all of us stil dey for here!"
44016029	Naim di warda sey mak dem bring lite and e rush enta insaid di prizin kon fal for Pol and Silas front dey shake.
44016030	E bring dem kom outsaid kon ask, "My oga dem, wetin I go du to dey save?"
44016031	Dem ansa am, "Biliv Jisos Kraist and yu go dey save, both yu and all yor famili."
44016032	Den, dem prish God wod giv en and all di pipol wey dey en haus.
44016033	Dat nite, di warda kon wosh all dia sore; den en and en famili kon baptaiz.
44016034	Di warda bring dem enta en haus kon put fud for tabol mak dem chop. E hapi wel-wel sey en and en famili don biliv God.
44016035	Wen day break, di joj dem kon send polis men sey, "Mak una go riliz doz men."
44016036	Di warda kon tel Pol, "Di joj dem don giv orda sey mak wi fri una. So mak una kon dey go."
44016037	Bot Pol tel di polis men, "Dem sey mak dem beat us for publik ivun wen dem neva joj awa kase, ivun doh sey wi bi Rome pipol, dem stil trow us for prizin. Naw, dem won fri us from bak mak pipol nor for no? Wi nor gri! Mak dem kom here by demsef kon riliz us!"
44016038	Di polis men kon ripot wetin Pol tok giv di joj dem. Fear kash dem wen dem hear sey Pol and Silas na Rome pipol,
44016039	so dem kon beg dem sey mak dem nor ves. Afta dem bring dem kom out, dem kon beg dem wel-wel sey mak dem liv di tawn.
44016040	Wen dem don komot for prizin, dem enta Lydia haus and wen dem si di brodas, dem enkorage dem bifor dem liv di tawn.
44017001	Afta dem pas Amfipolis and Apollonia, dem kon rish Tesalonika wer won Ju sinagog dey.
44017002	Pol go mit di Ju pipol for di sinagog as e dey du bifor and for tiri Sabat Day, e kon dey tish dem God wod,
44017003	dey show dem haw God wod sey Kraist must sofa and e go raiz from grave. E tel dem, "Dis Jisos Kraist wey I dey tel una abaut so, naim bi di Kraist."
44017004	Som of dem wey biliv kon join Pol and Silas and meni Greek pipol wey dey fear God and som big-big wimen, join dem tu.
44017005	Bot di Ju pipol kon dey jelos, naim dem gada aria boys wey dey waka abaut for market, tak form gang to skata di tawn. Dem atak Jason haus, bikos dem tink sey Pol and Silas dey der, so dat dem go bring dem out kon tak dem go di tawn hall.
44017006	Wen dem nor si dem, dem kon drag Jason and som of en brodas go mit di tawn oga, dey shaut, "All dis pipol wey don start wahala for di wold, don rish here tu
44017007	and Jason put dem for en haus laik visitor! Dem dey du wetin dey against Caesar law, dey tok sey anoda king dey wey en name bi Jisos Kraist!"
44017008	Dem kause konfushon among di pipol wey gada and di tawn oga dem wey hear all dis tins.
44017009	Afta di oga dem don kolet moni from Jason and di brodas, dem kon alow dem go.
44017010	At wons, di brodas send Pol and Silas go Berea for nite. Wen dem don rish der, dem kon go di Ju sinagog.
44017011	Dis Ju pipol get beta maind pas di wons wey dey for Tesalonika, bikos dem opun maind tak biliv di mesage and dem dey read God wod evriday to shek weda all di tins wey dem hear, na tru.
44017012	Na so meni of dem tak biliv, ivun wit som big-big men and wimen wey bi Greek.
44017013	Bot wen di Ju pipol wey dey for Tesalonika hear sey Pol don rish Berea dey prish God wod, dem kon go der go kause wahala and spoil di pipol maind.
44017014	Naim di brodas send Pol go di wotasaid, bot Silas and Timoti stil stay for Berea.
44017015	Di pipol wey folo Pol, eskot am go rish Atens and afta, e orda dem sey mak Silas and Timoti kom mit am kwik-kwik for der, so dem kon go bak.
44017016	As Pol dey Atens dey wait for dem, e kon dey ves for en spirit, bikos e si sey na so-so juju ful di tawn.
44017017	So e tok to di Ju and Gentai pipol wey dey fear God wey dey insaid di sinagog and e stil tok to evribodi wey dey di market.
44017018	Na so som wise men wey dey folo Epikorian and di wons wey bi Stoik dey folo am tok and som dey ask ish oda, "Wetin dis mumu and toku-toku tink sey e no wey e won tel us?" som stil sey, "E bi laik sey e dey prish abaut som gods from anoda tribe." (Dem tok so, bikos e dey prish di Gud News abaut Jisos Kraist and en resureshon.)
44017019	So dem tak Pol go Areopagus kon tel am, "Wi beg, mak yu tel us abaut dis new tin wey yu dey tish so?
44017020	"Bikos di tins wey yu dey tok, wi neva hear am bifor and wi laik to no wetin dem min."
44017021	(Atens pipol and odas wey dey der, nor get eni oda wok pas mak dem sidan dey tok stori abaut eni new tin wey dey hapun.)
44017022	So Pol stand for Areopagus front kon sey, "My pipol wey dey for Atens, I si sey una laik God mata wel-wel.
44017023	"Bikos as I waka roun dey luk all di tins wey una dey woship, I ivun si won shrine wey dem rite put sey: 'To di god wey pipol nor no.' So wetin una dey woship wey una nor no, naim I kon tel una abaut today.
44017024	"God wey mak di wold and evritin wey dey insaid, wey bi di Oga for hevun and eart, nor dey stay insaid haus wey humanbin build
44017025	and E nor wont mak humanbin gi-am somtin laik sey E nid enitin, bikos naim dey giv life and air wey wi dey breat.
44017026	"Na tru won man E mak all di tribes wey dey for di wold and E tok di taim and boundari wer dem go stay rish,
44017027	so dat dem go luk for God kon si-am, ivun doh E nor dey far from all of us.
44017028	"Bikos na insaid am wi dey liv, waka, get life and som of una wey dey rite poem tok sey, 'Wi tu na God pikin.'
44017029	"So, as e bi sey wi bi God pikin, mak wi nor tink sey God bi laik image wey humanbin yuz gold, siliva or stone tak mak.
44017030	"God don forgiv us for di taim wen wi nor no wetin wi dey du, bot naw, E dey komand pipol for evriwer sey mak dem turn from sin kom mit am,
44017031	bikos E don shuz won day wey E go tak joj di wold wit raitiousnes tru di man wey E shuz and show evribodi wen E raiz-am from deat."
44017032	Wen di pipol hear sey pipol go raiz from deat, som kon dey laff, bot odas kon sey, "Wi go hear dis mata from yu anoda day."
44017033	So Pol kon komot from Areopagus.
44017034	Bot som pipol wey biliv Kraist kon join am. Insaid dis pipol wey biliv so, na Dionysius wey bi memba for Areopagus and won wuman wey dem dey kol Damaris, wit oda pipol wey join dem.
44018001	Afta dis tins, Pol komot from Atens go Korint.
44018002	For der, e kon si won Ju wey dem dey kol Akwila, wey kom from Pontus and e jos kom bak from Itali wit en wife Prisila, bikos Klaudios orda sey mak all Ju pipol komot from Rome. Pol go mit dem
44018003	and bikos dem dey du di same wok, e kon stay wit dem dey folo dem wok (na tent dem dey mak sel).
44018004	E dey tok to both Ju and Greek pipol for di sinagog evri Sabat, so dat dem go biliv.
44018005	Wen Silas and Timoti kom from Masidonia, Pol kon yuz all en maind dey prish di wod, dey bear witnes giv di Ju sey, na Jisos bi di Kraist.
44018006	Wen dem opoz and kos am, e shake en dress kon sey, "Mak una blood dey una head, bikos I nor du eni bad tin and from today go, I go-go prish for Gentai pipol!"
44018007	Den Pol komot for di sinagog go Titus Justus haus; di man na Gentai wey dey woship God and en haus dey near di sinagog.
44018008	Krispus, di oga for di sinagog and en famili, plus meni Korint pipol wey hear abaut Jisos Kraist, biliv and dem kon baptaiz dem.
44018009	Jisos kon tel Pol for vishon for nite, "Mak yu nor kwayet bikos of fear, bot mak yu opun yor mout dey tok,
44018010	I dey for yor side and nobodi go fit du yu enitin, bikos I get plenti pipol for dis tawn."
44018011	So e stay der for won year and sis monts dey tish di pipol God wod.
44018012	Wen Gallio dey rule for Akaya, Ju pipol join togeda atak Pol kon kari am go di jojment seat.
44018013	Dem sey, "Dis man dey bribe pipol to woship God and dat tin dey against awa law!"
44018014	Bot jos as Pol won start to tok, Gallio kon tel di Ju pipol sey, "If na bikos of won offens or serious wayo, I for listin to una komplain,
44018015	bot since na mata abaut wod, name and una own law, mak una go setol am by unasef. I nor go joj all doz kaind tins!"
44018016	So e driv dem komot from di jojment seat.
44018017	Dem kon sieze Sostenes, wey bi oga for di sinagog kon start to beat am for di jojment seat front. Bot Gallio du laik sey all dis tins nor konsan am.
44018018	Afta e don stay meni days for Korint, Pol kon tel all di brodas bye-bye, den e enta ship go Syria and Prisila and Akwila folo am go. For Senkria, e kon kut en hair bikos e mak vow.
44018019	Wen dem rish Efisos, Pol kon liv Prisila and Akwila for der, bot en ensef enta di sinagog go folo di Ju pipol tok.
44018020	Wen dem sey mak e stay wit dem smol, e nor gri,
44018021	bot e tel dem bye-bye kon sey, "If God wont, I go kom again kon si una." Den e enta ship from Efisos
44018022	and wen e rish Sizeria, e pas go Jerusalem go salot di pipol for di shosh wey dey der, bifor e go Antiok.
44018023	Afta e don stay smol for der, Pol komot kon travol pas all di aria wey dey Galatia and Frigia, dey enkorage all di disaipols.
44018024	E get won Ju man, en name na Apollos and e from Alexendria go Efisos. Apollos sabi tok and e no di Bibol wel-wel.
44018025	Dem don tish am abaut Jisos and na wit high spirit e tak dey tok and tish abaut Jisos Kraist, bot na onli Jon baptism, e no rish.
44018026	E kon dey tok wit boldnes for di sinagog, bot wen Prisila and Akwila hear am dey tok, dem kol am go kona kon explain God wod giv am wel-wel.
44018027	Wen Apollos won kros go Akaya, di brodas enkorage am kon giv am leta mak e giv di disaipols, so dat dem go welkom am. Wen e rish der, e kon join dey help di bilivas,
44018028	bikos e nor gri wit wetin di Ju pipol dey tok for publik and e show dem from di Bibol sey na Jisos Kraist, bi di Mezaya.
44019001	For di same taim wen Apollos dey Korint, Pol travol pas insaid tawn ontil e rish Efisos. For der, e mit som disaipols
44019002	kon ask dem, "Una don risiv di Holi Spirit, since una don biliv Kraist?" Dem ansa, "No! Wi neva ivun hear sey Holi Spirit dey."
44019003	Pol ask dem, "Na haw dem kon tak baptaiz una?" Dem ansa, "Na Jon baptism."
44019004	Pol kon tel dem, "Jon baptaiz pipol wey turn from sin kom mit God wit wota kon tel dem mak dem biliv di pesin wey go kom afta am and na dat pesin, bi Jisos Kraist."
44019005	Wen dem hear wetin Pol tok, dem kon baptaiz dem wit Jisos Kraist name
44019006	and as Pol put hand for dia head, di Holi Spirit enta dem and dem kon start to speak difren language, dey profesai.
44019007	(Na twef disaipols Pol folo tok.)
44019008	So Pol enta di sinagog kon dey tok wit boldnes for tiri monts. E dey show di pipol haw dem go tak biliv God Kindom.
44019009	Bot wen som of di stuborn pipol nor gri biliv, dem kon dey spoil Jisos Kraist name for all di pipol front, so Pol wit en disaipols kon liv dem. Pol kon dey tak en disaipols folo bodi evriday, go tish for Tiranus Hall.
44019010	Dis tin kontinu for tu years ontil evribodi wey dey stay for Asia aria, weda na Ju or Greek, hear God wod.
44019011	Dat taim, God yuz Pol dey du meni wondaful mirakols,
44019012	ivun handkachef and klot wey dem tak tosh Pol bodi, dey heal sik pipol and driv evil spirit from pipol bodi, wen dem yuz am tosh dem.
44019013	Bot som Ju wey dey waka abaut kon trai to kol Jisos Kraist name for pipol wey evil spirit dey disturb dey sey, "I kommad yu wit Jisos Kraist name wey Pol dey prish."
44019014	(So, Skeva wey bi Ju prist, get sevun sons wey dey du dis kaind tin.)
44019015	Bot di evil spirit ansa dem, "Yes! I no hu Jisos Kraist bi, I stil no Pol tu, bot hu una bi?"
44019016	Naim di man wey di evil spirit dey insaid en bodi kon jump for dia bodi beat dem wel-wel, ontil dem start to beg. E beat dem til dem run komot from di haus wit nakednes and all dia bodi ful wit sore.
44019017	Wen evribodi wey dey stay Efisos, both Ju and Greek, hear di stori, fear kash dem and Jisos Kraist name kon dey reign.
44019018	Meni pipol wey nor biliv, kom out kon dey konfes all di bad tins wey dem dey du.
44019019	Som wey dey du magic, bring all dia books kon burn dem to ashes for evribodi front. Wen dem add di price for all di books, e rish fifti tazon silva koins (50,000).
44019020	So God wod kon dey grow more-more and dem kon dey win meni souls.
44019021	Afta all dis tins hapun, Pol kon sey e go-go Jerusalem tru Masidonia and Akaya. E plan sey, "Afta I don rish der, I go stil go Rome."
44019022	So, afta e send tu men wey dey help am, Timoti and Erastus go Masidonia, e kon stil stay Asia smol.
44019023	Dat taim serious wahala hapun bikos of "Kraist Way" wey dem dey prish.
44019024	E get won man, en name na Demetrius and e dey mod silva image. Na dis man mod Artemis shrine and dey help pipol wey dey mod, mak plenti moni.
44019025	Di man kon gada all di pipol wey dey mod, wit oda men wey dey du dat kaind wok, den e tel dem, "My pipol, una no sey na dis biznes wi tak dey chop.
44019026	And una don si and hear sey dis Pol don tak meni pipol komot from awa hand. Nor bi onli for dis Efisos, bot for di hol Asia, bikos e dey tel dem sey di gods wey dem mod, nor bi god at-all.
44019027	"So, if wi nor du somtin, awa biznes go spoil and nor bi onli dat won, bot pipol nor go respet di tempol wey awa juju, Artemis, dey stay again and dis wuman wey di hol Asia dey woship, nor go get pawa again."
44019028	Wen di pipol hear dis tins, dem ves wel-wel kon start to shaut, "Artemis wey dey Efisos, na yu bi awa god!"
44019029	Di hol tawn kon dey shake wit nois and all di pipol rush go di stadium dey drag Gaius and Aristakus and di Masidonia pipol wey dey eskot Pol.
44019030	Bot wen Pol won enta di stadium, di disaipols nor alow am.
44019031	Ivun som of di oga dem wey bi en frend, send mesage go mit am sey, mak e nor enta di stadium.
44019032	Na so all di pipol dey shaut enihaw and konfushon kon ful evriwer, meni pipol wey gada dey shaut, nor ivun no why dem gada.
44019033	Som pipol sey na abaut Alexander, bikos di Ju pipol don push am go front. Alexander wave en hand kon sey, mak dem kwayet, mak e for fit tok to difend di Ju pipol.
44019034	Bot wen dem si sey na Ju e bi, dem kon start to shaut again, "Artemis wey dey Efisos, na yu bi awa god!" Dem shaut laik dis rish tu hours."
44019035	Afta di tawn secretary don mak di pipol kwayet, e kon sey, "My pipol wey dey Efisos, wish pesin dey among una wey nor no sey na Artemis bi Efisos god wey fal from hevun?
44019036	"So bikos nobodi fit argue dis mata, mak una kwayet and mak una nor du enitin wey nor get head.
44019037	"Una don bring dis men kom here, nor bi bikos dem spoil di tempol or kos awa goddess.
44019038	"If Demetrius and di pipol wey dey wit am get eni komplain against enibodi, kourt dey and joj dem dey der tu. So mak dem tak dia kase go der.
44019039	"Bot if una wont enitin wey pas dis won, na kourt dem go for setol am.
44019040	"Bikos dem fit tak all of us go kourt today sey wi dey riot, bikos wi nor get eni rizin for dis konfushon wey dey hapun so."
44019041	Afta e tok finish, e kon sey mak evribodi go dia haus.
44020001	Afta di wahala for Efisos, Pol send for di disaipols and afta e enkorage dem, e tel dem bye-bye kon komot der go Masidonia.
44020002	Afta e waka roun di aria, e enkorage di bilivas wey dey der kon go Greece.
44020003	E stay for der for tiri monts. Bikos Ju pipol don plan to wait mak dem kash am, as e won enta ship go Syria, e kon go bak tru Masidonia.
44020004	Pipol wey folo Pol go, na Sopater, wey bi Frius pikin wey kom from Berea; Aristakus and Sekondus wey kom from Tesalonika; Gaius from Derbe; Timoti wit Tikikus and Trofimus wey kom from Asia.
44020005	All dis pipol don go for front go wait us for Troas.
44020006	Wi enta ship from Filipai afta di Passova Fist and afta faiv days, wi mit dem for Troas kon stay der for sevun days.
44020007	For di first day for di wik, wen wi hol mitin to break bread togeda, Pol kon start to tok wit di pipol and bikos e won go di next day, e kon prish til mid-nite.
44020008	(For di room for upstair wer wi for dey mit, lamp meni for der),
44020009	won boy wey dem dey kol Eutikus, sidan for di window kon dey slip as Pol dey prish. Di slip kari am go, so e fal from di tiri storey and wen dem rush go kari am, dem si sey e don die.
44020010	Bot Pol go dan, laidan on-top di boy, kon put en hand roun am sey, "Mak una nor wori, bikos e stil dey alaif!"
44020011	Den Pol go upstair and afta e don break bread wit dem, e folo dem tok til day break. Den e kon komot from der.
44020012	Dem tak di boy go haus kon dey hapi sey e dey alaif.
44020013	Wi waka go wer di ship dey kon go Assos, so dat wi go kari Pol for der, bikos e plan sey e go pas land go der.
44020014	Wen e mit us for Assos, wi kari am for di ship kon go Mitilene.
44020015	From der, wi move and di next day, wi kon rish Miletus.
44020016	Pol don sey e go travol pas Efisos mak e for nor spend taim for Asia, bikos e dey hurri mak e for kwik rish Jerusalem for Pentecost Day.
44020017	From Miletus, e send mesanga go Efisos sey mak di eldas wey dey di shosh kon mit am der.
44020018	Wen dem kom, e tel dem, "All of una no haw I dey liv my life since di taim wey I dey wit una and from di first day wey I enta Asia,
44020019	haw I nor dey kari bodi up as I dey serv Jisos wit pain and wahala wey I dey face, bikos of wiked plan wey Ju pipol get for mi.
44020020	"Una no sey I nor stop to dey tel una enitin wey go help una and I tish una for publik and for una haus.
44020021	"I dey prish giv Ju and Greek pipol sey mak dem turn from sin kom mit and serv God and put dia fate for awa Oga Jisos Kraist.
44020022	"Naw, di Spirit dey lid mi go Jerusalem, ivun doh I nor no wetin go hapun to mi for der,
44020023	esept sey di Holi Spirit dey warn mi sey, from tawn to tawn, na prizin and sofa dey wait for mi.
44020024	"Bot I nor kount my life to min enitin, so dat I go fit finish my wok and di ministri wey I risiv from Jisos Kraist, wey bi to prish abaut di Gud News wey go mak pipol undastand God grace.
44020025	"Naw, I no sey non of una wey I prish God kindom giv, go si mi again.
44020026	"So, I won tel una naw sey, nobodi blood dey for my head.
44020027	"Bikos I nor hide enitin from una, as I dey tel una abaut God plan.
44020028	"Mak una tak kare of unasef and all di pipol wey di Holi Spirit don put unda una, bikos na una bi di lidas for God shosh, wey E buy wit en onli pikin blood.
44020029	"I no sey afta I don go, wiked pipol wit bad maind go kom join una. Pipol wey nor go sori for di ship.
44020030	"Ivun among una, som men go stand dey tish lai-lai tins kon draw pipol folo bodi.
44020031	"So mak una shine una eye and rimemba sey, for day and nite for tiri years, I nor stop to dey krai, as I dey warn una.
44020032	"Naw, I liv una for God hand, so mak en wod wey get grace, kip una. Dis wod wey get grace fit mak una grow and get share wit all God pipol.
44020033	"Since una no mi, I nor put eye for enibodi gold, silva or koat.
44020034	"Una no sey na dis my hand I tak dey wok and get evritin wey I wont and ivun dey help pipol wey dey wit mi.
44020035	"Laik dis, I don show una sey wi must help oda pipol wey wik and una rimemba wetin Jisos Kraist tok, wen e sey, 'E beta mak pesin dey giv pipol tins, dan mak e dey kolet from dem.'"
44020036	Wen e tok all dis tins finish, e nil dan wit all of dem kon pray.
44020037	All of dem start to krai, as dem draw Pol near bodi kon dey kiss am.
44020038	Wetin Pol tok kon mak dem wik, bikos e sey, "Una nor go si mi again." So dem folo am go rish wer di ship dey.
44021001	Afta wi don liv dem, wi enta ship kon travol go Kos. Di next day, wi go Rhodes and from der, wi kon go Patara.
44021002	Wi si won ship dey kros go Fonicia, so wi kon enta am.
44021003	Afta wi rish Syprus, wi kon liv der travol go Syria, kom stop for Tyre, bikos di ship won put load dan.
44021004	Wi kon go faind di disaipols wey dey for di tawn, wen wi si dem, wi stay wit dem for sevun days. Dem kon tel Pol meni taims sey mak e nor go Jerusalem.
44021005	Wen wi don stay der for somtaim, wi kon travol komot der. All of dem wit dia wife and pikin eskot us go outsaid di tawn. Wi nil dan pray for di riva
44021006	kon tel dem bye-bye and as wi enta ship, dem kon go bak to dia haus.
44021007	Wi kontinu awa joni from Tyre go rish Ptolemais and wen wi don grit di brodas, wi stay wit dem for won day.
44021008	Di next day, wi liv der kon go Sizeria. For der, wi enta Filip haus. Dis Filip na evangelist and e dey among di sevun dikins wey dem shuz for Jerusalem, den wi kon stay der wit am.
44021009	(E get for dotas wey neva mari, wey dey profesai.)
44021010	As wi stay der for som days, won profet wey en name na Agabush kom from Judea.
44021011	E waka kon mit us, tak Pol belt tie en hand and leg kon sey, "Di Holi Spirit sey, 'Na so di Ju pipol wey dey Jerusalem go tie di man wey get dis belt kon kari am giv Gentai pipol.'"
44021012	Wen wi hear wetin e tok, wi and di pipol wey dey der kon beg Pol sey mak e nor go Jerusalem.
44021013	Bot Pol ansa, "Wetin una dey du so, una dey krai dey won break my heart? I redi, nor bi onli mak dem tie mi, bot to die for Jerusalem, bikos of Jisos Kraist name."
44021014	Bikos wi nor fit stop am again, wi kon kip kwayet and onli en kon sey, "Wetin God wont mak e hapun, go hapun."
44021015	Afta dat day, wi priper kon go Jerusalem.
44021016	Som disaipols from Sizeria folo us go, dem kon bring us kon Mnason for Syprus haus, wey bi won of di first disaipols and wi stay der wit am.
44021017	Wen wi rish Jerusalem, di brodas welkom us wit hapines.
44021018	Di next day, Pol kon folo us go si James and all di eldas wey dey der.
44021019	Wen Pol don grit dem, e kon start to tok di stori abaut wetin God don du for Gentai pipol tru en ministri.
44021020	Wen dem hear dis, dem kon dey praiz God. Den, dem tel am, "Yu si, awa broda, haw meni tazon Ju don biliv and dem stil dey obey di law?
44021021	"Dem hear sey yu dey tish Ju pipol wey dey stay wit Gentai pipol, sey mak dem trowey Mosis law; mak dem nor sekonsaiz dia shildren again and mak dem nor folo awa laws again.
44021022	"So, wetin wi go du? Bikos dem go rili hear sey yu don kom.
44021023	"So mak yu du wetin wi won tel yu: For men dey wit us here wey mak vow;
44021024	tak dem folo bodi mak una go du wetin Mosis law tok and mak yu pay all di moni wey dem spend tak shave dia head. Den, evribodi go no sey all di stori wey dem hear abaut yu, nor bi tru and dem go si sey yu yorsef dey obey di law.
44021025	"Bot konsanin Gentai pipol wey don biliv, wi don rite leta go giv dem sey, mak dem forbid meat wey dem sakrifais giv juju, anima wey dem kil and e blood nor tosh groun and mak dem nor slip wit hu dem nor mari."
44021026	Di next day, Pol tak di men and afta e don join dem du wetin Mosis law tok, e go di Tempol kon sey, dem don obey di law and dem redi to offa di sakrifais.
44021027	Wen di sevun days don dey finish, di Ju pipol wey kom from Asia kon si-am for di Tempol, naim dem start wahala and pipol kon gada. Dem seize Pol
44021028	dey shaut sey, "Izrel pipol, mak una kom o-o! Dis na di man wey dey tish pipol for evriwer, abaut tins wey dey against awa pipol, awa law and against dis Tempol. Ivun sef e don bring Greek dem enta insaid di Tempol kon mak dis holi place dirti."
44021029	(Bikos dem si Trofimus wey kom from Efisos for di tawn wit am bifor, so dem kon tink sey, Pol don kari am enta di Tempol.)
44021030	Di hol tawn start to shake and all di pipol kon gada. Dem seize Pol, drag am komot from di Tempol kon klose di door.
44021031	As dem dey trai to kil-am, news kon rish di komandin ofisa for di Roman armi wey dey gaid di tawn sey, di hol Jerusalem don skata.
44021032	At wons, e kari plenti sojas and offisas kon run go wer di pipol gada. Wen dem si di komandin ofisa and di sojas, dem kon stop to beat Pol.
44021033	Den di komandin ofisa arres am kon giv orda sey mak dem tie am wit tu chain. E ask am hu e bi and wetin e du.
44021034	Som pipol for di crowd kon dey tok difren-difren tins and wen di komandin ofisa nor fit no wetin kause di wahala, e kon giv orda sey, mak dem kari Pol go barrak.
44021035	Wen e rish di step for di Tempol, di sojas kon kari Pol, bikos of di crowd wey won kil-am.
44021036	So dem folo di sojas for bak kon dey shaut, "Kil am!"
44021037	As dem won kari Pol enta di barrak, e kon ask di komandin ofisa, "I go fit tok to yu first?" Di ofisa ansa, "So yu dey hear Greek language?
44021038	"So nor bi yu bi dat Egypt man wey start wahala kon kari for tazon men wey dem dey kol 'Assasins' go insaid desert?"
44021039	Pol ansa, "I bi Ju wey kom from Tarsus wey dey Silicia. I bi citizin for dis tawn and dem no mi wel-wel. Abeg alow mi folo di pipol tok."
44021040	Wen di komandin ofisa alow am, Pol kon stand for di step, wave en hand sey mak dem kwayet. Wen evriwer don kwayet, e kon yuz Aramaic language folo dem tok.
44022001	"My brodas and fadas, mak una hear mi as I dey difend mysef."
44022002	(Wen dem hear sey e dey tok to dem wit Aramaic language, dem kon kwayet wel-wel.) Den Pol sey,
44022003	"I bi Ju wey dem born for Tarsus wey dey Silicia, bot na for dis tawn I for grow, I go school and learn awa gran-gran papa dem law wel-wel unda Gamaliel and I get maind to serv God wel-wel, jos as una bi today.
44022004	"I sofa Kristens and I dey kil pipol wey dey serv God, dey tie pipol trow for prizin, weda dem bi man or wuman
44022005	and ivun di High Prist and di kansol eldas no abaut mi. From dem, I kolet leta go giv dia brodas wey dey for Damaskus, so dat I go arres pipol wey biliv Kraist kon bring dem kom Jerusalem put for prizin.
44022006	"As I dey go, near Damaskus, aroun aftanun, won kaind lite from hevun kon shine roun mi.
44022007	"Den I fal for groun kon hear won vois wey sey, 'Sol, Sol, why yu dey ponish mi?'
44022008	"I ansa, 'Hu yu bi Oga?' E kon sey, 'I bi Jisos Kraist wey kom from Nazaret, wey yu dey ponish.'
44022009	"Di pipol wey folo mi si di lite, bot dem nor undastand di vois wey dey tok to mi.
44022010	"So I ask am, 'Oga! Wetin yu wont mak I du?' Di Oga ansa, 'Get up mak yu go Damaskus; for der, dem go tel yu evritin wey God don shuz sey yu go du.'
44022011	"Bikos of haw di lite shine for my eye, I nor fit si again, so di pipol wey dey folo mi kon hol my hand go Damaskus.
44022012	"Won man wey dem dey kol Ananias, wey dey holi and dey serv God akordin to di law and di Ju pipol wey dey stay der, dey tok gud abaut am.
44022013	"Na di man kom mit mi, stand near mi sey, 'Broda Sol, mak yu bigin si again!' So for dat same taim, I luk up kon si-am.
44022014	"Den e sey, 'God wey awa gran-gran papa dem serv don alredi shuz yu to du wetin e wont and to tak yor eye si di Raitious Pesin. So mak yu hear and listin to am,
44022015	bikos yu go bi en witnes to all di pipol, abaut wetin yu don si and hear.
44022016	'Naw, wetin yu dey wait for? Get-up, mak dem baptaiz yu, so dat God go forgiv yu yor sin, as yu kol en name.
44022017	"Wen I go Jerusalem bak and dey pray for di Tempol, I kon si vishon
44022018	and Jisos Kraist sey, 'Mak yu komot for Jerusalem kwik-kwik, bikos dem nor go asept wetin yu dey tok abaut mi.'
44022019	"I ansa, 'Oga, dem diasef no sey I dey beat and trow pipol wey biliv yu put for prizin.
44022020	"And wen dem kil yor savant Steven, I stand der sopot dem kon kip dia klot for dem.'
44022021	"Bot di Oga sey, 'Go, bikos I go send yu go far-far go mit Gentai pipol.'"
44022022	As e tok finish, pipol wey gada dey listin to am kon dey shaut, "Kari dis man komot! Mak dem nor alow am liv!"
44022023	As dem dey shaut dey ves pul shirt and trowey san-san,
44022024	di komandin ofisa kon giv orda sey mak dem tak Pol go insaid barrak. E sey mak dem flog and ask Pol kweshon, so dat dem go fit no why di pipol dey shaut for Pol head laik dat.
44022025	Wen dem don put am for groun mak dem start to flog am, Pol kon ask di soja wey stand near am, "E dey rite mak una flog pesin wey bi Roman citizin, wen dem neva joj en kase?"
44022026	Wen di soja hear dis, e go tel di komandin ofisa, "Wetin yu won du so? Dis man kom from Rome o-o."
44022027	So di komandin ofisa ask Pol, "Tel mi, yu bi Roman citizin?" Pol ansa, "Yes."
44022028	Di komandin ofisa kon sey, "Na big moni I spend to bi Roman citizin." Pol ansa, "Bot dem born mi for Rome."
44022029	Den doz men wey bi won ask am kweshon kon komot and fear kash di komandin ofisa wen e no sey Pol, wey dem tie, na Roman citizin.
44022030	Di next day, bikos di komandin ofisa won no di rizin wey mak di Ju pipol dey akiuz Pol, e riliz am kon orda di prist oga dem and di hol kansol mak dem gada. So e bring Pol kon stand for dia front.
44023001	Pol luk di kansol pipol kon tel dem, "My brodas, I dey liv my life wit klin maind for God eye kon rish today."
44023002	Bikos of wetin e tok, Ananias wey bi di High Prist kon orda di pipol wey stand near Pol sey mak dem slap am for mout.
44023003	So Pol tel am, "God go slap yu tu, yu wey dey pritend! Yu sidan dey joj mi wit di law, yu nor dey disobey di law wen yu sey mak dem slap mi?"
44023004	Di pipol wey stand near am kon sey, "Yu dey kos God High Prist?"
44023005	Pol ansa, "I nor no bifor sey naim bi di High Prist, bikos God wod sey, 'Mak yu nor tok bad abaut di pesin wey dey rule yor pipol.'"
44023006	Den wen Pol no sey som pipol wey dey der na Sadusi and odas na Farisis, e kon shaut mak di hol kansol hear, "My brodas, I bi Farisi, na Farisi pesin born mi. Dem dey joj mi today, bikos I put hope sey pipol wey don die go wak again!"
44023007	Wen e tok dis tin, kworel kon start bitwin di Farisi and di Sadusi pipol and di kansol kon divide.
44023008	(Bikos Sadusi pipol biliv sey pipol wey don die, nor go wak again and dem nor biliv sey enitin laik angel or spirit dey sef, bot Farisi pipol biliv all dis tins.)
44023009	So kworel kon start bitwin dem and som oga for law mata wey bi Farisi pipol kon stand-up dey opoz di Sadusi pipol sey, "Wi nor si enitin bad wey dis man du. Una no weda na spirit or angel tok to am?"
44023010	Wen di arguement kon tu mush and di komandin ofisa dey fear sey dem go tear Pol to pisis, e kon orda en sojas mak dem enta di mitin and kari Pol komot for der by fos.
44023011	For nite for di next day, Jisos kon stand near Pol tel am for vishon, "Mak yu nor fear, bikos as yu don testifi abaut mi for Jerusalem, na so yu go stil du for Rome."
44023012	Wen mornin rish, som Ju pipol kon gada dey mak bad plan and dem swear sey dem nor go chop or drink enitin ontil dem kil Pol.
44023013	Di pipol wey mak dis bad plan pas forti.
44023014	Dem go mit di prist oga dem and di eldas tel dem sey, "Wi don swear sey wi nor go chop enitin ontil wi kil Pol.
44023015	So mak una and di kansol tel di komandin ofisa mak e bring Pol kom mit una, laik sey una won joj en kase again. Wi redi to kil-am, bifor e go rish dis place."
44023016	Bot wen Pol sista pikin hear abaut dis plan, e run go insaid di barrak go tel Pol.
44023017	Pol kon kol won soja oga tel am, "Tak dis boy go mit di komandin ofisa, bikos e get somtin wey e won tel am."
44023018	So di soja oga tak di boy go mit di komandin ofisa kon sey, "Pol, wey dey prizin, sey mak I bring dis boy kon mit yu, bikos e get somtin wey e won tel yu."
44023019	Di komandin ofisa hol di boy for hand go won kona kon ask am, "Wetin yu won tel mi?"
44023020	Di boy ansa, "Ju pipol dey plan sey dem go ask yu mak yu bring Pol kom di kansol tumoro, laik sey dem won ask am kweshon again.
44023021	"So mak yu nor alow dem disiv yu, bikos dem pas forti wey hide for bush won kil-am. Dem don swear sey dem nor go chop or drink enitin, ontil dem don kil Pol. Naw, dem dey wait for yu to gri for wetin dem won ask yu."
44023022	So di komandin ofisa tel di boy mak e dey go kon warn am sey, "Nor tel enibodi sey yu don ripot dis mata giv mi."
44023023	Den e kol tu soja oga kon tel dem, "For nain o' klok dis nite, mak una redi tu ondred sojas wey go-go Sizeria, plus sevunti, wey go ride horse and tu ondred, wey go kari spear.
44023024	"Mak una arange horse wey Pol go sidan put, so dat una go fit gaid am wel-wel go mit Felix wey bi di govnor.
44023025	E rite leta laik dis:
44023026	"From Klaudios Lysias to Govnor Felix, I salot yu!
44023027	"Di Ju pipol seize dis man and dem nearli kil-am bifor I rish der wit my sojas. Wi kon save am from dia hand, bikos I faind out sey, e bi Roman citizin.
44023028	"Bikos I won no di offence wey e komit, I kon kari am go dia kansol.
44023029	"I kon si sey en offence, na abaut wetin dem dey argue abaut for dia law, bot e nor du enitin wey rish to kil-am or put am for prizin.
44023030	"Wen won pesin tel mi sey dem dey plan to kil-am, naim I send am kon mit yu at wons and I stil orda di pipol wey dey akuiz am mak dem kom tok wetin e du for yor front."
44023031	So di sojas kari Pol for nite ontil dem rish Antipatris, jos as dia oga komand dem.
44023032	Di next day, di tu soja oga liv di men wey dey ride horse folo Pol and dem kon go dia barrak bak.
44023033	Wen di men wey dey ride horse rish Sizeria, dem kon tak Pol and di leta giv di govnor.
44023034	Wen di govnor don read di leta, e ask dem wer Pol from kom. Wen e hear sey e kom from Silicia,
44023035	e kon sey, "I go hear yor kase wen di pipol wey akuiz yu rish here." Den e orda sey mak dem gaid Pol for insaid Herod palise.
44024001	Wen faiv days don pas, Ananias, wey bi di High Prist, kom wit som eldas and won lawya wey dem dey kol Tertullus and dem read wetin dem sey Pol du, giv di govnor.
44024002	Wen dem orda mak dem bring Pol kom out, Tertullus tel di govnor sey, "E don tey wen wi dey enjoy peace, bikos of haw yu dey rule and all di beta-beta tins wey yu dey du tak shange di kontri.
44024003	"Oga Felix, wi dey si all dis tins wey yu dey du for evriwer. Na evriday wi dey tok abaut am and dey tank yu.
44024004	"Bot mak my stori for nor long tu mush, I beg mak yu hear us wel-wel as yu dey always du.
44024005	"Bikos wi don si dis man sey e faind trobol and kause wahala among all di Ju pipol for di wold and naim dey lid di gang wey dem dey kol, 'Di Nazarenes'.
44024006	"E ivun tak Greek pipol enta di Tempol, so wi kon arres am.
44024007	"Bot Lysias, di komandin ofisa kon tak am komot from awa hand wit fos.
44024008	"So wen yu ask am kweshon, yu go fit hear by yorsef all di tins wey wi sey e du."
44024009	As e dey tok, di Ju pipol tu dey sopot sey, wetin e tok, na tru.
44024010	Wen di govnor sey mak Pol tok, e kon sey, "I no sey yu don bi joj for dis kontri for meni years naw, so I nor go fear dey tok as I dey difend mysef.
44024011	"As yu go fit shek for yorsef, e neva pas twef days naw wey I go Jerusalem go woship.
44024012	"Dem nor si mi dey argue wit enibodi or dey gada crowd for di Tempol veranda or insaid di sinagog or ivun for di hol tawn,
44024013	dem nor fit show yu di offence wey dem akuiz mi sey I komit.
44024014	"Bot I go let yu no sey I dey woship di God wey awa gran-gran papa dem dey woship, as dia tradishon tok (wey dis pipol sey na won kaind gang). Dem biliv evritin wey di law tok and wey di profets rite dan.
44024015	"I get hope for God (di kaind won wey dis men get tu) sey won day, pipol wey don die, weda na bad or gud pipol, go wak-up.
44024016	"Na bikos of dis I dey always trai my best to get klin bele for God and pipol front.
44024017	"Afta meni years, I kom Jerusalem bak kon giv gift to poor pipol and offa sakrifas.
44024018	"Dis na wetin I dey du wen dem si mi for di Tempol; I dey klin and I nor gada eni crowd or disturb enibodi.
44024019	"Bot som Ju from Asia sopoz dey here dey tok di tin wey dem get against mi, if dem get enitin to tok at-all.
44024020	"Or mak dis men wey dey here tok di krime wey I komit as I face di kansol,
44024021	bikos if e pas dis won, I go shaut as I stand for dia front sey, 'Una dey joj mi today, bikos I biliv sey pipol wey don die, go wak-up.'"
44024022	Den Felix, wey bi sey e no di tru stori abaut di Way, prospone di kase kon sey, "Wen Lysias, di komandin ofisa kom, I go joj yor kase."
44024023	E kon orda di soja oga mak e gaid Pol, bot mak e gi-am smol fridom and mak e nor driv en frends if dem won gi-am enitin.
44024024	Afta somdays, wen Felix wit en wife Drusilia wey bi Ju, sidan togeda, dem kon sey mak dem bring Pol, so dat dem go listin to am, as e dey tok abaut haw pesin go fit tak biliv Jisos Kraist.
44024025	Fear kash Felix, as Pol dey tok abaut di Gud News, sef kontrol and haw God jojment go tak kom, so e kon tel Pol, "Mak yu go first, wen I get taim, I go sey mak dem bring yu kom again."
44024026	Bikos e dey hope sey Pol go bribe am, naim mak am sey mak dem bring Pol kom mit am meni taims.
44024027	Afta tu years, Porcius Festus tak ova from Felix and bikos Felix won mak di Ju pipol hapi, e kon liv Pol for prizin.
44025001	Wen tiri days don pas, Festus komot from Sizeria go Jerusalem.
44025002	So di prist oga dem and all di big men among di Ju pipol kon tel am wetin dem sey Pol du.
44025003	Dem beg am sey mak e giv orda sey mak dem bring Pol kom Jerusalem bak, bikos dem plan to atak and kil-am for road.
44025004	Den Festus ansa, Pol dey for Sizeria and mi mysef go soon go der.
44025005	So e sey, "Mak yor lidas folo mi go der and if dis man du enitin wey bad, mak dem akiuz am."
44025006	Festus nor stay rish ate or ten days wen e go Sizeria and di next day, e sidan for di jojment seat kon giv orda sey mak dem bring Pol kom.
44025007	Wen Pol rish der, di Ju pipol wey kom from Jerusalem kon stand roun am, dey akiuz am sey e komit sin wey dem nor fit show.
44025008	Pol difend ensef sey, "I nor komit eni offence against di Ju law or di Tempol or against Caesar."
44025009	Bikos Festus won mak di Ju pipol hapi, e kon ask Pol, "Yu redi to go Jerusalem mak I joj yor kase for der?"
44025010	Pol ansa, "I stand for Caesar jojment seat, na here dem go joj my kase. I nor komit eni offence to Ju pipol and ivun yu yorsef no.
44025011	"I nor du bad and I nor komit eni offence wey dem fit tak kil mi, I nor dey trai to run sey mak dem nor kil mi, bot if evritin wey dem tok against mi nor bi tru, nobodi go fit kari mi, giv dem. I sey mak dem kari my kase go giv Caesar!"
44025012	Festus kon sey, "Yu don tok sey mak Caesar joj yor kase, so, na Caesar yu go-go mit!"
44025013	Afta som days, King Agrippa and Bernice go Sizeria, go salot Festus.
44025014	As dem dey der for meni days, Festus kon tel dem abaut Pol kase, so dat e go hear wetin dem go tok abaut di mata, so e kol Agrippa kon sey, "Won man dey for here wey Felix liv for prizin.
44025015	"Wen I dey Jerusalem, di prist oga dem and di eldas kon tel mi abaut am sey mak I kil-am.
44025016	"Bot I ansa dem, 'Rome law nor gri mak dem kondem enibodi wen e neva face and difend ensef bifor pipol wey dey akiuz am.'
44025017	"So afta dem folo mi kom here, I kon prospone di kase, bot di next day I sidan for jojment seat kon orda mak dem bring di man kom.
44025018	"Wen pipol wey dey akiuz am stand-up, dem nor tok eni bad tin against am as I bin suspet.
44025019	"Insted, dem dey argue mata wit am, abaut haw dem dey serv God and won man wey dem dey kol Jisos Kraist wey don die, wey Pol sey e stil dey alaif.
44025020	"Bikos I nor no haw I go tak joj di mata, I kon ask am weda e go laik go Jerusalem mak dem joj am der.
44025021	"Bot Pol sey mak dem tak am go Rome, so dat Caesar go joj en kase, so I kon orda sey mak dem kip am for prizin, ontil I go fit send am go mit Caesar."
44025022	Agrippa kon tel Festus, "Mi tu go laik hear from di man." So Festus tel am, "Yu go hear from di man tumoro."
44025023	So di next day, Agrippa and Bernice kon dey mak yanga enta di hall, wit all di big men wey dey di tawn. Afta Festus don giv orda, dem kon bring Pol.
44025024	Den Festus sey, "King Agrippa and all of una wey dey here wit us, mak una si dis man wey di hol Ju pipol dey beg mi both for here and for Jerusalem sey, mak I kil.
44025025	"Bot I kon si sey e nor du enitin wey go mak dem kil-am and wen e sey e won mak di emperor joj en kase, I gri sey I go send am go mit Caesar.
44025026	"Bot I nor no wetin I go rite go giv di emperor abaut am. So naim mak mi bring am kom all of una and king Agrippa front, so dat afta una don kweshon am finish, I go get somtin wey I go fit rite.
44025027	"Bikos for my maind, e nor dey rite to send prizina go kourt, wen yu nor rite wetin e du."
44026001	So Agrippa tel Pol, "Mak yu tok for yorsef naw." Den Pol raiz en hand kon start to tok.
44026002	"King Agrippa, abaut all dis tins wey di Ju pipol dey akuiz mi sey I du, I tank God sey I won difend mysef giv yu today,
44026003	bikos yu no all awa tradishon and di mata wey di Ju pipol dey akuiz mi abaut. So, I beg, mak yu listin to wetin I won tok.
44026004	"Naw, all di Ju pipol no sey na from smol pikin I dey liv my life wit my own pipol for Jerusalem.
44026005	"Since dem no mi, if dem go gri kon tok, dem go gri sey na haw wi dey serv God, naim I tak liv as Farisi.
44026006	"Naw, I stand mak dem joj mi, bikos I put hope for di promis wey God mak giv awa gran-gran papa dem
44026007	sey, awa twef tribes go gain as dem dey yuz all dia maind dey serv God, both day and nite. My king, na bikos of dis hope wey I get, naim mak di Ju pipol dey akuiz mi so!
44026008	"Why una tink sey God nor fit raiz pipol wey don die?
44026009	"Ivun mi mysef, I biliv bifor sey mak wi fite Jisos Kraist wey kom from Nazaret.
44026010	"And na wetin I du for Jerusalem bi dat. Nor bi onli sey I put meni of di bilivas for prizin wit di pawa wey di prist oga dem giv mi, bot I ivun dey sopot wen dem sey mak dem kil dem.
44026011	"I ponish dem meni taims for all di sinagog and I trai to fos dem mak dem kos God. Bikos dat taim, I dey ves for dem wel-wel, I ivun travol go oda tawns go sofa dem, bikos of wetin dem biliv.
44026012	"Bot won day, as I dey du all dis tins, I kon dey go Damaskus wit ful pawa wey di prist oga dem giv mi.
44026013	"My king, aroun aftanun for road, I kon si won kaind lite from hevun wey shine pas di sun. Di lite shine roun mi and di pipol wey dey folo mi travol.
44026014	"Wen wi don fal for groun, I hear won vois wey yuz Aramaic language tel mi, 'Sol, Sol, why yu dey ponish mi? Yu dey fite yorsef, bikos na stone yu dey kick so.'
44026015	"So I ask am, 'Oga! Hu yu bi?' Di Oga ansa, 'I bi Jisos Kraist wey yu dey ponish.
44026016	'Bot mak yu get up, bikos I don show mysef to yu and don shuz yu as my savant and witnes to di tins wey yu don si and di wons wey I go show yu.
44026017	'I go save yu from yor own pipol and from Gentai pipol wey I dey send yu go mit, so dat
44026018	yu go opun dia eyes mak dem for waka komot from daknes enta lite. Mak dem komot from Satan hand, go mit God, so dat God go forgiv dem dia sins and dem go folo di pipol wey God don mak klin, bikos dem biliv am.'
44026019	"So King Agrippa, I nor du strong head wen I risiv dis vishon wey kom from hevun,
44026020	bot I first go Damaskus, go tel di pipol wey dey der and den, I kon go mit di pipol wey dey for Jerusalem and Judea. Afta, I go mit Gentai pipol sey, mak dem turn from sin kom mit God and mak dem du tins wey go show sey, dem don rili turn from sin kom mit God.
44026021	"Bikos of dis, di Ju pipol seize mi for di Tempol front, won kon kil mi.
44026022	"Bot God don dey help mi til today, so I stand dey tel evribodi, weda dem bi smol pikin or big pesin. So, wetin di profets and Mosis tok sey go hapun, naim I dey tel una so,
44026023	sey Kraist sofa and e go bi di first to raiz from deat, so dat e go show di lite to awa pipol and ivun Gentai pipol."
44026024	As Pol dey difend ensef, Festus kon shaut, "Yu dis Pol, yu don dey krase o! All di plenti book wey yu no don dey won mak yu mad!"
44026025	Bot Pol ansa am, "I nor dey mad oga Festus, bot na beta wod wey mak sense naim I dey tok so.
44026026	"Ivun di king wey I dey tok to so, I biliv sey e no abaut all dis tins, bikos dem nor hapun for sikrit.
44026027	"King Agrippa! Yu biliv di tin wey di profets tok?"
44026028	So Agrippa ask Pol, "So yu tink sey jos naw-naw, yu fit turn mi to Kristen?"
44026029	Pol ansa, "I pray to God sey, weda na naw or leta, nor bi onli yu, bot evribodi wey dey here, go bi laik mi, bot mak una nor sofa, as I dey sofa so."
44026030	So di king, di govnor and Bernice kon get up
44026031	and as dem dey go, dem kon tel ish oda, "Dis man nor du enitin wey go fit mak dem kil-am or put am for prizin."
44026032	Agrippa kon tel Festus, "Wi for fit riliz dis man, if to sey e nor sey mak Caesar joj en kase."
44027001	Wen dem don gri sey wi go travol insaid ship go Itali, dem kon kari Pol and som oda prizinas giv Julius, won komanda wey dey Augustan grup.
44027002	Wi enta won ship from Adramyttium wey won travol go difren place for Asia sea kon bigin travol go Aristakus and won Masidonia man wey dey stay Tesalonika, folo us.
44027003	Di next day, wi enta Sidon and Julius kon du gud giv Pol, e alow am go mit en frends mak dem giv am all di tins wey e nid.
44027004	From der, wi enta wota travol again face Syprus island, bikos briz dey blow di ship.
44027005	Afta wi don travol enta di opun sea wey dey insaid Silicia and Pamfilia, wi kon stop for Myra, wey dey Lycia.
44027006	For der, di soja komanda kon si won ship wey kom from Alexandria dey driv go Itali and e kon put us for insaid.
44027007	Wi dey go smol-smol for meni days and nor bi smol wahala bifor wi fit rish Cnidus. Bikos di briz nor mak us fit go front again, wi kon driv smol-smol dey go Krete, wey dey oposite Salmone.
44027008	Bifor wi rish Krete wotasaid, e hard us wel-wel and wi kon rish won place wey dem dey kol, "Fair Havens" wey dey near Lasea tawn.
44027009	As e bi sey taim don go wel-wel and di joni don hard laik dis, bikos di taim wey dem dey fast don pas, Pol kon advise dem sey,
44027010	"My pipol, I dey si sey dis joni na wit wahala e go tak end and nor bi onli di load and di ship go loss, bot meni pipol go die tu."
44027011	Bot di komanda nor listin to am and na wetin di kaptain and di ship owna tok, naim e biliv.
44027012	Bikos di place wer ship dey park put wen dem si, nor gud for kold weda; som of di pipol kon gri sey mak wi dey go. Dem dey hope sey wi go fit rish Finix, wey dey Krete, wey face soutwest and nortwest, so dat wi go fit spend kold season for der.
44027013	Wen won kaind kwayet briz blow kom from sout, dem tink sey dem go fit du wetin dem plan, so dem kon dey go smol-smol pas Krete wotasaid.
44027014	Afta di kold briz, won strong briz wey dem dey kol, "Hurricane", kon dey blow kom from di Island.
44027015	Wen dis briz trap di ship and wi nor fit si wel-wel again, wi liv di ship giv di briz and e kon dey kari us go wer e laik.
44027016	As wi dey run go hide unda won smol island wey dem dey kol Kauda, nor bi smol wahala, bifor wi fit kontrol di ship.
44027017	Afta dem don drag di ship komot from di wota, dem kon tak rope tie am. Wi dey fear sey wi go run aroun for Syrtis, so wi hook di ship for groun kon liv di briz mak e kari us go.
44027018	Di next day, bikos di briz wori us wel-wel, wi kon dey trow awa load put for wota
44027019	and wen di ted day rish, dem yuz dia hand trow wetin dem tak dey kontrol di ship put for wota.
44027020	Wen wi nor si sun or star for meni days and di briz stil dey wori us, wi kon luz hope sey wi don die bi dat.
44027021	Afta dem don stay witout fud for meni days, Pol stand for dia front kon sey, "My pipol, if to sey una listin to mi wen I sey mak wi nor komot for Krete, wi for nor si all dis wahala.
44027022	"Naw, I won mak una heart strong, bikos nobodi go die among us, bot na onli di ship go skata.
44027023	"Bikos yestiday nite, God wey I dey serv, en angel apier to mi
44027024	kon sey, 'Mak yu nor fear Pol! Yu must face Caesar and God go save yu and evribodi wey dey folo yu travol.'
44027025	"So, my pipol, mak una heart strong, bikos I biliv sey na as God tel mi, na so e go bi.
44027026	"Bot wi go sureli rish land."
44027027	Afta fortin days, as di briz dey kari us pas di Adriatic Sea for midnite, di sailors kon dey suspet sey wi don dey near land.
44027028	Dem trow long rope wey dem tie somtin put insaid di wota to measure haw e deep rish and dem si sey di wota stil deep rish 40 metres. Afta e don tey smol, dem trow am again kon si sey e don bi 30 metres.
44027029	Dem dey fear sey di ship go jam rock for di land, so dem trow for big-big chain from di ship bak kon dey pray mak day kwik break.
44027030	Den di sailor trai to run liv di ship, dem tak di smol boat for di ship, put am for wota kon dey play wayo sey dem won go put big chain dan for di ship front,
44027031	bot Pol tel di ofisa and sojas, "Unles all dis men stay insaid di ship, all of us go die."
44027032	So di sojas kon kut di rope for di boat mak e float go.
44027033	As day won break, Pol enkorage dem mak dem chop kon sey, "Today mak am fortin days wey una dey wori, sotey una nor gri chop.
44027034	"So naw, I dey beg una to chop, bikos una nid am to sovaiv. And nobodi among una go luz ivun won hair for en head."
44027035	Wen Pol tok finish, e tak bread kon tank God for dia front mak all of dem si and e start to chop.
44027036	All of dem get strong heart kon tak fud chop.
44027037	(Wi bi 276 wey dey insaid di ship.)
44027038	Wen dem don chop beleful, dem kon trowey all di rimainin bread insaid di wota mak di ship nor for heavi again.
44027039	Wen day break, dem nor no wer dem dey, bot dem si won smol land wey near di sea and dem tok for dia maind sey, if e dey posibol dem go yuz di ship tak enta.
44027040	So dem kut all di chains wey hol di ship kon let dem fal insaid di sea. Dem stil luz di wons wey dey hol wetin dey kontrol di ship. Dem let briz blow di ship go front and wi kon move face land.
44027041	Bot dem mit san-san for di sea. So di ship front kon hook and e nor fit move again, di bak skata, bikos of di way di wave dey blow am.
44027042	Di sojas kon plan to kil all di prizinas mak dem nor for fit swim kon eskape.
44027043	Bot bikos di soja ofisa won save Pol life, e nor kon let dem du wetin dem plan. E komand di pipol wey fit swim, mak dem first jump komot from di ship swim go land
44027044	and di res pipol kon folo for bak, som hol di wud and odas hol di ship bodi wey break. Na so all of dem tak rish land and nobodi die.
44028001	Afta wi don rish land and nobodi die, wi kon hear sey, na Malta dem dey kol di island.
44028002	Di pipol wey dey stay for der trit us wel. Dem mak fire for us, bikos rain don start to dey fal and kold dey kash us.
44028003	Wen Pol dey gada plenti stick mak e put insaid di fire, won snake wey dem dey kol, "Viper", kom out bikos of di heat kon put e mout for Pol hand.
44028004	Wen di pipol wey dey stay der si sey di snake put e mout for Pol hand, dem kon dey tel demsef, "E bi laik sey dis man hand nor klin! Ivun doh e nor die insaid sea, hand don stil tosh am for here!"
44028005	Bot Pol shake di snake komot from en hand enta di fire and nor-tin du-am at-all.
44028006	Bot dem dey tink sey en bodi go swel-up or e go fal for groun die. So afta dem don wait for somtaim kon si sey nor-tin hapun to am, dem kon shange maind sey, “Pol na god. ’’
44028007	Dat taim for dat aria, Publius, wey bi di oga, get som land. E welkom us kon giv us fud for tiri days.
44028008	Publius papa kon get fiva and en bele dey pain am. Pol go si-am kon heal am.
44028009	Afta dis don hapun, meni pipol wey nor wel for der kon stil kom and e heal dem.
44028010	Dem kon dey praiz us wel-wel and wen wi won go, dem giv us evritin wey wi nid.
44028011	Afta wi don dey der for tiri monts, wi kon enta ship from Alexandria wey stop for di island for kold taim and sign wey dey di ship front, na "Twins god".
44028012	Wi stop for Syracuse kon stay der for tiri days.
44028013	From der wi kon rish Regium and afta won day, won kaind briz from sout kon start to dey blow and di sekon day, wi kon rish Puteoli.
44028014	For der, wi si som brodas and dem kon beg us to stay wit dem for sevun days. Na so wi tak rish Rome.
44028015	Wen di brodas for Rome hear abaut us, dem waka ontil dem rish "Appius Forum" and di "Tiri Taverns" kom mit us. Wen Pol si dem, e tank God and di tin kon mak en heart strong wel-wel.
44028016	Wen e enta Rome, dem alow Pol stay e own haus wit di sojas wey dey gaid am.
44028017	Afta tiri days, Pol kol all di Ju pipol oga dem togeda. Wen dem don gada, e kon tel dem, "My pipol, ivun doh I nor du enitin against awa pipol or awa gran-gran papa dem tradishon, from Jerusalem naim dem turn mi to prizina kon kari mi giv Rome pipol.
44028018	"Wen dem don kweshon mi, dem won riliz mi, bikos dem nor si enitin wey go mak dem kil mi.
44028019	"Bot wen di Ju pipol nor gri mak dem fri mi, di tin kon mak mi sey, I won go Rome mak Caesar for joj my kase, nor bi bikos I get enitin wey I dey komplain against my pipol.
44028020	"Bikos of dis, I kon sey I won si and folo una tok first sey, na bikos of di hope wey Izrel get, naim mak dem yuz dis chain tie my hand so."
44028021	Di pipol ansa, "Dem nor send us eni leta abaut yu from Judea and no won for awa brodas don kom from der kon sey yu dey du bad tins.
44028022	"Bot wi go laik to hear wetin yu dey tish from yor own mout, bikos wi no sey evribodi for di hol wold dey tak mout kondem dis grup wey yu dey insaid."
44028023	Dem kon gri for di day wen dem go mit am and dem plenti wey kom en haus kon mit am. So, from mornin til evenin, Pol kon dey explain tins giv dem. E dey tok abaut God kindom and dey trai to show dem wetin Mosis law and di profets tok abaut Jisos Kraist.
44028024	Som of dem biliv wetin e tok, bot som nor biliv.
44028025	So dem kon go, bot dem nor gri among demsef afta Pol sey, "Di wod wey di Holi Spirit tok tru di Profet Isaia na tru
44028026	sey, 'Una go mit and tel dis pipol sey, "Una go dey hear, bot una nor go undastand, una go dey luk, bot una nor go fit si.
44028027	'Una heart nor dey undastand, una ear nor dey hear wel again. Devol don klose una eye, mak una nor for fit si; hear wit una ears or undastand wit una heart, so dat una nor go fit turn kom mit God, mak E for heal una.'
44028028	"So mak una no sey, dis salvashon wey God bring, dem don kari am go mit Gentai pipol, bikos dem go asept am!"
44028029	Wen e tok finish, di Ju pipol kon liv der dey ves among demsef.
44028030	So for tu ful years, Pol stay der for en own haus wey e rent and e welkom all di pipol wey kom mit am
44028031	kon dey tel dem abaut God Kindom. E tish dem wit strong heart abaut Oga Jisos Kraist and nobodi fit stop am.
45001001	Pol wey bi Jisos savant and apostol wey e shuz mak e prish God wod, na en rite dis leta.
45001002	Na dis gospol God promis us for en Holi Book tru en profets sey,
45001003	my Pikin kom dis wold from David famili
45001004	and naim bi my onli Pikin wey I wak-up from deat wit di Holi Spirit pawa.
45001005	Na tru am, God giv us favor and pawa to bi apostols and na dis pawa wi dey yuz tak dey kol Gentai pipol, mak dem obey and biliv en name.
45001006	Unasef dey among di pipol wey God kol to bi Jisos Kraist own.
45001007	Rome pipol wey God luv and kol mak dem bi en own, na una I dey rite dis leta giv. Mak God awa Papa for hevun and Jisos awa Oga giv una grace and peace.
45001008	Today, I tank my God tru en pikin Jisos Kraist for all of una, bikos na for di hol wold dem dey tok abaut haw una fate for God strong rish.
45001009	God wey I dey serv and prish en pikin gospol, na-im fit bear mi witnes sey I dey always rimemba una
45001010	and I always dey pray dey ask God if E go let mi kom si una again.
45001011	Bikos I dey hungri to si una, so dat I go giv una di Holi Spirit blessin wey go mak una strong,
45001012	so dat mi and una go dey hapi and Jisos Kraist wey wi biliv, go giv us res for awa maind.
45001013	My brodas and sistas, I wont mak una no sey I don plan to kom visit una meni taims, bot God nor let mi kom ontil naw. Bikos I won gain from una fate as I don du wit Gentai pipol.
45001014	Bikos God sey mak I prish to evribodi, weda na Greek or Gentai pipol or weda dem wise or foolish.
45001015	Na dis mak mi won kom prish God wod giv una wey dey Rome.
45001016	I nor dey shame to prish God wod, bikos na-im bi di pawa wey God tak dey save doz wey biliv am, weda dem bi Ju or Gentai pipol.
45001017	Bikos na di Gospol dey show haw God dey tak mak pipol klin for en eye. From di biginin go rish di end, God sey, "Na onli fate go mak pesin dey klin for my eye."
45001018	Bikos of all di sins and bad tins wey wiked pipol dey du, God vesnashon dey show from hevun and di sins dey kova di trut.
45001019	So God kon ponish dem, since dem no evritin wey dem sopoz to no abaut God, bikos na-im show dem.
45001020	From di taim wen God kreate di wold, E don show us di tins wey odinari eye nor dey fit si; en pawa and life, tru di tins wey E kreate. So wiked pipol nor get eskuze at-all.
45001021	Ivun doh dem no sey God dey, dem nor dey gri gi-am glori as God. Dem nor dey tank am for all di tins wey E dey du. Insted, na nonsense tins dem dey du and dia wiked maind nor fit undastand di trut again.
45001022	Ivun doh dem tink sey dem wise, dem bi fools;
45001023	bikos insted mak dem woship God wey dey hevun, dem kon dey woship image wey dem mold or karve laik pesin, bird, anima or snake.
45001024	So God don liv wiked pipol mak dem dey du di bad tins wey dia maind, wey bi sey man dey slip wit man and wuman dey slip wit wuman.
45001025	Dem don turn di trut abaut God to lai. Dem dey woship di tins wey E kreate, insted for dem to serv God wey deserv all di praiz foreva! Amen.
45001026	Bikos of dis, God liv dem for dia yeye life. Ivun di wimen shange and dem kon dey du tins wey nor gud.
45001027	And na so tu, men nor kon laik wimen again, bot dem kon dey laik to slip wit oda men. So, God kon ponish dem bikos of wetin dem dey du.
45001028	Since dem nor gri put God for maind and serv am, E kon liv dem mak dem yuz dia bad maind dey du tins wey dem nor sopoz du.~
45001029	Wetin ful dia maind na wikednes, evil tins, long-trot, bad bele, bad-bad tins; jelosi, to kil and fite, to lai, to kip enemi wit pipol, to joj pipol waka,
45001030	to tok bad abaut odas and hate God. Dem dey kari bodi up, dem nor get respet and na bad tins ful dia maind. Dem nor dey respet dia papa and mama.
45001031	Dem nor get sense, dem dey promis and fail, dem nor dey du gud or sori for pipol.
45001032	Aldoh dem no sey God law sey, pipol wey dey liv laik dat go die, yet dem nor onli dey du dis tins, bot dem ivun dey sopot pipol wey du-am.
45002001	Pesin wey dey joj odas nor get eskuze for wetin e dey du and e nor mata hu e bi. Bikos wen yu joj odas and yu dey du di same tin wey dem dey du, yu dey kondem yorsef.
45002002	Wi no sey God nor dey lai wen E dey joj pipol wey dey du bad tins.
45002003	Yu wey dey du tins wey yu sey mak odas nor du! Yu tink sey yu go eskape God jojment?.
45002004	May bi una dey tak God kindnes, patient and endurance as yeye tins. Una nor no sey God dey kaind, bikos E wont mak una turn from sin kom mit am?
45002005	Bot una stubornes and strong heart nor let una turn from sin kom mit God, so una dey mak una ponishment meni more-more, for di Day wen God go joj di wold, bikos en na joj wey nor dey sopot bad tins.
45002006	God go pay evri man akordin to wetin e du.
45002007	God go giv life wey nor dey end to di pipol wey dey du gud, wey wont glori, onor and long life.
45002008	Bot E go show en vesnashon and ponish doz wey bikos of long-trot rejet di trut kon dey du bad tins.
45002009	Enibodi wey dey du bad tin, weda e bi Ju or Gentai, must sofa and risiv ponishment.
45002010	Bot God go giv glori, onor and peace to enibodi wey dey du gud, weda e bi Ju or Gentai,
45002011	bikos God go joj evribodi di same way.
45002012	Ivun doh Gentai pipol nor get Mosis law, God stil dey ponish dem wen dem sin, so Ju pipol wey get di law, wen dem sin, na di law go joj dem.
45002013	Bikos yu dey hear di law nor min sey yu gud for God eye, bot na wen yu du wetin di law tok.
45002014	Gentai pipol nor get di law, bot dem dey yuz dia sense du wetin di law tok and dat won don turn law for dem, ivun doh dem nor no Mosis law.
45002015	Di way dem dey bihav show sey wetin Mosis rite for di law, dey dia heart and dia maind dey tel dem sey, "Dis tins dey rite and e go kondem or fri us from wetin wi du."
45002016	So jos as I prish giv una, na so e go bi for dat day, wen God go joj all di sikrit tins wey dey pipol heart tru Jisos Kraist wey bi en pikin.
45002017	Wot of yu wey sey yu bi Ju? Yu wey put yor hope for di law kon dey yuz God dey boast;
45002018	yu no wetin God wont mak yu du and yu don learn haw to du gud tins, bikos yu no di law.
45002019	Yu dey show blind pipol road and dey help doz wey dey for daknes si lite,
45002020	and yu dey tish foolish pipol and smol shildren wey nor no enitin, bikos yu no sey, di trut and evritin wey man nid to no, dey for di law.
45002021	Why e bi sey yu wey dey tish odas nor fit tish yorsef? Yu wey dey prish sey mak pipol nor tif, yu sure sey yu nor dey tif?
45002022	Yu wey sey mak pipol nor komit adultri, yu nor dey komit adultri? Yu wey sey yu hate juju, yu nor dey tak tins wey dem kip for juju haus?
45002023	Yu wey dey tak di law boast, yu dey bring shame to God name, bikos yu dey disobey di law!
45002024	Jos as God wod sey, "Bikos of una wey bi Ju pipol, Gentai pipol kon dey tak God name mak yeye."
45002025	Sekonsishon get value onli if yu dey du wetin di law tok, bot if yu nor dey obey di law, yu and di pesin wey dem neva sekonsaiz na di same.
45002026	So if Gentai pipol wey dem nor sekonsaiz dey obey evritin for di law, yu nor tink sey God go tak dem as pipol wey dem sekonsaiz?
45002027	Yu nor no sey di pesin wey dem nor sekonsaiz go joj yu wey bi Ju, since yu dey break di law?
45002028	Pesin nor bi Ju bikos of wetin pipol si from outsaid. Di ril sekonsishon nor bi wetin pipol dey si,
45002029	bot di ril Ju na pesin wey bi Ju for insaid en heart, bikos sekonsishon nor dey tosh pesin heart. Na di Holi Spirit dey du dis kaind wok, nor bi di law wey dem rite dan and dat pesin go dey risiv praiz from God, ivun doh humanbin nor praiz am.
45003001	Haw Ju pipol tak beta pas Gentai pipol sef? Or beta tin dey bikos dem sekonsaiz pesin?
45003002	E rili dey gud to sekonsaiz pesin! And wi no sey na Ju pipol God first giv en mesage.
45003003	Bot wot if som of dem nor gri biliv? Dat min sey God dey lai?
45003004	Ivun doh evri humanbin dey lai, God nor fit lai. God wod sey: "Mak yu dey tok wetin bi trut; so dat yu go fit win yor kase wen dem dey joj yu."
45003005	If God nor ponish us for di bad tins wey wi dey du, e min sey God dey sopot us? No! So if God ponish us, wi go sey E dey wiked? (Na so som pipol dey tok).
45003006	Wi nor fit tok so at-all! If God nor dey rite, na haw E go kon tak joj di wold?
