45003007	If my lai-lai life dey show sey God wod na trut, wetin go mak am kondem mi sey I bi sina?
45003008	Den e go dey rite if wi sey, "Mak wi dey du bad tins so dat gud tins go kom out from wetin wi dey du?" Bot som pipol dey lai for my head, bikos of wetin I tok and God go ponish dem.
45003009	So wetin wi go tok? Wi go sey na wi wey bi Ju beta pas? Dat na lai! Bikos as I don alredi show una, Ju and Gentai pipol dey komit sin.
45003010	Jos as God wod sey, "Nobodi dey raitious.
45003011	"Nobodi dey wey wise or undastand God.
45003012	"Evribodi don turn liv God, all of dem don bi yeye for God eye. Nobodi dey du wetin gud at-all.
45003013	"Na lai wey fit kil pesin ful dia mout and wiked wods ful dia tongue.
45003014	"Bad bele dey dia maind and na so-so swear dem dey swear.
45003015	"Dem go fit kwik kil pesin.
45003016	"Eniwer dem go, dem must fite skata di place
45003017	and dem nor no haw to dey kwayet.
45003018	"Dem nor dey fear God at-all."
45003019	Wi no sey wetin di law tok, na for di pipol wey dey unda di law. Di law tok laik dis, so dat nobodi go get eskuze wen God go joj di wold.
45003020	Nobodi dey gud for God eye, bikos e dey obey di law. Bot na tru di law, wi tak no wetin sin min.
45003021	Naw, God don show us haw wi go tak dey gud for en eye and nor bi tru di law, ivun doh na so Mosis law and di profets tok.
45003022	Na di fate wey pesin get for Jisos Kraist go mak am dey gud for God eye. Enibodi wey biliv Jisos, God dey mak en fate strong, weda e bi Ju or Gentai pesin.
45003023	Evribodi don sin and wi don fal komot from God glori,
45003024	bot God don mak us dey rite wit am tru en fri gift wey E giv us, bikos of Jisos Kraist wey save us.
45003025	Na God giv us Jisos Kraist, so dat tru en blood, E go forgiv us awa sins wen wi biliv Kraist. God du dis to show sey bifor-bifor, E dey patient to forgiv pipol dia sins.
45003026	Dis stil show sey God dey rite wen E asept pipol wey biliv Jisos Kraist. E dey ponish sinas, so dat wi go no sey en na God wey nor laik sin. Laik dis, God show sey en dey rite and enibodi wey biliv Jisos Kraist, E dey mak dem dey rite tu.
45003027	So, wetin mak us dey boast? Wi nor fit boast at-all! Why e bi laik dis? Na bikos wi dey obey di law? No! Na bikos wi biliv Jisos Kraist.
45003028	So, na tru fate pesin go dey rite wit God, nor bi as e obey di law rish.
45003029	Abi na onli Ju pipol God dey dia side? E nor dey Gentai pipol side tu? Tru-tru, God dey Gentai pipol side.
45003030	Since na onli won God dey, E dey for Ju and Gentai pipol, bikos of dia fate.
45003031	So mak wi trowey di law bikos of fate? No way! E nor go wok! Insted, wi go mak di law strong wel-wel.
45004001	Na wetin Abraham awa gran papa learn from dis mata?
45004002	If na di gud tins wey e du mak am dey gud for God eye, den e sopoz to dey boast for pipol, bot e nor go eva fit boast for God.
45004003	Wetin dem rite for God wod? "Abraham biliv God tru fate and God kon si-am as raitious pesin."
45004004	Wen pesin wok, dem must pay am en moni, nor bi dash e bi, bot na moni wey e wok for.
45004005	Doz wey nor depend on wetin dem dey du, bot dem get fate and biliv sey God dey forgiv sinas, na dis fate God dey yuz tak forgiv dem dia sins.
45004006	David tok di same tin wen e tok abaut di blessin wey pesin dey get wen God don asept am, ivun doh dem nor deserv dat kaind blessin. David stil sey,
45004007	"God don bless pipol wey E forgiv kon tak dia sins komot.
45004008	"God don bless di pesin wey E don forgiv en sins!"
45004009	Dis blessin wey David dey tok abaut so, na onli Ju pipol e tok am for, bikos dem sekonsaiz dem? No! Na stil for Gentai pipol wey dem nor sekonsaiz. Bikos wi read for God wod sey, "Abraham biliv God and bikos of en fate, God kon asept am as raitious pesin."
45004010	Na wen all dis tins tak hapun? Na bifor dem sekonsaiz Abraham or afta dem sekonsaiz am? Na bifor, nor bi afta dem sekonsaiz am!
45004011	Bot lata, dem kon sekonsaiz am. Dis sign show sey, bikos of en fate, God don si-am as raitious pesin, so dat e go bi papa to evribodi wey biliv God, pipol wey God don asept, ivun doh dem neva sekonsaiz.
45004012	Doz wey don sekonsaiz, na Abraham bi dia papa and dia fate bi laik en own, afta dem sekonsaiz am.
45004013	Wen God promis Abraham and en shildren sey dem go inherit di hol wold, E du-am, nor bi bikos Abraham dey obey di law, bot bikos e biliv God and God si-am as raitious pesin.
45004014	If God promis na for onli doz wey dey obey di law, den fate nor min enitin and God promis go dey yuzles.
45004015	Di law dey bring God vesnashon, bikos wer sin nor dey, law nor go dey.
45004016	Na dis won mak God promis dey kom by fate and wi dey get-am tru favor. Nor bi onli pipol wey dey obey di law bi Abraham shildren, bot pipol wey biliv God laik Abraham, na en shildren dem bi tu, bikos na Abraham bi awa spiritual papa.
45004017	God wod sey, "I don mak yu papa for meni nashons." So for God eye, Abraham na awa papa, bikos e get fate for God wey get pawa to raiz pipol wey don die and to komand tins wey nor dey bifor, laik sey dem dey.
45004018	Ivun wen tins hard, Abraham stil biliv God and e hope sey God go du-am, ivun wen e bi laik sey, nor-tin go hapun. Bot naw, e don bikom, "Papa for meni nashons." Jos as God tel am, "Yor shildren go meni laik di stars wey dey hevun."
45004019	Abraham nor komplain for won day, ivun wen e don old nearli rish ondred years. Ivun doh E no sey en bodi don nearli die and en wife Sarah nor go fit born again,
45004020	e nor doubt God promis. En fate mak am strong and e tank God for evritin.
45004021	E dey sure sey God go du wetin E promis.
45004022	Na dis mak God kol am raitious pesin.
45004023	Ivun doh God kol am 'Raitious pesin', E tok dis wod bikos of onli Abraham?
45004024	No! E tok am for wi tu wey God go stil asept as raitious pipol; wi wey biliv sey God raiz Jisos Kraist from deat.
45004025	Na awa sins mak God giv Jisos Kraist to dem mak dem kil-am and God raiz-am from deat, so dat e go mak us raitious pipol.
45005001	Since fate don mak us dey gud for God eye, wi don get peace tru awa Oga Jisos Kraist.
45005002	Na fate e tak buy us so dat wi go enta God grace, di place wer wi dey naw. So wi fit boast wit God glori wey wi dey enjoy.
45005003	Wi stil dey hapi insaid di wahala wey wi dey face, bikos wi no sey trobol go mak us endure,
45005004	and endurance dey bring gud karata, wey go mak us get hope.
45005005	Dis hope nor dey disappoint pesin at-all, bikos God pour en luv laik riva wey dey flow insaid awa heart, tru di Holi Spirit wey E giv us.
45005006	For di taim wen wi nor fit help awasef, Kraist kon die for us wey bi sinas.
45005007	Nobodi go won die for anoda pesin wey dey gud for God eye, aldoh sombodi go fit die for pesin wey gud wel-wel.
45005008	Bot God show haw en luv for us big rish, wen E send Kraist kom die for us, ivun doh wi stil dey sin.
45005009	Naw, wi dey rite bikos of Kraist blood and na dis blood go save us from God vesnashon.
45005010	Wi bi God enimis bifor, bot E don mak us en frends tru en Pikin deat. Naw, since wi don bi God frends, E go save us tru di life wey en pikin get.
45005011	Nor bi onli dis won mak us dey hapi, bot wi stil dey hapi bikos of wetin God don du tru awa Oga Jisos Kraist wey mak us bi God frends.
45005012	Na tru won man sin enta dis wold and deat kom tru sin. So wi must die, bikos evribodi don sin.
45005013	Sin dey di wold bifor di law kom, bot if law nor dey, wi nor go fit joj pipol sin.
45005014	From Adam kon rish Mosis taim, na deat dey rule for dis wold, ivun doh nor bi evribodi disobey God komand laik Adam. Dis Adam bi laik Kraist wey kom leta.
45005015	Bot tu of dem nor bi di same, bikos God fri gift nor bi laik Adam sin. Na tru sey meni pipol die, bikos of won man sin. Bot God grace big wel-wel and e dey giv fri gift to pipol tru en pikin Jisos Kraist!
45005016	God gift and won man sin nor bi di same. Jojment folo di won man sin kon kondem evribodi, bot na God gift dey fri us, ivun doh wi bi sinas.
45005017	Bot if na bikos of won man sin deat kil evribodi, naim bi sey, doz wey don get favor and Kraist gift, dey gud for God eye and dem go enjoy life tru Jisos Kraist!
45005018	God go ponish evribodi bikos of Adam sin. Bot bikos of di gud tins wey Jisos du, God don asept and giv us di gift wey dey giv life.
45005019	Bikos Adam nor obey God, meni pipol bigin sin. Bot since Jisos obey God, meni pipol go obey God tu.
45005020	Di law kom so dat sin go inkrease, bot wer sin get pawa, God grace strong pas am
45005021	and as sin dey kontrol us tru deat, na so God grace dey rule tru raitiousnes wey dey bring life wey nor dey end, bikos of Jisos Kraist wey bi awa Oga.
45006001	So wetin wi go tok? Mak wi kontinu to dey sin so dat God grace go dey wit us?
45006002	No! Why wi wey don turn from sin go stil dey liv insaid am?
45006003	Abi una nor no sey all di pipol wey dem baptaiz insaid Kraist don die wit am?
45006004	Dem bere us wit am wen wi baptaiz, so as God raiz Kraist from deat tru en pawa wit glori, na so wi tu go get life wey nor dey end.
45006005	Bikos if wi don die wit Jisos Kraist tru baptism, God go raiz us up wit am.
45006006	Wi no sey di pesin wey wi bi bifor, dem don nail am for kros wit Jisos. So awa bodi nor bi sin savant again.
45006007	Bikos pesin wey don die, don fri from sin.
45006008	As wi die wit Kraist, wi biliv sey wi go liv wit am.
45006009	Wi no sey since God don raiz Kraist up, e nor go die and deat nor get pawa for en bodi again.
45006010	Bikos as e die, e don ovakom sin foreva, so di life wey e dey liv naw, e dey liv am for God.
45006011	So mak una no sey, una don ovakom sin tu and una get life tru Jisos Kraist.
45006012	Derfor, mak una nor alow sin kontrol una bodi again, so dat una nor go dey du bad tins.
45006013	Mak una nor let Satan yuz una bodi tak du bad tins, bot mak una kari unasef giv God as pipol wey don wak-up from deat, so dat una go dey du gud tins.
45006014	Sin nor go fit kontrol una, bikos una nor dey unda di law again, bot na God grace dey kontrol una naw.
45006015	So na wetin wi go tok? Mak wi stil dey sin, bikos wi get God grace and wi nor dey unda di law again? God forbid!
45006016	Yu nor no sey wetin yu giv yor bodi to, na-im go kontrol yu? If na sin, e go kause deat, bot if na God, E go mak yu dey liv raitious life.
45006017	Bot wi tank God sey, ivun doh una bi slave to sin bifor, una don yuz una heart dey obey all di tins wey wi dey tish una.
45006018	And as e bi sey una don fri from sin, una don bikom slave to gud tins.
45006019	(I dey tok wit humanbin sense, bikos I no sey una dey wik.) Bifor, una dey giv una bodi laik slave to bad tins, bot naw, una must yuz una ful bodi tak serv God, so dat una go dey du onli wetin God wont.
45006020	Bikos wen una bi sin savant, una nor nid to dey raitious.
45006021	So wetin una gain from all doz bad tins wey una du? Na shame and deat doz tins dey bring.
45006022	Bot naw, una don dey fri from sin kon bi God savant. Dis go mak una dey holi and God go giv una life wey nor dey end.
45006023	Bikos, di riwod for sin, na deat, bot God gift wey Jisos Kraist dey giv us, na life wey nor dey end.
45007001	My brodas and sistas, I no sey I dey tok to pipol wey no di law. Na onli wen pesin stil dey for life, naim di law dey get pawa for en bodi.
45007002	As di law tok, wuman wey don mari dey unda en husban as long as di man dey alaif. Bot if di man die, di wuman don fri.
45007003	So if wuman mari anoda man wen en husban stil dey alaif, e min sey e don komit adultri. Bot if en husban die, e don fri from wetin di law tok and e go fit mari anoda man again.
45007004	So my brodas and sistas, na so e bi wit una tu. Una don bikom part for Jisos Kraist bodi and una don die to di law pawa. Naw, una dey fri to bi Kraist own; di pesin wey God raiz from deat mak una for dey serv am.
45007005	Wen wi stil dey di wold, di law dey mak us du bad tins wey awa bodi wont and all dis tins dey bring deat.
45007006	Bot naw, wi don fri from di law. Wi bi laik deat bodi and di law nor get pawa for awa bodi again. Naw wi sopoz to serv God wit di new life wey di Spirit dey giv, nor bi di old life, wey bi to obey di law wey pesin rite.
45007007	Dis min sey di law nor gud? No! Bot na di law mak mi no wetin sin bi. If to sey di law nor sey, "Nor get long-trot for anoda man tin," I nor for no sey I nor sopoz to du dat kaind tin.
45007008	Bot bikos of di law, di sin pawa wey dey insaid mi kon dey mak mi tink abaut tins wey nor gud and if law nor dey, sin nor for get pawa for my life.
45007009	Bifor I no di law, I dey alaif, bot wen I hear God komandment, sin jos enta my life
45007010	and I kon die. So di law wey sopoz giv mi life, don kil mi!
45007011	Since sin pawa yuz di law disiv mi, I kon die.
45007012	Bot di law dey holi, rite and gud.
45007013	So dis min sey na wetin gud kil mi? No! Bot na sin pawa wey dey insaid mi, na-im kil mi; bikos e yuz wetin gud bring deat and naw, wi dey si haw sin bad and wiked rish.
45007014	Wi no sey di law dey spiritual. Bot I bi humanbin and dem don sel mi giv sin.
45007015	I nor undastand wetin I dey du; bikos I nor dey du wetin I won rili du. Insted na wetin I nor laik, I dey du.
45007016	Since I dey du wetin I hate to du, e show sey di law dey koret.
45007017	Nor bi mi rili dey du wetin I dey du, bot na di sin pawa wey dey insaid mi.
45007018	I no sey wetin dey insaid mi nor go let mi du gud. Ivun wen I won du gud, I nor dey fit.
45007019	Insted of mak I du wetin dey gud, na bad tins I dey du.
45007020	So if I du wetin I nor won du, e show sey nor bi mi dey du-am again, bot na di sin pawa wey dey insaid mi.
45007021	So I si sey dis law dey wok, bikos wen I won du gud, na onli bad tins dey enta my maind.
45007022	I dey laik to obey God law wit my hol maind,
45007023	bot insaid mi, I kon undastand sey somtin dey fite against my maind and e dey mak mi bi sin savant, bikos e dey kontrol my bodi.
45007024	I nor dey hapi at-all! Hu go save mi from dis bodi wey dey push mi go die?
45007025	Tank God! Jisos Kraist don save mi. So, I go obey God law wit my maind, ivun doh sin pawa stil dey insaid mi.
45008001	So, God nor go kondem pipol wey biliv Jisos Kraist.
45008002	Since di Holi Spirit don giv una life wey kom from Jisos Kraist, e go fri una from sin and deat.
45008003	Mosis law nor fit du dis tins, bikos di yeye life wey wi dey liv don mak di law wik. Bot God don fri us wen E send en pikin kom laik humanbin wey bi sina, mak e for sakrifais ensef for awa sins.
45008004	God du so, so dat wetin di law tok, go hapun wen wi obey di Spirit, insted of awa own maind.
45008005	Bikos pipol wey dey liv by dia own maind, dey tink of onli demsef. Bot evribodi wey di Holi Spirit dey rule, dey tink of tins wey di Spirit wont.
45008006	If wi let sin rule awa maind, wi go die. Bot if na di Spirit dey rule us, wi go get life and peace.
45008007	Pipol wey dey sin, na God enemi dem bi, bikos dem nor obey en law, since dem nor fit obey am.
45008008	Doz wey dey obey sin, nor go fit mak God hapi.
45008009	Bot una nor dey obey sin, insted, na as di Spirit sey mak una liv, na so una dey liv.
45008010	Kraist dey liv insaid una. So una dey alaif, bikos God don asept una, ivun doh una bodi must die, bikos of una sins.
45008011	If God Spirit wey raiz Jisos Kraist from deat dey insaid una, den en wey raiz Kraist from deat, go giv una bodi life, bikos of en Spirit wey dey insaid una.
45008012	So my brodas and sistas, wi get wok to du for God, so mak wi nor liv as awa bodi wont.
45008013	Bikos if una dey folo sin, una go die. Bot di Spirit pawa go kil all di bad tins wey una dey du, so dat una go get life.
45008014	Na doz wey God Spirit dey lid, bi God shildren.
45008015	Di Spirit wey God giv us nor go mak us fear laik slave, insted, wi bi God shildren and wi dey kol am, "Awa Papa!"
45008016	Na God Spirit mak us no sey wi bi God shildren.
45008017	And if wi bi God shildren, den wi go inherit God propati. Yes, wi go folo Kraist inherit God propati, bikos if rili wi sofa wit am, wi go folo am enjoy.
45008018	I dey sure sey, wi nor go fit kompare all di sofa wey wi dey sofa naw, wit di glori wey God go giv us.
45008019	Evritin wey God kreate for dis wold, dey wait for God to show en shildren to di wold.
45008020	Bikos of sin, di wold dey sofa from God kos naw and nor bi bikos dem wont am laik dat. Bot di wold dey hope
45008021	sey won day, God go fri dem from deat and wahala and dem go-go join en shildren wey E don save.
45008022	Wi no sey evritin wey God kreate, dey krai, jos laik di way wuman wey won born dey krai.
45008023	Di Holi Spirit don mak us dey sure of haw tumoro go bi. Bot naw, wi dey strogol as wi dey wait mak God show sey wi bi en shildren, den E go kon save us.
45008024	Na dis hope save us. Bot if wi don alredi get wetin wi dey hope for, den wi nor nid to dey hope again. Abi hu dey hope for wetin e don alredi get?
45008025	Bot if wi put hope for wetin wi nor fit si, wi go tak all awa maind wait for am wit patient.
45008026	Na so tu di Holi Spirit dey help us bikos wi dey wik. Bikos wi nor no wetin wi sopoz to pray for, di Spirit by ensef dey krai beg God, for di way awa wod nor go fit esplain.
45008027	And God wey dey si evritin insaid awa bele, no wetin dey di Spirit maind, bikos di Spirit dey pray for all God pipol, as God wont.
45008028	And wi no sey evritin dey wok for awa gud, bikos wi luv God and dey du wetin E wont.
45008029	God no doz wey E don shuz, so E don mak dem bi laik en Pikin, so dat en pikin go bi di first born.
45008030	Doz wey God don asept, na dem E kol; doz wey E kol, na dem E mak raitious and E kon share en glori wit dem.
45008031	Wetin wi go tok abaut all dis tins? If God dey for awa side, hu go fit dey against us?
45008032	Tru-tru, if E let dem kil en own pikin for awa sins, den E go fit giv us evritin wey wi ask from am fri of charge!
45008033	Hu go fit akiuz pesin wey God don shuz? Na God no hu gud or bad.
45008034	Hu bi di pesin wey go kondem us? Na Jisos Kraist wey die for us; di pesin wey God raiz from deat and naw, e dey for God rite hand side dey pray for us.
45008035	Na hu go fit seprate us from Kraist luv? Na trobol or opreshon; hunga or poverti; wahala or deat; or na bikos klot nor dey to wear?
45008036	As dem rite am, "Bikos of una, wi dey face deat from mornin go rish nite, wi bi laik ship wey dem won go kil."
45008037	Insaid all dis tins, awa joy don dey ful, bikos Jisos luv us!
45008038	Bot I dey sure sey, weda na deat or life; angels or wiked pawas; tins wey dey naw or di wons wey dey kom;
45008039	tins wey dey hevun; tins for unda dis eart or enitin wey God kreate, non of dem go fit seprate us from God luv, bikos of Jisos Kraist wey bi awa Oga.
45009001	Na di trut I dey tok, na Jisos get mi and di Holi Spirit dey bear witnes for my maind sey, I nor dey lai wen I sey,
45009002	e dey pain mi for maind and sorrow ful my heart,
45009003	bikos I for laik sey God go kos and seprate mi from Kraist, so dat my own flesh and blood,
45009004	wey bi Izrel pipol, go fit asept Kraist. Na dem God shuz as en own shildren, E mak agriment wit dem kon giv dem en law. Na dem get di Tempol and wetin God promis.
45009005	Awa gran-gran papa dem wey folo God waka bifor, na from dem dis pipol from kom. So I dey pray mak dem praiz God wey dey rule evritin foreva and eva! Amen.
45009006	Nor bi sey God promis don fail; bikos nor bi evribodi wey dey Izrel rili bi God pipol.
45009007	And nor bi all Abraham pikin bi God shildren. Insted, God tel Abraham, "Na tru Izik yu go get di shildren wey I promis yu."
45009008	Dis min sey di pikin wey Abraham born (Hagar pikin, Ishmael) bifor God promis am, nor bi di won wey God shuz. Insted, di pikin wey e born tru God promis, na dat won bi Abraham tru pikin.
45009009	Bikos na so God tok for en promis, "Wen di taim don rish, I go kom bak and Sarah go born boy."
45009010	Nor bi onli dat, bikos Rebeka shildren na won papa dem get and naim bi awa gran papa, Izik.
45009011	Ivun bifor dem born di shildren or sey dem du eni bad or gud tin, God tel Rebeka, "Di senior pikin go serv en junior broda, so dat my promis go stand:
45009012	nor bi bikos of wetin dem du, bot na as I wont mak e bi."
45009013	Jos as God wod sey, "I luv Jacob, bot I hate Esau."
45009014	Wetin wi go tok? God dey show parsha? No!
45009015	Bikos E tel Mosis sey, "I go sori for hu I won sori for and I go show mesi to hu I laik show mesi to."
45009016	Derfor, evritin dey for God hand, nor bi by wetin pipol won du.
45009017	God tel Fero for en wod sey, "I mak yu king, so dat I go yuz yu show my pawa and pipol go fear my name for di hol wold.
45009018	So, God dey sori for hu E won sori for and dey ponish hu E won ponish.
45009019	I no sey yu go ask sey, "Wetin mak God dey faind fault for pipol bodi, since na-im mak us dey du as wi dey du?"
45009020	Bot, my frend, I dey ask, "Hu yu tink sey yu bi, wey mak yu dey ask God kweshon? Pot wey dem mold fit ask di pesin wey dey mold am sey, 'Why yu dey mold mi laik dis?'"
45009021	Di man wey mold di pot fit yuz di clay as e laik. E fit yuz di clay mak tu pot, won for big parti and di oda won for haus.
45009022	Bot God won show sey E dey ves, so E kon yuz en pawa against doz wey E won ponish.
45009023	E dey du laik dis to show en glori wen E piti for pipol wey E shuz to show en glori.
45009024	Weda wi bi Ju or Gentai pipol, E don shuz us.
45009025	As E tok for Hosea book sey; "Doz wey nor bi my pipol bifor and di pipol wey nobodi luv bifor, I go kol dem, 'Di pipol wey I luv.'
45009026	"For wer God for tel dem sey, 'Una nor bi my pipol, na der dem go stil kol dem God shildren.'"
45009027	And dis na wetin Isaia tok abaut Izrel pipol, "Izrel shildren meni laik san-san wey dey wotasaid. Bot na few of dem, God go save.
45009028	"Bikos God go kwik du wetin E sey E wont du for dis wold, E go kom joj di wold."
45009029	Jos as Isaia tok bifor sey, "If to sey Almighti God nor save som for awa shildren, wi for don die finish laik Sodom and Gomora."
45009030	Wetin wi go tok? Ivun doh Gentai pipol nor dey raitious bifor, dem don dey raitious naw, bikos of fate.
45009031	And Izrel pipol wey dey trai to du wetin God wont, nor fit du-am.
45009032	Why dem nor fit du-am? Na bikos dem dey trai to du gud laik sey na by wok, nor bi wit fate. Na dis mak dem dey strogol kon dey fal on-top stone.
45009033	God wod sey, "Si, for Zion, I dey arange stones wey go mak pipol fal, yet doz wey biliv am, E nor go disapoint dem.
45010001	My brodas and sistas, I dey wish and pray to God from my heart evriday sey, mak God save dem wey kom from Izrel.
45010002	I no sey dem luv God, bot dem nor undastand am,
45010003	as e bi sey dem nor no haw God dey tak mak pipol gud, insted, dem dey trai to mak demsef gud by dia own pawa, since dem nor gri du wetin God wont.
45010004	Since Jisos Kraist kom, di law nor get pawa again and enibodi wey biliv God, go dey raitious.
45010005	Na dis raitiousnes wey di law tok, naim Mosis rite abaut sey: "Di pesin wey folo di law must du evritin wey di law tok."
45010006	Bot di raitiousnes wey fate dey giv pesin na sey: "Nor tok for yor maind sey, 'Hu go-go hevun go bring Jisos kraist kom dan?
45010007	or Hu go-go bring Kraist kom out from hell wer deat bodi dey?'"
45010008	Bot wetin e tok? "God wod dey near yu. Di wod wey wi dey prish near yu, e get fate and e dey yor mout and heart."
45010009	Bot if yu konfes wit yor mout sey, "Jisos Kraist na Oga and yu biliv for yor heart sey, God raiz-am from grave, yu go dey save."
45010010	If yu biliv and prish wit yor heart giv pipol sey Jisos Kraist na Oga, God go save yu.
45010011	Bikos God wod sey, "Enibodi wey biliv am, nor go shame."
45010012	Ju and Gentai pipol nor dey difren for God eye and E dey bless evribodi wey dey pray to am,
45010013	bikos E go save doz wey dey kol en name.
45010014	Haw dem won tak kol God mak E help dem, wen dem nor biliv am? And haw dem go fit biliv, wen dem neva hear abaut am? Haw dem go tak hear abaut am, if nobodi prish to dem?
45010015	Haw pesin go prish God wod wen God nor send am? As God wod sey, "Pipol wey dey prish di Gud News dey waka wel, bikos na gud tins dem dey bring!"
45010016	Bot nor bi evribodi gri asept di Gud News, ivun profet Isaia sey, "God, enibodi don biliv awa mesage?"
45010017	So, nobodi go fit get fate wen e neva hear di mesage and na tru Kraist wod, wi go fit hear am.
45010018	Bot mak I ask, dem neva hear di mesage bifor? Yes! Dem don hear am, bikos God wod sey, "Dem prish di mesage and dia vois rish evriwer for di wold."
45010019	I dey ask una again, "Izrel pipol nor undastand?" Mosis first tok sey, "I go yuz pipol wey nor bi enitin, so dat una go dey jelos dem. Na pipol wey nor get sense, na dem I go yuz tak mak una ves."
45010020	And profet Isaia ivun get strong heart to tel di pipol sey, "Pipol wey nor luk for mi, na dem si mi. Doz wey nor ask for mi, na dem kon no mi wel-wel."
45010021	Bot Profet Isaia stil tok abaut Izrel pipol sey, "I don dey kol dis my stuborn pipol, bot dem nor dey hear wod."
45011001	I dey ask, God don rejet Izrel, en pipol? No! Mi tu, na Izrel pesin, I bi Abraham pikin wey kom from Benjamin tribe.
45011002	God nor rejet en pipol wey E shuz from di biginin. Dem rite for God wod abaut haw Elija beg God for Izrel pipol sey,
45011003	"Oga, dem don kil all yor profets. Dem don skata yor alta, na onli mi rimain and dem dey trai to kil mi tu!"
45011004	Na wish ansa God gi-am? E tel am, "I stil get sevun tazon men wey neva woship Baal juju at-all."
45011005	Na so e bi naw tu, som Izrel pipol stil dey woship God bikos of en grace.
45011006	If na by grace God shuz dem, dat min sey, nor bi by pesin pawa: bikos if na by pesin pawa, den grace nor min enitin again.
45011007	Dis min sey, na onli few pipol for Izrel fit get wetin all of dem dey faind. Di res nor gri listin to God, bikos of dia stubornes,
45011008	jos as God wod sey, "God mak dem foolish sotey dia eye nor dey si and dia ear nor dey hear til today."
45011009	Bot David sey, "Mak di fud wey dem dey chop, kause trobol for dem kon fal laik stone for dia head and mak God ponish dem.
45011010	"Mak dia eye blind, so dat dem nor go fit si. Mak wahala bend dia bak foreva."
45011011	I dey ask again, Izrel pipol wey fal nor go get up again? No! Bot bikos of dia sins, Gentai pipol don get salvashon and dis tin, dey mak Izrel pipol jelos.
45011012	If Izrel pipol sin fit mak Gentai pipol dey save, dat min sey, wen Izrel pipol turn go mit God, pipol wey go dey save, go plenti wel-wel.
45011013	Naw, I dey tok to una wey bi Gentai pipol and as long as I bi una apostol, I dey hapi wit di wok wey I dey du,
45011014	so dat my pipol go dey jelos, bikos of wetin God dey du for Gentai pipol. Dis go mak dem turn from sin kom mit God and E go save dem.
45011015	Bikos wen God rejet Izrel pipol, di hol wold kon get savalshon. Na haw e go kon bi, wen God asept dem bak? E go giv life to pipol wey won die.
45011016	If dem giv God di first part for bread, den na God get all di bread and if dem giv God tri root, den di hol tri don bi en own tu.
45011017	Gentai pipol, una bi laik bransh wey dem add join olive tri. Una don tak di place for som bransh wey God first kut komot. So una dey enjoy di blessins, wey di root dey giv.
45011018	So mak una nor boast, bot mak una rimemba sey, nor bi una dey mak di root stand, bot na di root dey sopot una.
45011019	So una go sey, "God break di bransh komot, mak E for fit si place wey E go put us."
45011020	Tru-tru, God break Izrel pipol komot from di tri, bikos dem nor biliv am. Bot una dey wer una dey, bikos una get fate. So, mak una nor dey boast, insted, mak una dey fear wetin God fit du.
45011021	If God nor sori for Izrel pipol wey bi di natura bransh, una tink sey E go sori for una if una sin?
45011022	Naw, una don si haw God dey gud and harsh. Ivun doh E dey ves for doz wey fal, E stil dey kaind to una. And E go always dey kaind to una, as long as una dey du wetin E wont. If not, E go rejet una tu.
45011023	If Izrel pipol turn bak kon mit God, E go put dem bak for di tri, bikos E get pawa to du-am.
45011024	Una wey bi Gentai pipol bi laik olive tri bransh wey dem kut for bush kon go put for anoda beta olive tri (and e nor sopoz bi laik dat). Na Ju pipol bi di beta olive tri; so e go eazi for God to join dem bak to di origina tri again.
45011025	My frends, I nor won mak una dey boast abaut unasef. So I go tel una wetin hapun to Izrel pipol. Som of dem stuborn wel-wel and na so dem go bi ontil di numba of Gentai pipol wey God wont, don komplit.
45011026	Na so God go save all Izrel pipol jos as en wod sey, "Di pesin wey go save Izrel pipol go kom from Zion, den, Jacob shildren nor go dey du bad tins again.
45011027	"And na dis go bi my agriment wit dem wen I don forgiv dem dia sins."
45011028	As e bi sey Ju pipol rejet God wod, dem don turn to God enemi, bikos of una wey bi Gentai pipol. Bot as God wont am, dem bi pipol wey E luv, bikos of dia gran-gran papa dem.
45011029	God nor dey tak bak wetin e don alredi giv pipol or shange en maind abaut di pipol wey E don shuz.
45011030	As for una wey bi Gentai pipol, una don disobey God bifor, bot naw, God don sori for una, bikos Ju pipol nor gri obey am.
45011031	Bikos God don sori for una, E go stil sori for dem tu.
45011032	God trit evribodi as prizinas, bikos wi nor gri du wetin E tel us. Bot E du-am laik dat, so dat E go fit sori for all of us.
45011033	Hu fit no haw God big rish? Hu fit no haw God wisdom and undastandin bi? Hu fit esplain why God dey du wetin E dey du!
45011034	Na hu no wetin dey God maind? Hu go fit advise God?
45011035	Wish pesin don boro God somtin kon sey God go pay am bak?
45011036	Bikos na God kreate evritin and na tru am evritin dey. Mak praiz bi en own foreva and eva! Amen.
45012001	My brodas and sistas, God dey gud. So I beg, as una dey alaif, mak una dey offa una bodi giv am as sakrifais. Mak una dey du wetin E tok and wetin go mak bele swit am. Na dis bi di best way to serv God.
45012002	Mak una nor bi laik pipol for di wold, bot mak una alow God shange una maind, den una go no haw to serv God and du tins wey dey mak bele swit am.
45012003	By di grace wey God giv mi, I dey tel all of una, mak una nor tink sey una tu dey important. Insted, mak una yuz gud sense tink and undastand di fate wey God giv una.
45012004	Pesin bodi get difren parts and all di parts get dia own wok.
45012005	Na so e bi wit us. Wi meni, bot wi bi difren parts for Kraist bodi and wi bilong to ish oda.
45012006	Tru God grace, E don giv us difren-difren gift to yuz. If wi dey profesai, mak wi du-am akordin to di fate wey wi get.
45012007	If wi dey serv odas, mak wi serv dem wel. If wi dey tish, mak wi tish wel.
45012008	If wi dey prish, mak wi prish wel. If wi dey giv, mak wi du-am wit beta maind. If wi dey lid odas, mak wi du awa best. If wi dey du gud to odas, mak wi du-am wit hapines.
45012009	Mak wi luv ish oda wel-wel. Mak una hate enitin wey dey bad, bot una must luv enitin wey get trut.
45012010	Mak una luv ish oda laik brodas and sistas and mak una respet oda pipol pas unasef.
45012011	Mak una nor taya, bot wit di Holi Spirit help, mak una serv God wit beta maind.
45012012	Mak una let una hope giv una hapines. Mak una dey patient wen trobol kom and nor stop to pray.
45012013	Mak una giv fud to God pipol wey dey hungri and mak una dey welkom dem for una haus.
45012014	Mak una nor kos pipol wey dey opres una, bot mak una pray mak God bless dem.
45012015	Wen pipol dey hapi, mak una folo dem hapi and wen dem dey krai, mak una folo dem krai tu.
45012016	Mak una trai to bi frend wit evribodi. Mak una nor kari bodi up kon feel sey una wise pas evribodi, insted, mak una dey mak frend wit doz wey nor dey important.
45012017	Mak una nor pay evil for evil, bot mak sure sey wetin una dey du, gud for God and pipol eye
45012018	and mak una trai to liv for peace wit evribodi.
45012019	Mak una nor trai to pay enibodi for di bad tin wey dem du una, bot mak una liv am for God, bikos God wod sey, "Na mi go revenge for una. I go pay dem bak."
45012020	God wod stil sey, "If yor enemi dey hungri, mak yu gi-am fud chop, if en trot dry, mak yu gi-am wota drink, bikos as yu dey du so, na wahala yu dey kari put for en head."
45012021	So, mak una nor let bad tins kontrol una, bot mak una let di gud tins wey una dey du, plenti pas wikednes.
45013001	Mak evribodi obey di pipol wey dey rule dem. Bikos na onli God dey giv autoriti and put pipol for pawa.
45013002	So enibodi wey dey disobey dia rula, dey disobey God and God go ponish am.
45013003	Bikos doz wey dey du gud, nor go get problem wit dia rulas, so dem nor nid to fear. Mak una jos du wetin dey gud and dem go praiz una.
45013004	Bikos all rulas na God savant and na dia duti to help yu. If yu du bad, den mak yu fear, bikos dis rulas get pawa to ponish yu. Dem bi God savants wey dey ponish doz wey du wrong tins.
45013005	Bot yu must obey di rulas, bikos yu no sey naim bi di rite tin to du, nor bi bikos God go ves for yu.
45013006	Yu must stil pay yor tax tu. Di rulas na God savants and na dia wok to kare for all dis mata.
45013007	Mak yu pay evritin wey yu dey hol; weda na tax, respet or onor.
45013008	Mak luv bi di onli tin wey yu dey hol! If yu luv odas, yu don du evritin wey di law tok.
45013009	Di law get difren-difren komand laik, "Nor komit adultri; nor kil pesin; nor tif; nor put eye for anoda man propati." All dis na jos won komand wey sey, "Mak pipol luv odas, jos as dem luv diasef."
45013010	lf yu luv pesin, yu nor go du-am bad. So, na luv bi di main tin wey di law dey tok abaut.
45013011	Since una no di taim wey wi dey naw, mak una dey bihav wel, bikos di taim don rish wen una go wak-up from slip. Una no sey di day wey God go giv us salvashon, don near wel-wel pas as e bi wen wi first biliv.
45013012	Nite don nearli finish and day go soon break. So mak wi stop to bihav laik pipol wey dey daknes and mak wi redi to waka for lite.
45013013	So mak wi dey bihav wel as pipol dey du for day taim. Nor go enihaw parti or drink tu mush, den kon dey bihav enihaw. Nor kworel or joj pipol.
45013014	Insted, mak una wear Jisos Kraist laik klot for bodi. Den wi nor go du di tins wey awa bodi won t.
45014001	Mak una dey welkom God pipol. Ivun doh dia fate nor tu strong, mak una nor kos dem, bikos of wetin dem dey tink sey dey gud or bad.
45014002	Som pipol tink sey e dey rite to chop eni fud and odas wey dia fate dey wik, dey chop onli vegetabol.
45014003	Since God dey welkom evribodi, mak una nor kondem odas bikos dem chop or dem nor chop wetin una laik.
45014004	Wish rite yu get to kondem anoda pesin savant? Na onli dia oga fit tok weda dem dey du wel and e must mak sure sey, dem dey du di rite tin.
45014005	Som pipol tink sey won day beta pas anoda and som tink sey, evriday na di same. Bot mak evribodi biliv wetin dem won biliv.
45014006	Enibodi wey tink sey won day beta pas anoda, dey du so to onor God. And enibodi wey chop meat, dey tank God jos laik di pesin wey nor won chop.
45014007	Nobodi dey liv or die for ensef. Weda wi die or wi liv, na God stil get us.
45014008	If wi liv, na God wi dey liv for; if wi die, na God wi stil die for. So, weda wi die or wi liv, na God stil get us.
45014009	Dis na bikos Kraist die and e kom bak to life, so dat e go bi Oga to pipol wey don die and doz wey dey alaif.
45014010	Bot why yu dey kondem oda Kristains? Why yu dey si dem as smol shildren? Di day dey kom wen God go joj all of us.
45014011	God wod sey, "Weda dem laik am or not, evribodi go nil dan for my front kon sey na mi bi God."
45014012	So, all of us go tel God wetin wi du wit awa life.
45014013	So, mak wi nor dey joj won anoda and mak wi nor spoil anoda pesin fate.
45014014	As I don no Kraist, e don mak mi no sey all fud dey klin. Bot if yu tink sey e nor gud mak yu chop som fud, dat nor min sey, e nor gud for anoda pesin.
45014015	Bikos if di fud wey yu chop mak yor broda or sista ves for yu, den yu nor dey show luv again. So mak yu nor let di kaind fud wey yu dey chop, offend di pesin wey Jisos Kraist die for.
45014016	Nor let pipol kos Jisos Kraist, bikos of di fud wey yu dey chop.
45014017	Bikos God kindom nor bi fud and drink mata, bot na abaut raitiousnes, peace and joy wey di Holi Spirit dey giv pipol.
45014018	If yu serv Kraist laik dis, God go dey hapi wit yu and pipol go respet yu.
45014019	So, mak wi liv for peace, den wi go help ish oda grow as dem dey serv God.
45014020	Nor skata God wok bikos of fud. Evri fud dey okay, bot e nor gud mak yu chop wetin go spoil anoda pesin fate.
45014021	E beta mak yu nor chop meat, drink wine or du enitin wey fit spoil yor brodas fate.
45014022	Enitin wey yu biliv abaut dis mata, mak yu kip am to yorsef and God wey dey hevun, dey si-am. God don bless di pesin wey nor kondem ensef, bikos of wetin e du.
45014023	Bot if yu dey doubt wetin yu chop, den yu dey kondem yorsef and yu no sey dat nor gud, bikos enitin wey yu du against wetin yu biliv, na sin.
45015001	If awa fate dey strong, den mak wi dey patient wit doz wey get wik fate. Mak wi trai to mak dem hapi, insted of awasef.
45015002	Mak wi tink of tins wey gud for dem, den du wetin go mak dem grow.
45015003	Ivun Kraist nor du tins wey go jos mak ensef hapi, bot jos as dem rite for God wod, "Di pesin wey kos yu, don kos mi."
45015004	Bikos evritin wey dem rite from biginin, na to tish, enkorage and giv us hope.
45015005	So, I pray sey, God wey dey giv komfort and patient, go help una liv for peace wit won anoda as una dey folo Jisos Kraist.
45015006	So dat as una dey togeda, una go fit yuz won vois praiz God, wey bi awa Oga Jisos Kraist, Papa.
45015007	So mak una asept won anoda jos as Kraist asept una, so dat God go get all di glori.
45015008	Mak I tel una di trut, Kraist kom as Ju pipol savant to show sey, God don kip di promis wey E mak wit dia gran-gran papa dem. Kraist stil kom,
45015009	so dat Gentai pipol go praiz God sey e dey gud to dem. Jos as God wod sey, "I go tel Gentai pipol abaut Yu and I go sing, dey praiz yor name."
45015010	God wod stil sey, "Gentai pipol! Mak una hapi wit God pipol."
45015011	Dem rite am for God wod sey, "Una wey bi Gentai pipol, mak una praiz God. Mak evribodi praiz am."
45015012	Profet Isaia sey, "Sombodi dey kom from David famili (Jesse root). E go rule Gentai pipol and dem go biliv am."
45015013	I pray mak God wey dey giv hope, bless una wit joy and peace bikos of una fate. So mak di Holi Spirit pawa ful una bodi wit fate.
45015014	My frends, I dey sure abaut una sey una gud and una no God wel-wel and fit tish won anoda.
45015015	Bot for dis leta, I rite som tins wit boldnes, so dat una go rimemba dem we-wel. God dey gud to mi and
45015016	naim mak am shuz mi to bi Jisos Kraist savant for Gentai pipol and mak I for dey prish di Gud News. Dis tin hapun, so dat di Holi Spirit go mak God dey hapi wit Gentai pipol.
45015017	So I dey boast abaut di tins wey I dey du, bikos of Jisos Kraist.
45015018	Wit beta maind, evritin wey I dey tok abaut, na haw Kraist let mi tok and wok, so dat Gentai pipol go obey am.
45015019	Yes! I go tok haw Kraist tak du meni mirakols and wondas tru di Holi Spirit pawa. I don prish di Gud News from Jerusalem go rish Ilyrikum.
45015020	Bot I laik to prish di Gud News for wer pipol nor no Kraist, so dat I nor go build haus on-top anoda man foundashon,
45015021	jos as God wod sey; "Doz wey dem tel abaut am, go si-am and doz wey neva hear abaut am, dem go undastand."
45015022	My wok neva let mi kom si una.
45015023	Bot naw, nor-tin rimain wey I go du for dis part of di wold again and e don tey wey I dey plan to kom visit una.
45015024	I go plan to stop si una wen I dey go Spain, so dat una go help mi for di joni, afta I don stay wit una for somtaim.
45015025	Bot naw, I dey tak mesage go giv God pipol for Jerusalem,
45015026	bikos God pipol for Masidonia and Akaya giv mi moni mak I giv di poor Kristains for der.
45015027	Dis na wetin dem rili won du. Bikos wen den share di tins wey dem get wit Ju pipol, naim bi sey dem don folo Ju pipol share dia spiritual blessins tu.
45015028	So, afta I don finish dis wok kon dey sure sey di bilivas don get dia blessins for Jerusalem, I go visit una wen I dey go Spain.
45015029	And I no sey wen I kom visit una, I go bring plenti blessins from Kraist kon giv una.
45015030	My brodas and sistas, I dey beg una wit Jisos Kraist and di Holi Spirit luv; mak una help mi pray to God.
45015031	Mak una pray mak God save mi from pipol wey nor biliv am for Judea and mak di bilivas wey dey Jerusalem, asept wetin I dey prish.
45015032	Mak una pray giv God, so dat I go kom visit una wit hapines.
45015033	So mak God wey dey giv peace, dey wit all of un a. Amen.
45016001	I get beta tins to tok abaut awa sista, Fibi, wey bi lida for di shosh wey dey Senkria.
45016002	Mak una welkom am wit God name as God shildren sopoz du. And mak una giv am enitin wey e nid; bikos e don help mi and oda pipol bifor.
45016003	Mak una salot Prisila and Akwila for mi. Dem bi my co-wokas for awa Oga Jisos Kraist wok,
45016004	dem don ivun risk dia life bikos of mi. So, mi and di hol shosh dey tank dem wel-wel.
45016005	Mak una stil help mi salot di pipol for di shosh wey dey mit for dia haus. Salot Epaenetus, my gud frend (di first pesin to biliv Kraist for Asia).

45016015	Grit Filologus and Julia, Nereus and en sista, Olympas and all di bilivas wey dey wit dem.
45016016	Mak una salot won anoda wit kiss for jaw. All di shosh wey bi Kraist own, dey grit una.
45016017	Naw, my brodas and sistas, I dey beg una, mak una no di pipol wey dey kause wahala and opoz di tishin wey una don learn from us. Den mak una nor go near dem!
45016018	Bikos dis kaind pipol nor dey serv awa Oga Jisos Kraist, bot na dia bele dem dey kare for. Wit dia swit and wayo mout, dem go praiz and disiv pipol wey nor wise.
45016019	I dey hapi, bikos evribodi don no haw una dey obey God. Bot I wont mak una dey wise wen e rish mata wey dey gud or bad. Mak una nor du eni bad tin.
45016020	And God wey dey giv peace, go soon distroi Satan for una. Mak awa Oga Jisos Kraist grace dey wit una.
45016021	Timoti, my co-woka; Lucius, Jason and Sosipater my kontriman, all of dem dey grit una.
45016022	Ivun mi, Tertius wey rite dis leta, dey grit una wit Kraist name.
45016023	Gaius, wey dey kare for mi and di shosh, dey grit una. Erastus wey bi di tawn treasura and awa broda Kwatus, dey grit una.
45016024	Mak awa Oga Jisos Kraist grace dey wit una!
45016025	Mak wi praiz God, bikos e don mak una strong tru dis Gud News wey I dey prish abaut en pikin, Jisos Kraist. For meni years naw, dem kip dis mesage for sikrit,
45016026	bot naw, dem don tok am at last. God wey nor dey die, komand en profets mak dem rite abaut di Gud News, so dat pipol for evriwer, go obey am and get fate.
45016027	Naw, bikos of Jisos Kraist, wi fit praiz di onli God wey dey wise foreva! Amen.
46001001	Na Pol, wey God kol to bi Jisos Kraist apostol and Sosthenes, awa broda, na dem rite dis leta.
46001002	To God holi pipol for di shosh wey dey Korint, wey bi en own bikos of Jisos Kraist and pipol for evriwer wey dey woship awa Oga Jisos Kraist as dia Oga and Savior.
46001003	Mak grace and peace wey God and Oga Jisos Kraist dey giv, bi una own!
46001004	I dey always tank God bikos of di grace wey E giv una, tru Jisos Kraist.
46001005	Bikos wi dey wit Kraist, God mak us dey rish for evri side, both for wisdom and undastandin,
46001006	bikos di mesage abaut Kraist dey insaid us,
46001007	so una nor go miss eni gift wey di Holi Spirit dey giv, as una dey wait for di day wen God go bring awa Oga Jisos Kraist kom bak.
46001008	God go help una rish di end, so dat E nor go si fault for una life for di day wen Jisos go kom bak.
46001009	God dey fateful, bikos na-im kol una to waka wit en pikin, Jisos Kraist, wey bi awa Oga.
46001010	My brodas and sistas, I dey beg una wit awa Oga Jisos Kraist name sey, mak una nor kworel, bot mak una get won maind for evritin wey una dey du.
46001011	Bikos I don hear tru Khloe famili sey, una dey kworel among unasef.
46001012	Wetin I hear bi sey, som of una dey sey, "Na Pol side I dey;" odas sey, "Na Apollos side I dey;" som stil sey, "Na Pita side I dey" or "Na Kraist side I dey."
46001013	Una hear sey dem divide Kraist? Na Pol dem hang kil for kros? Abi na Pol name dem tak baptaiz una?
46001014	I tank God sey I nor baptaiz eni of una esept Krispus and Gaius,
46001015	so nobodi go fit sey na my name dem tak baptaiz am.
46001016	(I rimemba sey I stil baptaiz Stephanas famili. Apart from dem, I nor rimemba eni oda pesin wey I baptaiz.
46001017	Bikos Kraist nor send mi go baptaiz, bot na to prish di gospol and nor bi wit ordinari wisdom wey go mak di sofa wey Kraist sofa for kros, yeye.
46001018	Di mesage abaut Kraist deat for kros bi laik foolish mata to pipol wey don loss, bot for wi wey God don save, di mesage na God pawa.
46001019	Bikos God wod sey, "I go distroi di wisdom wey wise pipol feel sey dem get. I go konfuz doz wey tink sey dem no tu mush."
46001020	Wetin hapun to di wise pipol? Wetin hapun to doz wey no Mosis law wel-wel? Wetin hapun to doz wey tink sey dem get all di ansa? Abi God nor sey dis wold wisdom, nor min enitin?
46001021	God wise wel-wel, so E nor let pipol for dis wold no-am wit di wisdom wey dem get. Insted, E save onli di pipol wey biliv di foolish mesage wey wi dey prish.
46001022	Ju pipol won si mirakol bifor dem go biliv and Greek pipol, na wisdom dem won hear,
46001023	bot di tru mesage abaut Jisos wey dem kil for kros, naim wi dey prish and di mesage bi laik stone wey Ju pipol kick by mistak kon fal, bot to Gentai pipol, na yeye tin e bi.
46001024	Bot for wi wey God don kol, weda wi bi Ju or Greek; na Kraist bi God pawa and wisdom wey svae us.
46001025	Bikos God foolishnes wise pas all di sense wey humanbin get and God wiknes strong pas all di pawa wey dem get.
46001026	My brodas and sistas, mak una rimemba haw God kol una, nor bi bikos una wise, strong or get moni wel-wel.
46001027	Bot God shuz wetin di wold tink sey dey foolish and wik, so dat wise and strong pipol go shame.
46001028	Wetin di wold tink sey nor gud, naim God shuz; tins wey dem tink sey nor min enitin, na doz tins E mak important.
46001029	God du laik dis, so dat nobodi go fit boast for en front.
46001030	Una don bi Kraist frends bikos of God and na tru Kraist wi get wisdom, gudnes and holines wey kom from God;
46001031	bikos, God wod sey, "Enibodi wey won boast, mak e yuz Kraist tak boast."
46002001	My brodas and sistas, wen I kom tel una abaut God wod, I nor tok to una wit big-big wod or trai to show sey I get sense.
46002002	Bikos wen I dey wit una, I plan sey, Kraist wey dem kil for kros, na onli en mesage I go tok to una abaut.
46002003	So wen I kom mit una, I dey wik and dey fear.
46002004	Wen I dey tok and prish to una, I nor trai to show sey I get sense, bot I dey du evritin wit God pawa wey di Holi Spirit dey giv,
46002005	so dat una fate go dey for God pawa, nor bi humanbin wisdom.
46002006	Wi dey tok wit wisdom to doz wey rili no God wod, bot nor bi wit dis wold or eni rula wisdom, bikos dia wisdom nor min enitin.
46002007	Di tin wey I dey tok abaut, na God sikrit wisdom wey E shuz for us, ivun bifor E kreate di wold.
46002008	No rula for dis wold fit undastand God wisdom, bikos if to sey dem fit, dem for nor nail and kil Kraist wey get glori.
46002009	Bot God wod sey, "No eye don eva si; no ear don hear, ivun pesin maind nor fit tink abaut di tins wey God don priper for pipol wey luv am."
46002010	God show us dis tins tru en Spirit, bikos di Spirit dey faind evritin; ivun di deep tins wey dey God maind.
46002011	Na onli pesin spirit no wetin dey di pesin maind and na onli God Spirit no wetin dey God maind.
46002012	God giv us en Spirit, so wi nor dey tink as dis wold pipol dey tink and naim mak us no di blessins wey God don giv us.
46002013	Evri wod wey wi dey tok, na God Spirit tish us and nor bi human wisdom. And na dis same Spirit dey help us tish spiritual tins to pipol wey get God Spirit.
46002014	So, na onli hu get God Spirit fit unadastand spiritual blessins. Pesin wey nor get God Spirit, nor go fit undastand wetin di Spirit dey tok.
46002015	Pesin wey dey listin to di Spirit fit joj oda pipol, bot nobodi go fit joj dem:
46002016	bikos God wod sey, "Hu fit no wetin God dey tink so dat e go advise am?" Bot wi wey get di Spirit, undastand wetin Kraist dey tish.
46003001	My brodas and sistas, wen I dey wit una bifor, una dey bihav laik pipol for dis wold. Na dis mak mi nor fit tok to una as pipol wey get God Spirit. Dat taim, una fate for Kraist bi laik smol pikin own.
46003002	So I dey fid una wit milk laik smol pikin and as e bi naw, una neva stil fit chop strong fud,
46003003	bikos una neva get di Spirit since jelosi and kworel stil dey among una. Dis min sey una neva get di Spirit and una stil dey liv laik pipol wey dey di wold.
46003004	Som of una dey sey, "Na Pol I dey folo," odas sey, "Na Apollos bi awa lida." Na pipol wey nor no God dey du laik dat!
46003005	Mi and Apollos na God savant and E yuz us tak prish to una mak una for fit biliv and ish of us dey du di wok wey God sey mak wi du.
46003006	I dey plant di sid and Apollos dey wota dem, bot na God dey mak di sid grow.
46003007	Pesin wey plant and di won wey wota, nor min enitin, bikos na God dey mak di sid grow.
46003008	Di pesin wey plant di sid and di won wey wota am, na di same wok dem dey du, bot ish pesin go get en pay from God akordin to en wok.
46003009	All of us na co-wokas for God and na una bi God farm and en buildins.
46003010	Na God grace mak mi sabi build wel-wel. I lay foundashon wey anoda pesin build put. Bot mak wi tak kare as wi dey build,
46003011	bikos na Kraist bi di onli foundashon.
46003012	So if enibodi yuz gold, silva, fine stones, wud, or difren grass tak build on-top dis foundashon,
46003013	mak e no sey, God go expoz en wok, bikos E go test am wit fire for Jojment Day. Di fire go test di wok wey evribodi dey du.
46003014	God go riwod us if di fire nor burn wetin wi build.
46003015	Bot if di fire distroi am, wi nor go get enitin. Bot wi go dey save laik pesin wey dem drag komot from insaid fire.
46003016	Una nor no sey una bi God tempol and en Spirit dey insaid una?
46003017	So If enibodi distroi God tempol, God go distroi dat pesin tu, bikos God tempol dey holi and na una bi dat tempol.
46003018	Mak una nor let enibodi disiv una. If enibodi tink sey e get sense for dis life, mak e turn to fool, so dat e go rili get sense.
46003019	Dis wold wisdom, na foolishnes for God front. Bikos God wod sey, "God dey ponish pipol wey tink sey dem wise."
46003020	God no sey na yeye tins wise pipol dey tink,
46003021	so, mak wi stop to dey boast abaut wetin pesin du. Bikos both
46003022	Pol, Apollos, Pita, di wold, life or deat; tins wey dey naw or tins wey go dey tumoro, all of dem na una own.

46004001	Mak una dey tink abaut us as Kraist savant wey God don show en sikrit.
46004002	God wont mak wi dey fateful to am.
46004003	So, e nor konsan mi if yu or eni human kourt dey joj mi. Ivun mi nor fit joj mysef.
46004004	My maind dey klear, bot dat nor min sey I dey inosent. Na onli God go fit joj mi.
46004005	So, mak una nor joj enibodi ontil Kraist go kom bak. E go expoz evritin wey dey daknes and di tins wey dey insaid pesin heart. Dat taim, na God go praiz evribodi akordin to wetin dem du.
46004006	My frends, I don yuz mysef and Apollos as ezampol for una, so dat tru us, una go no wetin e min to obey di law. I nor wont mak una dey sey won of us beta pas di oda pesin.
46004007	Wetin mak una tink sey, una beta pas anoda pesin? Nor bi God giv una evritin? So wetin mak una dey boast, wen e bi sey evritin wey una get, na God giv una?
46004008	Una don rili get evritin wey una nid! Una don get plenti moni! Una don turn king wit us! Haw I wish sey una rili bi king, so dat wi go dey rule wit una.
46004009	Bikos e klear sey, di place wey God giv us wey bi en apostols, na wer wos pas for di wold; wi bi laik prizinas wey dem dey go kil. Angels and dis wold pipol jos dey tak us mak yeye.
46004010	Bikos of Kraist, pipol dey si us as fools, bot God don mak us wise. Wi wik and dem hate us, bot dem dey respet una wey dey strong.
46004011	Ivun today, wi dey hungri for fud and wota, na onli rag wi get to wear. Dem dey trit us enihaw and wi nor get haus to stay.
46004012	Wi dey wok hard bifor wi go fit chop and as pipol dey kos us, na blessin wi dey giv dem bak. Wen wi dey sofa, wi dey-dey patient.
46004013	Wen pesin kos us, wi nor dey ansa bak wit kworel. So til today, dem dey si us as dirti for dis wold.
46004014	I nor dey rite dis tins mak una for shame, bot na to koret una as shildren wey I luv.
46004015	Bikos ivun if ten tazon pipol kon tish una abaut Kraist, na onli won papa una go stil get. Bikos una don turn to my pikin, wen una risiv di mesage abaut Kraist from mi.
46004016	So, I dey enkorage una sey, mak una bi laik mi.
46004017	Na to enkorage una mak mi send Timoti, my son wey I laik and wey luv Kraist kom mit una. E go tel una haw I dey folo Kraist and di tins wey I dey prish abaut Kraist, for evri shosh.
46004018	Som of una don dey kari bodi up, bikos una tink sey I nor go kom bak again.
46004019	Bot if God alow mi, I go soon kom mit una. Den I go no if pipol wey dey boast, rili get pawa.
46004020	Bikos God kindom mata, nor bi abaut ordinari tok, bot na abaut pawa.

46005001	I don dey hear bad-bad tins abaut som of una. And una own ivun wos pas wetin doz wey nor no God dey du. Sotey man dey slip wit en papa wife.
46005002	And shame nor ivun dey kash una! Una sopoz to feel bad kon driv di pesin wey du dis kaind tin.
46005003	I no sey I nor dey der wit una naw, bot I dey wit una for spirit. And I don alredi joj di pesin, jos as I go du if I dey der.
46005004	Wen una gada togeda for awa Oga Jisos Kraist name, I dey wit una for spirit and Kraist pawa dey wit una tu.
46005005	So mak una giv am to Satan mak e ponish am, so dat en sin go komot for en bodi and Kraist go save am for di last day.
46005006	E nor gud mak una dey boast! Una nor no sey, smol yist wey dem put for bread, na-im dey mak di hol bread raiz?
46005007	Mak una rimov di old yist, den una go bi laik fresh bread wey nor get yist and dat na wetin una bi. Bikos awa Passova lamb, na Kraist wey dem don alredi sakrifais.
46005008	So wen wi dey celebrate Passova, mak wi nor du-am wit di old yist wey bi wikednes and bad bele, bot mak wi du-am wit di fresh bread wey nor get yist, wey bi trut and beta maind.
46005009	For di leta wey I first rite giv una, I sey mak una nor mak frend wit bad pipol.
46005010	Bot I nor dey tok abaut pipol wey bad, wiked, dey serv juju and get long-trot for dis wold. If to sey na dem I dey tok abaut, den una nid to komot for dis wold.
46005011	Bot naw, I dey rite to una sey, pipol wey sey dem bi Kristins and dem dey du bad tins, mak una nor folo dem mak frend. Mak una nor ivun chop wit dat kaind pesin.
46005012	Wetin go mak mi joj pipol wey nor dey di shosh? Nor bi doz wey dey insaid wi sopoz to joj?
46005013	Na God go joj doz wey dey outsaid, bikos en wod sey, "Mak una driv doz wey dey du wiked tins among una, komot for di shosh."
46006001	Wen pesin nor dey agri wit anoda pesin, una dey tak una kase go kourt wer sinas go joj di mata, abi una dey tak am go mit God pipol?
46006002	Una nor no sey na God pipol go joj di wold? And if na una go joj di wold, una nor fit setol smol-smol mata among unasef?
46006003	Una nor no sey wi go joj angels? Since na so, den wi sopoz to joj di tins wey dey dis wold!
46006004	So, na wetin mak us dey tak awa kase go giv joj wey nor no God?
46006005	I dey tok laik dis, so dat una go shame! So una nor get wise pesin among una wey fit joj bitwin una wey bi Kristens?
46006006	Wetin dey mak una kari unasef go mit joj wey nor no God?
46006007	Wen una tak unasef go kourt, dat min sey all of una don lose.
46006008	Insted, una dey play wayo among unasef!
46006009	Una nor no sey wiked pipol nor go enta God kindom? So mak una nor fool unasef! Pipol wey dey slip wit hu dem nor mari, doz wey dey serv juju, men wey dey slip wit oda men,
46006010	tif, long-trot, drunkard, doz wey dey kos pipol and doz wey dey play wayo; non of dem go enta God kindom.
46006011	Na so som of una bi bifor, bot naw, God don wosh una klin tru Jisos Kraist name and en Spirit pawa, don mak una klin for en eye.
46006012	Som of una sey, "Wi fit du enitin wey wi wont." Bot I dey tel una sey nor bi evritin dey gud for us. So I nor go gri mak enitin kontrol mi.
46006013	Una stil dey sey, "Fud dey gud for awa bodi and awa bodi nid fud." Bot I dey tel una, "God go distroi di tu of dem." So mak wi nor yuz awa bodi tak du yeye tins.
46006014	God go raiz us from deat wit di same pawa wey E yuz tak raiz Jisos.
46006015	Una nor no sey una bodi na part for Kraist bodi? So e dey gud mak wi put awa bodi for ashawo wok? God forbid!
46006016	Una nor no sey, pesin wey dey slip enihaw wit oda pipol, don bi part for di pipol bodi?
46006017	So enibodi wey join Kraist, don get won spirit wit am.
46006018	Mak una run liv ashawo life. Evri oda sin wey man dey komit na for outsaid en bodi, bot di pesin wey dey du ashawo, dey sin against en own bodi.
46006019	Abi una nor no sey una bodi na di tempol wer di Holi Spirit dey stay? So, nor bi una get unasef.
46006020	God don pay beta prize for una, so mak una onor am wit una bodi.
46007001	Naw I go ansa di kweshon wey una ask for una leta. Una ask sey, "E dey gud mak pesin nor mari?"
46007002	Bot mak una nor for dey du ashawo, e beta mak una mari.
46007003	Mak husban and wife du di rite tin wey dem sopoz du for won anoda.
46007004	Nor bi di wife get en own bodi, bot na di husban get am and na so tu di wife get en husban bodi.
46007005	Mak una nor refuse ish oda, esept una agri sey una go dey laik dat for somtaim, so dat una go fit pray. Den Satan nor go fit tempt una, bikos una go fit kontrol una bodi.
46007006	Na advise I dey giv una, nor bi komand.
46007007	Haw I wish sey all of una bi laik mi. Bot di gift wey God giv us nor bi di same.
46007008	Dis na di advise wey I go tel di pesin wey neva mari and doz wey dia husban or wife don die; mak una dey as una dey, jos as I bi.
46007009	Bot if dem nor fit kontrol demsef, mak dem mari, bikos e beta mak pesin mari, dan mak e dey tink bad tin for en maind.
46007010	Na doz wey don mari I won giv dis komand to (Nor bi mi, bot na God): Mak wife nor liv en husban.
46007011	Bot if e liv am, mak e nor mari again or mak e go bak go setol wit di man. And mak husban nor liv en wife tu.
46007012	Ivun doh I dey tok on my own, I nor tink sey God go tok enitin difren from wetin I dey tel una abaut marage. Di onli tin wey I fit du na to giv una my advise. If yor wife nor dey folo Kraist, bot e sey e go folo yu stay, mak yu nor driv am.
46007013	If yor husban nor dey folo Kraist, bot e sey e go folo yu stay, mak yu nor run liv am.
46007014	Bikos di husban wey nor biliv, God go save am, bikos of en wife wey biliv and di wife wey nor biliv, God go save am, bikos of en husban wey biliv.
46007015	Bot if di won wey nor biliv komot from di marage, mak e bi laik dat. For dis kaind kase, di broda or sista wey biliv, don dey fri; bikos God wont mak wi enjoy peace.
46007016	Yu wife! Haw yu tak no sey yu nor go fit save yor husaban? Yu husban! Haw yu tak no sey yu nor go fit save yor wife?
46007017	For evri shosh, I dey tel di pipol sey mak dem rimain as dem bi wen Oga Jisos shuz and kol dem to bi en own. Naw, na di same tin I dey tel una so.
46007018	If yu don alredi sekonsaiz, mak yu dey laik dat. If dem neva sekonsaiz yu, mak yu nor sekonsaiz.
46007019	Weda dem sekonsaiz yu or not, nor min enitin. Wetin dey important, na to obey God law.
46007020	So mak una nor trai to shange as una bi wen God shuz una.
46007021	If God kol yu wen yu bi slave, mak yu nor let am wori yu. Bot if yu fit get yor fridom, mak yu get-am.
46007022	Slave wey God shuz mak e folo Jisos, don bikom fri man tru Jisos Kraist. So fri man wey God shuz mak e folo Jisos, don turn to Kraist savant.
46007023	God pay big prize for una. So mak una nor bi slave to eni oda pesin.
46007024	Mak una stay as una bi wen God shuz and kol una.
46007025	Konsanin pipol wey neva mari bifor, I nor get eni komand from Kraist to giv una, bot I go advise una as pesin wey una fit trust, bikos God dey show mi mesi.
46007026	Dis taim wey wi dey nor eazi at-all and wetin I tink bi sey, e go gud mak una stay as una bi naw.
46007027	If yu don mari, nor liv yor marage. If yu neva mari, mak yu nor wori yorsef abaut am.
46007028	If pesin wey neva mari bifor kon mari, e nor sin. Bot, pipol wey don mari go face plenti wahala and I dey trai to help una, so dat una nor go face dat kaind wahala.
46007029	My frends, wetin I min bi sey Kraist go soon kom and e nor mata if yu don mari or not.
46007030	If yu dey krai or laff; dey buy somtin or yu nor get moni, all na di same tin.
46007031	E nor go mak eni difrens ivun if yu get all di tins for dis wold or sey yu laik di wold wel-wel, bikos as wi no, di wold go soon vanish komot.
46007032	And I nor wont mak enitin trobol una. Man wey neva mari, mak e dey du tins wey go mak Kraist hapi for am.
46007033	Bot man wey don mari get plenti tins to wori abaut. E go must wori abaut tins for dis wold, bikos e go wont mak bele dey swit en wife,
46007034	so e go dey tink abaut difren tins. Wuman wey neva mari dey onli tink of haw to mak bele swit Kraist and dia bodi and maind dey pure. Bot wuman wey don mari dey wori abaut dis wold tins, bikos e wont mak bele swit en husban.
46007035	Wetin I dey tok na for una own gud, nor bi to mak una slave. I wont help una to dey liv beta life and to luv Kraist pas eni oda tin.
46007036	Bot if yu dey engage and yu nor fit kontrol yorsef, den mak yu go mari. Nor tin dey bad for dat won.
46007037	Bot e beta, if yu fit kontrol yor bodi sey yu nor won mari naw.
46007038	E dey rite and okay to mari, bot e beta sey yu nor mari at-all.
46007039	Wife sopoz to stay wit en husban ontil di man die. Den e fit go mari again, bot di new husban must bi pesin wey dey folo Kraist.
46007040	Bot I biliv sey, I dey obey God Spirit wen I sey mak di wuman nor mari, so dat e go dey hapi wel-wel.
46008001	For di leta wey una rite, una ask mi abaut juju fud. And all of us no somtin konsanin dis mata. Bot if wetin wi no, dey mak us dey proud, den bikos of luv, wi sopoz help won anoda.
46008002	Di man wey tink sey e no som tin, neva stil no as e sopoz no.
46008003	Bot God no di pesin wey luv am.
46008004	So, ivun if pipol dey offa fud giv juju, all of us no sey di juju dem nor get life, bikos na onli won God dey.
46008005	Dem dey kol meni tin for hevun and eart, "gods and mastas," bot non of dem rili bi god or masta.
46008006	Bot wi (wey bi Kristen), na onli won God wi get and naim bi awa Papa. Na-im kreate evritin and wi dey liv for am. Na Jisos Kraist bi awa onli Oga. Na-im mak evritin and na tru am wi get life.
46008007	Nor bi evribodi no dis tins. Som pipol don grow wit di biliv sey juju dey alaif. So wen dem dey chop meat wey dem giv juju, dem go dey fear.
46008008	Bot wi no sey fud nor fit bring us klose to God. Wi nor go lose enitin if wi nor chop or sey wi gain enitin if wi chop.
46008009	Bot mak una dey kareful, so dat wik pesin among una nor go fal, bikos una don dey fri to chop enitin.
46008010	Bikos if wik pesin si yu wey no di wod dey chop juju fud, e go fit join yu chop di fud wey dem sakrifais giv juju.
46008011	Den wetin yu no don distroi pesin wey Kraist die for.
46008012	If yu sin against yor brodas or sistas wey nor get strong heart and fate, yu don sin against Kraist.
46008013	So, if fud wey I dey chop go wound pesin wey dey folo Kraist, I nor go eva chop meat again, so dat my brodas and sistas nor go sin.
46009001	I nor dey fri? I nor bi apostol? Abi I neva si awa Oga Jisos? Nor bi una dey show di wok wey I don du?
46009002	If I nor bi apostol to oda pipol, at list I bi apostol to una, bikos na una bi di sign wey show sey I bi Jisos Kraist apostol.
46009003	Wen pipol ask mi kweshon, I dey tel dem sey,
46009004	mi and Banabas fit chop and drink wetin wi laik,
46009005	abi wi nor get rite to mari biliva for Kraist?
46009006	Na onli wi must wok bifor wi go chop?
46009007	E get eni soja man wey dey pay ensef salari? Abi hu plant vegetabol, nor dey chop for insaid? Or hu dey kip ship nor dey drink from dia milk?
46009008	Una tink sey na onli kommon sense I tak dey tok all dis tins? Abi una don forget sey di law tok laik dis tu?
46009009	Mosis sey, "Mak una alow anima wey grind korn chop from wetin e dey grind." So, una tink sey na di melu God dey wori for?
46009010	No! Na wi God dey tok abaut. Dem rite all dis tins for di law, so dat evribodi wey wok, go fit chop for havest taim.
46009011	So if wi don plant spiritual sid among una, e go dey tu mush if wi ask for ordinari fud and drink from una?
46009012	If odas dey du laik dis, dat min sey wi ivun get beta rite to du laik dat tu. Bot, wi dey bear evritin, so dat wi nor go kause trobol for Kraist mesage.
46009013	Una nor no sey doz wey dey wok for di Tempol dey chop fud wey pipol bring kon giv God for der? Abi una nor no sey pesin wey dey serv for alta na from der e for dey chop?
46009014	Na so tu God komand sey, doz wey dey prish di gospol, go chop tru di gospol, wey dem dey prish.
46009015	Bot I nor dey yuz all dis rite and I nor dey rite dis tins, so dat pesin go giv mi somtin. E beta mak I die, dan mak enibodi kon mak mi stop to dey tok laik dis.
46009016	Bikos if I dey prish di gospol, I nor get eni reason to boast, bikos I nor fit du eni oda tin dan to dey prish di gospol! Na wahala for mi, if I nor prish di gospol!
46009017	If I prish bikos I wont prish, dem go pay mi, bot ivun if I nor wont prish, di prishin na wetin God send mi kom du.
46009018	Wetin kon bi my gain? Na to prish di gospol witout pay or na to yuz di rite wey I get, bikos I dey prish di gospol?
46009019	I nor bi enibodi savant. Bot I don turn savant to evribodi, so dat I go fit win meni pipol for Kraist.
46009020	Wen I dey wit Ju pipol, I dey liv laik dem, so dat I go win dem for Kraist. Na Mosis law dem dey folo, bot I nor dey folo dat won. Bot I dey liv as di law tok, so dat I go win souls kom mit Kraist.
46009021	And wen I dey wit pipol wey nor dey liv by di law, I nor dey yuz di law for dem, so dat I go fit win dem. Bot dat nor min sey, I go forget God law, bikos na Kraist law dey rule mi.
46009022	Wen I dey wit pipol wey get wik fate, I dey liv as dem dey liv, so dat I go fit win dem. I dey du evritin wey I fit du, so dat I go fit win evribodi wey I fit win, kom mit Kraist.
46009023	Na di gospol mak mi dey du all dis tins, so dat I go fit share for di blessins.
46009024	Una nor no sey, wen pipol dey run, na onli won pesin go win di race and di prize? So mak una run, so dat una go fit win!
46009025	Pipol wey dey run, dey train wel-wel, so dat dem go win krawn wey nor dey last, bot wi dey run for krawn wey go last foreva.
46009026	So I nor dey run for nor-tin and I nor dey folo briz fite.
46009027	Insted, I dey kontrol my bodi kon mak am my slave, so dat afta I don prish di Gud News giv odas, God nor go rejet mi.
46010001	My brodas, I wont mak una rimemba wetin hapun to awa papa dem wey folo Mosis. God kloud protet dem as dem dey waka pas di Red Sea.
46010002	Na der dem for baptize dem wen dem dey folo Mosis wey bi God savant.
46010003	All of dem chop and drink di same spiritual
46010004	bread and milk. Dem drink from di spiritual Rock wey folo dem go and dat Rock, na Jisos Kraist.
46010005	Bot den, God nor dey hapi wit som of dem, so meni of dem kon die for insaid desert.
46010006	Naw, all dis na ezampol for us, so dat wi nor go du bad tins as dem du,
46010007	or woship juju laik som of dem. Jos as God wod sey, "Di pipol sidan to chop and drink, den dem kon start to play."
46010008	Mak wi nor folo ashawo life laik som of dem, wey mak twenti-tiri tazon pipol die for won day.
46010009	So mak wi nor tempt Kraist as som of dem dey du bifor snake kon distroi dem.
46010010	Mak una nor komplain as som of dem dey du bifor distroshon angel kon distroi dem.
46010011	Dem rite dis tins wey hapun to dem to tish us lesson and na ezampol for doz wey go dey wen di wold go end.
46010012	So pesin wey tink sey e stand, mak e tak kare, if not, e go fal.
46010013	E nor get enitin wey dey hapun to una naw, wey neva hapun to odas bifor, bot God dey kip en promis and E nor go alow una pas tru wetin una nor go fit bear.
46010014	So my brodas, mak una run from bad tins.
46010015	I dey tok to pipol wey get sense. Mak una tink abaut wetin I dey tok.
46010016	Wen wi drink from di Lord Supa cup, dat min sey wi dey share from Kraist blood. Wen wi chop from di bread wey wi divide, dat min sey wi dey share from Kraist bodi.
46010017	Bikos wi dey chop from won bread, all of us don bi won bodi, ivun doh wi meni.
46010018	Izrel pipol dey chop juju fud, bot dem stil dey share for Kraist alta.
46010019	I nor dey sey juju fud or di won wey dem sakraifais min enitin.
46010020	Bot wetin I min bi sey, wetin bad pipol dey sakrifais, na for dimon, nor bi for God.
46010021	Yu nor fit drink from God cup and dimon cup for di same taim.
46010022	Abi wi dey trai to mak Kraist ves? Wi strong pas God?
46010023	Pipol sey, wi fit du evritin. Dat na tru, bot nor bi evritin dey gud. Wi fit du evritin, bot nor bi evritin dey gud for di bodi.
46010024	Mak pesin nor dey tink for ensef alone, bot for oda pipol tu.
46010025	Mak una maind dey okay as una dey chop eni meat wey dem dey sel for market.
46010026	Bikos God wod sey, "Di eart and evritin wey dey insaid, na di Oga own."
46010027	If pesin wey nor no God invait yu kom chop for en haus, mak yu chop wetin e giv yu, nor ask kweshon, bikos of wetin dey yor maind.
46010028	Bot if di pesin tel yu sey, "Dem sakrifais dis fud giv juju," mak yu nor chop am, bikos of di pesin wey tel yu and en konscience.
46010029	I nor min yor konscience, bot di oda pesin own. So bikos of wetin anoda pesin dey tink, I nor go fit du wetin I wont du?
46010030	If I tank God for my fud, wetin go mak enibodi fite mi bikos of di fud wey I tank God for?
46010031	Bot enitin wey una dey du, weda una dey chop or drink, mak una du-am to onor God.
46010032	Liv yor life so dat yu nor go kause trobol for Ju or Greek pipol or for pipol wey dey God shosh.
46010033	Mak una dey du as I dey du; bikos I dey always trai to please evribodi insted of mysef, bikos I wont mak God save dem.
46011001	Mak una folo mi as I dey folo Kraist.
46011002	I dey praiz una, bikos una always dey du di tins wey I tel una,
46011003	bot I wont mak una undastand sey as Kraist bi evribodi head, na so tu husban bi head for en haus and na God bi Kraist head.
46011004	So eni man wey dey pray or prish God mesage kon kova en head dey woship God, dey disgrace Kraist.
46011005	And eni wuman wey dey pray or prish God mesage and e nor kova en head, dey disgrace en head, wey bi en husban; e for beta sey di wuman shave en head.
46011006	If di wuman nor won kova en hair, den mak e go shave am.
46011007	Man nor nid to kova en head, bikos e dey show as God glori bi. Bot wuman dey show as man glori bi;
46011008	bikos God nor kreate di man from wuman, bot E kreate di wuman from man.
46011009	God nor kreate man bikos of wuman, bot E kreate wuman, bikos of man.
46011010	Bikos of di angels, di wuman must kova en head to show sey na en husban dey protet am.
46011011	As wi dey serv Kraist, di wuman and di man, dey togeda for Kraist bodi.
46011012	Aldoh God mak wuman from man, bot na wuman dey born evribodi, ivun doh na God kreate evribodi.
46011013	Mak una joj by unasef weda e dey gud for wuman to dey prish God wod wen e nor kova en head.
46011014	Wetin mak pipol for di wold dey sey, na disgrace for man to kari long hair?
46011015	Bot long hair dey mak wuman fine wel-wel. God giv di wuman di long hair, so dat di hair go kova di wuman head.
46011016	Dis na haw dem dey du tins for God shosh, so nobodi go fit folo mi kworel for wetin I dey tok.
46011017	Di way una dey woship God, dey kause wahala pas di gud wey E dey du for una. Bikos of dis, I nor go fit praiz una.
46011018	Bikos I hear sey wen una gada dey woship God for shosh, na so-so kworel una dey kworel and I biliv sey som of wetin I hear, na tru.
46011019	Bikos if una nor kworel, wi nor go no di gud wons among una.
46011020	Wen una dey togeda, nor bi di Lord Supa una dey chop?
46011021	Bot bifor evribodi go rish di mitin, som of una go don start to chop and drink, wen odas dey hungri.
46011022	Una nor get haus wey una go for chop and drink? Abi una hate God shosh? Una won disgrace pipol wey nor get enitin to chop? Wetin I go fit tel una naw? I nor go fit praiz una at-all.
46011023	I don alredi tel una wetin awa Oga Jisos du for di nite wen dem sel am. And na Kraist tok am by ensef. E tak som bread for en hand
46011024	and afta e don tank God, e divide am kon sey, "Dis na my bodi wey I dey giv una. Mak una always dey chop am to rimemba mi."
46011025	Afta dem chop finish, Jisos tak di cup kon sey, "Dis na my blood wey God tak mak new kovenant wit una. Mak una always dey drink am to rimemba mi."
46011026	Jisos min sey, wen una chop di bread kon drink from di cup, una dey tel odas abaut Kraist deat ontil e go kom bak.
46011027	Bikos of dis, enibodi wey chop di bread or drink di wine enihaw wey e laik, dat pesin don sin against Kraist bodi and en blood.

46011029	Bot if una nor undastand sey na una bi Kraist bodi, una don alredi kondem unasef wit di way wey una dey chop and drink from di cup.
46011030	Na dis mak meni of una wey nor wel, wik and som among una don ivun die.
46011031	Bot if wi joj awasef, God nor go ponish us.
46011032	Bot wen God joj and ponish us, E dey du-am, so dat E nor go kondem us wit dis wold.

46011034	Bot if enibodi rili dey hungri, mak e chop kom from en haus. Den wen una dey togeda, una nor go kondem unasef. So wen I kom, I go tel una oda tins wey una sopoz no.
46012001	My frends, una bin ask mi abaut spiritual gifts.
46012002	I won mak una rimemba sey, bifor una bigin folo Kraist; na juju una dey serv.
46012003	Naw, I wont mak una no sey, enibodi wey God Spirit dey lid, go sey, Jisos naim bi Oga and e nor go eva kos am.
46012004	Na meni spiritual gifts God dey giv pipol, bot all of dem na from di same Spirit.
46012005	And wi get difren ways to serv God
46012006	and ish of us dey du difren tins. Bot na di same God dey wok for awa life and E dey help us du evritin.
46012007	Ish of us get difren gift wey di Spirit giv us and wi dey yuz am du gud.
46012008	Som of us dey fit speak wit wisdom and odas wit knowledge, bot na di same Spirit dey giv us all dis gifts.
46012009	To oda pipol, di same Spirit dey giv dem fate or di pawa to heal sik pipol.
46012010	Di Spirit dey giv odas di pawa to du mirakol and e mak som pipol profets and som of us dey fit no wen God Spirit dey among us. Odas dey tok wit difren-difren language and som of us go tel una wetin di tins wey dem dey tok min.
46012011	Bot na di same Spirit dey du all dis tins and e dey shuz di kaind gift wey e wont giv ish pesin.
46012012	Kraist bodi get difren part laik evri oda bodi.
46012013	Som of us na Ju and odas na Gentai. Som of us na slave and odas dey fri. Bot God Spirit baptiaz us kon mak us part for Jisos Kraist bodi. Naw, all of us dey drink from dat same Spirit.
46012014	Nor bi onli won part awa bodi get, bot dem meni.
46012015	If di leg for awa bodi sey, "I nor bi hand, so I nor bi part for di bodi." Nor bi di bodi di leg stil dey?
46012016	And if di ear sey, "I nor bi eye, so I nor bi part for di bodi." Nor bi di bodi di ear stil dey?
46012017	If to sey di hol bodi na eye, wi nor for fit hear enitin and if to sey all di bodi na ear, wi nor for fit smel enitin.
46012018	Bot God don put evri part for awa bodi, jos as E wont am.
46012019	If na onli won part dey di bodi, den di bodi nor go bi as e sopoz bi again.
46012020	Bot as e bi so, na meni parts dey mak won bodi.
46012021	So, di eye nor go fit tel di hand sey, "I nor nid yu" and di head nor go fit tel di leg sey, "I nor nid yu tu."
46012022	So, wi nor go fit du enitin wit awa bodi witout di part wey wi feel sey, e dey wik.
46012023	Di part wey wi tink sey dey important, wi dey trit dem wit respet and di part wey nor rili dey outsaid, wi dey trit dem wel.
46012024	Bot awa bodi nor nid all dis treatment. Bikos na God mak awa bodi, so di part wey wi fit sey nor dey important, dey important wel-wel.
46012025	God du-am laik dis, so dat all di parts for di bodi go dey wok togeda and ish part go dey kare for oda part.
46012026	If won part dey sofa, di oda parts dey sofa tu. Bot if dem praiz won part, di oda parts go dey hapi.
46012027	All of una dey Kraist bodi. And ish of una, na part for di bodi.
46012028	So for di shosh, God first shuz apostols, bifor profets and tishas. E stil shuz som wey dey du mirakol, odas wey dey heal sik pipol, som wey bi lidas and odas wey dey tok wit difren-difren language.
46012029	Nor bi evribodi bi apostol. Nor bi evribodi bi tisha. Nor bi evribodi fit du mirakol.
46012030	Nor bi evribodi fit heal sik pipol. Nor bi evribodi fit tok wetin dis language min.
46012031	Bot I wont mak una ask for di gift wey beta pas, so dat I go show una di way wey beta pas all dis tins.
46013001	If I dey tok di language wey humanbin and angels dey tok,
46013002	if I dey profesai and fit undastand evri sikrit and knowledge or if I get fate wey fit move mountins and I nor luv oda pipol, I go bi nor-tin.
46013003	If I giv pipol evritin wey I get kon sey mak dem burn mi alaif, bot I nor luv odas, I nor go gain enitin.
46013004	Luv dey kaind and patient, e nor dey jelos or boast
46013005	or dey proud. Luv nor get long-trot or dey ves. E nor dey rimemba di bad tins wey odas du.
46013006	E nor dey hapi wit wiked pipol, bot e dey hapi wit di trut.
46013007	Luv dey bear evritin and e get fate, hope and patient.
46013008	Luv nor dey fail and e go dey foreva. Pipol nor go profesai foreva and doz wey dey tok wit difren-difren language, go stop. For dat taim, wi go forget evritin wey wi no.
46013009	Naw, wi nor no evritin and awa profesi nor komplit.
46013010	Bot won day, wetin dey pafet go kom and wetin nor dey pafet, go vanish.
46013011	Wen wi neva no Kraist, wi dey tink and tok laik smol shildren. Bot naw wen wi don no am, wi nor dey du laik smol shildren again.
46013012	Evritin wey wi dey si naw bi laik ordinari image for mirror; bot for dat taim, wi go si-am, face to face. Naw wi nor no evritin, bot den wi go no, jos as God rili no us.
46013013	And naw wi get fate, hope and luv. Bot di won wey big pas for di tiri, na luv.
46014001	Na luv sopoz gaid una. So mak una dey fite to get di gift wey di Holi Spirit dey giv, especiali di gift to profesai.
46014002	Bikos if una dey tok wit difren-difren language wey odas nor undastand, God go undastand wetin una dey tok, aldoh no oda pesin go no wetin e min. Tins wey una go dey tok abaut, na onli di Spirit go fit undastand dem.
46014003	Bot wen una profesai, pipol go undastand una and odas go help una. Dem go get komfort kon dey okay.
46014004	Pesin wey dey tok wit difren language, dey help ensef. Bot di won wey dey profesai, dey help di shosh.
46014005	I for laik mak all of una dey tok wit difren language, bot I wont mak una dey profesai. Bikos profesi go du una more gud, dan sey una dey tok wit difren language wey pipol nor fit undastand, unles sombodi esplain di minin giv di pipol for di shosh.
46014006	My brodas and sistas, wetin una go gain if wen I kom, I dey tok wit difren language wey una nor undastand and I nor esplain am? Haw I go fit help una den, unles I tel una wetin God tel mi or mak una no wetin dem profesai and tish?
46014007	If all muzik instrument get di same sound, haw una go tak no di won wey bi trumpet or harp?
46014008	If trumpet mak sound wey pipol nor undastand, hu go dey redi to go fite war?
46014009	Na so e bi wen una dey tok wit difren-difren language wey pipol nor undastand. If nobodi fit undastand wetin una dey tok abaut, dat min sey na briz una dey folo tok.
46014010	Dis wold get difren language and all of dem dey mak sense.
46014011	Bot if odas nor undastand wetin una tok, den dem go bi laik stranjas to una.
46014012	Na so e bi wit una tu. If una rili wont di gift wey di Spirit dey giv, mak una shuz di won wey di shosh go gain from.
