46014013	So wen wi tok wit difren-difren language wey odas nor undastand, mak wi pray mak God giv us di pawa to esplain wetin e min.
46014014	For ezampol, if I pray wit language wey nobodi undastand, my spirit dey pray, bot my maind nor undastand di tins wey I dey pray for.
46014015	So wetin I go du? Bikos e get taim wey I go pray wit my spirit and taim wey I sopoz pray wit my maind. Somtaims, I sopoz sing wit my spirit and oda taim, I go sing wit my maind.
46014016	If som stranjas dey for wer una for dey woship God for spirit and dem nor undastand una, haw dem go tak no wen to sey, "Amen"?
46014017	Una fit rili dey woship God wel-wel, bot nobodi go gain from am, bikos dem nor undastand wetin una dey tok.
46014018	I tank God sey I dey tok wit difren-difren language pas all of una.
46014019	Bot wen I dey shosh, e beta mak I speak faiv beta wods to tish odas, dan to speak ten tazon wods wey pipol nor undastand.
46014020	My brodas and sistas, mak una stop to tink laik smol shildren. Insted mak una dey tink laik mature pipol and inosent laik pikin wey dem jos born.
46014021	God wod sey: "I go yuz stranjas wey dey speak wetin odas nor undastand, tak tok to my pipol. Dem go tok to dem wit stranj language, bot my pipol nor go listin to mi."
46014022	So, language wey odas nor undastand, fit min somtin to pipol wey nor biliv, bot nor bi to pipol wey biliv.
46014023	So if di hol shosh bigin tok wit difren-difren language, den som pipol wey bi unbilivas or doz wey nor undastand kon waka enta di shosh, dem nor go tink sey all of una don dey krase?
46014024	Bot if evribodi dey profesai and unbilivas or pipol wi nor undastand enta di shosh, dem go no sey dem bi sinas and dem go won turn kom mit God, bikos of wetin una dey tok.
46014025	Den God go tel una di sikrit wey dey dia heart. Den dem go nil dan kon tel God sey, "Wi don rili biliv sey Yu dey wit dis pipol."
46014026	My frends, wen una gada to woship, una must du evritin to help won anoda. Na so e sopoz bi wen sombodi dey tish, sing, profesai, tok wit difren-difren language or dey esplain wetin di pesin tok.
46014027	Wen una dey togeda, mak e nor pas tu or tiri pipol wey go tok wit difren-difren language wey pipol nor undastand. Won pesin go tok, bifor anoda and mak pesin dey, wey go esplain giv odas wetin di pesin dey tok.
46014028	If nobodi dey wey go fit esplain wetin yu dey tok, mak yu nor tok at-all for di mitin, bot yu fit tok am bitwin yu and God.
46014029	Tu or tiri pesin fit profesai and evri oda pesin must listin wel-wel.
46014030	And if won among di pipol wey sidan risiv mesage from God, di pesin wey dey tish must stop mak di pesin for tok.
46014031	Mak di pipol nor tok at once, so dat all of una go learn somtin and una go dey okay.
46014032	Pesin wey bi profet must dey redi to stop, so dat anoda pesin go tok, bikos profet sopoz to fit kontrol en own spirit,
46014033	bikos God wont mak dem du evritin wel. Wen God pipol mit for shosh,
46014034	mak wimen nor dey tok. Mak dem kwayet dey listin, jos as Mosis law tish.
46014035	If dem won no abaut somtin, dem fit ask dia husban wen dem rish haus. Bikos na disgrace for wuman to tok for shosh.
46014036	God mesage nor start wit una and nor bi onli una don hear am.
46014037	If una dey tink of unasef as profet or pesin wey di Spirit dey yuz, den una go no sey I dey rite onli di tins wey God komand mi.
46014038	So mak una nor listin to enibodi wey nor biliv wetin I dey rite.
46014039	My frends, mak una dey trai to profesai and mak una nor stop enibodi wey dey tok wit difren-difren language ivun doh odas nor undastand wetin e dey tok.
46014040	Bot mak una dey du tins as e sopoz to bi.
46015001	My brodas and sistas, I wont mak una rimemba di gospol wey I prish giv una,
46015002	di won wey una asept and dey stand on. Na dis gospol go save una, if una hol di mesage wey I prish giv una wel-wel, unles una biliv nor strong.
46015003	Bikos na wetin I risiv, naim bi di first important tin wey I giv una; sey Kraist die for awa sins as dem rite for God wod
46015004	and dem bere am, den God raiz-am up afta tiri days as dem rite for God wod.
46015005	Kraist apier to Pita, den to di twef apostols.
46015006	Den e apier to more dan faiv ondred bilivas. Som of dem stil dey alaif, bot som don die.
46015007	Den e apier to James, den to all di apostols.
46015008	Finali, e apier to mi; ivun doh I bi laik pikin wey dem born last.
46015009	Na mi smol pas among di apostols. Bot, I kause meni wahala for God shosh, so dem nor sopoz kol mi apostol.
46015010	Bot God kaind! I bi wetin I bi and God mesi for mi, nor bi yeye tin. I dey wok pas eni oda apostol; aldoh na God grace dey help mi.
46015011	Bot e nor min enitin if I prish or dem prish, as long as all of una biliv di mesage wey wi dey prish.
46015012	Naw, if wi dey prish sey God raiz Jisos from deat, wetin mak som of una dey sey resureshon nor dey?
46015013	If resureshon nor dey, dat min sey Kraist nor raiz-up from grave.
46015014	And if Kraist nor raiz-up, den awa prishin and una fate nor min enitin.
46015015	So, if resureshon nor dey, dat min sey, evritin wey wi don tok abaut God, na lai, bikos wi sey E raiz Jisos from deat wen E nor raiz-am.
46015016	If resureshon nor dey, na-im bi sey Kraist nor raiz-up from deat.
46015017	If God nor raiz Kraist from grave, den una fate dey yuzles and una stil dey insaid una sin.
46015018	And doz wey biliv Kraist bifor dem die, don loss bi dat.
46015019	Bikos if na onli for dis life wi get hope for Kraist, den awa kase wos pas eni oda pesin own for dis wold.
46015020	Bot God don raiz Kraist from deat! And E mak us dey sure sey, oda pipol go raiz-up from deat tu.
46015021	Jos as pipol go die bikos of Adam, na so tu wi go raiz-up kom life, bikos of Kraist.
46015022	Adam bring deat kom mit all of us, bot Kraist bring life kom.
46015023	Bot all of us must wait for awa turn. Na Kraist God first raiz kom life and Kraist go raiz en pipol wen e kom bak.
46015024	Den afta Kraist don distroi all pawas, di wold go end and e go giv di kindom to God wey bi di Papa.
46015025	Kraist go rule ontil e don put all en enemis unda en pawa
46015026	and di last enemi wey e go distroi, na deat.
46015027	Wen God wod sey, e go put evritin unda en pawa, e nor min sey, God dey among dem. Bikos na God put evritin unda Jisos Kraist pawa.
46015028	And wen evritin don dey unda God pikin pawa, e go kon put ensef unda God wey put evritin unda en pikin pawa. Den God go kon bi evritin to evribodi.
46015029	If resureshon nor dey, wetin mak dem dey baptaiz pipol for kraist?
46015030	And wetin mak us dey risk awa life
46015031	kon dey face deat evriday? Na di pride wey I get for una, bikos of awa Oga Jisos Kraist, naim mak mi dey tok all dis tins.
46015032	If resureshon nor dey, wetin kon bi my gain, afta I don fite wiked anima for Efisos? Na bikos of pride mak mi du-am? If na so, e go gud mak wi dey chop and drink bikos tumoro wi go die.
46015033	Mak una nor let enibodi disiv una, "Bad frends dey spoil gud karata."
46015034	Mak una get sense and stop to dey komit sin. I stil dey sopraiz sey som of una nor no God.
46015035	Som of una dey ask sey, "Haw pipol wey don die go tak kom dis wold bak? Wish kaind bodi dem go get?
46015036	Una bi fool! Wetin pesin plant nor dey grow, unles di sid first die.
46015037	Wetin una plant, na ordinari sid, bot na di ful plant dey grow kom out.
46015038	Dis na bikos God dey giv dem di kaind bodi wey E wont mak di plant get.
46015039	Pipol, animas, birds and fish, na flesh God tak mak all of dem, bot all of dem get difren flesh.
46015040	As evritin for hevun get bodi, na so tu evritin for dis eart get bodi. Bot won bodi difren from di oda wons.
46015041	Di sun nor bi laik di moon; di moon nor bi laik di star and di stars difren from ish oda.
46015042	Na so e go bi afta wi don raiz-up from deat. Dis bodi wey wi get naw, go die, bot di bodi wey wi go tak raiz from deat, go dey foreva.
46015043	Dis awa bodi wey nor fine, dey wik and go rotin, go kon fine, strong and go dey foreva.
46015044	As fisica bodi dey, na so tu spiritual bodi dey. And awa fisica bodi go shange to spiritual bodi.
46015045	Di first man na Adam and God wod sey, "Dis Adam na pesin wey God kreate laik us." Bot Jisos, wey bi di last Adam, na pesin wey dey giv life to pipol."
46015046	Wi si sey di won wey get spiritual bodi nor first kom. E kom afta di won wey get fisica bodi.
46015047	Na sand God tak mak di first man, bot di sekon man kom from hevun.
46015048	Evribodi bodi for eart, bi laik di first man and evribodi bodi for hevun, bi laik di sekon man own.
46015049	Jos as wi bi laik di first man wey kom from eart, wi go bi laik di sekon man wey kom from hevun.
46015050	My frends, I wont mak una no sey awa bodi wey get blood go rotin. Dat min sey dis kaind bodi, nor go fit enta God kindom wey go dey foreva.
46015051	I won tel una won big sikrit: Nor bi all of us go die, bot all of us go shange.
46015052	Bifor wi klose awa eye opun am, e go don hapun. As dem dey blow di last trumpet, all doz wey don die go raiz. All of us go shange, so dat wi nor go die again.
46015053	Awa bodi wey don die and rotin go kon shange to bodi wey nor go eva die or rotin.
46015054	Di bodi wey wi get naw, dey wik and e go die. Bot God go shange am to bodi wey go dey foreva. So wetin dem rite for God wod go kon hapun sey, "Deat nor fit win di fite!
46015055	"Yu deat! Wer yor pawa? Yu deat! Haw yu go tak shaut sey yu win?"
46015056	Na sin dey mak deat win and na di law dey kause sin.
46015057	So, mak wi tank God wey giv us victori tru awa Oga Jisos Kraist.
46015058	So my frends, mak una dey strong and nor let enitin shake una. Mak una always dey du God wok, bikos una no sey, evritin wey una du for God, get gain.
46016001	Wen una kolet moni from God pipol, I wont mak una du as I tel di pipol wey dey di shosh for Galatia sey mak dem du.
46016002	Evri Sunday, mak ish pesin dey kip som moni for kona from di won wey e don wok, as God help am rish, so dat una nor go nid to kolet moni wen I kom.
46016003	Wen I kom, I go send pipol wey una shuz kon giv dem leta as dem dey kari una gifts go Jerusalem.
46016004	Bot if una sey mak I go tu, den, dem go folo mi go.
46016005	And afta I don finish for Masidonia, I hope to kom si
46016006	and stay wit una for somtaim. May-bi I fit stay til dry season finish, so dat una go fit help mi for eniwer wey I won go.
46016007	If God go let mi, I nor go won bransh si una for smol taim naw, bikos I go laik kom lata, so dat I go fit spend more taim wit una.
46016008	Bot I go stay for Efisos ontil Pentecost go finish,
46016009	bikos plenti wok dey wait for mi for der, ivun doh di shalenge strong wel-wel.
46016010	Wen Timoti kom, mak una nor mak am fear at-all, bikos na God wok wey I dey du, naim e dey du tu.
46016011	So mak evribodi respet am, den mak una send am kom mit mi wit peace, bikos I dey espet am wit di oda brodas.
46016012	I don trai wel-wel mak Apollos for fit folo oda bilivas kom visit una, e nor won kom naw, bot e go kom lata.
46016013	Mak una shine una eye and dey strong for fate and stand wit boldnes.
46016014	For evritin wey una dey du, mak una dey show luv.
46016015	Una no sey na Stefanas and en famili first biliv God for Akaya. Dem don du evritin wey dem fit du for God pipol. My frends, I wont mak una
46016016	dey obey dis lidas and doz wey dey folo una du God wok.
46016017	I dey hapi sey Stefanas, Fortunatus and Akaicus don kom; dem kom represent una
46016018	and dem don let bele swit mi, jos as dem mak bele swit una. E gud mak wi dey tok abaut pipol laik dem.
46016019	Pipol for di shosh wey dey Asia aria dey grit una; Akwila and Prisila wit di shosh pipol wey dey mit for dia haus, dey grit una tu.
46016020	All di brodas sey mak I grit una.
46016021	Na mi Pol, rite dis leta wit my own hand.
46016022	Enibodi wey nor luv Kraist, kos dey en head!
46016023	Mak awa Oga Jisos Kraist grace dey wit una.
46016024	Mak my luv for Jisos Kraist, dey wit all of una tu.
47001001	Pol, wey bi Jisos Kraist apostol, bikos na so God wont am, naim and Timoti awa broda, rite dis leta go giv God pipol for di shosh wey dey Korint and to all di gud brodas for Akaya.
47001002	Mak God awa Papa and Oga Jisos Kraist giv una grace and peace.
47001003	Mak wi tank God wey bi awa Oga Jisos Kraist Papa, di God wey dey giv mesi and komfort,
47001004	E dey help us wen wi dey trobol, so dat wi go fit help odas tru di help wey E help us.
47001005	Jos as wi sofa wit Kraist, na so tu wi go get help from God tru Kraist.
47001006	If wi sofa, na for una gud and savashon; if wi dey okay, den una go fit bear di kaind sofa wey wi bear.
47001007	So, wi get hope abaut una, bikos wi no sey as una dey folo us sofa, na so una go stil folo us get komfort.
47001008	My brodas and sistas, wi wont mak una no abaut di wahala wey wi face for Asia aria. Di trobol wey wi face, heavi wel-wel and life kon taya us.
47001009	Tru-tru, wi tink sey wi go die. Bot dis hapun so dat wi nor go jos trust awasef, bot wi go trust God wey dey wak pipol from deat.
47001010	E save us from deat and E go diliva us. Wi don put awa hope for en hand sey E go diliva us again.
47001011	As una don join dey pray for us, na so tu God go ansa all di meni prayas wey una dey pray for us, den E go bless us and meni pipol go kon tank am, bikos of wetin E dey du for us.
47001012	Wi dey hapi, bikos wi no sey di way wi dey liv awa life for dis wold and haw wi dey bihav wit una, dey show sey na God send us tru en pawa, nor bi humanbin own.
47001013	Bikos evritin wey I rite, na wetin una go fit read and undastand. Bot I hope sey una go undastand am wel,
47001014	jos as una don undastand us rish and na wi mak una dey proud and na una go mak us proud tu, for di day wey Jisos go kom.
47001015	Na wit dis maind I bi won kom mit una bifor, so dat wi go bless una again.
47001016	Bikos I plan to visit una wen I dey go Masidonia and wen I dey kom bak, so dat una go help mi wen I dey travol go Judea.
47001017	So, wen I dey plan dis tins, I nor tink bifor I du-am? Wen I dey plan, I dey plan bikos of wetin I wont? Or na bikos I redi to sey, "Yes, yes" or "No, no" at wons?
47001018	Bot as God dey fateful, wetin wi dey prish giv una nor bi mak e for bi jos "Yes" or " No."
47001019	Bikos God Pikin, Jisos Kraist, di Won wey mi, Silvanus and Timoti dey prish giv una, nor bi "Yes" and "No". Bot from biginin, na Jisos bi God "Yes".
47001020	And evritin wey God promis us, na "Yes" tru Jisos Kraist. Dat na why awa "Amen" tru Jisos Kraist dey giv God glori.
47001021	Na God mak wi and una dey sure sey wi dey insaid Kraist. Na God shuz us from odas
47001022	and E don mark us as en own kon put en Spirit for awa heart, so dat wi go dey sure of all di oda tins wey E sey E go giv us.
47001023	Na God bi my witnes, bikos E no my heart! Na bikos I nor won disturb una naim mak mi nor go Korint again.
47001024	Wi nor dey trai to fos una to biliv us; wi no sey una fate strong wel-wel. Bot wi dey wok wit una so dat una go dey hapi wel-wel.
47002001	So I sey I nor go kom visit una, so dat una nor go ves again.
47002002	Bikos if I mak una ves, hu go mak mi dey hapi apart from una wey dey ves for mi?
47002003	Na dis mak mi rite dis tin giv una, so dat wen I kom, I nor go kon dey ves for di pipol wey sopoz mak mi hapi, bikos I no sey if I dey hapi, una go dey hapi tu.
47002004	Na pain for my heart I tak rite dis leta giv una, nor bi to mak una ves, bot na to let una no di kaind luv wey I get for una.
47002005	Naw if enibodi don mak pesin ves, nor bi onli mi e mak ves, bot na all of una.(I dey tok laik dis bikos I nor won tu ves for di pesin).
47002006	Di way wey una ponish dis pesin, don rish.
47002007	So mak una forgiv and help am, so dat e nor go luz hope and life nor go taya am.
47002008	So mak una let am no sey una rili luv am.
47002009	I rite dis leta giv una, so dat I go no weda una dey obey wetin I tel una.
47002010	Wen una forgiv pesin for wetin e du, misef go forgiv am. Bikos wen I forgiv (if I rili nid to forgiv), I du-am for Kraist present, bikos of una,
47002011	so dat Satan nor go disiv us, bikos wi no en wayo.
47002012	Wen I go prish di Gud News for Troas, ivun doh Kraist opun door for mi,
47002013	my maind nor res, bikos I nor si awa broda, Titus, for der. So I liv der kon go Masidonia.
47002014	Bot mak wi tank God wey mak us winnas insaid Kraist. Bikos tru us, meni pipol don no tins abaut Kraist, laik beta perfume wey dey smel for evriwer.
47002015	Bikos wi bi laik swit insent wey Kraist offa giv God wey dey spread among doz wey dey save and doz wey don lost.
47002016	To doz wey don lost, e bi laik somtin wey dey kil; bot for doz wey Kraist don save, e bi laik smel wey dey giv life. So, hu go fit handol all dis tins?
47002017	Wi nor bi laik odas wey dey du God wod laik sey na som tin wey dem fit sel; bot bikos na God sent us kom, wi dey tok di trut for en present, as Kraist savant.
47003001	Wi don dey boast abaut awasef again? Wi nor nid una to rite sey, wi dey gud, ivun doh odas dey wont am laik dat!
47003002	Na una bi di leta wey Kraist rite for awa heart, wey evribodi no and dey read.
47003003	E klear sey na Kraist rite dis leta by ensef kon send am tru us. Nor bi ink dem tak rite am, bot di God wey dey alaif, naim Spirit dem tak rite am, nor bi for paper, bot na for awa heart.
47003004	Wi get dis kaind maind for God, bikos of Jisos Kraist.
47003005	Wi nor dey sey wi go fit du all dis tins by awasef, bot na God giv us di pawa wey wi tak du dem.
47003006	Na God mak us fit du dem, so dat wi go serv di new kovenant; dis nor bi di law wey dem rite, bot na di won wey konsan God Spirit, bikos di law wey dem rite dey bring deat, bot di Spirit dey giv life.
47003007	Di ministri wey dem rite for slate bring deat kom and di glori wey folo am, nor let Izrel pipol fit luk Mosis face. If di glori wey dey Mosis face, fade bikos e dey unda di law,
47003008	den haw di Spirit ministri wey get glori, go kon bi, since e nor dey fade?
47003009	Bikos if glori dey for di law wey mak God kondem pipol, den di Spirit glori wey dey giv life, na haw E go beta rish?
47003010	Wetin get glori naw, nor get glori again, bikos di glori wey di Spirit wey dey kom afta am get, big wel-wel.
47003011	If Mosis face get glori, den haw di glori wey dey di Pesin face wey nor dey die, go bi?
47003012	Na dis hope wi get, naim dey mak us tok witout fear.
47003013	Wi nor bi laik Mosis wey tak klot kova en face, so dat Izrel pipol nor go si di glori wey go fade komot.
47003014	Bot dia maind dey klose. And til today, dia maind stil blok wen dem dey read di old kovenant. Dem neva rimov am, bikos na for onli Kraist bodi, dem go fit tak rimov am.
47003015	So til today, enitaim wey dem read wetin Mosis rite, somtin dey kova dia maind,
47003016	bot wen pesin turn kom mit God, dat tin go komot from en life.
47003017	Na God bi di Spirit and eniwer en Spirit dey, pipol go dey fri.
47003018	All of us wey don biliv Kraist, God glori dey show for awa face. So di Spirit dey help us shange, so dat wi go bi laik Kraist.
47004001	So as wi get dis ministri, jos as God don show us mesi, awa hope don strong wel-wel.
47004002	Bot wi don stop to dey du wiked tins wey pipol dey hide dey du; wi nor dey du wayo or lai join God wod, bot wit trut wey evribodi fit si, wi dey mak evribodi no for dia maind sey, wetin wi dey du, dey gud for God eye.
47004003	Bot ivun if dem yuz klot tak kova di gospol wey wi dey prish, doz wey don lost, na onli dem nor go si-am,
47004004	bikos doz wey nor biliv, di gods for dis taim don blind dia maind, so dem nor go si lite wey dey dis gospol wey get glori and dis gospol na Kraist wey bi God image.
47004005	Wi nor dey tok abaut awasef, bot wi dey prish sey, na Jisos Kraist bi Oga and wi bi una slave, bikos of am.
47004006	Bikos God wey sey, "Mak lite shine from daknes," Na-im dey shine insaid awa heart, so dat E go giv us di lite wey show us en glori wey dey Kraist face.
47004007	Bot dis beta tin wey God giv us, wi dey kari am for insaid awa bodi wey dey die laik clay pot wey dey break and na God giv us di pawa.
47004008	Wi dey face wahala for difren kona, bot awa bodi nor skata; wi dey konfuz somtaim, bot wi nor dey luz hope,
47004009	pipol dey ponish us, bot God nor let us die; dem dey nak us for groun, bot dem nor fit distroi us.
47004010	As wi dey waka, wi kari Kraist deat for awa bodi, so dat pipol go si Jisos life for awa bodi tu.
47004011	As wi dey alaif, dem always dey won kil us bikos of Jisos Kraist, so dat dem go si Jisos life for awa ordinari bodi.
47004012	Bikos of dis, deat dey wok insaid us, bot life dey wok insaid una.
47004013	Bot as e bi sey wi get di same spirit wey dey giv fate, jos as dem rite sey, "I biliv; naim mak mi dey tok." Derfor wi sef biliv, naim mak us dey tok tu.
47004014	Wi du laik dis, bikos wi no sey di Pesin wey raiz-up Jisos, go stil raiz us up wit Jisos and E go tak wi and una enta en kindom.
47004015	All dis tins na for una gud, so dat God grace wey dey rish meni pipol evriday, go mak pipol dey tank God more-more and all di glori go bi en own.
47004016	So, mak wi nor luz hope, bikos ivun if awa bodi dey die go smol-smol, di Pesin wey dey insaid us, dey fresh evriday.
47004017	Bikos di smol trobol wey wi dey face naw, go bring glori wey big wel-wel, wey go last foreva and wey beta pas enitin for dis wold.
47004018	Wi nor dey luk for wetin eye fit si, bot na wetin eye nor fit si. Bikos wetin eye fit si nor go last, bot di tins wey eye nor fit si, dey last foreva.
47005001	Wi no sey if dis awa haus for eart, wey bi awa bodi skata, God get di won wey wi go stay, wey e bi sey nor bi humanbin hand build am and e go last foreva for hevun.
47005002	Bikos for dis awa haus for eart, wi dey strogol, bikos wi nor fit wait to wear awa new bodi for hevun.
47005003	Afta wi don wear awa new bodi for hevun, wi nor go dey naked again.
47005004	Wi dey strogol as wi dey dis awa bodi. Wi dey kari heavi load, bikos wi nor won rimov di klot wey bi awa bodi, bot wi won wear hevun own join am, so dat life go swalow dis awa bodi wey fit die.
47005005	Naw, di Pesin wey priper us for dis tins, na God wey giv us di Spirit, so dat wi go dey sure of all di oda tins wey E get for us.
47005006	So, wi dey always get maind and wi no sey, as long as wi dey alaif for dis eart, wi nor dey wer God dey,
47005007	bikos wi dey liv awa life wit fate, nor bi wit wetin wi dey si.
47005008	So wi dey always get di maind sey wi go die komot from dis wold, so dat wi go-go stay wit Jisos Kraist for wer e dey.
47005009	So, weda wi dey alaif or wi don die, wi dey du evritin wey wi fit du to mak Kraist hapi.
47005010	Bikos all of us must stand for Kraist front and e go joj us akordin to di tins wey wi du wen wi dey dis eart; weda dem gud or bad.
47005011	So, bikos wi no wetin e min to fear God, naim mak us dey prish and beg pipol. Bot God no us wel-wel and I hope sey una no us wel-wel for una maind tu.
47005012	Wi nor dey trai to tok mak una for sey wi dey gud, bot wi dey giv una shanse to boast, so dat una go fit ansa pipol wey dey boast wit wetin eye fit si, bot nor bi wetin dey dia maind.
47005013	If wi dey krase, na bikos of God; bot if wi nor dey krase, na bikos of una.
47005014	Bikos na Kraist luv dey kontrol us since wi no sey, Kraist die for evribodi; so evribodi don die.
47005015	And e die for evribodi, so dat evribodi wey dey liv nor go liv for diasef again, bot for di Pesin wey die and wak-up afta tiri days.
47005016	So naw, wi nor dey luk enibodi laik odinari humanbin. Ivun doh wi bin no Kraist laik dat bifor, wi nor no am laik dat again.
47005017	So, if eni man dey insaid Kraist, e don dey new, Kraist don klin di bad tins wey e du bifor and evritin don turn to new won!
47005018	All dis tins dey kom from God wey mak us en frends bikos of Kraist and E stil giv us di ministri wey go mak pipol bi en frend.
47005019	So, bikos of Kraist, God dey turn di wold from en enimi, to en frend. E nor dey kount pipol sins against dem and E don giv us di mesage wey go mak pipol bi en frend.
47005020	Wi dey represent Kraist, so dat God go tok to una, tru us. Wi dey beg una bikos of Kraist sey, "Mak una shange kon bi God frend!"
47005021	Di Won wey nor dey sin, God mak am awa sin, so dat insaid am, wi go kon dey gud for God eye.
47006001	Naw, bikos wi bi felow wokas, wi dey beg una mak una nor waste God grace wey una don risiv.
47006002	Bikos E sey, "I hear una for di rite taim and wen di day for Mi to save una rish, I help una." Si, na di rite taim bi dis; na naw bi di day for salvashon!
47006003	Wi nor dey du enitin wey go mak enibodi ves, so dat nobodi go si eni fault for awa wok.
47006004	Bot wi dey show sey wi bi God savant for evritin wey wi dey du. Wi dey sofa wel-wel and face trobol for dis taim; ivun for wiked taims;
47006005	for di taim wey dem dey beat us and put us for prizin; for di taim wey dem dey fite; for wahala taim; for nite wey wi nor fit slip and for hungri taim.
47006006	Wi dey du all dis tins wit awa klin life, di tins wey wi no; di patient wey wi get; di gud wey wi dey du for pipol; di Holi Spirit wey wi get; beta luv wey wi show pipol;
47006007	tru di wod wey wi dey tish wit God pawa; wit wetin wi tak dey difend awa raitiousnes both for awa rite and left hand;
47006008	for di taim wey dem onor or disgrace us; for di taim wen dem tok bad abaut us or praiz us; di taim wey dem du us laik sey wi dey tok lai, bot wi dey tok trut.
47006009	Dat taim, e bi laik sey nobodi no us, bot evribodi no us; e bi laik sey wi dey die, bot wi dey alaif; wi stil dey alaif laik pipol wey dem dey ponish, bot dem nor fit kil us;
47006010	wi dey laik sey wi dey ves, bot wi dey always hapi; wi bi laik poor pipol, bot wi dey mak meni pipol rish; wi bi laik hu nor get enitin, bot wi get evritin.
47006011	So, una wey bi Korint pipol, wi don opun awa heart tel una evritin.
47006012	Wi nor dey hol awa luv from una, bot na una dey hol una luv from us.
47006013	So mak wi mak am equal. I dey tok to una laik sey una bi my shildren, so mak una opun una heart for us tu.
47006014	Mak una nor mak frend wit pipol wey nor biliv, bikos, na wish kaind frend raitiousnes and bad tin won bi, or na wetin lite and daknes get togeda?
47006015	And na wish kaind agriment Kraist and devol get? Wetin konsan pesin wey biliv and pesin wey nor biliv?
47006016	Wish kaind biznes God tempol and juju get? Bikos wi bi God tempol, jos as God sey, "I go stay insaid dem and waka among dem, den, I go bi dia God and dem go bi my pipol."
47006017	Kraist stil sey, "Mak una kom out and seprate unasef from dem," and "Mak una nor tosh enitin wey nor dey klin, den I go welkom una
47006018	kon bi una Papa and una go bi my shildren." Na so God wey get all di pawa, tok.
47007001	So, as God don promis us all dis tins, mak wi wosh awasef komot from evritin wey go fit mak awa bodi or awa soul dirti, so dat wi go dey holi as wi dey respet God.
47007002	Mak una alow di gospol enta una heart bikos wi nor du bad to enibodi or fal enibodi biznes or play enibodi wayo.
47007003	I nor dey tok dis won to kondem una, bikos I don tel una bifor sey, una dey awa maind and wi wit una go die and liv togeda wit Kraist.
47007004	For insaid all dis sofa wey wi dey sofa, I stil trust and dey boast wel-wel abaut una, bikos I get maind for una and my hapines ful dey trowey.
47007005	Ivun wen wi enta Masidonia, wi nor res at-all, bot dem trobol us from difren kona; wahala for outsaid, fear for insaid.
47007006	Bot God wey dey help pipol wey nor hapi, naim kon help us wen Titus kom.
47007007	Wi kon dey hapi, nor bi onli sey Titus kom, bot bikos of di advise wey una giv am, bikos e tel us haw una won si mi; haw una dey ves and wori for mi and my hapines kon pas as e bi bifor.
47007008	Bikos ivun if I mak una ves wit my leta, e nor pain mi sey I rite am (ivun doh e pain mi as I no sey e mak una ves, aldoh una vesnashon nor tey).
47007009	Naw I dey hapi, nor bi bikos una dey ves, bot bikos una vesnashon mak una turn from sin kom mit God. Na so God plan una vesnashon, so dat bad tins nor go hapun to una bikos of dis vesnashon wey wi kause for una.
47007010	Bikos wen God mak pipol sori for di sin wey dem komit, dem go turn kom mit am, den God go save dem and dem nor go rigret again. Bot di vesnashon wey dis wold dey bring, na deat dey end am.
47007011	Naw, mak una si wetin dis vesnashon wey God plan don du for una: si haw una wok for God bi naw; si haw una won show sey una hand klin; si as una dey ves bikos of di bad tin wey hapun; si haw una dey sopraiz; si as una dey won si and wori abaut us; si haw una redi to ponish enibodi wey du bad! For evritin, una don show sey una hand klin for dis mata.
47007012	I nor rite dis leta giv una bikos of di pesin wey du bad or di pesin wey dem du di bad to, bot na to show una haw una won wok for God bikos of us.
47007013	So, Kraist don mak awa maind strong. Ivun as awa heart don strong rish, wi dey hapi more-more, bikos of Titus wey kom, bikos all of una don let en maind res.
47007014	I don boast gi-am abaut una and una nor let mi shame, bot as evritin wey wi tel una na tru, na so all di boast wey wi boast abaut una giv Titus, na trut tu.
47007015	And wen e rimemba haw una obey and welkom am wit respet and fear, di luv wey e get for una, kon strong wel-wel.
47007016	Evritin dey mak mi hapi, bikos di trust wey I trust una, nor dey shake.
47008001	Awa brodas and sistas, wi don tel una abaut di grace wey God giv di pipol for di shosh for Masidonia sey,
47008002	ivun wen dia sofa strong wel-wel; dem stil dey hapi and wen dem nor get moni at-all; dem stil dey fine moni giv us.
47008003	I bi witnes sey dem dey giv akordin to wetin dem get. Somtaims, dem dey giv pas wetin dem get. Nobodi dey fos dem to du laik dat, bot dem dey du-am from dia own maind
47008004	and dem dey beg us mak wi let dem du-am, so dat dem go get di blessin wey dey folo pipol wey dey giv.
47008005	Dem dey du laik dis, nor bi onli as wi wont am, bot na bikos dem don first giv demsef to God, den dem kon giv demsef to us as God wont am.
47008006	Naim mak us beg Titus sey, as e don start, e gud mak e finish dis gud wok wey e dey du, bikos e luv una.
47008007	Bot as una dey du wel for evritin: for fate; for tok; for wetin una no and as una won du di wok wel, bikos una luv us, mak una mak sure sey una dey du dis gud wit all una heart.
47008008	Nor bi sey I dey komand una, bot I won si weda una luv na ril won laik di oda pipol own.
47008009	Una no di grace wey awa Oga Jisos Kraist get; ivun doh e dey rish, e kon turn poor man bikos of una, so dat tru en porvati, una go dey rish.
47008010	Na wetin I tink for di mata bi dis: Una start wel last year for haw una dey giv and haw una dey wont giv,
47008011	so e beta mak una jos finish wetin una start, so dat di way wey una tak start am, na so tu una go stil tak finish am as una pawa rish.
47008012	Bikos if e rili dey una maind to du-am, enitin wey una giv akordin to wetin una get, God go asept am, bot nor bi wetin una nor get.
47008013	I nor dey tok dis won, so dat wen una don giv oda pipol, dem go kon get and una go kon dey sofa, bot na to mak sure sey tins dey equal.
47008014	As tins bi naw, di moni wey una get go help dem as dem nor get, so dat won day, di moni wey dem go get go stil help una wen una nor get, dat taim evritin go kon dey equal, bikos
47008015	dem rite for God wod sey: "Di pesin wey gada plenti, nor go get plenti and di pesin wey gada smol, go get di won wey go rish am."
47008016	Wi tank God wey giv Titus di kaind maind wey I get to help una.
47008017	Bikos e nor onli gri for wetin wi ask am, bot e dey help una wel-wel and nobodi fos am kom mit una.
47008018	And di broda wey all di shosh dem dey praiz, bikos of haw e dey prish di gospol, wi dey send am folo Titus tu.
47008019	Bikos of di wok wey di broda dey du, di shosh don shuz am as di pesin wey go dey folo us travol as wi dey giv dis gud gift, so dat all di glori go bi God own and dis go show sey wi dey redi to help.
47008020	Wi dey du laik dis, so dat nobodi go komplain as wi dey share dis gift.
47008021	Bikos wi dey trai to du wetin dey rite, nor bi onli for God eye, bot for pipol eye tu.
47008022	So wi dey send awa broda folo dem; awa broda wey wi don test plenti taims kon si sey e get di maind to help and e redi to help naw, bikos e trust una wel-wel.
47008023	Bot for Titus, en na my patina and e dey folo mi wok to help una. As for di oda brodas wey dey folo am, na all di shosh sey mak dem kom mit una, so dat dem go tel una abaut di glori wey dey insaid Kraist.
47008024	So mak una show dem sey, una luv dem, so dat all di pipol for di shosh go no sey, di way wey wi dey boast abaut una, na tru.
47009001	I nor nid to rite to una abaut haw to help God pipol wey dey Jerusalem,
47009002	bikos I no sey una won help dem. I always dey boast giv Masidonia pipol sey, una wey dey Akaya, dey always won help and una don redi to giv moni since last year. And di way wey una dey won help, don mak som of dem won help tu.
47009003	Bot I dey send dis brodas kom mit una to mak sure sey una dey redi; as I don tel dem bifor sey, una don alredi kolet moni. So mak una nor let shame kash mi, as I dey boast abaut una.
47009004	Bot if enibodi for Masidonia folo mi kom mit una, den e si sey una neva redi to giv, shame go kash us, ( I nor go tok tu mush) bikos wi trust una.
47009005	Naim mak mi beg dis brodas mak dem go for my front bifor di taim go rish and mak dem help una arange di moni wey una promis, so dat una go du-am wit una maind and nobodi go fos una.
47009006	Na wetin I dey tok bi dis; Pesin wey plant smol, go havest smol, bot di pesin wey plant plenti, go havest plenti.
47009007	Mak ish of una giv as e plan for en maind; nor bi wit rigret or laik sey dem fos am, bikos God luv pesin wey dey giv wit hapines.
47009008	God go provide evritin wey una nid. Den, una go always get evritin wey una nid and di won wey una go fit giv odas.
47009009	Jos as dem rite for God wod, "E don skata for evriwer, e don giv to poor pipol and en raitiousnes, go dey foreva."
47009010	Bikos na God dey giv sid to farma and provide bread wey pipol go chop. Laik dis tu, E go provide and di tins wey una nid, go plenti wel-wel and dem go last foreva.
47009011	E go mak una get enof moni for evritin, so dat evritaim, una go fit dey giv wel-wel and di pipol wey una giv moni, go always dey tank God.
47009012	Bikos dis wok wey una dey du so, nor jos dey help onli God pipol, bot e dey always mak pipol, tank God.
47009013	Bikos of una wok, pipol go praiz God, bikos una dey obey Kraist wod wey una biliv and una dey share evritin wey una get wit gud maind.
47009014	So, bikos of God big grace wey E giv una, pipol dey pray for una wit strong luv.
47009015	Na dis mak us dey tank God for dis gift wey pesin mout nor fit tok.
47010001	Naw mi, Pol (I kwayet wen I dey wit una, bot my mout dey sharp naw wen I don liv una). Kraist wey nor dey kari bodi up, wey dey gentol,
47010002	I tak am beg una, so dat wen I kom, I nor nid to tok wit vesnashon abaut pipol wey si us laik yeye pipol (bikos I dey fear sey na so e go bi).
47010003	Bikos ivun doh wi dey for dis wold, wi nor dey fite as pipol wont am.
47010004	Di tins wey wi tak dey fite, nor bi dis wold own, bot na God mak am strong, so dat wi go fit skata all di strong place wer wiked pipol dey. Wi dey skata trobol;
47010005	pipol wey dey kari bodi up; doz wey nor wont mak odas no God and as wi dey du laik dis, pipol dey obey Kraist.
47010006	And wen una don show sey una dey fear God, wi go always dey redi to ponish doz wey dey disobey God.
47010007	Na onli tins wey eye fit si, naim una no. If enibodi dey sure sey e bilong to Kraist, mak e tink abaut am again: If e bilong to Kraist, den wi na Kraist own tu.
47010008	Bikos if I boast smol abaut di autoriti wey Jisos giv us mak wi tak build, insted of to distroi una, I nor go shame to du-am.
47010009	I nor wont mak una dey fear, bikos of wetin I rite,
47010010	bikos som pipol dey sey, "En letas dey heavi and get pawa wel-wel, bot if yu si-am for groun, e nor get pawa and e nor ivun fit tok wel."
47010011	Mak doz pipol no sey, "Wetin wi tok for leta wen wi nor dey wit una, wi dey du-am wen wi dey wit una."
47010012	Wi nor go kompare awasef wit doz wey sey dem gud wel-wel or kon put awasef for di same grup. Bot wen dem dey measure and kompare demsef wit demsef, e dey show sey dem nor get sense.
47010013	Bot wi nor go boast pas as wi sopoz boast; wi go boast akordin to di wok wey God giv us and una dey insaid dat wok tu.
47010014	Wi nor dey du awa wok pas as wi sopoz du-am wen wi dey wit una, bikos na wi bi first to bring Kraist mesage kom mit una.
47010015	Wi nor dey boast enihaw abaut di wok wey oda pipol du, bot wi dey hope sey as una fate dey grow wel-wel, awa wok among una go big, jos as God share am giv us,
47010016	so dat wi go fit prish di gospol for oda kontris wey far pas una own. So mak wi nor boast abaut di wok wey odas du for oda aria.
47010017	Bot pesin wey won boast, mak e boast abaut di wok wey Jisos du.
47010018	Bikos nor bi hu praiz ensef dey rite, bot na di pesin wey God decide to praiz.
47011001	For weitn I won tok naw, mak una bear wit mi laik sey I nor get sense!
47011002	I dey jelos for una wit God jelosi, bikos I promis sey na won man una go mari. Laik wuman wey nor no man, na so I won giv una to Kraist.
47011003	Bot I dey fear sey, jos as di snake disiv Eve wit en wayo, una maind fit spoil komot for di tru and di way wey una dey folo Kraist.
47011004	So, if enibodi kon prish anoda kraist wey wi nor prish for una and una risiv anoda spirit wey una nor risiv bifor, or anoda gospol wey una neva hear bifor, dat min sey, una don asept dem wel.
47011005	I nor tink sey doz "supa apostol" beta pas mi.
47011006	Bot ivun doh I nor no haw to tok, I no book. Tru-tru, wi don let una no dis tins wey hapun.
47011007	As I humbol mysef dey du di wok, na sin I komit? I dey du-am, so dat una go fit grow up and wen I prish giv una, I nor kolet moni.
47011008	I shit di oda shosh dem, bikos I dey kolet moni from dem, so dat I go dey wok wit una for fri!
47011009	Wen I nid enitin for di taim wen I dey wit una, I nor put my load for enibodi head, bikos awa brodas wey Masidonia dey giv mi evritin wey I nid. I nor alow mysef to bi problem for enibodi and I nor go eva du-am.
47011010	Tru-tru, as Kraist trut dey insaid mi, nobodi go fit stop mi for di way I dey boast for Akaya.
47011011	Why? Na bikos I nor luv una? No! God no sey I luv una!
47011012	And I go kontinu to du wetin I dey du, so dat doz apostols nor go get rizin to boast sey, dem dey du di same wok wit us.
47011013	Bikos dem bi fake apostols; pipol wey dey lai and pritend laik sey dem bi Jisos Kraist apostols.
47011014	E nor sopraiz us, bikos ivun Satan dey pritend sey en na angel wey get lite.
47011015	So e nor sopraiz us sey, en savants dey pritend tu laik sey dem bi savant wey dey du wetin gud for God eye. For di end, dem go gain wetin fit di tins wey dem dey du.
47011016	I dey tel una again, mak enibodi nor tink sey I bi fool. Bot if una tink so, den mak una asept mi as fool, so dat misef go boast smol.
47011017	Wetin I dey boast abaut so, nor bi as Kraist wont mak I boast, insted, I dey tok laik fool.
47011018	Since som pipol dey boast laik dis wold pipol, mak mi mysef stil boast.
47011019	Una sey una get sense wel-wel, yet una dey yuz hapines asept wetin fool dey tok.
47011020	Una laik mak pesin turn una to slave; yuz and shit una; tak evritin wey una get, den beat and slap una enihaw.
47011021	(Na shame for mi, bot I must tel una sey awa heart nor strong rish to du una doz kaind tins!) Bot enitin wey enibodi fit boast abaut (I dey tok laik fool naw o-o), misef fit boast abaut dat tin tu.
47011022	Na Hebrew pipol dem bi? Misef na Hebrew pesin tu. Dem bi Izrel pipol? Mi na Izrel pesin tu. Na Abraham bi dia gran papa? Na dat same Abraham bi my gran papa tu.
47011023	Na Kraist savant dem bi? (I don dey tok laik sey I dey krase again!) Misef na Kraist savant wey beta pas dem! I don wok hard pas dem, I don dey prizin plenti taims pas dem, dem don beat mi wel-wel pas dem, I don nearli die plenti taims.
47011024	Na faiv taims Ju pipol don kane mi tati-nain (39) taims.
47011025	Roman pipol don beat mi tiri taims. Dem stone mi wons ontil I nearli die. Ship wey I dey insaid, don spoil for wota tiri taims. I don float wons for wota from mornin go rish di next day.
47011026	I don travol meni taims wey I enta trobol for wota; for tif hand, ivun for my kontri pipol and Gentai pipol hand; both for insaid tawn; for desert and from pipol wey dey pritend sey dem bi awa brodas.
47011027	I don du hard wok; nor slip for meni nites; fud and wota go dey hungri mi; meni taims, I nor get fud to chop. I don dey for kold and I nor get klot to kova bodi.
47011028	Apart from dis tins, my maind dey heavi mi evriday as I dey tink of haw I go tak help all di pipol wey dey God shosh.
47011029	If pesin dey wik, misef dey wik tu. If dem disiv pesin enta sin, e dey pain mi wel-wel.
47011030	If I go must boast, den I go boast abaut di tins wey show sey I dey wik.
47011031	God wey bi awa Oga Jisos Kraist Papa, wey dem go praiz foreva, no sey nor bi lai I dey tok.
47011032	For Damaskus, King Aretas sey mak di govnor put sojas for di tawn gate, so dat dem go arres mi.
47011033	Bot awa pipol for der kon put mi for basket wey dem tie rope put kon drop mi smol-smol from di window and na so I tak eskape from di man hand.
47012001	E gud to dey boast, ivun doh gain nor dey insaid. I go stil dey tok abaut di vishon and revelashon wey Jisos Kraist show mi.
47012002	Fortin years ago, I no won man wey bi Kraist savant. Weda na for vishon or fisica, I nor no, bot God no. God kari am go di hevun wey high pas.
47012003	And I no dis man (bot na onli God no weda e dey for en bodi or for spirit).
47012004	God kari am go paradise and e hear tins wey dey tu holi to tok; tins wey God nor giv humanbin pawa to tok.
47012005	Na dat pesin mak mi dey boast and I nor go boast abaut mysef, esept di tins wey show sey, I nor dey strong.
47012006	Ivun if I won boast, I nor go bi fool, bikos na trut I go stil tok, bot I nor du-am mak enibodi for tink sey na mi no pas, bikos e si and hear mi dey tok
47012007	abaut di beta tins wey I si for vishon. Mak I for nor dey kari bodi up, God put somtin insaid mi, wey bi Satan mesenja, so dat e go dey trobol mi.
47012008	Na tiri taims I ask Kraist sey, mak e tak dis tin komot from my bodi.
47012009	Bot e tel mi, "Di grace wey I giv yu strong rish, bikos my pawa dey show wen yu dey wik." So, I go boast wel-wel abaut haw I nor dey strong, so dat Kraist pawa go dey show for my bodi.
47012010	I dey hapi as I dey wik wit all di kos, trobols, ponishment and wahala wey I dey sofa bikos of Kraist, bikos enitaim wey I dey wik, na dat taim, I dey-dey strong.
47012011	I don turn to fool! Na una fos mi, bikos una sopoz to praiz mi. Ivun if I nor bi enitin, e nor get enitin wey doz una "supa apostols" tak beta pas mi.
47012012	Tru-tru for una present, wi du mirakols and wondas to show sey wi bi apostols tu.
47012013	Bikos di way wey dem trit us wos pas di oda shosh, esept sey I nor dey put my load for una head. Mak una forgiv mi for dis tins wey I du!
47012014	Si, for di ted taim, I don redi to kom visit una and I nor go put my load for una head, bikos na una I wont and nor bi wetin una get. Nor bi pikin sopoz pay for dia papa and mama fud, bot na papa and mama, dey pay for dia pikin fud.
47012015	I go dey hapi to spend all my moni and ivun my life, as long as una soul go dey save. Una luv for mi dey smol, bikos my luv for una plenti?
47012016	Ivun if e bi laik dat, I nor put my load for una head. Bot dem sey, bikos I bi wayo pesin, I dey disiv una!
47012017	I nor play enibodi wayo tru di pesin wen I send kom mit una, abi I dey lai?
47012018	I beg Titus mak e visit una and I send dat broda mak e folo am kom. Dem play una wayo? Nor bi di same maind wi awasef tak folo una? Abi nor bi di same way wi dey bihav?
47012019	May bi una dey tink sey wi dey tok dis tins to difend awasef. No! Wi dey tok to una laik dis as Kraist savant and na God bi awa witnes. Evritin wey wi dey du, na to mak una strong.
47012020	Bikos I dey fear sey wen I kom, I nor go laik wetin I go si and una nor go laik as I go tok. I dey fear sey una go dey kworel, dey jelos ish oda; dey ves; dey tink of onli unasef; dey tok bad abaut ish oda; dey du aproko; dey kari bodi up and dey bihav enihaw.
47012021	I dey fear sey wen I kom again, God go disgrace mi for una front. And I go krai, bikos meni of una stil dey sin. Una neva turn from sin kom mit God; una neva turn komot from di ashowo and yeye life wey una dey liv.
47013001	Na di ted taim wey I dey kom visit una bi dis. If dem sey pesin du bad, tu or tiri pipol must sey, na tru, bifor pipol go biliv am.
47013002	Wen I dey wit una for my sekon visit, I tel una dis tins. Ivun doh I nor dey wit una naw, I dey tok am again sey, if I kom again, I nor go sori for enibodi, bot I go ponish am,
47013003	bikos una sey mak I show sey Kraist dey tok tru mi. Kraist nor dey wik to una, bikos e show en pawa among una.
47013004	Tru-tru, bikos e nor show en pawa, na dat mak dem fit nail am for kros, bot e dey alaif naw, bikos of God pawa. Aldoh wi dey wik wit am, bot wi go dey alaif togeda wit am, bikos of God pawa wey wi get.
47013005	Mak una test unasef to no weda una stil dey insaid di fate; e gud mak una shek unasef wel-wel! Una nor no sey Kraist dey insaid una? May bi una don fail di test!
47013006	I hope sey una go no sey wi neva fail di test!
47013007	Wi dey pray to God mak una nor du enitin bad; wi nor dey du-am to show sey wi pas di test, bot mak una for du wetin gud, ivun if e bi laik sey wi fail di test.
47013008	Wi nor go fit du enitin against di trut, bot na di trut go mak us du evritin.
47013009	Bele dey swit us wen eva wi dey wik and una dey strong. And na wetin wi dey pray for bi dis, "Una go get evritin wey una sopoz get."
47013010	Na dis mak mi dey rite all dis tins since I nor dey wit una, so dat wen I kom, I nor go ves for una bikos of di autoriti wey I get and God giv mi dis autoriti to build; nor bi to distroi.
47013011	Finali my brodas and sistas, mak una dey hapi dey du tins as dem sopoz bi. Mak una tak heart, dey grit ish oda and liv togeda for peace and di God wey get luv and peace, go dey wit una.
47013012	Mak una grit ish oda for Kristen way.
47013013	All God pipol for here dey grit una.
47013014	Mak di grace wey awa Oga Jisos Kraist giv us and di luv wey God get for us, plus di Holi Spirit feloship, dey wit una.
48001001	Na mi Pol, rite dis leta, (nor bi humanbin mak mi apostol, bot na Jisos Kraist and God awa Papa wey raiz-am from deat).
48001002	Mi and di brodas wey dey here, dey grit una wey dey Galatia.
48001003	Mak God awa Papa and Oga Jisos Kraist grace and peace, dey wit una.
48001004	Na Jisos die for awa sins, bikos na so God awa Papa wont am.
48001005	Mak all glori bi en own foreva and eva! Amen.
48001006	I sopraiz sey una kwik turn bak from di Pesin wey kol una wit en grace kon bigin folo oda tishin.
48001007	Nor bi sey anoda gospol rili dey, bot som pipol dey disturb una, bikos dem won shange wetin wi prish abaut Kraist.
48001008	Bot if wi (or angels wey kom from hevun) tish una difren tins from di won wey wi prish giv una bifor, mak God distroi us wit fire!
48001009	As I tok bifor, I dey repeat am again, if enibodi dey tish difren tins from di wons wey wi prish giv una bifor, mak God trow dat pesin for hell!
48001010	Una tink sey, I dey trai to du tins mak pipol for laik mi? Abi I dey du wetin God wont? Or I dey trai to mak bele swit pipol? If I dey trai to mak bele swit pipol, den I nor bi Kraist savant again!
48001011	My brodas and sistas, I wont mak una no sey di gospol wey I dey prish, nor bi humanbin giv mi.
48001012	Bikos I nor get or learn am from enibodi, bot I get-am tru di revelashon wey Kraist giv mi.
48001013	Una don hear abaut di kaind life wey I dey liv bifor as Ju pesin; haw I trobol di shosh kon dey trai to distroi am.
48001014	I grow among Ju pipol kon no di religion pas meni of my mates for my kontri and I no my gran-gran papa dem tradishons.
48001015	Bot God kol mi wit en grace kon seprate mi ivun bifor dem born mi.
48001016	E show mi en pikin, so dat I go fit prish abaut am giv Gentai pipol. I nor go mit enibodi mak e advise mi
48001017	and I nor go Jerusalem go mit pipol wey bi apostol bifor mi, bot I komot der go Arabia, den I kon go bak to Damaskus.
48001018	Afta tiri years, I go visit Pita for Jerusalem, so dat e go tel mi wetin I go du and I stay wit am for fiftin days.
48001019	Bot I nor go si eni oda apostol apart from James, wey bi Jisos Kraist broda.
48001020	God dey si wetin I dey rite, bikos evritin wey I dey rite to una so, na tru!
48001021	Afta dis, I kon go Syria and Silicia aria.
48001022	Bot di pipol for di shosh wey dey Judea, nor no mi.
48001023	Dem onli dey hear sey, "Di pesin wey dey trobol us bifor, don dey prish di mesage wey e bin dey trai to distroi."
48001024	So dem kon dey praiz God bikos of mi.~
48002001	Afta fortin years, I kon go bak to Jerusalem wit Banabas and Titus.
48002002	I go der bikos of di revelashon wey I risiv, den I tel dem abaut wetin I dey prish giv Gentai pipol. Bot I tok wit di oga dem, so dat dem go dey sure sey, I dey prish Kraist mesage.
48002003	Titus dey wit mi; ivun doh en na Greek pesin, dem nor sey e must sekonsaiz.
48002004	Dem diskos dis mata, bikos of di fake brodas wit dia wayo, wey dem tak dey spy di fridom wey Kraist giv us, so dat dem go fit mak us dia slave.
48002005	Bot wi nor giv dem shanse, so dat di trut wey dey di gospol, go last for una.
48002006	Bot doz wey tink sey dem bi oga, (wetin dem bi, nor min enitin to mi; bikos God nor dey sopot bad tin); dem wey bi lidas for di shosh nor add enitin to my mesage.
48002007	Bot dem kon si sey na God sey mak I prish en wod to pipol wey dem nor sekonsaiz, jos as E sey mak Pita prish to doz wey dem sekonsaiz,
48002008	(Bikos na tru God pawa Pita tak prish to Ju pipol and na di same pawa I tak dey prish giv Gentai pipol tu),
48002009	so wen James, Pita and Jon wey bi lidas for di shosh, si sey God giv mi grace, dem kon dey sopot mi and Banabas sey, "Mak wi dey prish giv Gentai pipol and doz wey dem sekonsaiz."
48002010	Bot dem sey mak wi always rimemba poor pipol and na wetin ivun dey my maind to du, bi dat.
48002011	Bot wen Pita kom Antiok, I kon shalenge am, bikos wetin e du, nor gud.
48002012	Pita dey chop wit Gentai pipol ontil som pipol wey James send, kom rish der. As Pita si dem, e kon stop to chop wit Gentai pipol, bikos e dey fear di pipol wey kom, since dem biliv sey evribodi must sekonsaiz.
48002013	Oda Ju pipol kon dey pritend laik Pita, sotey Banabas join dem tu.
48002014	Bot wen I si sey dem nor dey du wetin dem rite for God wod, I kon tel Pita for dia front, "If yu wey bi Ju, dey du laik Gentai pipol, haw yu wont tak mak Gentai pipol liv laik Ju pipol?"
48002015	Wi bi Ju pipol bikos of haw dem born us and wi nor bi Gentai pipol wey bi sinas.
48002016	Wi no sey nobodi dey fri from God jojment, bikos na so di law tok and pipol go onli dey fri, if dem get fate for Kraist. Since wi don biliv Kraist, wi sopoz to dey du gud tru di fate wey wi get for Kraist and nor bi to dey du wetin di law tok and wi nor go dey fri from jojment, wen wi du onli wetin di law tok.
48002017	Mak wi dey komit sin, as wi dey trai to du gud, bikos wi get fate for Kraist? If na so, dat min sey Kraist don dey sopot sin!
48002018	Naw, if I dey ripair di law wey I don first skata, dat min sey I dey break God law.
48002019	As for di law, I don die to am, so dat I go fit dey alaif wit God.
48002020	I don die wit Kraist for kros, so nor bi mi dey liv again, bot na Kraist dey liv insaid mi. Di life wey I dey liv naw, na bikos of di gud tins wey God pikin du insaid mi, bikos e luv and die for mi.
48002021	I nor go trowey God grace; bikos if na wetin di law tok go mak pesin gud, den Kraist die for nor-tin!
48003001	Galatia pipol, una nor get sense at-all! Hu turn una to fool naw? Bikos na for una front wi for show sey Jisos Kraist die for kros!
48003002	Na di tin wey I won no from una, bi dis: Una risiv di Spirit, bikos una dey du wetin di law tok or na bikos una biliv wetin wi prish giv una?
48003003	Na so una mumu rish? Tru-tru, una start wit di Holi Spirit, bot naw, una won finish di wok wit human-bin pawa.
48003004	Una sofa dis meni tins for nor-tin? Tru-tru, una rili sofa for nor-tin.
48003005	Wetin mak God giv una di Spirit to du mirakol? Na bikos una du wetin di law tok or bikos una biliv wetin una hear?
48003006	Jos as Abraham biliv God and God kol am raitious man,
48003007	na so tu, doz wey biliv, go bi Abraham shildren.
48003008	Dem rite for God wod bifor sey, "E go asept Gentai pipol, wen dem get fate" and na dis mak am tel Abraham bifor di taim rish sey, "E go bless evribodi, bikos of am."
48003009	So pipol wey biliv, God go bless dem togeda wit Abraham, bikos dem biliv.
48003010	Pipol wey dey unda di law and dem nor dey du evritin wey di law tok, dey unda kos, bikos dem rite am sey, "E nor go beta for enibodi wey nor dey du evritin wey dey di law."
48003011	Dis won show sey, nobodi dey gud for God eye, bikos e dey obey di law. So enibodi wey dey raitious, must liv by fate.
48003012	Di law nor dey bring fate, bot di pesin wey dey du wetin di law tok, go liv by wetin e dey du.
48003013	Kraist don save us from di kos wey di law bring, bikos e die for kros for us (jos as dem rite am, "Enibodi wey dem hang for tri, kos dey en head"),
48003014	so tru Kraist, Abraham blessins go kom mit Gentai pipol and wi go risiv di Spirit wey God promis us, tru fate.
48003015	My brodas and sistas, mak I yuz wetin dey hapun evriday for life tak mak ezampol for una: Wen pipol don mak agriment, nobodi go fit trow di agriment for kona or add enitin join am.
48003016	Wi no sey God mak dis promis wit Abraham and en pikin. God wod nor sey, "to di shildren", bot e sey "and to yor pikin," and e min onli won and dat won, na Kraist.
48003017	Na wetin I dey tok bi dis: Di law wey kom afta 430 years, nor get pawa to break di agriment and promis wey God and Abraham don mak bifor.
48003018	Bikos if promis dey kom tru di law, den e nor bi promis again. Bot wi no sey, na tru promis, God tak bless Abraham.
48003019	Na awa sin mak law dey and na so e go bi, ontil di pikin wey God promis, go kom and na tru angels, God tak giv us di law tru en profet.
48003020	Wi no sey pesin wey bi middleman dey stand bitwin tu pipol, bot na onli won God dey.
48003021	So di law dey against God promis? No! Bikos if di law dey giv pesin life, den raitiousnes go must kom tru di law.
48003022	Bot God wod kondem evritin and evribodi unda sin, so dat wi; di pipol wey biliv, go get God promis tru Jisos Kraist.
48003023	Bifor fate kom, wi dey unda di law, bikos di law hol us laik prizinas.
48003024	So na di law bi awa tisha bifor Kraist kom, so dat wi go fit tok sey wi dey raitious tru fate.
48003025	Bot since fate don kom, wi nor dey unda eni tisha again.
48003026	Bikos tru Jisos Kraist, all of us don bikom God shildren by fate.
48003027	Una wey dem don baptaiz insaid Kraist, don wear Kraist for bodi laik klot.
48003028	E nor mata weda una bi Ju or Greek pipol, savant or fri pesin, man or wuman, bikos all of una dey insaid won bodi for Kraist.
48003029	And if e bi sey una bilong to Kraist, den una bi Abraham shildren and pipol wey go inherit wetin God promis.
48004001	Wetin I min bi sey, di pesin wey inherit en papa propati and e stil bi smol pikin, e nor dey difren from savant, ivun doh na en get evritin.
48004002	Bot e go dey unda hu dey gaid am, ontil di taim wey en papa tok, go rish.
48004003	Na so e bi wit us wen wi smol; wi dey unda di pawa wey dey kontrol dis wold,
48004004	bot wen di rite taim rish, God kon send en pikin wey wuman born unda di law,
48004005	mak e save pipol wey dey unda di law, so dat God go mak us en own shildren kon giv us awa own propati.
48004006	Since wi bi God shildren, E put en Holi Spirit insaid us and naim mak us dey fit kol am, "Abba! Fada!"
48004007	So, una nor bi slave again, bot una don bi God pikin and since una bi God shildren, una go get God propati tu.
48004008	Bifor-bifor, wen una nor no God, una dey du bad-bad tins.
48004009	Bot naw wey una don no am (or abi mak I sey God don no una), why una stil dey folo all dis wik and yeye pawas? Una won bi dia slave again?
48004010	Dat taim, una folo dia tradishon.
48004011	I dey fear sey mak di wok wey I du among una, nor waste.
48004012	My brodas and sistas, I beg, mak una bi laik mi, as I don bi laik una, bikos una nor du mi eni bad tin!
48004013	Bot wen I first prish di gospol giv una, una no sey I wey nor wel,
48004014	ivun doh my siknes na problem to una, una nor laff or driv mi. Insted, una welkom mi laik God angel; laik sey na mi bi Jisos Kraist!
48004015	Naw, na wetin don hapun to una hapines? I no sey, if to sey e dey posibol, una for pul una eye giv mi!
48004016	So, I don bikom una enemi, bikos I dey tel una di trut?
48004017	Di pipol wey won disiv una dey trit una wel, bot dem nor dey du-am wit beta maind; bikos dem wont mak una liv mi kon folo dem.
48004018	Bot e gud mak una dey trit odas wel, so-far na for gud rizin and nor bi onli wen I dey wit una.
48004019	My shildren! Jos laik wuman wey won born, I dey feel pain for una, ontil Kraist pawa go dey insaid una life!
48004020	Haw I wish sey I dey wit una naw, so dat I go no haw to trit una, bikos I dey wori abaut una wel-wel.
48004021	Mak una tel mi, wish of una won dey unda di law? Una nor no wetin di law tok?
48004022	Dem rite am sey, Abraham get tu boys, won wey di savant wuman born and di oda pikin, na di ril wife born am.
48004023	Di won wey savant born, na ordinari pikin e bi, bot na tru God promis di ril wife tak born.
48004024	Beta sense dey for dis stori, bikos dis tu wimen bi laik tu kovenant. Won na from Mount Sinai wey bi laik di shildren wey Hagar, di savant wuman, born.
48004025	Hagar bi laik Mount Sinai for Arabia kontri and na di same wit Jerusalem wey dey naw, bikos e dey insaid der as slave wit en pikin.
48004026	Bot di Jerusalem wey kom from hevun, dey fri and na-im bi awa mama.
48004027	Bikos dem rite am sey, "Wuman! Yu wey neva born, mak yu shaut dey hapi, bikos yu neva labor laik wuman wey won born. Di wuman wey neva born, get plenti shildren pas di wuman wey get husban."
48004028	Bot my brodas and sistas, una bi shildren wey get promis, jos as Izik bi.
48004029	For dat taim, di won wey dem born for normal way, trobol di won wey dem born wit di Spirit and na so e bi wit una naw.
48004030	Bot wetin dem rite for God wod? "Mak yu driv di savant wuman and en pikin komot, bikos di savant pikin nor go share wit di pikin wey di ril wife born."
48004031	So my brodas and sistas, wi nor bi savant shildren. Na di ril wuman shildren, wi bi.
48005001	Mak una nor dey kari load for head laik slave again, bot mak una stand strong for groun, bikos Kraist don mak us fri.
48005002	Una dey hear! Mi wey bi Pol dey tel una sey, if dem sekonsaiz una, den Kraist nor min enitin to una again.
48005003	And I dey warn evribodi; enibodi wey gri mak dem sekonsaiz am, must obey evri oda tin wey di law tok.
48005004	Pipol wey wont mak pipol no sey dem dey gud, bikos dem dey kip di law, dem don alredi fal komot from God grace.
48005005	Bikos na tru fate for God Spirit, naim wi hope sey, God go mak us dey gud for en eye.
48005006	For Kraist, e nor mata weda dem sekonsaiz pesin or not; di onli tin wey mata, na fate wey dey wok tru luv.
48005007	Bifor, una dey du wel; bot naw, hu sey mak una nor obey di trut?
48005008	Nor bi God wey kol una sey mak una dey du laik dis!
48005009	Na smol yist dey mak bread raiz!
48005010	I get maind sey, God nor go let una listin to anoda pesin. Bot di pesin wey dey konfuz una, go face jojment, no mata hu e bi.
48005011	Naw, my brodas and sistas, if I stil dey prish abaut haw dem go tak sekonsaiz una, why pipol dey trobol mi? If na so, my tishin abaut Kraist kros nor sopoz kause eni trobol.
48005012	I wish sey doz wey dey disturb una go-go sekonsaiz demsef!
48005013	My brodas and sistas, God don kol una mak una dey fri; bot mak una nor yuz di fridom wey God giv una enihaw, insted mak una luv ish oda.
48005014	Bikos if dem add di hol law togeda, dem go kon bi won komandment wey sey, "Mak yu luv yor nebor as yu luv yorsef."
48005015	Bot if una kontinu to kworel among unasef; una go fit wound or kil ish oda by mistak.
48005016	I tel una, mak una let di Spirit direct una life and una nor go du wetin di flesh wont.
48005017	Bikos di tins wey di bodi laik, difren from wetin di Spirit laik and wetin di Spirit wont, nor dey gri wit wetin di flesh wont.
48005018	Bot if una alow di Spirit kontrol una, den una nor dey unda di law again.
48005019	Na di tins wey di flesh dey du bi dis: to slip wit pesin wey yu nor mari; to get bad maind; to opres pipol;
48005020	to dey serv juju; dey du magic; kworel-kworel life; faiti-faiti; jelosi; enihaw vesnashon; long-trot; tins wey dey skata pipol;
48005021	bad bele; kili-kili; to dey drink enihaw and dey du oda tins laik all dis wons. I dey warn una naw as I don warn una bifor sey, pipol wey dey du dis kaind tins, nor go enta God kindom!
48005022	Bot di frut wey di Holi Spirit dey bear insaid us; na luv, joy, peace, patient, kindnes, gudnes, faithfulnes,
48005023	gentolnes and to kontrol awasef. Di law nor dey against all dis tins.
48005024	Pipol wey dey insaid Kraist don kil dia flesh wit all di bad tins wey di flesh dey laik to du.
48005025	If di Holi Spirit dey insaid us, den mak wi dey liv awa life as di Holi Spirit wont.
48005026	Mak wi nor dey kari bodi up and dey du wetin go ves pipol or dey jelos won anoda.
48006001	My brodas and sistas, if una si pesin dey sin, mak una wey dey spiritual, kol am bak. Bot mak una wosh unasef, so dat una nor go fal insaid temtashon tu.
48006002	Mak una help kari ish oda load and if una du laik dis, una dey obey Kraist.
48006003	Bikos if enibodi tink sey, en tu big wen e nor bi enitin, e dey disiv ensef.
48006004	Mak evribodi shek ensef, den e go fit tok abaut ensef, insted of am to dey kompare ensef wit anoda pesin.
48006005	Bikos ish pesin go kari en own load by ensef.
48006006	Di pesin wey dem dey tish God wod, must share di gud tins wey e get wit di pesin wey dey tish am.
48006007	Mak una nor let enibodi disiv una. Nobodi go fit disiv God. Enitin wey pesin plant, naim e go reap,
48006008	bikos di pesin wey dey liv akordin to en flesh, go reap bad tins, bot di pesin wey dey liv akordin to God Spirit, go reap life wey nor dey end.
48006009	So mak to du gud, nor taya us, bikos wen taim rish, wi go gain am.
48006010	So enitaim wey wi get shanse, mak wi dey du gud, especiali to pipol wey bi God shildren.
48006011	Mak una si as di wod wey I tak my hand rite giv una, big rish!
48006012	Pipol wey won show sey dem gud, dey trai to fos una to sekonsaiz. Dem dey du so, so dat dem nor go sofa, bikos of Kraist kros.
48006013	Pipol wey sekonsaiz nor dey obey di law, bot dem wont mak una sekonsaiz, so dat dem go fit yuz una tak boast.
48006014	I nor go boast abaut enitin esept for di sofa wey awa Oga Jisos Kraist sofa and bikos of dat sofa, di wold nor min enitin to mi and I don die to di wold tu.
48006015	Weda pesin sekonsaiz or not, e nor min enitin, di onli tin wey mata bi sey, una don turn to new pesin.
48006016	Una wey dey obey dis rule wey I dey giv so, mak peace and mesi dey wit una and all God pipol.
48006017	From naw go, mak nobodi wori mi, bikos I get Jisos Kraist mark for my bodi.
48006018	My brodas and sistas, mak awa Oga Jisos Kraist grace dey wit una spirit. Amen!
49001001	Dis leta na from Pol, wey bi Jisos Kraist apostol, bikos na so God wont am. I dey rite to God pipol wey dey for Efisos, di wons wey dey folo Jisos Kraist wit fate.
49001002	Mak di grace and peace wey dey kom from God awa papa and from awa Oga Jisos Kraist, dey wit una.
49001003	I bless God wey bi awa Oga Jisos Kraist Papa; wey don bless us wit difren spiritual blessin from hevun, bikos of Kraist.
49001004	Bifor God kreate di wold, E shuz us tru Kraist bikos E luv us, so dat for en front, wi nor go get eni fault and wi go dey holi.
49001005	Bifor, God don alredi decide tru Jisos Kraist sey, wi go bi en shildren, bikos na so E wont am.
49001006	So, mak all praiz and glori bi en own, bikos of en fri grace wey E giv us, tru en pikin wey E luv wel-wel.
49001007	Na tru Kraist blood wi tak get salvashon and na dis blood mak God dey forgiv us awa sins, bikos en grace big wel-wel.
49001008	Di grace wey E giv us, get plenti wisdom, sense and undastandin.
49001009	E du laik dis wen E show us di sikrit plan wey E get and di gud maind wey E show evribodi, tru Kraist.
49001010	God go komplit en plan wen di taim don rish, den E go gada evritin wey dey hevun and eart togeda unda Kraist, wey bi di head.
49001011	All tins dey hapun as God wont am and tru Kraist, E shuz us to bi en own pipol, bikos na so E plan am from di taim wen E kreate di wold,
49001012	so dat wi wey first biliv Kraist, go dey giv am praiz and glori.
49001013	Since una don hear di trut kon biliv Kraist, God don giv una di Holi Spirit as special mark to show sey naim get una.
49001014	God deposit dis Holi Spirit for di tins wey wi go inherit, ontil di taim wen E go save en pipol, so dat all praiz and glori go bi en own.
49001015	So, since I hear abaut una fate for Kraist and haw una luv all God pipol,
49001016	I nor dey stop to tank God for una, wen eva I dey pray.
49001017	I pray mak God, awa Oga Jisos Kraist Papa wey get glori, giv una spiritual wisdom and revelashon, wey go mak una no am wel-wel.
49001018	Una eye don opun to undastand di grace wey God kol una kom enta and una don si haw di blessin wey E promis en pipol, plenti rish.
49001019	Una don si haw en pawa big rish, bikos una biliv am. Dis na di pawa wey dey du big-big tins for us.
49001020	E show dis pawa tru Kraist, wen E raiz-am from deat, kon mak am sidan for en rite hand for hevun;
49001021	di place wey far wel-wel, wey high pas wer wiked pipol dey rule; wey strong pas evri pawa wey dey dis wold; big pas evri name wey dey for dis wold and di wons wey dey kom.
49001022	God put evritin unda Kraist leg, kon mak am head for di shosh and Oga for evritin.
49001023	Na di shosh bi Kraist bodi and naim dey mak evritin for evriwer ful and komplit.
49002001	Bifor-bifor, na stubornes and sin dey kontrol una life,
49002002	bikos una dey du wetin di wold wont. Una dey obey wiked pawas wey dey rule di air and kontrol stuborn shildren.
49002003	All of us dey liv dis kaind life bifor. Wi dey du difren tins wey awa bodi and maind wont. Dat taim, wi bi shildren wey God won ponish laik oda sinas.
49002004	Bikos God luv us wel-wel, E don show us plenti mesi
49002005	(aldoh sin dey kontrol awa life bifor), E kon giv us life tru Kraist, den E save us wit en grace!
49002006	E raiz us up wit Kraist kon mak us sidan wit am for hevun.
49002007	E du dis, to show evribodi for di wold wey dey kom sey, en grace wey dey show us kaindnes tru Jisos Kraist, big wel-wel.
49002008	God save una wit en grace, bikos una get fate (as una don biliv Kraist), nor bi wit una own pawa, bot na God giv una.
49002009	E nor save una bikos of di wok wey una du, so mak nobodi dey boast.
49002010	God kreate us tru Jisos Kraist as di gud wok wey E don priper dan bifor, so dat wi go dey du as E plan.
49002011	Mak una rimemba sey bifor-bifor, una bi Gentai pipol wey dey du wetin di flesh wont and som pipol dey kol una, "pipol wey dem neva sekonsaiz" laik di way dem dey sekonsaiz humanbin.
49002012	Dat taim, una dey witout di Mezaya and una nor get share for Izrel blessins and since una nor get hope and una dey witout God for dis wold, una kon bi strenja to God kovenant wey E promis Izrel pipol.
49002013	Bot tru Jisos Kraist blood, una wey bin dey far, God don draw una near ensef,
49002014	bikos na Kraist bi awa peace. Na Kraist mak Ju and Gentai pipol bi won. E don break di wall wey divide and seprate dem as enimis.
49002015	E don kansol Ju pipol law wit all en komand and rules, so dat e go fit mak Ju and Gentai pipol to bi won wit am and laik dis, peace go dey among dem.
49002016	E yuz di sofa wey e sofa for kros tak end dia kworel kon mak dem won bodi as dem dey serv God.
49002017	And e prish peace to una wey dey far and near,
49002018	so dat tru am, all of us wit won Spirit, go fit rish wer awa Papa dey for hevun.
49002019	So, una nor go bi strenja and pipol wey nor get share for Izrel blessins again, bot una go bi God shildren wit all di pipol wey dey en haus.
49002020	Dis na bikos, God don build una on-top di apostols and profets foundashon and na Jisos Kraist bi di numba won stone wey God tak lay di foundashon.
49002021	Na for insaid Kraist di hol buildin for join togeda, kon grow as won Holi Tempol for God and
49002022	tru am, God don build una togeda as wer E go dey stay tru di Spirit.
49003001	Bikos of dis, mi, Pol wey bi prizina for Kraist, bikos of una wey bi Gentai pipol, dey pray giv God.
49003002	Tru-tru, una don hear sey na God giv mi dis wok tru en grace and na for una own gud.
49003003	God opun my eye to undastand en sikrit, as I rite to una bifor,
49003004	so dat wen una read am, una go fit undastand di sikrit wey God show mi.
49003005	Di pipol wey dey bifor nor no dis sikrit as God don show en holi apostols and profets wey dey naw, tru di Holi Spirit.
49003006	So, bikos of di gospol, Gentai pipol don folo Ju pipol get share for God blessin. Dem don bi membas for Kraist bodi and dem get share for God promis.
49003007	I bi dis gospol savant, bikos of God grace wey E giv mi tru di wok wey en pawa dey du.
49003008	Na mi smol pas for all God pipol, bot God don giv mi grace to prish di Gud News giv Gentai pipol and dis grace wey Kraist giv mi, nor dey finish.
49003009	Di grace na to mak evribodi undastand God sikrit plan. Na God kreate evritin and E hide di plan since e kreate di wold.
49003010	E mak dem undastand, so dat tru di shosh, all di rulas and pawas wey dey hevun go kon no God komplit wisdom, wey dey show ensef for difren ways.
49003011	Dis hapun akordin to en plan wey go stand foreva and E mak am hapun tru awa Oga Jisos Kraist
49003012	and na bikos Kraist dey fateful, naim mak us get di heart to fit rish wer God dey.
49003013	Na dis mak mi tel una sey, mak una nor fear bikos of di tins wey I dey sofa, bikos na for una own gud.
49003014	Bikos of dis, I dey nil dan for awa Papa front,
49003015	wer all di famili for hevun and eart from get dia names.
49003016	I dey pray sey as en glori big rish, E go mak una strong wel-wel wit pawa tru en Spirit wey bi di ril pesin insaid una.
49003017	So dat Kraist go dey insaid una heart tru fate and wen una don strong wel-wel insaid God luv,
49003018	una go fit join all God pipol undastand haw God luv wide, long, high and deep rish.
49003019	Den una go rili no di luv wey Kraist get, wey big pas evritin wey una go fit undastand and evritin insaid God, go ful una life.
49003020	So, mak all di glori bi God own; di Pesin wey dey du pas di tins wey wi go fit ask or tink, tru en pawa wey dey wok insaid us.
49003021	Mak all glori for Kraist shosh bi en own from generashon to generashon. Amen!
49004001	Mi wey bi prizina, bikos I dey serv di Oga; I dey beg una mak una dey liv una life as God wont.
49004002	Mak una dey get piti for won anoda wit quietnes, gentolnes and patient, bikos of di luv wey una get.
49004003	Mak una dey du evritin wey una fit du to kip di uniti wey di Spirit dey giv, as una dey liv togeda for peace.
49004004	Na won bodi and Spirit dey, bikos jos as all of una get won hope from God wen E kol una,
49004005	na so tu una get won Oga, won fate, won baptism,
49004006	won God and Papa wey dey above evribodi; dey yuz evribodi and dey insaid evribodi.
49004007	Bot God don giv grace to all of us akordin to haw Kraist gift plenti rish.
49004008	Na dis mak dem sey, "Wen e raiz-up go hevun, E kari meni prizinas wey E fri folo bodi and E giv plenti gift to pipol."
49004009	Na wetin dis wod, "E raiz-up," min? E min sey Kraist first die and dem bere am for di eart.
49004010	En wey dem bere, naim stil bi di pesin wey raiz-up pas di hevuns, so dat e go komplit evritin.
49004011	Na Kraist mak som of us apostols, profets, evangelist, pastors and tishas.
49004012	Kraist du laik dis to priper us for di ministri wok, wey go mak God shosh grow,
49004013	so dat wi go bi won for di tins wey wi biliv and wey go mak us rili no God Pikin. Den, wi go dey tink laik Kraist.
49004014	So mak wi nor bi laik shildren wey briz dey kari up and dan; shildren wey dey folo yeye tins wey humanbin dey tish and na dis tins dem dey tak disiv pipol.
49004015	Bot, as wi dey du wetin dey gud and koret wit luv, wi go dey grow for evri side kon mit Kraist wey bi di head.
49004016	Na from Kraist di hol bodi dey grow wel and join togeda tru di pawa wey dey sopot am. As ish part dey du en wok, na so di bodi go dey grow insaid God luv.
49004017	So, I dey yuz Kraist pawa tak tel una dis tins sey, mak una nor liv una life laik Gentai pipol wey dey tink onli bad and tins wey nor get sense.
49004018	Dia maind dey for daknes and dem nor get part for di life wey God dey giv, bikos dem stuborn and nor fit undastand.
49004019	Dem dey du wayo, dey giv dia bodi to yeye tins; tins wey nor dey pure and dey wiked.
49004020	Bot wi nor tish una laik dat abaut Kraist.
49004021	If na tru, den una don hear and learn di trut abaut am, jos as di trut dey insaid Kraist.
49004022	Konsanin di kaind life wey una dey liv bifor, wi sey mak una trowey dat bad spirit wey dey mak una du bad-bad tins
49004023	and mak una dey tink beta tins for una maind.
49004024	Den, tru raitiousnes and holines wey di trut dey bring, mak una wear di new man wey God don kreate laik ensef.
49004025	Since una don stop to lai, mak una start to tok trut giv una nebor, bikos all of us na membas for Kraist bodi.
49004026	If una dey ves, mak una nor sin and mak day nor dak stil mit una dey ves.
49004027	Mak una nor giv di devol eni shanse.
49004028	Pesin wey dey tif, mak e nor tif again. Insted, mak e wok hard and du gud wit en own hand, so dat e go fit giv pipol wey nor get.
49004029	Mak una nor alow eni bad wod kom out from una mout, bot mak una wod dey giv poor pipol hope, so dat e go bless pipol wey hear am.
49004030	Mak una nor du wetin go mak di Holi Spirit ves. Bikos na di Holi Spirit bi di mark wey God put for una bodi, so dat for jojment day, E go no doz wey E go save.
49004031	Una must stop to get bad bele, to dey ves, kworel and to dey tok bad-bad wod.
49004032	Mak una dey gud to won anoda; dey sori for pipol and dey forgiv ish oda, jos as God forgiv una tru Kraist.
49005001	So, mak una dey bihav laik shildren wey God luv wel-wel.
49005002	Mak wi luv won anoda, jos as Kraist luv and sakrifais ensef as ofrin wey get beta smel to God, bikos of us.
49005003	To dey slip wit pesin wey yu nor mari; dey du tins wey nor dey pure and get long-trot; mak una nor alow dis tins dey among una, bikos dem nor gud for God pipol.
49005004	Mak una nor alow yeye and foolish wod kom out from una mout. And mak una nor dey tok enihaw or yuz bad wod, bikos all dis tins nor gud. Insted, mak una dey tank God wit una mout.
49005005	Won tin wey una must no bi sey, pesin wey dey slip wit hu e nor mari, wey nor dey pure or wey get long-trot and dey serv juju, nor go enta Kraist and God kindom.
49005006	Mak una nor let enibodi disiv una wit yeye wod, na dis tins mak God dey ves for doz wey nor dey obey am.
49005007	So mak una nor join dem.
49005008	Bifor-bifor, una dey for daknes, bot naw, una bi lite wey dey shine insaid Kraist. So mak una dey du tins laik shildren wey get lite,
49005009	bikos di frut wey lite get, dey bring gudnes, raitiousnes and trut.
49005010	So, mak una always dey du tins wey go mak God hapi.
49005011	Mak una nor put hand for bad tins, insted, mak una dey expoz dem.
49005012	Shame nor go let wiked pipol tok abaut wetin dem dey du for sikrit.
49005013	Bot evribodi go si evritin wey kom out for lite.
49005014	Bikos na lite dey mak evritin shine kom out and na dis mak dem rite sey: "Wak-up; yu wey dey slip! Mak yu raiz from grave and Kraist go shine for yor life!"
49005015	Mak una dey kareful as una dey liv una life. Mak una nor bi laik pipol wey nor get sense.
49005016	Mak una yuz evri shanse wey una get wel, bikos dis taim wey wi dey so, dey evil and wiked.
49005017	Bikos of dis, mak una get sense to undastand wetin awa Oga wod tok and min.
49005018	Mak una nor dey drink strong drink, bikos e go distroi una. Bot mak una alow God Spirit fil una maind.
49005019	Mak una dey tok to unasef wit psalms, hymns and spiritual songs. For insaid una heart, mak una dey praiz God wit hymns and psalms.
49005020	Wit awa Oga Jisos Kraist name, mak una dey tank God awa papa for ish oda.
49005021	Bikos of di respet wey una get for Kraist, mak una dey respet won anoda.
49005022	Una wey bi wife, mak una dey respet una husban, jos as una dey respet Kraist,
49005023	bikos na di husban bi di wife head, jos as Kraist bi head for di shosh and naim en save di bodi.
49005024	As di shosh dey sumit to Kraist, na so tu, wife sopoz sumit to dia husban for evritin.
49005025	Husban, mak una luv una wife, jos as Kraist luv di shosh kon sakrifais en life for am,
49005026	so dat e go fit mak am klin, tru baptism and God wod.
49005027	E du laik dis, so dat di shosh go bi laik wife wey fine wel-wel, wey nor get eni stain, dey du enihaw or get eni oda tin wey fit spoil am.
49005028	Na so tu, husbans sopoz luv dia wife laik dia own bodi. Man wey luv en wife, luv ensef.
49005029	Nobodi don eva hate e own bodi, bot e dey fid and kare for am, jos as Kraist dey kare for di shosh,
49005030	bikos wi bi part for en bodi.
49005031	Na bikos of dis, man go liv en papa and mama go join en wife and di tu of dem, go bi won flesh.
49005032	Dis sikrit wey I dey tel una so big wel-wel, bot na di tin wey dey bitwin Kraist and di shosh, I dey tok abaut.
49005033	So, ish man sopoz luv en own wife, jos as e luv ensef and evri wife sopoz respet en husban.
49006001	Shildren, as una no God, mak una dey hear una papa and mama wod, bikos na wetin una sopoz du bi dat.
49006002	Mak una respet una papa and mama, bikos na dis bi di first komandment from God wey get promis.
49006003	So dat e go beta for una and una go get long life.
49006004	Una wey bi papa, mak una nor mak una shildren ves, bot mak una raiz dem to folo di tishin wey Kraist tish.
49006005	Una wey bi savant, mak una dey obey una masta wit fear, respet and wit klin maind laik sey, na Kraist una dey obey.
49006006	Mak una nor bi laik pipol wey dey du dia wok wen dem si sey, pesin dey luk dem; bikos dem dey fine gud face. Insted, as una bi Kraist savant, mak una dey du wetin God laik from una heart.
49006007	Mak una dey du una wok wit beta maind laik sey, na Kraist una dey du-am for and nor bi humanbin,
49006008	bikos una no sey, ish pesin; weda e bi slave or e dey fri, if e du wetin dey gud, Kraist go riwod am.
49006009	And una wey bi masta, mak una dey trit una savant wel. Mak una nor mak dem fear, bikos both yu and dem get di same masta for hevun and E nor dey favor enibodi enihaw.
49006010	Finali, mak una dey strong wit Kraist mighti pawa.
49006011	Mak una wear komplit soja uniform wey God dey giv, so dat una go fit stand fite di wayo wey devol dey yuz.
49006012	Bikos, wi nor dey fite against humanbin, bot na against di wiked rulas wey dey for dis wold, against evil spirits and pawas wey dey di hevuns.
49006013	Na dis mak mi sey, mak una wear komplit soja uniform wey God dey giv, so dat una go fit stand for groun wen trobol and wahala go kom and wen una don win, una go stil stand wel.
49006014	So, mak una stand wel-wel kon tie trut laik belt roun una waist, den wear bullet proof koat as raitiousnes for una bodi.
49006015	Mak una wear shu for leg wey go show sey, una dey redi to prish di Gud News wey dey giv pipol peace
49006016	and wit all dis, mak una kari fate wey go help una kwensh all di wiked arrows wey Satan dey trow.
49006017	Mak una wear salvashon laik cap for head kon hol di Spirit sword wey bi God wod.
