49006018	Wit difren prayas, mak una dey ask God to help una. Mak una always dey pray wit di Spirit and dey shine una eyes wel-wel. Mak una nor giv up, bot mak una kontinu to pray for all God pipol.
49006019	Mak una pray for mi tu sey, mak God giv mi beta wod enitaim wen I opun my mout to tok and mak I fit esplain di sikrit wey dey di gospol.
49006020	I bi God mesenja, ivun doh I dey for prizin naw. Bot mak una pray sey, I go dey tok wit boldnes as I sopoz to tok.
49006021	Tikikus wey bi my special broda and fateful savant for God wok, go tel una evritin, so dat una go no wetin dey hapun to mi for here.
49006022	Na bikos of dis I send am kom mit una, mak una for no haw tins dey wit us for here and mak e for fit enkorage una heart.
49006023	I pray sey mak God, awa Papa and Oga Jisos Kraist giv all my felow Kristen brodas and sistas peace, luv and fate.
49006024	Mak God grace dey wit evribodi wey luv awa Oga Jisos Kraist wit di luv wey nor dey die.
50001001	Dis leta na from Pol and Timoti, wey bi Jisos Kraist savant. To all God pipol for Filipai, wit dia bishops and lidas.
50001002	Mak God awa papa and Oga Jisos Kraist giv una grace and peace.
50001003	I dey tank my God evritaim I rimemba una.
50001004	Evritaim wen I dey pray for una, I dey du-am wit hapines,
50001005	bikos of haw una dey help mi prish di gospol from di first day wey una hear am kon rish today.
50001006	I dey sure sey, di Pesin wey start dis gud wok for una life, go mak am pafet ontil di day wen Kraist go kom.
50001007	So e dey gud for mi to dey tink abaut una laik dis, bikos una dey my heart. Una don folo mi share from God favor, ivun wen I dey prizin and wen I dey prish di trut abaut di gospol.
50001008	God no sey, bikos of Kraist luv wey dey my heart, I dey miss una wel-wel.
50001009	I pray mak una luv dey strong more-more for God tins wey una learn and mak E help una undastand,
50001010	so dat una go fit shuz wetin beta pas and as una dey du so, una go dey redi for di day wen Kraist go kom.
50001011	Mak di wok wey Kraist du for us and haw to please God, ful una maind. Den all di glori and praiz go bi God own.
50001012	My brodas and sistas, I wont mak una no sey my sofa na to mak di gospol stand.
50001013	Di sojas wey dey gaid di prizin and all di oda pipol don no sey, na bikos of Kraist, I dey prizin
50001014	and bikos of di prizin wey dem put mi so, almost all di brodas and sistas fate for Kraist, don strong wel-wel. And naw, dem don dey prish God wod witout fear.
50001015	Tru-tru, na jelosi and kworel mak som dey prish abaut Kraist, bot odas dey du-am wit beta maind.
50001016	I no sey dis wons na luv mak dem dey du-am, bikos dem no sey I dey here to difend wetin dem dey prish.
50001017	Doz oda wons wey dey prish abaut Kraist dey du so, bikos dem dey tink abaut diasef and bikos of wetin dem go gain. Dem nor dey du tins wit klin maind and dem tink sey dem fit kos more trobol for mi, bikos I dey prizin.
50001018	Bot dat won nor mata to mi. So, weda dem dey pritend or du-am wit klin maind, di mesage abaut Kraist dey kontinu and na dat won dey mak mi hapi. I go kontinu to hapi,
50001019	bikos I no sey na una praya and di help wey Kraist Spirit dey giv, dey save mi.
50001020	Di hope wey I get bi sey, shame nor go eva fit kash mi; my heart go strong wel-wel and as I dey du naw, na so I go always dey du. Evritin for my bodi go praiz Kraist, weda I dey alaif or don die.
50001021	Bikos to mi, to dey dis life, na to liv for Kraist and to die insaid Kraist, na dat won beta pas.
50001022	If I kontinu to dey liv insaid dis bodi, e min sey I go du beta wok, bot I nor no wish won I go laik pas;
50001023	Naw, I no wish won I go shuz, bikos I won go dey wit Kraist and na dat won beta pas.
50001024	Bot e go gud for una as I stil dey for dis bodi.
50001025	I dey sure of dis tins: I no sey I nor go die naw, so dat I go kontinu wit una and as una dey insaid di fate, una life go dey beta more-more.
50001026	So wen I go kom mit una again as una dey serv Kraist, una go get more rizin to dey hapi bikos of mi.
50001027	Mak una life dey show sey una biliv Kraist mesage, so dat weda I kom si una or not, I go dey hear sey una dey strong wit won spirit, won maind and dey fite togeda mak di gospol for stand.
50001028	Mak una nor fear una enimis, bikos dem go soon skata and dat na sign to show sey God go save una.
50001029	God don giv una dis sign, nor bi onli mak una for biliv Kraist, bot mak una for stil sofa for am,
50001030	bikos una dey face di same sofa wey una si mi dey face. And I wont mak una no sey, ivun naw, I stil dey sofa di same tin.
50002001	Gain dey to serv Kraist? Komfort dey for en luv? Feloship dey bitwin pipol and God Spirit? Una heart gud rish to show pipol mesi?
50002002	Den, mak una let my joy dey komplit, as una dey agri wit ish oda and dey luv and wok togeda wit won maind.
50002003	Mak una nor dey kari bodi up, bot mak una trit ish oda laik unasef. Insted, una dey du wetin una laik, bikos of di tins wey una go gain, so dat una go fit boast.
50002004	Mak una nor dey tink abaut unsef alone and wetin una wont, bot mak una dey tink abaut wetin gud for odas tu.
50002005	Mak una get di same maind wey Kraist get,
50002006	wey bi sey, ivun doh en wit God na di same, e nor boast abaut am.
50002007	Bot e liv evritin wey e get for hevun kon bi laik savant. So e kom dis wold as humanbin.
50002008	E put en bodi dan kon obey God, ontil Ju pipol kil and nail am for kros!
50002009	Bikos of dis, God raiz-am up kon gi-am di name wey big pas evri oda name,
50002010	so dat wen dem kol Jisos name, evribodi and evritin must nil dan, weda dem dey hevun, eart or for unda di eart
50002011	and evri tongue go konfes sey, "Na Jisos Kraist bi di Oga." Den all di glori go bi God own.
50002012	So, my frends wey I luv; pipol wey dey always obey mi, (nor bi onli wen I dey wit una, bot una dey obey wel-wel, ivun wen I nor dey wit una). Mak una kontinu to du God wok wit all una heart, so dat una salvashon go ful wel-wel,
50002013	bikos na God dey wok insaid una, so dat una go fit du gud tins and get di pawa wey go mak una hapi.
50002014	Mak una nor yuz vesnashon tak wok for God,
50002015	so dat una nor go get eni blame and una go dey klin. God Pikin nor get fault; ivun doh una dey liv for di wold wey bad pipol dey, una go dey shine laik stars,
50002016	bikos una get God mesage wey dey giv life. So, di day wen Kraist go kom, I go get rizin to boast sey I nor run dis race or wok for nor-tin.
50002017	Bot ivun if dem tak mi offa sakrifais for una, I go dey hapi,
50002018	so mak una kom folo mi rejoice.
50002019	As Jisos Kraist wont am, I go send Timoti kom mit una, so dat my heart go strong smol, wit di news wey I go hear abaut una.
50002020	Among all di pipol for here, na onli Timoti get di kaind maind wey I get for una and naim dey mak mi tink of una and haw una dey manage.
50002021	Di odas dey bizi wit dia own mata, bot nor bi mata wey konsan Kraist.
50002022	Una no haw mi and Timoti bi, sey as pikin dey wok wit en papa, na so e dey folo mi wok, so dat di gospol go stand.
50002023	I go soon send am kom mit una, so dat una go no haw my kondishon bi.
50002024	Aldoh I biliv Kraist sey, e nor go tey, bifor mi mysef go kom visit una.
50002025	Bot bifor dat taim, I don tink am sey, e gud mak I send Epafroditus kom mit una. En na my broda, co-woka and soja. Na una mesenja e bi and e dey help mi enitaim wey I nid enitin.
50002026	Tru-tru, e miss all of una wel-wel and en maind dey wori am, bikos una hear sey e nor wel.
50002027	E sik wel-wel sotey e nearli die. Bot God get mesi for am; nor bi onli for am, bot for mi tu, so dat I nor go krai join di won wey I dey so.
50002028	Na dis mak mi won rili send am kom mit una, so dat wen una si-am, una go dey hapi again and I nor go dey wori abaut una.
50002029	So mak una welkom and respet am as una broda for Kraist wit hapines,
50002030	bikos e nearli die bikos of Kraist. E put en life for danga, so dat e go fit help mi du wetin una for du, since una nor dey here.
50003001	Finali, my brodas and sistas, mak una hapi bikos una get Kraist. I dey rite di same tin giv una again, bikos e go help una.
50003002	Mak una shine una eye, bikos of doz wey dey bihav laik dogs and wiked pipol wey dey ponish dia bodi!
50003003	Na wi bi di ril sekonsishon; di pipol wey dey woship God tru en Spirit; pipol wey dey hapi insaid Kraist and wi nor dey put awa hope for wetin pipol dey du.
50003004	Aldoh my own rizin important tu. If enibodi tink sey e get beta rizin to put hope for wetin humanbin dey du, mi Pol, get pas dem.
50003005	Dem sekonsaiz mi, ate days afta dem born mi. I kom from Izrel, Benjamin tribe and I bi Hebrew man. I bin dey liv akordin to di law, bikos I bi Farisi.
50003006	Bikos I rili won du God wok, I kon dey kause serious wahala for di pipol wey dey di shosh. I du evritin jos as di law sey mak wi du, so dat wi go dey gud for God eye. So, I nor get eni fault.
50003007	Bot all dis tins wey I si as gain, I kon kount dem to bi nor-tin, bikos of Kraist.
50003008	Nor bi onli doz wons, bot naw, I dey luk evritin as nor-tin, wen I kompare am wit Kraist, my Oga wey I no and I trowey evritin, bikos of am. Tru-tru, I dey luk all doz tins as yeye, so dat I go fit gain Kraist,
50003009	kon bi won wit am. My raitiousnes nor kom from di law, bot I dey raitious tru my fate for Kraist. Bikos na tru fate God tak mak us dey raitious wit am.
50003010	Wetin I wont na to no am and di pawa wey wak Kraist from deat; to sofa wetin e sofa; to bi as e bi wen e die,
50003011	so dat mi tu go stil wak-up from deat, as e wak.
50003012	Nor bi sey I don get evritin wey I wont or God don mak mi pafet, bot I dey trai mak I get di prize kon hol am as Jisos Kraist hol mi.
50003013	My brodas and sistas, I nor luk mysef laik sey I don get evritin wey I wont. Bikos I dey tink of onli won tin wey bi: to forget di tins wey don pas kon dey porshu di wons wey dey front
50003014	and as I put my maind for dis tins, I dey trai to get di prize wey bi life for hevun; prize wey mak God kol us tru en pikin, Jisos Kraist.
50003015	So doz of us wey don mature for Kraist, mak wi get dis kaind maind. Bot if una dey tink difren tins, I biliv sey God go show una di trut.
50003016	So, mak wi kontinu to folo di rules wey wi dey folo.
50003017	My brodas and sistas, mak una dey liv laik mi and dey learn from odas wey dey folo us as ezampol.
50003018	Bikos l don tel una bifor and I dey tok am again wit tears for my eye sey, di way meni pipol dey bihav, dey show sey dem bi enimis to Kraist kros.
50003019	Dem go end for hell; na dia bele bi di god wey dem dey serv. Tins wey sopoz mak dem shame, naim dey mak dem hapi and na onli tins for dis wold dem dey tink abaut.
50003020	Bot wi bilong to hevun and wi dey wait awa Savior wey kom from der, wey bi Oga Jisos Kraist.
50003021	E go yuz en pawa wey mak am Oga for evritin, tak shange dis awa ordinari bodi and awa bodi go kon bi laik en own wey get glori.
50004001	My brodas, sistas and frends wey I luv, I dey hungri to si una, bikos una dey mak mi proud. My frends wey I luv, mak una stand wel insaid Kraist!
50004002	I dey beg Udia and Sintike mak dem agri togeda insaid Kraist.
50004003	Yes, my gud frends, I stil dey tel una, mak una help dem. Dem trai as dem dey prish di gospol wit mi, both Klement and my oda co-wokas, wey dia name dey insaid Kraist Life Book.
50004004	Mak una always dey hapi insaid Kraist. I dey tok again sey, mak una dey hapi!
50004005	Mak evribodi no sey una nor laik wahala, bikos Jisos go soon kom.
50004006	Mak una nor let enitin wori una for maind. Insted, for evri kondishon wey una dey face, mak una ask God tru praya for evritin wey una nid and mak una always dey tank am, as una dey pray.
50004007	Den God peace wey pas wetin humanbin fit undastand, go gaid una heart and maind insaid Kraist.
50004008	Finali, my brodas and sistas, tins wey bi tru; wey get respet; wey fine; wey pipol dey tok gud abaut; wey gud wel-wel; wey rish to praiz; na dis kaind tins una sopoz to dey tink abaut.
50004009	So enitin wey una learn, hear and si mi dey du, mak una dey du dem tu. And di God wey dey giv us peace, go dey wit una.
50004010	I dey hapi wel-wel insaid Kraist, bikos una don finali show sey, una dey tink abaut haw I dey manage. (I no sey una get mi for maind bifor, bot una nor get shanse to du enitin for mi).
50004011	I nor dey tok dis won bikos I nid enitin, bot na bikos I don learn to dey okay for eni kondishon wey I si mysef.
50004012	E get somtaim wey I nor get and somtaims, I dey get plenti. Bot for evri kondishon, I don learn haw to dey okay; weda my bele ful or I dey hungri; weda I get plenti or I nor get enitin at-all.
50004013	I fit du evritin tru Kraist wey dey giv mi pawa.
50004014	Bot una trai wel-wel as una help mi wen I dey trobol.
50004015	Filipai pipol, una no sey, wen I komot from Masidonia, for di taim wen I jos start to prish di gospol, na una bi di onli shosh wey help mi and na onli una dey folo mi share for my hapines and sofa.
50004016	Bikos ivun for Tesalonika, una stil send tins kom giv mi.
50004017	I nor dey tok dis bikos I wont gift, bot mak una for gain from dis wok wey una dey du.

51001001	Dis leta na from mi Pol, Jisos Kraist apostol and Timoti my broda, bikos na so God wont am.
51001002	To all God pipol for Kolosey, wey bi awa brodas and sistas for Kraist. Mak God awa Papa giv una grace and peace.

51001004	since wi hear abaut haw una biliv Kraist and di luv wey una get for God pipol.

51001006	kom mit una. Dis gospol dey bear frut for di hol wold and since di day wey una hear am, una don undastand as God grace big rish and e don dey bear frut and grow among una.
51001007	Awa broda Epafras, wey dey wok for Kraist wit all en maind, ivun doh wi nor dey der, na-im tish una di gospol
51001008	and e kon tel us abaut di luv wey di Spirit giv una.

51001010	den una life go beta jos as Kraist wont. For all di gud tins wey una dey du, mak una dey bear frut and learn to no God more-more.
51001011	Wi stil dey pray sey una go dey strong wit God pawa wey get glori. Una go show sey una dey patient and get strong maind for God wok wit hapines.

51001015	God wey wi nor dey si, na Jisos bi en image and for evritin wey E kreate, na Jisos bi di first.
51001016	Bikos God kreate evritin for hevun and eart tru en pikin; both fisica and spiritual tins; weda dem get pawa or dey rule for difren-difren place; God kreate dem tru am and E kreate dem for am.
51001017	Kraist dey bifor evritin and bikos e dey, evritin stil dey wer dem dey.
51001018	Na-im bi head for di bodi wey bi di shosh and from di biginin, na-im bi di firstborn wey raiz-up from grave, so dat e go bi numba won for evritin.
51001019	God dey hapi sey evritin wey dey insaid am, dey insaid en pikin tu
51001020	and tru Kraist blood wey e pour out for us for di kros, God go draw evritin bak to ensef, afta E don mak peace wit tins for hevun and eart.
51001021	Bifor-bifor, bikos of di wiked tins wey una dey du and tink, una dey far from God and una bi en enemi.
51001022	Bot naw, wit en pikin blood, E don draw una klose kom en present, so dat E go mak una en frends wey nor get stain or fault and wey dey holi.
51001023	If tru-tru una get fate and una leg strong for groun, den una go get hope kon hol di gospol wey una hear. Dem don prish dis gospol giv evribodi for di wold and mi, Pol, I don kon bi di gospol savant.
51001024	I dey hapi for di sofa wey I dey sofa for una and for di shosh wey bi Kraist bodi, so I dey tak my bodi komplit wetin rimain for Kraist sofa.
51001025	I bi savant for di shosh, bikos of di wok wey God sey mak I du for una and I dey du-am to komplit God wok.
51001026	So di sikrit wey E hide from awa gran-gran papa dem and evribodi wey dey di wold bifor, E don opun am mak en pipol si.
51001027	God wont mak dem no di rishis wey dey en glori; wey di sikrit get for evribodi and na-im bi Kraist wey dey insaid una. So una get hope sey una go share for God glori.
51001028	As wi dey tel evribodi wetin dem go du, wi dey prish Kraist and tish wit wisdom, so dat wen wi go show una to Kraist, una go don dey pafet.
51001029	So na dis tins I dey strogol and wok for, akordin to en pawa wey dey wok insaid mi.
51002001	Pipol for Laodisia and doz wey neva si mi face to face, I wont mak una no haw I dey wok for una rish.

51002007	Mak una dey strong for groun and dey grow insaid Kraist, so dat una fate go strong as wi dey tish una and una go dey tank God wel-wel.
51002008	Mak una tak kare and nor let enibodi fool una wit wayo tok abaut humanbin wisdom and spiritual pawas wey dey rule di wold, bot mak una dey du as Kraist wont.
51002009	Bikos na Kraist dey show us evritin abaut God.
51002010	And una dey komplit insaid am; bikos na-im bi di head for all di pawas wey dey for hevun and eart.
51002011	Dem sekonsaiz una insaid am. Dis nor bi humanbin sekonsishon, bot na di spirit own, wey Kraist dey du.
51002012	Bikos wen dem baptaiz una, dem bere una wit am and una folo am raiz-up tru di fate wey God pawa dey giv and na dis God raiz-am up.
51002013	And ivun doh una bin don die insaid una sin bikos dem nor sekonsaiz una bodi, God kon mak una dey alaif wit am, bikos E don forgiv una sins.
51002014	E don distroi doz bad-bad tins wey una dey du and wetin dem rite abaut awa debt wey fit kil us, God rimov am kon nail dem for di kros.
51002015	God disgrace wiked and evil rulas for publik, wen E win dem for di kros.
51002016	So mak una nor let enibodi tak fud, drink, parti, new moon or Sabat mata, tak joj una.
51002017	Bikos all dis tins na shadow for di tins wey go kom, bot di ril tin, na Kraist!
51002018	Mak una nor let doz wey dey pritend and woship angels joj una. Dat kaind pesin dey tok enihaw abaut vishon wey e sey e si, bot na yeye tins and sin ful en maind.
51002019	Dat pesin nor dey wit Kraist wey bi di head. Bikos na Kraist join di hol bodi togeda, as dem dey grow insaid God.
51002020	Since una don die wit Kraist and e don fri una from wiked pipol, den why una stil dey bihav as pipol wey nor no God?
51002021	Wen dem sey, mak pipol nor hol, chop or tosh som tins, e nor min enitin.
51002022	All dis tins dey yuzles as pipol dey yuz dem, bikos na humanbin mak all dis rules.
51002023	E bi laik sey dis tins get wisdom, bikos pipol dey woship angels, dey pritend sey dem gud and dey sofa dia bodi; bot dis wisdom nor get value, bikos e nor fit stop pesin mak e nor du di yeye tins wey dey en maind.
51003001	So, if God raiz una wit Kraist, den mak una put maind for tins wey dey hevun; di place wer Kraist for sidan for God rite side.
51003002	Mak una dey tink abaut tins for hevun, nor bi tins for dis eart,
51003003	bikos una don die and una life dey safe wit Kraist for insaid God.
51003004	Wen Kraist (wey bi una life) go kom, una go folo am kom wit glori.
51003005	So mak una kil evri bad karata wey dis wold dey bring: laik to dey slip wit pesin wey una nor mari; dey bihav enihaw; folo dis wold tins; dey du bad tins; long-trot and to serv juju.
51003006	Na dis tins dey mak God ves for doz wey nor dey obey am.
51003007	Na so una dey liv una life bifor wen una bi sinas,
51003008	bot naw, to dey ves enihaw; to get bad maind for pesin; to tak mout spoil pesin and to dey kos pipol, mak una rimov dem from una life.
51003009	Since una don kil una old sef and di tins wey una dey du bifor, mak una nor dey lai giv ish oda.
51003010	Mak una wear di new pesin, so dat una go dey new as una dey learn to no and bi laik di Pesin wey kreate una.

51003012	So, as pipol wey God don shuz, wey holi and wey E luv wel-wel, mak una kwik dey sori for pipol; dey gentol; nor dey kari bodi up and wear patient laik klot for bodi.
51003013	Mak una dey bear wit ish oda; dey forgiv ish oda; ivun doh una get wahala wit enibodi. Jos as Kraist don forgiv una, mak una forgiv odas tu.
51003014	Wit all dis gud tins, mak una luv won anoda, bikos na luv bi di best tin wey fit hol una togeda.
51003015	Mak Kraist peace dey rule una heart (bikos na tru dis peace, Kraist tak kol una as won bodi) and mak una dey tank God.
51003016	Mak Kraist wod stay insaid una and mak una dey tish ish oda wit wisdom wey go mak una heart strong. Mak una dey sing psalm, hymns and spiritual song and dey du all dis tins to rili tank God from una heart.
51003017	For enitin wey una dey du, weda una dey tok or du oda tins, mak una du-am wit awa Oga Jisos Kraist name and tank God tru am.
51003018	Una wey bi wife, mak una dey du wetin una husban wont, as Kraist pipol sopoz du.
51003019	Una wey bi husban, mak una luv una wife and nor dey wiked to dem.
51003020	Una wey bi pikin, mak una dey obey una papa and mama for evritin, (dey du evritin wey una papa and mama tok), bikos na wetin Kraist laik bi dat.
51003021	Una wey bi papa, mak una nor du wetin go mak una shildren ves, so dat life nor go taya dem.

51003024	bikos una no sey God go giv una di gift wey E promis en pipol.
51003025	Pesin wey du bad, God go pay am bak for wetin e du, bikos God dey joj evribodi akordin to wetin dem du, since E nor dey sopot enibodi enihaw.
51004001	Una wey bi masta, mak una trit una savants wel and nor shit dem, bikos una no sey, unasef get masta for hevun.

51004007	Tikikus, my broda wey I luv and awa Oga savant; wey dey wok wel-wel laik mi, go tel una evritin wey dey hapun to mi.

51004018	Mi Pol, dey rite dis gritin wit my own hand. Mak una rimemba di chains wey dem tak tie mi and mak God grace dey wit una.
52001001	Na Pol, Silas and Timoti rite dis leta go giv God and Jisos Kraist pipol wey dey di shosh for Tesalonika. Mak God grace and peace dey wit una.
52001002	Wen eva wi dey pray, wi dey always tank God for all of una.
52001003	Wi rimemba di wok wey una don du tru fate and as una dey bear bikos of di hope wey una get abaut awa Oga Jisos Kraist.
52001004	Awa brodas and sistas wey God luv, wi no sey God don shuz una as en own.
52001005	Nor bi onli tru ordinari wod wi tak prish di gospol giv una, bot na wit di Holi Spirit pawa and wi show sey, evritin wey e tok, na tru. Una no haw wi dey liv and help una.
52001006	So, una kon bigin du as wi and Kraist dey du; ivun doh una sofa wel-wel, una risiv di mesage wit joy wey di Holi Spirit dey giv.
52001007	So una bi ezampol to all di pipol wey biliv Jisos for both Masidonia and Akaya.
52001008	Bikos nor bi onli sey di mesage abaut Kraist don rish evriwer for Masidonia and Akaya, bot dem don hear di news abaut una fate for evriwer. So wi nor ivun nid to tok abaut una again.
52001009	Pipol dey tok abaut haw una welkom us and liv di juju wey una dey serv bifor kon folo di tru God wey get life.
52001010	And una dey wait en pikin wey dey kom from hevun. En pikin, Jisos wey E wak from deat and na-im go save us from God vesnashon wey dey kom.
52002001	Awa brodas and sistas, una no sey awa visit nor dey yuzles.
52002002	Bifor wi kom mit una for Tesalonika, dem sofa and trit us enihaw for Filipai and meni pipol nor wont mak wi tok, bot awa God giv us pawa to prish en Gud News.
52002003	Bikos wetin wi dey prish nor bi wit mistak, dirti maind or wayo,
52002004	bot na God shuz us to prish di gospol and na so wi dey prish am. Wi nor dey du-am mak pipol for praiz us, bot mak God wey dey si awa heart, praiz us by ensef.
52002005	Wi nor eva trai to win una wit swit wods, as una no. And God na awa witnes sey wi nor dey pritend to bi una frends bikos of una moni.
52002006	Wi nor eva sey mak pipol praiz us; weda na una or odas.
52002007	Wen wi dey wit una, wi dey gentol laik as mama dey kare for en pikin, ivun doh wi for fit kolet moni from una since wi bi Kraist apostols.
52002008	Bikos wi luv una, wi dey hapi as wi dey share God wod and awa own life wit una.
52002009	Bot brodas and sistas, wi hope sey una rimemba as wi dey wok for both day and nite, so dat as wi dey prish di gospol, wi nor go bi problem to una.
52002010	As wi dey liv wit una wey biliv Kraist, una and God na awa witnes sey, wi dey holi and dey du gud tins for God eye witout fault.
52002011	As unasef no, wi dey trit una as papa dey trit en shildren.
52002012	Wi dey advise, beg and tok to una sey, una must liv una life as God wont, bikos na-im kol una enta en own kindom and glori.
52002013	Wi stil dey tank God evritaim, bikos wen una asept God mesage wey una hear from us, una nor asept am laik sey na humanbin mesage, bot una asept am as God mesage and tru-tru na God mesage e bi and God dey wok insaid una wey don biliv.
52002014	My brodas and sistas, na di same tin hapun to God shosh for Judea and una wey biliv Kraist for der don stil sofa pain from una kontri men wey bi Ju pipol.
52002015	Di same Ju pipol wey dey ponish us, na dem stil kil awa Oga Jisos Kraist and di profets. Dem dey wiked to evribodi and nor dey du wetin God wont.
52002016	Dem ivun trai to stop us, so dat wi nor go prish di mesage wey go giv salvashon to Gentai pipol. As dem dey du so, dia sins dey plenti more-more. Bot naw, God vesnashon wit ponishment dey kom mit dem.
52002017	My brodas and sistas, afta wi liv una (ivun doh wi stil dey tink abaut una), wi kon dey trai to mak sure sey wi si una again bikos of di luv wey wi get for una.
52002018	Wi bin won kom si una (mi, Pol don trai to kom meni taims), bot Satan spoil awa plan.
52002019	Nor bi una bi awa hope, joy and krawn wey wi go tak boast giv Jisos wen E kom? Yes! Na una!
52002020	Bikos na una bi awa joy and glori!
52003001	Wen wi nor fit bear am again, wi kon sey wi go stay for Atens by awasef.
52003002	So wi kon send Timoti, awa broda wey dey folo us du God wok sey, mak e kom enkorage una konsanin una fate,
52003003	so dat nobodi among una go dey fear, bikos of all dis sofa. Unasef no sey all wetin dey hapun, na as God plan am.
52003004	Wen wi dey wit una, wi dey tel una bifor di taim rish sey, wi go sofa wel-wel and e don dey hapun as una dey si-am.
52003005	So wen I nor fit bear again, I send pesin mak e help mi shek haw una fate bi, bikos I dey fear sey devol wey dey tempt pipol, don tempt una and all di wok wey wi du among una, don dey yuzles.
52003006	Bot naw, Timoti don kom mit us afta e si una and e tel us di Gud News abaut di fate and luv wey una get. E stil tel us sey, una dey always rimemba and dey hungri to si us, jos as wisef dey hungri to si una.
52003007	So, awa brodas and sistas, for all awa trobol and sofa, awa heart dey strong abaut una, bikos of una fate.
52003008	Naw, wi dey alaif again, bikos una stand wel for Kraist
52003009	and wi dey tank God for una. Wi dey tank am for di joy wey wi get for en present bikos of una.

52003011	Mak God awa papa and Oga Jisos priper road for us, so dat wi go si una again.
52003012	Mak Kraist mak una luv for ish oda and for evribodi, grow more-more and big, jos as awa luv for una bi,
52003013	so dat una heart go dey strong for holines. And for di taim wey Kraist go kom wit en pipol, una go dey witout fault for God present.
52004001	Finali, my brodas and sistas, wi dey ask and beg una bikos of Kraist sey, as una don hear from us abaut haw una sopoz liv as God wont (as una dey du naw), mak una kontinu to dey liv laik dat.
52004002	Una no di komands wey wi giv una tru Kraist.
52004003	Na wetin God wont bi dis: mak una dey holi; komot hand for bad tins; nor slip wit hu nor bi yor wife or husban.
52004004	Una wey bi man, mak una dey liv wit una wife for holines and wit respet,
52004005	nor bi to dey folo hu yu nor mari, jos as Gentai pipol wey nor no God dey du.
52004006	Mak nobodi shit en Kristen broda or mak am ves, bikos na God go fite for di pesin wey yu shit and wi don tel una bifor and wi stil dey warn una sey, God go rili ponish pipol wey dey du laik dat.
52004007	Bikos God nor kol us to liv yeye life, bot na to liv holi life.
52004008	So, enibodi wey rejet wetin wi tok; nor bi humanbin autoriti e rejet, bot na God wey giv una en Holi Spirit.
52004009	No nid to rite giv una abaut luv for una felow Kristens, bikos God ensef don tish una abaut haw una sopoz luv ish oda.
52004010	And una rili dey show luv to di Kristen brodas and sistas for Masidonia. My brodas and sistas, wi dey beg una sey, mak una kontinu to dey du laik dat.
52004011	Mak una dey du wel, so dat una go liv kwayet life and dey maind una own biznes; dey wok wit una hand as wi komand una bifor.
52004012	Laik dis, doz sinas go dey respet una and una go get evritin wey una nid.
52004013	Awa brodas and sistas, wi wont mak una no di trut abaut doz pipol wey don die, so dat una nor go dey sad laik pipol wey nor get hope.
52004014	Since wi biliv sey Jisos die and e wak-up; na so tu wi biliv sey, doz wey bi Kristens bifor dem die, God go raiz dem up.
52004015	Bikos wetin wi dey tish una naw, na wetin Kraist tish sey: wi wey dey alaif wen Jisos go kom, nor go folo am go kon liv doz wey don die bikos, all of us go-go wit am.
52004016	God big angel go shaut dey komand as Kraist dey kom dan from hevun; di angel vois go dey loud wit God trumpet and doz wey bi Kristens bifor dem die, go first go up.
52004017	God go kari wi wey rimain for dis wold go mit dem for skai, den all of us go-go mit Kraist for hevun.
52004018	So mak una dey enkorage ish oda wit all dis wod.
52005001	Brodas and sistas, konsanin di taim and season wen dis tins go hapun, wi nor nid to rite enitin giv una.
52005002	Bikos una rili no sey, di day wen Kraist go kom, e go bi laik wen tif dey kom for nite.
52005003	Wen pipol dey sey, "Evritin dey okay and peaceful," na dat taim wahala wey go skata evriwer go kom and e go bi laik di pain wey wuman dey face wen e won born and nobodi go eskape from am.
52005004	Bot una wey bi awa brodas and sistas, mak una komot from daknes, so dat, dat day nor go kom mit una as tif dey kom wen nobodi dey espet,
52005005	bikos all of una na lite shildren. Wi nor bi nite or daknes shildren,
52005006	so mak wi nor dey slip as odas dey du, bot mak wi shine awa eye wel-wel.
52005007	Na for nite pipol dey slip and dey drink enihaw.
52005008	Bot since wi bilong to lite, mak wi dey kwayet, yuz fate and luv tak protet awa chest, den wear di hope wey wi get, laik cap for head.
52005009	Bikos God nor shuz us to sofa en vesnashon, bot to get salvashon tru awa Oga Jisos Kraist
52005010	wey die for us, so dat weda wi dey alaif or wi don die wen e kom, wi go stay togeda wit am for hevun.
52005011	So mak una dey enkorage and help ish oda, jos as una dey du naw.
52005012	Naw wi dey beg una, awa brodas and sistas, mak una dey respet doz wey dey wok, gaid and tel una wetin to du abaut dis mata wey konsan Kraist.
52005013	Bikos of di wok wey dem dey du, mak una luv and respet dem wel-wel.
52005014	Wi dey beg una, awa brodas and sistas, mak una tel pipol wey dey bihav enihaw sey, wetin dem dey du nor gud, den mak una help doz wey dey wik, bot mak una dey patient wit evribodi.
52005015	Mak una dey sure sey nobodi pay bad for bad, bot for evritaim, mak una always dey du gud for ish oda and for evribodi.
52005016	Mak una dey hapi evritaim.
52005017	Mak una dey pray evritaim.
52005018	Mak una dey tank God for evritin, bikos na so God wont sey mak una wey dey insaid Kraist dey du.
52005019	Mak una nor driv God Spirit komot for una life.
52005020	Mak una nor tak God wod wey pesin tok as yeye tin.
52005021	Mak una test evritin kon dey du wetin gud.
52005022	Mak una nor put hand for wiked and evil tins.
52005023	Mak God wey dey giv peace, help una to dey holi go rish di end, so dat for di day wen Kraist go kom, una spirit, soul and maind go dey witout fault.
52005024	Di Pesin wey kol una to du en wok dey fateful.

53001003	Wi get beta rizin to dey tank God evritaim for una, bikos una fate dey grow more-more and di luv wey una get for ish oda, dey grow tu.
53001004	So, bikos of una fate and haw una dey bear wahala and sofa, wi dey yuz una boast to all di pipol for God shosh.
53001005	Dis na sign sey God dey giv koret jojment. E wont mak una dey gud to inherit en kindom and na bikos of dis kindom, una dey sofa so.

53001010	e go driv sinas komot from en present, en pawa and en glori. Dat day, evribodi wey biliv, go praiz am and tru-tru, una biliv evritin wey wi tel una.
53001011	Na dis mak us dey always pray for una sey, as God kol una, E go mak una dey gud and evri gud tin wey una wont, go hapun to una tru en pawa, so dat una wok wey una dey du wit fate, go komplit.
53001012	So, bikos of una, pipol go dey praiz awa Oga Jisos Kraist and akordin to awa God and Oga Jisos Kraist grace, unasef go dey risiv en blessin.
53002001	Naw my brodas and sistas, for di taim wen Jisos go kom and wen God go gada us go mit am, wi won tel una sey,

53002003	Mak nobodi disiv una. Bikos dat day nor go kom ontil trobol go first kom and tru-tru, di pesin wey God go distroi, go kom out.
53002004	E go opoz and kari ensef pas God and oda tins wey pipol dey woship. E go ivun sidan for God tempol dey tok sey e bi God.
53002005	Una rimemba sey wen I dey wit una bifor, I tel una all dis tins.
53002006	And una no wetin dey stop am, bikos e go onli kom out wen en taim don rish.
53002007	Dis wikednes don alredi dey wok for sikrit and dem go dey sikrit ontil di pesin, wey bi di Holi Spirit wey dey hol dem, go komot for road.
53002008	Den evribodi go no hu dis wiked man bi and God go distroi am wit briz from Kraist mout kon bere am wit di glori wey dey kom.
53002009	Di wiked man go kom wit Satan pawa and e go du difren mirakols and wondas.
53002010	E go yuz wayo disiv doz wey go perish, bikos dem nor won luv and respet di trut wey for save dem.
53002011	So God go mak dem disiv dis pipol wel-wel and dem go biliv dia lai-lai.
53002012	Den God go distroi dem, bikos dem enjoy sin insted of di trut.
53002013	Bot my brodas and sistas wey God luv, wi dey always tank God for una evritaim, bikos God don shuz una from di biginin sey, E go save una wit di Holi Spirit pawa wey go mak una dey holi, since una get fate and trut.
53002014	E kol una enta en salvashon tru awa mesage, so dat una go fit get share for Kraist glori.
53002015	So, my brodas and sistas, mak una stand wel for groun kon hol wetin wi tish una tait; weda na tru di wods wey wi tok or letas wey wi rite.

53003001	Finali, my brodas and sistas, mak una pray for us, so dat Kraist mesage go kontinu to spread kon get glori jos as e rili get among una.
53003002	Mak God diliva us from wiked and evil pipol, bikos nor bi evribodi get fate.

53003004	Wi get maind sey Kraist go help una and una go du all di tins wey wi tel una.
53003005	I pray mak God gaid una heart to undastand en luv more-more, so dat una go get Kraist patient.
53003006	My brodas and sistas, wi dey komand una wit awa Oga Jisos Kraist name sey, mak una nor folo bilivas wey dey du enihaw and nor dey du as wi tel dem.
53003007	Una no sey una sopoz to dey imitate us, bikos wi nor bihav enihaw wen wi dey wit una.
53003008	Wi nor chop enibodi fud wey wi nor pay for. Insted, wi dey strogol and wok hard for day and nite, so dat wi nor go bi wahala to una.
53003009	Nor bi sey wi nor get rite to ask una, bot wi won yuz awasef as ezampol for una,
53003010	bikos ivun wen wi dey wit una, wi tel una sey, "Pesin wey nor redi to wok, mak e nor chop."
53003011	Wi hear sey som pipol among una dey liv enihaw and dem nor dey maind dia biznes, insted dem dey put eye for anoda pesin tin.
53003012	Wi dey komand and enkorage dis kaind pipol wit awa Oga Jisos Kraist name sey, mak dem du dia wok wel, so dat dem go fit fid demsef.
53003013	My brodas and sistas, mak e nor taya una to du gud.
53003014	Bot if enibodi nor obey awa mesage tru dis leta, mak una luk dat kaind pesin wel-wel and mak nobodi folo am waka or du enitin togeda, so dat shame go kash am.
