54001001	Pol wey bi Jisos Kraist apostol tru God awa Savior komand, na-im rite dis leta and na Jisos Kraist bi di hope wey wi get:
54001002	To Timoti, my own pikin for di fate. Mak favor, mesi and peace wey dey kom from God awa papa and Jisos Kraist awa Oga, dey wit yu.
54001003	As I tel yu wen I dey go Masidonia, mak yu koret doz pipol for Efisos wey nor dey tish di trut.
54001004	Nor let dem waste oda pipol taim wit dia yeye tok, insted of God wod wey dey mak pesin fate strong.
54001005	Bot di rizin why I dey giv dis komand, na bikos I luv dem from my heart wit beta maind and fate.
54001006	Som disobey dis komand kon dey tok tins wey nor mak sense.
54001007	Dem wont tish pipol di law, bot dem nor undastand wetin dem dey tok, ivun doh dem dey tok wit strong heart.
54001008	Bot wi no sey di law dey gud wen pipol dey obey am.
54001009	God nor giv di law, bikos of gud pipol, bot na for pipol wey dey disobey and du enihaw. Dis kaind pipol dey laik to sin and nor dey fear God. Dem nor dey holi or get respet for enitin and dem fit kil dia papa, mama or enibodi.
54001010	Di law na for pipol wey dey slip wit hu dem nor mari; man wey dey slip wit man; wuman wey dey slip wit wuman; pesin wey dey sel pipol as slave; lai-lai pipol; doz wey dey promis and den nor fit du-am or enibodi wey nor dey obey di rite tishins
54001011	wey dey dis beta gospol, wey awa blessed God sey mak I dey prish.
54001012	I tank Kraist awa Oga, wey giv mi pawa to du en wok. Ivun doh I dey tok bad abaut am and dey opres en pipol bifor,
54001013	e si mi as gud pesin kon shuz mi to serv am. Bot God sori for mi, bikos den I nor no wetin I dey du and I nor biliv en gospol.
54001014	Bot God grace big wel-wel wit fate and luv wey dey for Jisos Kraist.
54001015	Dis na tru wod and e gud for evribodi to asept and biliv am sey: "Jisos Kraist kom dis wold kon save sinas" and na mi wos pas.
54001016	Bot God sori for mi, so dat Kraist go yuz mi as beta ezampol to show sey, e dey patient wit ivun di pesin wey sin pas. Den odas go no sey, demsef go fit biliv am kon get life wey nor dey end.
54001017	Mak all di onor and glori bi God own foreva and eva! Na-im bi di King wey nor dey die, di Won wey nobodi dey si and na onli en bi God. Amen!
54001018	Timoti my pikin, na as dem tok for di wod wey dem profesai abaut yu bifor, na-im mak mi giv yu dis komands. So mak dis wods mak yu strong as yu dey fite for Kraist.
54001019	Hol yor fate for Kraist wel and mak yor maind dey klear. Bikos som pipol nor dey yuz gud maind and bikos of dat, dia fate don skata.
54001020	Himenaeus and Alexander na ezampol of doz kaind pipol. I don giv dem to Satan, so dat dem go stop to dey tok enihaw abaut God.
54002001	First of all, I tel una mak una dey pray, ask and tank God for evribodi.
54002002	Mak una pray for kings and doz wey dey rule, so dat wi go fit liv for peace, get beta karata and gud life wit fear for God.
54002003	Dis kaind tin gud and na wetin God awa Savior dey laik,
54002004	bikos E wont mak evribodi dey save and undastand di trut.
54002005	Bikos na onli won God dey and na Jisos Kraist wey kom as humanbin, bi di pesin wey dey bring God and humanbin togeda.
54002006	E die so dat evribodi go dey fri. Na dis mesage God go giv di wold, wen di taim don rish.
54002007	Na dis tins mak God shuz mi as prisha, apostol and tisha to Gentai pipol, so dat I go prish fate and wetin bi trut (na tru wod I dey tel una so, I nor dey lai).
54002008	So, I wont mak evribodi dey pray for evriwer, dey raiz dia holi hand witout vesnashon or kowrel.
54002009	I wont mak wimen dey dress wel wit sef kontrol. Nor mak yeye hair style; nor wear tu mush gold or stones and klot wey dear wel-wel.
54002010	Insted, mak dem get gud karata as wimen wey dey fear God, sopoz bi.
54002011	Mak wimen dey kwayet and listin wel as dem dey learn.
54002012	I nor alow wuman tish or giv dem authoti ova men. Mak dem kwayet dey listin,
54002013	bikos na Adam God first kreate, nor bi Eve.
54002014	And nor bi Adam, Satan disiv. Satan disiv di wuman and na so sin tak kom dis wold.
54002015	Bot God go save di wuman wen e won born, so-far e kontinu to get fate, luv, holines and dey kontrol ensef.
54003001	Dis na tru wod: If eni man laik to bi lida, na beta wok e wont.
54003002	Leada for shosh must bi pesin wey nor get fault; wey get onli won wife; fit kontrol ensef; get sense and respet; dey welkom pipol and e bi gud tisha.
54003003	Mak e nor bi drunkard or pesin wey laik to fite; bot e must dey gentol. Mak e nor bi pesin wey laik to kowrel or luv moni.
54003004	E must bi pesin wey dey manage en own haus wel and dey mak en shildren obey and respet am.
54003005	If pesin nor fit manage en own haus, na haw e go tak manage God shosh?
54003006	Hu won bi lida must bi pesin wey get strong fate, bikos if e nor strong for fate, e go start to kari bodi up, den Satan go ponish am.
54003007	Pipol wey nor dey di shosh must dey tok wel abaut di pesin wey bi lida, so dat dem nor go disgrace and mak am fal enta devol trap.
54003008	Laik dis tu, dikins must bi pipol wey get gud karata; nor bi pipol wey dey play wayo; dey drink enihaw or luv moni.
54003009	Dem must bi pipol wey get maind and dey prish di trut abaut di fate wey God don show us.
54003010	Bifor dem go shuz dikins, mak dem test dem wel-wel. If dem pas di test, den dem fit serv as dikins.
54003011	Laik dis tu, dia wives must get gud karata, nor bi wives wey dey lai or gossip, bot dem must fit dey kontrol diasef and dey honest for evritin.
54003012	Dikin must dey fateful to en wife and must fit kontrol en shildren and evritin for en haus.
54003013	Doz wey don serv wel as dikins, pipol go respet dem wel-wel and di fate wey dem get for Kraist, go dey strong.
54003014	I dey rite all dis komand to una naw, ivun doh I dey hope to kom si una soon,
54003015	so dat if I nor kwik kom, una go no haw pipol sopoz bihav for God shosh, wey bi di tru pillar and foundashon.
54003016	Wi no sey God ways dey great wel-wel: Kraist kom as humanbin; di Spirit show sey e dey fri; angels si-am wen e kom prish among Gentai pipol; pipol biliv am for di wold and God kari am go hevun wit glori.
54004001	Di Spirit tok sey for di last days, som pipol go liv di fate kon dey biliv lai-lai spirits and folo wetin dimons dey tish.
54004002	Dis pipol dey lai and na wayo dem sabi du and dia maind don skata.
54004003	Dem dey tish sey, e nor gud to mari or chop som kaind fud. Bot na God kreate dis fud and E sey pipol wey biliv di trut fit chop am afta dem don tank am.
54004004	Bikos evritin wey God kreate, dey gud and wi nor sopoz rejet eni fud, so-far wi don tank God for am,
54004005	bikos God wod and praya don mak am klin.
54004006	If yu giv all dis komands to di brodas and sistas, yu go bi gud savant for Kraist, bikos yu don fid yorsef wit God wod, wey bi di spiritual fud and naim bi di gud tishin wey yu dey folo.
54004007	Bot mak una rejet lai-lai and yeye stori. Insted mak una dey train unasef wit beta wods from God.
54004008	Fisica tranin dey gud, bot na to no God gud pas, bikos yu go get riwod for dis life and di won wey dey kom.
54004009	Dis na tru wod and e gud mak evribodi asept am wit beta maind.
54004010	Na dis mak wi dey wok hard and dey strogol, bikos awa hope dey wit God wey dey alaif and E dey save evribodi, especiali doz wey biliv am.
54004011	Mak yu tish di pipol dis tins and mak sure sey, dem du dem.
54004012	Nor let enibodi opres yu bikos of yor age; bot mak yu show ezampol to doz wey biliv tru yor wod, karata, luv, fate and as yu gud rish.
54004013	Ontil I kom bak, mak yu dey read God Wod for shosh, dey enkorage di bilivas and tish dem.
54004014	Nor stop to dey yuz di spiritual gift wey yu get; bikos yu get am tru profesi, wen eldas put hand for yor head dey pray.
54004015	Mak yu dey learn dis tins; dey du-am wit all yor maind, so dat pipol go si as yu dey progress.
54004016	Mak yu wosh as yu dey liv yor life and di tins wey yu dey tish. Get patient, bikos if yu dey du laik dis, yu go save yorsef and doz wey dey listin to yu.
54005001	Mak yu nor tok enihaw to pesin wey old pas yu, bot dey tok to am wit respet laik sey yu dey tok to yor papa. Tok to young men as yu go tak tok to yor broda.
54005002	Mak yu trit wimen wey old pas yu laik sey dem bi yor mama and wimen wey yu senior, mak yu trit dem wit gud maind laik sey dem bi yor sistas.
54005003	Respet and kare for wimen wey dia husban don die.
54005004	Bot if di wuman get shildren or grand-shildren, di first tin wey dem go du for dia famili, na to show sey dem dey fear God, as dem dey kare for dia papa and mama. Dis na wetin dey mak bele swit God.
54005005	Naw, wuman wey en husban don die and e rili dey alone for dis wold, dey trust God. E dey pray for nite and day sey mak God help am.
54005006	Bot if e jos dey enjoy ensef enihaw for dis wold, dat min sey en spirit don die, ivun doh e stil dey alaif.
54005007	Mak yu always dey giv dis komand so dat dem nor go get fault.
54005008	Bot if enibodi nor fit kare for en pipol, especiali en famili membas, e don denai di fate bi dat and e wos pas sina.
54005009	Wuman wey don pas sisti years and e dey fateful to en husban bi for di man die, mak una put am join doz wey di shosh dey help.
54005010	Evribodi go no am for di gud wok wey e dey du sey: e don train shildren; dey welkom stranjas; dey serv God pipol; dey help doz wey nor get and e dey du difren gud wok.
54005011	Bot young wuman wey en husban jos die, mak una nor put am join doz wey di shosh dey help, bikos wen dem dey hungri to mari again, dem go fit liv Kraist kon bigin sin.
54005012	So God go joj dem, bikos dem don break dia promis.
54005013	For di same taim, dem go dey lazi, dey waka from haus to haus, dey du aproko and tok enihaw.
54005014	So I wont mak di young wimen mari; born shildren; dey gaid dia haus, so dat enemis nor go get shanse to akuiz dem.
54005015	Bikos som pipol don alredi dey folo Satan.
54005016	If enibodi wey biliv get relashons wey en husban don die, mak e help dem. Mak e nor wori di shosh abaut dem, so dat dem go fit help di oda wimen wey dia husban don die.
54005017	Doz wey dey lid wel, mak dem pay dem wel, especiali doz wey dey wok and tish wel-wel, so dat di gospol go stand.
54005018	Bikos God wod sey, "Anima wey dey havest korn, mak una nor tie en mout." Enibodi wey dey wok, sopoz get en pay.
54005019	Mak yu nor asept eni wods wey dem tok against eni lida, unles tu or tiri pipol bear witnes sey na tru.
54005020	Doz wey dey sin, mak yu koret dem for evribodi front, so dat e go bi warnin to odas.
54005021	For God, Jisos Kraist and di angels wey dey wit us, I dey enkorage yu mak yu obey all di komands witout wayo.
54005022	Mak yu nor huri to mak pesin lida and nor rush put hand for en head, so dat yu nor go kari anoda pesin sin for yor head. Mak yu kip yorsef pure.
54005023	Nor dey drink onli wota, bot mak yu stil drink smol wine bikos of yor bele wey dey mak yu sik enihaw.
54005024	Rimemba sey som pipol dey sin mak evribodi si-am and dis dey joj dem. Bot e get som wey yu nor go no dia sins naw, bot leta, e go kom out for publik.
54005025	Laik dis tu, pipol dey si di gud wok wey odas dey du and won day, di gud wok wey dem du for sikrit, go kom out for publik.
54006001	Una wey bi savants, mak una dey respet una masta, so dat nobodi go tok bad abaut God and wetin wi dey tish.
54006002	Mak una nor disobey una masta, bikos dem bi bilivas. Bot mak una serv and luv dem wel, bikos di mastas wey una dey serv, na Kristen dem bi. Timoti, mak yu tish dis tins and dey enkorage evribodi to obey am.
54006003	If enibodi dey tish wetin nor koret and nor agri wit awa Oga Jisos Kraist tishin and as God wont mak wi dey liv awa life,
54006004	dat pesin dey proud and na onli to dey argue and kworel, e no. Dis kaind tin nor gud, bikos jelosi, kworel, lai-lai, to dey suspect odas enihaw
54006005	and wahala, naim e dey kause. Dia maind don spoil and dem nor no di trut again, bikos dem tink sey dem fit yuz God wok tak mak moni.
54006006	To liv as God wont and dey hapi wit wetin E giv yu, dey bring beta riwod.
54006007	Bikos wi nor bring enitin kom dis wold and tru-tru, wi nor go tak won singol tin komot from dis wold afta wi don die.
54006008	Bot if wi get fud to chop and klot to wear, mak dem rish us.
54006009	Pipol wey won get moni by fos, dey fal enta temtashon and dem dey get trot for yeye tins wey go distroi and put dem for wahala.
54006010	Pesin wey luv moni, go get wahala, wiked and evil tins. Bikos som pipol won get moni by fos, dem don fal komot from di fate kon wound demsef enihaw.
54006011	Bot yu wey dey serv God, mak yu nor put hand for all dat kaind tin. Insted, mak yu dey strogol to du wetin dey rite and gud; dey kip yor promis, dey luv, get patient and dey gentol.
54006012	Mak yu fite di fite wey dey mak fate strong and hol di life wey nor dey end, wey go mak pipol praiz God, bikos na dis mak am kol yu.
54006013	Bifor God wey dey giv life to all tins and Jisos Kraist wey tok wel for Pontius Pilate front, I dey tel yu from my heart sey,
54006014	mak yu obey dia komands witout fault or blame, ontil awa Oga Jisos Kraist go kom.
54006015	Bikos wen di taim don rish, Kraist go kom from hevun wit God mighti pawa: Na God bi di King for all kings and Oga of all oga.
54006016	Dis God nor fit die and E dey stay for lite wey nobodi dey fit waka near. Lite wey humanbin neva fit si. Mak all onor and pawa bi en own foreva and eva. Amen!
54006017	Mak yu giv dis komand to rish pipol. Tel dem sey, mak dem nor dey kari bodi up kon dey trust dia moni wey nor get value and mak dem dey trust God wey dey giv us evritin wey wi nid to tak enjoy dis life.
54006018	Tel dem sey, mak dem yuz dia moni tak du gud. Mak dem dey du plenti gud woks kon dey giv doz wey nor get and mak dem always dey redi to share wit odas.
54006019	If dem dey du laik dis, dem go dey yuz dia moni and propati tak lay gud foundashon for dia future, so dat dem go get life wey nor dey end.
54006020	Timoti, mak yu gaid wetin God giv yu wel-wel. Nor put yor mout for yeye tins or mata wey pipol wey nor no God dey tok and du, bikos dem dey opoz yu wit wetin dem feel sey dem no.
54006021	Som pipol don fal komot from di fate, bikos dem dey listin to pipol wey dey du doz bad tins. Mak God grace dey wit all of una.
55001001	Na Pol, Jisos Kraist apostol rite dis leta, bikos na so God wont am, so dat I go prish abaut di life wey God promis us tru Kraist.
55001002	To Timoti, my pikin wey I luv. Mak grace, mesi and peace dey wit yu from God awa Papa and awa Oga Jisos Kraist.
55001003	Eni taim I rimemba yu for my praya, weda na for nite or day taim, I dey always tank God wey I dey serv wit beta maind, jos as my gran-gran papa dem serv am.
55001004	Wen I rimemba as yu tak krai, e dey hungri mi to kom si yu, so dat joy go ful my maind.
55001005	I always dey rimemba di fate wey yu first get from yor gran mama, Lois and from yor mama, Eunice. I dey sure sey e dey insaid yu.
55001006	Na dis mak mi dey rimaind yu sey, mak yu dey yuz God gift wey yu get wel and yu risiv dis gift afta I lay hand for yor head.
55001007	Bikos God nor giv us di spirit wey go mak us fear, bot di spirit wey E giv us, get pawa, luv and sef-kontrol.
55001008	So mak yu dey proud to tok abaut Kraist or abaut mi wey dey prizin bikos of am and mak yu yuz di pawa wey God giv yu, tak folo mi sofa for dis gospol.
55001009	Bikos God save and kol us to liv holi life. E du laik dis, nor bi sey wi deserve am bikos of wetin wi du, bot na so E plan am ivun bifor di wold start, so dat wi go no en grace tru Jisos Kraist.
55001010	Bot naw, E don bring all dis plan out wen awa Oga Jisos Kraist kom dis wold. E distroi deat pawa kon bring life wey nor dey end tru di gospol.
55001011	Na dis gospol mak God shuz mi as prisha, apostol and tisha.
55001012	And naim mak mi dey sofa wetin I dey sofa so. Bot I nor dey shame, bikos I no di Pesin wey I dey serv and I dey sure sey, E go gaid di tin wey I gi-am hol, ontil di day wey Kraist go kom.
55001013	Mak yu kontinu wit di wod wey I tel yu kon dey du-am wit di fate and luv wey dey insaid Kraist.
55001014	Mak yu gaid di gud tins wey God giv yu tru di Holi Spirit wey dey insaid us.
55001015	Yu no sey evribodi for Asia, Figelus and Hermogenes aria, don run liv mi.
55001016	Mak God show en mesi to Onesiforus famili, bikos e dey always mak mi hapi and e nor dey shame sey I dey prizin.
55001017	Wen e kom Rome, e faind mi for evriwer ontil e si mi.
55001018	For di day wen Kraist go kom, mak e show am en mesi! And yu no haw e help mi wen I dey Efisos.
55002001	So yu, my pikin, mak yu dey strong for di grace wey Kraist dey giv.
55002002	Di tins wey yu hear mi tok for pipol present, mak yu tish oda pipol wey yu trust sey dem dey redi to tish odas.
55002003	Mak yu dey redi to sofa as mi and odas dey sofa, so dat yu go bi gud soja for Kraist.
55002004	Nor-tin konsan sojas wit tins wey ordinari pipol dey du; if not, e nor go du wetin en oga wont.
55002005	Bikos enibodi wey dey run race, nor go fit win unles e folo di rule wey dey di game.
55002006	Farma wey wok wel-wel, naim sopoz get di first share for di havest.
55002007	Mak yu tink abaut wetin I dey tok so and Kraist go help yu to undastand evritin.
55002008	Rimemba Jisos Kraist wey kom from David famili; di pesin wey God raiz from deat; bikos na so e bi for di mesage wey I dey prish
55002009	and na dis Gud News mak mi dey sofa, so-tey, dem kon put mi for prizin laik tif; bot dem nor fit put God wod for prizin!
55002010	So I dey redi to bear di sofa, as long as e go save doz wey God don shuz insaid Kraist, wit glori wey go dey foreva and eva.
55002011	Dis wod na tru: If wi die wit am, wi go liv wit am tu.
55002012	If wi bear wit am, den wi go reign wit am tu and if wi sey wi nor no am, en tu go sey, e nor no us.
55002013	Weda wi get fate for am or not, Kraist go stil bi hu e bi and e nor go shange.
55002014	Mak yu rimaind evribodi abaut dis tins, den mak yu komand dem for God present sey, mak dem nor dey argue abaut wods, bikos doz kaind tins nor dey gud and e fit konfuz doz wey dey listin.
55002015	Mak yu du evritin wey yu fit du, so dat God go si yu as beta pesin. Dey du yor wok wel as pesin wey nor dey shame, bot dey redi to esplain God wod wey bi trut.
55002016	Mak yu nor put mout for yeye tok, bikos pipol wey dey du doz tins, dey far from God.
55002017	Dia wod dey spread laik diziz and na dis tin hapun to Himenaeus and Filetus.
55002018	Dem liv di trut kon dey sey resurreshon don hapun alredi and laik dis, dem don mak som pipol fal from di fate.
55002019	Bot God strong foundashon stil stand and dem rite put sey, "God no en pipol" and "Evribodi wey bi Kraist own, must stop to du evil."
55002020	Wen yu go rish man haus, nor bi onli gold and silva tins dey der, bot tins wey dem yuz wud and clay tak mak stil dey der tu and som dey mak di haus fine and odas nor gud at-all.
55002021	So if yu kip yorsef witout fault, yu go bi beta pesin wey Kraist fit yuz as e dey du en gud wok.
55002022	Mak yu run from doz tins wey dey hungri young pipol to du, so dat yu go please God foreva. Den yu go fit luv and stay for peace wit odas wey dey serv God wit klin heart.
55002023	I dey tel yu again sey, mak yu nor put mout for yeye wod, bikos yu no sey dis kaind tin dey kause kworel.
55002024	Pesin wey bi Kraist savant nor dey kworel, insted e must dey gud wit evribodi, must sabi tish wel-wel and get patient wit stuborn pipol.
55002025	E must dey gentol as e dey koret pipol wey dey opoz en prishin. May bi God go let dem turn from sin kom mit am, so dat dem go no di trut.
55002026	Den dia sense go koret and dem nor go fal enta devol trap again. Bikos devol don kash dem put insaid en trap bifor and den dem dey du enitin wey e wont.
55003001	Mak yu undastand sey, for di last days bifor dis wold go end, tins go hard wel-wel.
55003002	Pipol go dey tink of diasef alone; dey laik moni; dey boast; dey kari bodi up; dey tok bad abaut God; dey disobey dia papa and mama and dem nor dey tank ivun pipol wey du gud for dem.
55003003	Dem nor get luv or forgivenes; dem go dey gossip odas and nor fit kontrol diasef. Dem go dey wiked and hate wetin gud.
55003004	Dem go betray dia frends; dey du tins bifor dem tink; dey feel sey dem dey important and dem go luv enjoyment pas God.
55003005	If yu luk dem wel-wel, dem bi laik God pipol, bot dem don rejet God pawa. So mak yu run from dis kaind pipol.
55003006	Bikos na dis pipol dey hide enta pipol haus kon slip wit wimen wey nor get sense; wey dey sin wel-wel and wetin dey swit dis wimen to du, na-im dey kontrol dem.
55003007	Doz kaind wimen dey trai to learn, bot dem nor dey fit no di trut.
55003008	Jos as Jannes and Jambres opoz Mosis; na so tu, dis pipol wey dia maind blok and nor get fate, dey opoz di trut.
55003009	Bot dem nor go du-am tey, bikos evribodi go si haw dem foolish rish, jos as e hapun to Jannes and Jambres.
55003010	Bot yu don no my tishins; di way I dey liv my life and why I dey du wetin I dey du: my fate, patient, luv and as I dey bear.
55003011	Yu no di wahala and sofa wey hapun to mi for Antiok, Ikonium and for Lystra. I bear all dis wahala and Kraist save mi from dem.
55003012	Tru-tru, enibodi wey won liv di kaind life wey God wont insaid Kraist, mak e no sey e must sofa.
55003013	Bot wiked and evil pipol nor go prospa. Dem go disiv odas and dem go disiv diasef tu.
55003014	Bot mak yu kontinu to du wetin yu learn. Yu no sey dis tins na tru and yu trust doz wey tish yu.
55003015	Dem don tish yu God wod since yu bi smol pikin and yu don get savashon to risiv di wisdom wey dey kom tru Kraist, wey yu trust.
55003016	Evri wod wey dey Bibol, kom from God and dem dey gud to tish us di trut and to no di tins wey dey wrong for awa life. God wod dey koret us wen wi dey wrong and e dey tish us to du gud tins,
55003017	so dat as wi dey du God wok, wi go fit du-am wel and wi go get evritin wey wi nid to tak du gud tins.
55004001	I dey tel yu wetin to du for God and Jisos Kraist present. Wen Kraist go apier to mak en kindom stand, e go joj pipol wey dey alaif and doz wey don die.
55004002	Mak yu dey prish God wod and dey redi, weda di taim dey okay or not. Mak yu yuz patient tak koret and enkorage yor pipol wit beta tishin.
55004003	Bikos taim dey kom wen pipol nor go won hear gud and beta tishin again. Insted, dem go dey folo wetin dey hungri dem to du kon dey faind tisha wey go tish dem wetin dem won hear.
55004004	Dem go rejet di trut and luv lai-lai stori.
55004005	Bot mak yu kontrol yorsef for evritin. Nor fear to sofa for Kraist. Dey du God wok and dey tel odas abaut di Gud News.
55004006	For mi, I don alredi yuz my life as ofrin for God wok, bikos di taim wey I go die, don near.
55004007	I don fite di gud fite for di fate wey I get; I don run di race finish; I don du wetin I promis sey I go du.
55004008	Naw, di prize for raitiousnes dey wait mi and na God wey dey joj rite go giv mi dis prize for di day wen Kraist go kom. Di prize nor bi for mi alone, bot na for evribodi wey dey wait for Kraist to kom bak.
55004009	Mak yu trai yor best to kom si mi soon.
55004010	Bikos Demas luv dis wold tins, e kon run liv mi go Tesalonika. Krescens don go Galatia and Titus go Dalmatia.
55004011	Na onli Luke dey wit mi. Mak yu kari Mark folo bodi wen yu dey kom, bikos e go fit help mi for di ministri wok.
55004012	I send Tikikus go Efisos.
55004013	Wen yu dey kom, bring di klot wey I liv wit Karpus for Troas. Mak yu bring my books, especiali my papers.
55004014	Alexander wey dey du iron wok, wiked mi wel-wel, bot Kraist go joj am for wetin e du.
55004015	Mak yu dey kareful wit am, bikos e fite against evritin wey wi tok.
55004016	Di first taim wen dem kari mi go kourt, evribodi abandon mi and all of dem run liv mi. Mak God nor joj dem bikos of wetin dem du!
55004017	Bot God dey for my side and E giv mi pawa, so dat tru mi, Gentai pipol go hear di Gud News and Kraist don save mi from lion mout!
55004018	And Kraist go stil save mi from evri evil plan ontil e tak mi enta en kindom. Mak glori bi en own foreva and eva. Amen!
55004019	Mak yu help mi grit Priska, Akwila and Onesiforus famili.
55004020	Erastus dey for Korint and bikos Trofimus wey nor wel, I kon liv am for Miletus.
55004021	Mak yu trai kom bifor kold season go rish. Eubulus, Pudens, Linus, Klaudia and all di brodas and sistas dey grit yu.
55004022	Mak Kraist dey wit yor spirit. Mak God grace and favor dey wit yu.
56001001	Na Pol, wey bi Jisos Kraist apostol and God savant rite dis leta to help pipol wey God don shuz, so dat dia fate go strong kon no di trut wey go help dem liv di kaind life wey God wont.
56001002	Di trut dey giv dem di maind sey dem get life wey nor dey end and na God wey nor fit lai promis dem dis life ivun bifor E kreate di wold.
56001003	As di taim don rish, E don giv us en mesage tru di wod wey wi dey prish giv evribodi and na God awa Savior giv mi pawa to du dis wok.
56001004	I dey rite to Titus, my own pikin for fate. Mak grace and peace wey dey kom from God awa Papa and from awa Savior Jisos Kraist, dey wit yu.
56001005	Titus! Na dis mesage mak mi liv yu for Krete, so dat yu go kontinu awa wok for der and pick new lidas for ish tawn, jos as I komand yu.
56001006	Enibodi wey won bi elda must dey gud. E must get onli won wife and en shildren must bi bilivas, dey gentol and dey respet demsef.
56001007	Mak pesin wey bi lida nor get fault, bikos na God wok e dey du. Mak e nor dey kari bodi up; dey kwik ves or drink enihaw; dey laik to beat pipol or luv moni.
56001008	Insted mak e dey welkom stranjas for en haus; luv wetin dey gud and e must get sense; mak e nor dey put hand for bad tin; e must dey holi and fit kontrol ensef.
56001009	E must biliv di mesage abaut God wey e dey tish, so dat e go fit tel pipol di trut and koret doz wey dey opoz am.
56001010	Meni pipol nor won du wetin God tok, insted, dem dey tok enihaw, dey disiv pipol and folo Ju pipol law wey sey, evribodi must sekonsaiz.
56001011	So wi must stop dem, bikos dem dey tish pipol tins wey go mak pipol komot from di trut and dem dey du laik dis, bikos of di moni wey dem go get.
56001012	Ivun won of dia own profets sey, "Krete pipol dey always tok lai, dem bi wiked animas and lazi pipol wey get long-trot."
56001013	Wetin di profet tok, na tru. So bikos of dis, mak yu stop dem, so dat di bilivas go strong for fate.
56001014	Mak dem stop to listin to Ju pipol lai-lai stori and nor dey bihav laik doz wey nor biliv.
56001015	Evritin dey pure to doz wey dia heart dey pure. Bot nor-tin dey pure to doz wey bad tins ful dia maind.
56001016	Dis kaind pipol dey sey dem no God, bot di way wey dem dey liv dia life, show sey dem nor no am, bikos dem get bad maind, dey disobey God and dem nor eva dey laik beta tin.~
56002001	Bot for yu Titus, yu must tish pipol haw to bihav wel.
56002002	Mak yu tish old men sey, mak dem nor dey bihav enihaw, so dat pipol go respet dem and mak dem dey kontrol demsef; get fate; dey show luv and dey patient.
56002003	Mak yu tish old wimen sey, mak dem liv life wey go mak God hapi. Mak dem nor tok bad abaut pipol; nor dey drink enihaw, insted mak dem tish oda wimen wetin dey gud.
56002004	So, mak di old wimen train and tish di young wons haw dem go tak luv dia husban and shildren;
56002005	to dey knotrol diasef; get pure maind; dey du dia haus wok wel; dey kare for pipol; dey du as dia husban wont, so dat pipol nor go tok enihaw abaut God wod wey wi dey prish so.
56002006	Mak yu tish young men to dey liv dia life wit beta sense
56002007	and mak yu yorsef bi gud ezampol to dem. Mak evritin wey yu dey du, show sey wetin yu dey tish, na trut.
56002008	Mak yu prish di trut, so dat pipol nor go get rizin to tok against yu. Den doz wey dey opoz yu, go shame and dem nor go get wod to tok abaut us.
56002009	Una wey bi savant, mak una dey du evritin wey una oga wont and wen una oga tok to una, mak una nor dey ansa am enihaw.
56002010	Mak una nor dey tif, insted mak una dey show sey una get fate, so dat evritin wey una dey du, go bring praiz to God awa Savior.
56002011	Bikos God grace wey bring salvashon, don kom out mak evribodi si-am.
56002012	Di grace dey tish us sey, mak wi nor liv laik pipol wey nor no God or dey bihav enihaw. So mak wi dey kontrol awasef; dey du gud and folo God for dis taim wey wi dey so,
56002013	bikos wi dey wait for di day wen God sey Kraist, wey bi awa Almighti God and Savior, go kom.
56002014	E die for us, so dat e go fri and klin us from wikednes kon turn us to en own pipol wey laik to du gud tins.
56002015	Mak yu tish dem dis tins and koret dem wit boldnes. So, mak yu nor let enibodi trit yu laik smol pikin.
56003001	Mak yu rimaind di bilivas sey, mak dem respet doz wey dey rule dem. Dem must obey and dey redi to du gud.
56003002	Mak dem nor eva tok bad abaut enibodi, insted mak dem dey liv for peace, dey gentol and dey bihav wel to evribodi.
56003003	Bifor naw, wi dey bihav laik fool; wi nor dey obey; wi dey disiv pipol; wi bi savant to tins wey dey swit us; wi dey du bad tins and dey jelos odas; pipol hate us and wi hate dem tu.
56003004	Bot wen God awa Savior show us di kiandnes and luv wey E get for us,
56003005	E kon save us. Nor bi bikos wi du gud, bot na bikos of en mesi. E forgiv awa sins and E mak us new shildren kon giv us new life tru di Holi Spirit.
56003006	God giv us dis Spirit for fri tru Jisos Kraist wey bi awa Savior.
56003007	Since Kraist grace don mak us klin for God eye, wi don bi pipol wey dey wait for di life wey nor go end and wi dey sure sey, wi go get am.
56003008	Dis wod wey I dey tok so na trut and I wont mak yu mak sure sey evribodi wey trust God dey du gud. Dis tishin dey gud and e go help evribodi.
56003009	Nor put mout for wod wey nor mak sense: laik mata wey konsan hu born hu and kworel or fite abaut Ju pipol law. All dis tin dey yuzles and dem nor min enitin.
56003010	If enibodi dey won kause kworel for di shosh and yu don warn am rish tu taims and e nor gri shange, den mak yu driv am.
56003011	Bikos dat kaind pesin don turn from di trut and en own sin go kondem am.
56003012	If I send Artemas or Tikikus kom mit yu, mak yu trai kom mit mi for Nikopolis, bikos I don diside sey, na der I go stay ontil kold season go end.
56003013	Mak yu du evritin wey yu fit du to help Zenas, wey bi lawya and Apollos for dia joni and mak sure sey dem get evritin wey dem nid.
56003014	Laik dis tu, awa pipol go learn haw to du gud and help pipol wey rili nid help. And as dem dey du laik dis, dem nor go liv yuzles life.
56003015	Evribodi wey dey wit mi dey grit yu! Mak yu grit all di pipol wey luv us. Mak God grace dey wit all of una.
57001001	Na Pol, wey bi prizina bikos of Jisos Kraist and awa broda Timoti rite dis leta to Filemon, awa dear broda and co-woka.
57001002	And to Afia awa sista, Arkippus awa felow soja and di shosh wey dey mit for en haus.
57001003	Mak God and awa Oga Jisos Kraist giv una grace and peace.
57001004	Evritaim wey I rimemba yu for my prayas, I dey tank my God,
57001005	bikos I don hear abaut di fate and luv wey yu get for awa Oga Jisos Kraist and all God pipol,
57001006	so I dey pray sey di fate wey yu get go mak yu undastand all di blessins wey bi yor own insaid Kraist.
57001007	I get joy and my heart dey strong bikos of yor luv and tru yu, all God pipol heart don strong tu.
57001008	Since I get strong biliv for Kraist sey, I fit tel yu mak yu du wetin dey rite,
57001009	mi, Pol, wey bi old man and prizina bikos of Kraist, won advise yu wit luv.
57001010	I beg, mak yu dey kaind to Onesimus, wey bi my pikin for God wok and e dey prizin wit mi.
57001011	Bifor, e nor dey yuzful to yu, bot naw, e dey yuzful to mi and yu.
57001012	I dey send am kom bak kom mit yu (ivun-doh I luv am wel-wel).
57001013	If to sey yu dey here, I for wont mak e help mi as I stil dey prizin bikos of di gospol wok.
57001014	Bot I nor won du enitin wey yu nor go laik, so dat di gud wey yu du, nor go bi by fos, bot e go kom from yor maind.
57001015	May bi na bikos of dis mak am nor dey wit yu since, bot naw, e go dey wit yu foreva.
57001016	Nor bi as slave, bot as broda wey wi luv, bikos e don big pas slave. E don bikom awa broda naw, bikos God don shange am.
57001017	So, if yu si mi as yor broda and patina, mak yu asept am as yu go tak asept mi.
57001018	If e tif or hol yu enitin bifor, mak yu tel mi and I go pay.
57001019	Na mi Pol tak my hand rite dis leta sey, I go pay bak, bot I fit stil sey, yu yorsef dey hol mi.
57001020	So my broda, mak yu du dis tin for mi bikos of Kraist, so dat bele go swit mi.
57001021	I dey sure sey yu go du wetin I ask yu, so I dey rite giv yu, bikos I no sey yu go du pas wetin I ask.
57001022	So, mak yu priper wer I go stay, bikos I no sey yor prayas go mak dem fri mi kom mit yu soon.
57001023	Epafras, wey dey prizin wit mi, bikos of Jisos Kraist, dey grit yu.
57001024	Mark, Aristakus, Demas and Luke, wey bi my co-wokas, dey grit yu tu.
57001025	Mak awa Oga Jisos Kraist grace dey wit yor spirit.
58001001	Bifor-bifor, God tok to awa gran-gran papa dem for meni ways, tru di profets,
58001002	bot naw, E dey tok to us tru en pikin wey get evritin and na tru am, E kreate di wold.
58001003	Na dis pikin bi God image and e dey show God glori. Naim dey kip evritin wey dey dis wold wit en pawa. Afta e don die mak God for forgiv evribodi dia sins, e kon go sidan for God rite side for hevun.
58001004	E big pas di angels, jos as di name wey God gi-am big pas angels own tu.
58001005	Na wish angel God tel sey, "Yu bi my pikin, today I don bikom yor Papa"? Or as E tok for anoda place sey, "I go bi yor Papa and yu go bi my pikin?"
58001006	Bot wen God won send en first born enta dis wold, E sey: "Mak all my angels woship am."
58001007	God tok abaut di angels sey, "I mak my angels and my savants spirit to dey burn laik fire,"
58001008	bot konsanin en pikin, E sey, "Yu bi God! Yor kindom go dey foreva and eva and yu go rule yor pipol wit autoriti.
58001009	"Yu luv to du gud and yu hate wikednes. So God, wey bi yor God don anoint yu wit oil wey dey bring joy and E mak yu dey above yor mates."
58001010	E stil tel di pikin sey, "For di biginin, na God kreate di eart and na wit en hand E tak mak di hevuns.
58001011	"Dem go skata, bot God go dey foreva. All of dem go grow kon old laik klot
58001012	and laik klot and koat, God go fold and shange dem, bot God nor dey shange and en life nor go eva end."
58001013	Na wish angel God tel, "Sidan for my rite hand ontil I go put all yor enemis unda yor leg"?
58001014	All di angels na savants and na dem God send go prish for pipol wey go get salvashon.
58002001	Mak wi listin to wetin wi don hear, so dat wi nor go fal komot from di rite road.
58002002	Bikos di mesage wey God tok tru en angels, na trut and enibodi wey disobey di law, God go ponish am.
58002003	Wetin mak us sey wi go dey fri if wi nor listin to dis koret salvashon mesage? Na God first tok am and pipol wey hear am kon show us sey na trut.
58002004	God yuz signs, mirakols and wetin di Holi Spirit du, tak show sey, dia wods na tru.
58002005	God nor sey mak en angels kontrol di wold wey dey kom and wey wi dey tok abaut so.
58002006	Insted, David tok for God wod sey: "Wetin humanbin bi wey mak Yu dey kare for am and hu bi yor pikin wey Yu dey kare for laik dis?
58002007	"Aldoh Yu mak angels high pas am smol. Bot Yu kon gi-am onor and glori.
58002008	"Yu don put evritin unda am sey mak e kontrol dem. Wen God sey na evritin E put unda am, E min sey na evritin and nor-tin rimain." And naw, wi neva si all dis tins dey hapun,
58002009	bot wi si Jisos wey angels big pas smol, bot e nor tu tey bifor God gi-am glori and onor, bikos e sofa and die for evribodi, jos as God plan am.
58002010	Dis na tru, bikos na from am and tru am evritin tak kom dis life, so dat salvashon go dey koret tru en sofa and e go kari meni pipol enta en glori.
58002011	Tru-tru, Jisos mak pipol dey holi, so en and di pipol wey e mak holi, na God kreate dem. Na dis mak am nor dey shame to kol dem en brodas and sistas.
58002012	Jisos tel God sey, "I go anounce yor name among pipol wey biliv and I go praiz Yu for dia present.
58002013	Kraist stil sey, "I go trust my God; both mi and di shildren wey E giv mi."
58002014	So as di shildren get flesh and blood, en tu get flesh and blood laik dem, so dat tru deat, e go fit distroi Satan wey get pawa to kil
58002015	and e go fri pipol wey deat don hol.
58002016	Jisos dey konsan abaut Abraham shildren and nor bi onli di angels.
58002017	So God mak Kraist laik us wey bi en brodas and sistas. Laik dis, Kraist go sori for us kon bi awa gud High Prist. And bikos Kraist dey konsan abaut God mata, e sakrifais ensef to rimov awa sins.
58002018	Bikos Jisos sofa and devol tempt am, e don get pawa to save pipol wey devol dey tempt.
58003001	My brodas and sistas wey God shuz, mak una tink abaut dis Jisos wey God send kom and na-im bi di High Prist wey wi biliv.
58003002	E obey God wey shuz am as High Prist, jos as Mosis obey God.
58003003	Jos as dem dey praiz pesin wey build fine haus, pas di haus wey e build, na so tu Jisos glori beta pas Mosis own wel-wel!
58003004	Na pesin build evri haus, bot di pesin wey build evritin, na God.
58003005	Tru-tru, Mosis rili obey God as savant and e tok abaut somtins wey God go tok abaut leta.
58003006	Bot as God Pikin, Jisos dey fateful for God haus. So wi tu go get share for di haus, if wi biliv and get kofident for awa hope wey dey insaid Kraist.
58003007	As di Holi Spirit tok, "If una hear God vois today, mak una listin to am!
58003008	"Mak una nor get strong heart for am, bikos na so Izrel pipol du wen God test dem for widanes.
58003009	"Na for di widanes una papa for test and trai mi for forti years, ivun doh dem si di mirakols wey I du.
58003010	"I ves wel-wel for dat generashon, so I kon tel dem, 'Una heart nor dey wit mi and una nor gri obey wetin I tok.
58003011	'So, una nor go eva get res.'"
58003012	Mak una mak sure sey non of una get bad maind wey go mak una nor biliv, so dat una nor go turn against God wey nor dey die.
58003013	Bot mak una dey enkorage won anoda evriday, so dat non of una go get bad maind, bikos of sin.
58003014	Bikos wi go bi Jisos Kraist frend, if wi hol awa fate strong go rish end.
58003015	Bot as dem rite am, "I wish sey una go du wetin e tok, so dat una nor go get strong heart laik Izrel pipol wen dem dey widanes."
58003016	Na hu bi di pipol wey nor listin to God, ivun doh dem hear en vois? Nor bi pipol wey Mosis lid kom out from Egypt?
58003017	Na hu mak God ves wel-wel for forti years? Nor bi doz sinas wey dia deat bodi skata for widanes?
58003018	Na hu God swear for sey, dem nor go eva get res of maind, nor bi doz wey disobey am?
58003019	So for dat taim, doz pipol nor enta di land wey God promis dem, bikos dem nor biliv am.
58004001	Ivun doh God promis us res, e gud mak wi dey kareful, so dat som of us nor go miss di promis.
58004002	Bikos dem prish God wod giv us, jos as dem prish am giv dem tu. Bot dem nor tak am serious, bikos wen dem hear am, dem nor gri biliv am.
58004003	Na onli wi wey biliv go fit enta di place wer God res dey, bikos God sey, "I ves kon swear for dem, so 'Dem nor go eva enta my place wer res dey!'"
58004004	Wi no sey God redi and dey wait, bikos Bibol sey, "Afta God don kreate evritin finish, E kon res for di sevunt day."
58004005	E stil sey, "Dem nor go eva enta my place wer res dey!"
58004006	God promis sey wi go enta di place wer en res dey, yet doz wey first hear di mesage, nor enta, bikos dem disobey am.
58004007	Bot God don plan anoda taim wen wi go enta en res and dat taim, "Na today", bikos E don tok am for en wod bifor tru David.
58004008	Bikos if to sey Joshua giv dem res of maind, God for nor tok abaut anoda day.
58004009	So, di ril "Sabat Day" res, stil dey kom for God pipol.
58004010	Bikos pesin wey enta God res, don res from all en wok, jos as God res from en own wok tu.
58004011	So mak wi trai wel-wel, so dat wi go enta dat place wer res dey and non of us go fal laik di odas wey nor obey.
58004012	God wod dey alaif, e get pawa and e sharp pas knife wey get tu mout. Di wod dey divide pesin soul from en spirit and e dey divide bone from bone; bikos God no wetin wi dey tink for awa maind.
58004013	Nor-tin wey God kreate fit hide from am and evritin dey naked to God, bikos wi go must tel am haw wi liv awa life.
58004014	Jisos wey bi God Pikin, na-im bi awa High Prist wey don go hevun. Mak wi hol am tait and always dey biliv am.
58004015	Dis awa High Prist undastand us wen wi dey wik, bikos all dis temtashon wey wi dey face so, e face dem tu, bot e nor sin.
58004016	Mak wi nor fear to enta wer God throne dey: di place wer grace dey, so dat wi go get mesi and God grace go help us wen wi nid help.
58005001	Na God dey shuz High Prist wey go represent pipol for en present. Di prist dey offa both gift and sakrifais for dia sins.
58005002	Di High Prist fit sori for doz wey sin, bikos dem nor no wetin dem sopoz no, since en ensef dey sin tu.
58005003	Bikos of dis, e dey offa sakrifais for en sin and di pipol own.
58005004	Nobodi dey fit bi High Prist wit en pawa bikos e wont mak pipol onor am, bot na onli doz wey God kol to bi prist, jos as E kol Aaron.
58005005	Kraist nor praiz ensef wen e bikom High Prist, bot na God praiz am wen E sey, "Yu bi my Pikin! Today, I don bikom yor Papa."
58005006	God stil sey, "Yu bi prist foreva as Melkizedek bi."
58005007	Wen Jisos stil dey dis eart, e pray and krai to God wey go save am from deat. God hear en prayas, bikos e obey God for evritin.
58005008	Ivun doh e bi God Pikin, na tru all di tins wey e sofa, e tak learn haw to obey.
58005009	Wen God don mak Kraist pafet finish, e kon save evribodi wey obey am.
58005010	God mak Kraist to bi High Prist laik Melkizedek.
58005011	Wi get meni tins to tok, bot dem nor eazi to esplain, bikos una nor dey gri obey.
58005012	E don tey wen una bi Kristen, so by naw, una sopoz to dey tish odas. Insted, una stil wont mak pesin kom tish una di first tin wey dey God wod. Una stil dey drink milk, insted of una to dey chop solid fud.
58005013	Enibodi wey stil dey drink milk, bi laik smol pikin wey nor no gud from bad.
58005014	Bot solid fud na for mature pipol and dem get beta sense to no wetin dey gud and bad.
58006001	E don rish wen wi go stop to learn onli di first tins wey Kraist tel us, so mak wi dey grow kon no Kraist more-more. Wi nor nid to stil dey tish una abaut tins wey dey kause deat; why wi must biliv God;
58006002	wetin baptism min; to put hand for pipol head; to wak pipol from deat and abaut God final jojment.
58006003	As God dey help us, na new-new tins wi go dey tish una abaut di fate.
58006004	Wen pesin don first no di trut; taste God gift from hevun; no di Holi Spirit;
58006005	don taste God gud wok and di beta wey dey kom,
58006006	den e kon start to sin, dat pesin nor go fit turn from sin kom mit God, since e don kil God Pikin for di sekond taim and disgrace am for publik.
58006007	Wen rain don sock groun and e bear beta fruts for di farma, dat min sey God don bless di man.
58006008	Bot if na so-so shuku-shuku and grass di groun dey bear, dat min sey e dey yuzles. So God go kos and distroi am wit fire.
58006009	Bot as for una wey bi my frends, ivun doh wi dey tok to una laik dis, wi no sey dis tins nor go hapun to una, bikos una don undastand God salvashon.
58006010	God nor dey sopot pipol enihaw. E go rimemba haw una help en pipol bifor-bifor and haw una stil dey help dem naw. Una bi God pipol and E nor go forget di luv wey una show en shildren.
58006011	As una stil dey dis wold, wi wont mak una kontinu to luv won anoda, so dat wetin una dey hope for, go kom.
58006012	So mak eni of una nor taya, bot mak una dey patient and biliv, so dat una go gain God promis.
58006013	Nobodi big pas God, bikos God swear wit en name wen E promis Abraham sey,
58006014	"Na mi bi Oga, I go bless yu wel-wel and yor shildren go plenti."
58006015	Bikos Abraham get patient, God kon gi-am wetin E promis am.
58006016	Wen pipol won setol mata, dem dey swear wit pesin wey big pas dem and di agriment wey dem mak, dey end di mata.
58006017	So wen God won show en pipol sey E nor go break en promis, E kon swear wit ensef.
58006018	God nor dey lai! So di promis wey E mak and ensef wey E tak swear, na tu tins wey nor go shange. Since wi don run go mit God mak E gaid us, e gud mak awa maind strong, so dat wi nor go fear as wi biliv en promis.
58006019	Dis hope strong for awa heart laik ship wey dem tie mak e nor for move, bikos di hope wey wi get dey kam-kpe and strong gidigba. Di promis go tak us pas di kurtain for hevun, ontil wi rish wer God dey;
58006020	di place wer Jisos don enta for us and don bikom High Prist foreva, jos as Melkizedek bi.
58007001	Melkizedek wey bi "Salem king" and "God prist", na-im bless Abraham, afta Abraham don win di kings for war.
58007002	So Abraham kon gi-am won from evri ten tin wey e bring kom bak from war. Melkizedek min, "King wey dey du wetin dey rite" and Salem min, "Peace."
58007003	E nor get papa or mama, e nor get stori at-all, en days nor get wer e for start or wer e go end, bot e bi laik Man Pikin and e bi prist foreva.
58007004	Bot si haw e big rish, bikos Abraham (awa gran papa wey evribodi no) gi-am won out of evri ten tins wey e bring from war.
58007005	Levi shildren wey bi prists, get pawa akordin to di law, to kolet won out of evri ten tins from dia own pipol, ivun doh di pipol demsef, na Abraham shildren tu.
58007006	Bot Melkizedek wey nor ivun relate to Levi pipol, stil kolet won out of evri ten tins from Abraham, den e kon bless Abraham wey God don promis.
58007007	Tru-tru, wi no sey pesin wey bless pesin, na-im big pas di pesin wey e bless.
58007008	Evri prists dey kolet won out of evri ten tins wey pipol bring, bot dem nor dey stay for di wold foreva, exept Melkizedek, bikos God wod tish us sey, e dey alaif.
58007009	Levi shildren dey kolet won out of evri ten tins from pipol, bot naw, wi go fit sey, wen Abraham giv won out of evri ten to Melkizedek, Levi pay tu,
58007010	bikos dat taim wen Abraham giv won out of evri ten tins wey e bring from war to Melkizedek, dem neva born Levi, bot Levi dey insaid am.
58007011	Ivun doh Mosis law sey prist must kom from Levi famili, dat kaind prist nor fit mak pesin dey pafet. So anoda prist laik Melkizedek must kom and e nor bi laik prist wey kom from Aaron famili.
58007012	Since dem don shange di rule to selet prist, di law must shange tu.
58007013	Di pesin wey wi dey tok abaut, na awa Oga wey kom from di tribe wer nobodi don eva serv as prist for alta bifor.
58007014	Evribodi no sey na from Juda tribe, Jisos from kom and Mosis law nor sey mak prist kom from dat tribe.
58007015	Dis mata klear wel-wel afta God selet anoda prist laik Melkizedek.
58007016	E nor selet dat pesin bikos of en gran-gran papa dem, bot na bikos en life nor go eva end.
58007017	God wod sey: "Yu bi prist foreva, jos as Melkizedek bi."
58007018	Bikos of dis, God put di old law for kona, since e dey wik and yuzles,
58007019	bikos di law nor fit mak enitin dey pafet. Bot naw, wi get beta hope wey go draw us near God.
58007020	God ensef mak promis wen E shuz dis prist, wey bi Jisos. E nor mak dis kaind promis wen E shuz di oda prists,
58007021	bot Jisos kon bi prist wen God sey, "I don swear and I nor go shange my maind sey yu go bi prist foreva."
58007022	Bikos God swear laik dis, Jisos don mak us dey sure of di new kovenant wey beta pas.
58007023	Meni prists don dey bifor and all of dem die,
58007024	bot Jisos nor go eva die. So, e go bi prist foreva.
58007025	So, di pipol wey Jisos tak go mit God, e go save dem for foreva and eva, bikos e dey alaif to pray for dem.
58007026	Na Jisos bi di High Prist wey wi nid. E nor dey du bad tin; e dey holi; nor dey mak mistak and e nor bi laik wi, wey bi sinas. God praiz am pas evritin wey dey hevun
58007027	and e beta pas eni oda high prists. Jisos nor nid to offa sakrifais evriday, laik di oda prists wey dey offa for dia own sins and for di pipol own. Bikos na wons and for all e sakrifais ensef for evribodi, wen e die for di kros.
58007028	Mosis law shuz humanbin wey get wiknes as High Prist, bot God promis wey kom afta di law, shuz di pikin and na-im bi di koret Prist foreva.
58008001	Wetin I min bi sey: Wi get High Prist wey sidan for God rite hand side for hevun.
58008002	Na-im bi di prist wey dey di Holi Tempol wey God build and na der dem for dey woship am.
58008003	Since all High Prist must offa gifts and sakrifais to God, Kraist tu must offa somtin.
58008004	If to sey e dey dis wold, e nor for bi prist at-all, since na tru Mosis law dem tak dey shuz prist wey go offa sakrifais.
58008005	Di prist wok for di Tempol bi laik wetin dey hapun for hevun. Bikos wen Mosis dey won build God haus, God tel am: "Mak sure sey evritin bi laik di design wey I show yu on-top di mountin."
58008006	Bot Kraist ministri big and beta pas dia own and na di new kovenant (wey bi di new agriment) beta pas. Bikos na tru God promis dis kovenant tak kom, so Kraist don bi di middo-man bitwin wi and God.
58008007	If to sey di first kovenant gud wel-wel, den wi nor for nid anoda won.
58008008	Bot God si fault for insaid, so E kon sey, "Di day wey I go mak new agriment wit Izrel and Juda haus, dey kom.
58008009	"E nor go bi laik di kovenant wey I mak wit dia gran-gran papa dem wen I tak dem komot from Egypt, bikos dem break dat kovenant and I kon turn against dem."
58008010	Bot naw, "Dis na my new kovenant (wey bi di new agriment): Di taim dey kom wen I go put my laws for dia mout and rite am for dia heart. I go bi dia God and dem go bi my pipol.
58008011	"Dem nor nid to tish won anoda abaut mi wey bi dia God, bikos all of dem, both smol and big, go no mi.
58008012	"I go forgiv dem for all di wiked tins wey dem don du and I nor go rimemba dia sins again."
58008013	Wen God tok abaut di new kovenant, E min sey di first won nor mata again. And enitin wey don old and nor get yuz again, go soon disapier.
58009001	Di first kovenant show how pipol go woship God for dis wold.
58009002	Di tent get tu rooms. Di first won wer lantan-stand dey, "Na di Holi Place." Won tabol and di bread wey dem offa giv God, dey der tu.
58009003	Anoda room wey dem rite, "Holi of Holis", dey for di kurtain bak.
58009004	Di gold alta wer dem dey burn insent and di kovenant box wey dem kova wit gold, dey der tu. Di gold jug wey dem put manna, Aaron rod wey grow leaf and di flat stone wey dem rite di law put, dey insaid dis box.
58009005	God angels wey kova di place wer God dey show mesi and forgiv sins, dey on-top dis box. Bot dis nor bi di taim for mi to esplain all dis tins giv una.
58009006	Wen all dis tins don redi, di prists dey enta di first room evriday go du dia wok.
58009007	Bot na onli di High Prist dey enta di Holi Place wons a year. For der, e go first offa blood for en sins, bifor e go offa for di pipol own, bikos dem nor no wetin dem sopoz to no.
58009008	Di Holi Spirit kon esplain sey, "Di way to rish di Holi Place neva opun as long as di old tent stil dey."
58009009	Dis na sign mak wi for fit undastand sey: Di gifts and sakrifais wey di prists dey offa for God pipol, nor fit mak dia maind klin.
58009010	To chop, drink and to du seremoni tak klin pesin bodi, na-im konsan dem. All dis won na rule for dis wold, ontil di taim wen God go bring di new law.
58009011	So Kraist don bi High Prist for di gud tins wey don kom. E don enta di Holi Place for hevun wey dey pafet. Nor bi humanbin mak di place and e nor dey among tins wey God kreate for dis wold.
58009012	Na wons Jisos enta di place wey holi pas. E nor enta wit goat or ram blood, bot na wit en own blood, so e don save us foreva and eva.
58009013	If goat or ram blood and ashes fit klin pesin akordin to di old tradishon,
58009014	wot of Kraist blood wey klin us from deat so dat wi go fit woship God? Dis na di Kraist wey offa ensef to God as di rite sakrifais for awa sins and e du-am wit di Holi Spirit pawa.
58009015	Na dis mak am bi middo-man for di new kovenant, so dat pipol wey e kol go fit risiv di inheritance wey go dey foreva. E promis us dis inheritance, wen e die to fri us from di bad-bad tins wey wi don du, wen di first kovenant stil dey.
58009016	Dis kaind agriment bi laik pesin wil. Di pesin must die first, bifor dem go fit yuz di wil.
58009017	Bikos pesin wil nor dey min enitin wen e stil dey alaif; e onli dey yuzful wen di pesin don die.
58009018	Na dis mak di first kovenant nor get pawa to save pipol, unles dem sakrifais blood.
58009019	Wen Mosis read all di komands giv Izrel pipol, e tak goat and ram blood wit wota and soap, kon sprinkle di blood on-top di law book and all di pipol bodi, den e kon sey,
58009020	"Na dis bi di blood for di kovenant wey God komand sey una must obey."
58009021	Mosis stil sprinkle di blood for di tent and all di plate wey dem dey yuz tak woship God.
58009022	Tru-tru, akordin to di law, na almost evritin blood dey mak klin and if dem neva pour blood, God nor go forgiv dem dia sins.
58009023	Na dis mak dem dey klin di holi place for dis eart wit anima blood, bikos e bi laik di won for hevun. Bot di tins wey dey for hevun, nid sakrifais wey beta pas dat won.
58009024	Kraist nor enta di holi place wey humanbin build laik di origina tent for hevun, bot na hevun e enta and naw, e stand for God front for awa sake.
58009025	Kraist nor nid to offa ensef evri year laik di high prists dey du for di Tempol wit anima blood,
58009026	bikos if na so, Kraist for dey kom die for us evri year since di taim wey God kreate di wold. Bot nor bi so! E die wons and for all, so dat awa sins go-go foreva.
58009027	Bikos God tok sey, na onli wons man go die and afta dat, jojment go kom,
58009028	na so tu Kraist die wons, as sakrifais to forgiv pipol foreva and naw, e go bring salvashon to doz wey dey wait for am.
58010001	Mosis law bi laik shadow wey dey show gud tins wey dey kom. Di shadow nor bi di tins, bikos di sikrifais wey dem dey offa evri year nor fit forgiv pipol dia sins.
58010002	If pipol wey dey woship God don fri from dia sins, dem nor for dey offa sakrifais again.
58010003	Doz sakrifais dey rimaind pipol of dia sins evri year,
58010004	since bull and goat blood nor fit rili klin pesin from all en sins.
58010005	So wen Kraist won kom dis wold, e tel God, "Nor bi sakrifais and ofrin Yu wont, bikos Yu don priper my bodi as ofrin,
58010006	since Yu nor laik anima blood as ofrin for sins again.
58010007	"Den I sey, 'Na mi bi dis, God na wetin Yu wont I kom du, jos as yor wod tok abaut mi for Mosis law.'"
58010008	Kraist first sey, "Yu nor wont anima or sin ofrin, (ivun wen dem dey offa am akordin to di law)".
58010009	Den e tok again sey, "Na mi bi dis, God na wetin Yu wont I kom du." So God rimov di first sakrifais, so dat E go fit bring di new won, wey bi Kraist.
58010010	Bikos Jisos du wetin God wont, all of us don dey holi tru di sakrifais wey e yuz en bodi mak for us.
58010011	Bifor-bifor, di prist dey serv evriday and dey offa di same sakrifais wey nor fit rimov sin.
58010012	Bot naw, Kraist offa onli won sakrifais for sin wons and for all, den e kon go sidan for God rite hand,
58010013	wer e dey wait ontil God go put en enemis unda en leg.
58010014	Na wit won sakrifais e tak klin pipol from dia sins and dem don dey klin foreva.
58010015	Di Holi Spirit dey bear witnes abaut dis tins sey,
58010016	"Dis na di kovenant wey I go mak wit una and afta dat taim,
58010017	e kon sey, 'I nor go rimemba dia sins and stubornes again.'"
58010018	Wen God don forgiv sins, e get eni nid to offa sakrifais again?
58010019	So my brodas and sistas, wi biliv sey wi go enta God Holi Tempol tru Jisos Kraist blood,
58010020	bikos e giv us dis new life and e go tak us pas di kurtain wey bi en bodi.
58010021	And wi get won High Prist wey dey kare for God Tempol.
58010022	So mak wi draw near God wit beta heart and strong fate, bikos God don wosh awa heart and bodi wit klin wota.
58010023	So mak wi hol di hope wey wi get strong wel-wel, bikos God wey promis us dey always kip en promis.
58010024	Mak wi always dey tink of haw wi go enkorage, luv and du gud for won anoda.
58010025	Mak wi nor stop to dey mit and feloship togeda, as som pipol dey du, bot mak wi enkorage won anoda more-more, since wi no sey, "Di Day wen Kraist go kom," don near.
58010026	If wi kontinu to sin afta God don show us di trut, e nor get eni oda sakrifais wey go fit forgiv us awa sins again.
58010027	Bot wetin wi go dey fear for na di Jojment Day wey dey kom and hell fire wey go distroi doz wey bi God enemis.
58010028	Wen tu or tiri pipol bi witnes sey sombodi rejet Mosis law, dem go kil-am witout sey dem sori for am.
58010029	If pipol wey nor dey obey Man Pikin; dey tak di kovenant blood mak yeye and dey kos di Spirit wey bring grace, na haw dia own ponishment go big rish?
58010030	Bikos God sey, "I go revenge, I go pay dem bak" and en wod stil sey, "God go joj en pipol."
58010031	Na big wahala if pesin fal enta God ponishment!
58010032	Bot mak una rimemba haw tins bi wit una bifor, haw una dey sofa afta una don risiv God lite, yet una nor alow di sofa shange una maind.
58010033	Dat taim, som pipol kos and sofa una and for oda taims, una dey help odas wey dey sofa laik una tu.
58010034	Tru-tru, una sofa laik oda prizinas and una dey hapi wen dem sieze all una propati, bikos una no sey una get beta tin wey go last foreva.
58010035	So mak una always dey strong, bikos una go get beta riwod.
58010036	Una nid to dey patient, so dat una go fit du wetin God wont and den, una go risiv en promis.
58010037	Bikos God wod sey: "E nor go tey again bifor di Pesin wey dey plan to kom, go kom.
58010038	"My raitious pipol go liv and biliv, bot if enibodi turn bak, I nor go dey hapi wit am."
58010039	Wi nor dey among pipol wey go turn bak kon perish, bot wi get fate wey go save us foreva.
58011001	Fate na wen wi dey sure sey wetin wi dey hope for go hapun and wi sure sey, di tins wey wi neva si, go kom.
58011002	Na fate awa gran-gran papa dem tak du tins wey mak God praiz dem.
58011003	Na tru fate wi tak undastand sey, God kreate evritin wit en wod. So di tins wey wi dey si so, na God mak dem from wetin dem nor dey si.
58011004	Na fate mak Abel giv God sakrifais wey beta pas Kain own and na tru dis fate Abel tak no sey God asept en ofrin, bikos God rili asept am. Ivun doh Abel don die, en blood stil dey tok for am, bikos of en fate.
58011005	Na fate nor let Enok die, bot God kari am tak and nobodi si-am. God wod sey, bifor God kari am, Enok don mak bele swit God.
58011006	Nobodi fit mak bele swit God witout fate, bikos enibodi wey dey kom mit am, must biliv sey, E dey alaif and E dey riwod pipol wey dey faind am si.
58011007	Na fate mak Noah build ark afta God warn am abaut wetin go hapun. E obey wetin God tok and na di ark save en and en famili. Na di same fate Noah tak kondem di wold, kon inherit di raitiousnes wey dey kom.
58011008	Na fate mak Abraham obey, wen God kol am mak e liv en haus, travol go anoda land wey God promis am, ivun doh e nor no wer e dey go.
58011009	Na fate mak am stay as stranja for di land wey God promis am. Na insaid canopi en, Izik and Jacob wey go inherit di same promis, stay.
58011010	Abraham du laik dis, bikos e dey wait for di tawn wey God ensef go build, wit strong foundashon.
58011011	Na fate mak Abraham born, ivun doh Sarah don tu old to get bele and Abraham don old tu, bot e no sey di Pesin wey promis am pikin, na Pesin wey e fit trust.
58011012	So from dis won man wey en bodi don die finish, shildren wey plenti rish stars for skai and sand for wotasaid kon ful evriwer.
58011013	All of dem fate stil strong wen dem die and dem nor get di tins wey God promis dem, bot dem si and welkom di tins from far and dem gri sey, dem diasef na strenja for dis wold.
58011014	Pipol wey tok laik dis, show evribodi sey dem dey espet dia own kontri.
58011015	Infact, if to-sey dem dey tink of di kontri wer dem from kom, dem for get maind to go bak.
58011016	Bot as tins bi so, dem dey espet kontri wey beta pas dia own and e dey kom from hevun. Naim mak God nor shame wen dem dey kol am dia God, bikos E don build big tawn for dem.
58011017	Na fate mak Abraham offa Izik wen God dey test am. Ivun doh na God gi-am di pikin, e stil redi to giv di onli pikin wey e get, bak to God.
58011018	God tel am bifor sey, "Tru Izik, yor famili go meni wel-wel."
58011019	Dis na bikos Abraham biliv sey, ivun if Izik die, God go raiz-am from deat and tru-tru Abraham rili kolet Izik bak from deat.
58011020	Na fate mak Izik bless Jacob and Esau abaut dia future.
58011021	Bifor Jacob die, na fate e tak bless Josef shildren and woship God as e res on-top en wokin stick.
58011022	Wen Josef life don dey end, na fate e tak tok abaut di long travol wey Izrel pipol go-go and e tel dem wetin dem go du wit en bones.
58011023	Na fate mak Mosis papa and mama hide am wen dem born am, bikos dem si sey di pikin fine and dem nor fear to disobey wetin di king komand.
58011024	Wen Mosis kon grow up, na fate mak am nor gri mak dem kol am Fero dota pikin.
58011025	Insted of am to enjoy tins wey go mak am sin, e kon shuz to sofa wit God shildren.
58011026	E feel sey e beta mak dem laff am, bikos of di Mezaya wey dey kom, insted of mak e dey enjoy di fain-fain tins for Egypt. E du laik dis, bikos e put en eye for God riwod.
58011027	Na di same fate mak Mosis komot from Egypt and e nor fear di king vesnashon, bikos e get hope for God wey ordinari eye nor fit si.
58011028	Na fate mak Mosis du di Passova and pour blood for pipol door-mot, so dat God angel wey dey kil all di first born for Egypt, nor go tosh dem.
58011029	Na fate mak Izrel pipol kros di Red Sea laik sey na dry land, bot wen Egypt pipol trai am, di wota swalow all of dem.
58011030	Na fate mak Jeriko wall fal afta Izrel pipol don mash roun am for sevun days.
58011031	Na fate mak Rahab, wey bi ashawo, eskape wen God distroi pipol wey nor obey am, bikos e welkom di pipol wey kom spy.
58011032	Wetin I go tok again? I nor get taim to tok abaut Gideon, Barak, Samson and di profets,
58011033	na fate dem tak win kindoms; du wetin gud for God eye; kon get di tins wey God promis dem; klose lion mout;
58011034	kwensh fire wey dey burn wel-wel and eskape wen dem won kil dem wit sword. God turn dia wiknes to pawa. Dem strong wel-wel for war front and sojas from oda kontris, dey run from dem.
58011035	Som wimen wey dia pipol don die, na fate mak dem risiv dem bak, alaif. Som pipol rejet fridom kon die for sofa, so dat dem go fit wak-up from deat and enta life wey beta pas dis won.
58011036	Pipol laff som; flog som; chain som and put odas for prizin.
58011037	Dem stone som; yuz saw kut som into tu; tak sword kil som; som dey hide waka insaid goat and ship skin wey dem wear and dem nor get enitin; dem sofa som and trit odas enihaw.
58011038	(Dis wold nor gud rish for dem); dem jos dey waka abaut for desert, on-top mountins, insaid rock and holes.
58011039	God praiz all of dem for dia fate, yet dem nor stil get wetin God promis.
58011040	Bikos God plan sey, witout us, dem nor go fit get di tins wey E promis dem.
58012001	Since wi get meni witnes wey soroun us, e gud mak wi drop evri load and sin wey dey mak us fal, so dat wi go yuz awa maind liv di life wey God wont.
58012002	Mak wi dey luk Jisos Kraist wey giv us awa fate and e go help us kip am. Bikos of di joy wey Jisos dey espet, e sofa for kros and nor maind di shame wey folo am. Bot naw, e don sidan for di rite hand side for God throne.
58012003	If una dey tink of haw Jisos sofa for wiked pipol hand and haw dem hate am, una maind go strong for fate.
58012004	As una dey strogol mak una nor for sin, una strogol neva rish to kil una, as Kraist die.
58012005	Abi una don forget di advise wey God tel una as en shildren? "My pikin, mak yu listin wel-wel wen God dey koret yu and nor ves wen God ponish yu.
58012006	"Bikos na di pesin wey God luv, na-im E dey koret and E dey ponish all di shildren wey bi en own."
58012007	So mak una bear as una dey sofa, since e bi sey na una Papa dey ponish una; dat won go show sey God dey trit una laik en shildren. Abi e get pikin wey en papa nor dey ponish?
58012008	Bot if God nor ponish yu as e dey ponish all en shildren, dat min sey yu nor bi beta pikin and yu nor get papa.
58012009	If awa papa for eart ponish us and wi dey respet dem, e nor gud mak God ponish us, so dat awa life go beta?
58012010	Awa papa dey ponish us for dis wold as e gud for dia eye, bot God dey ponish us for awa own gud, so dat wi go folo am share en holines.
58012011	No ponishment dey swit pesin wen dem dey ponish am, bikos e dey pain. Bot di pesin wey God ponish, go get life wey nor dey end.
58012012	So una hands and knees wey don taya, mak una mak dem strong.
58012013	And mak una waka for strate road, so dat una leg wey don taya, go strong.
58012014	Mak una trai to liv for peace wit evribodi and dey holi, bikos enibodi wey nor dey holi, nor go si God.
58012015	Mak una mak sure sey nobodi turn bak from God grace and mak nobodi get bad bele and kause trobol wey go mak pipol sin.
58012016	Mak una mak sure sey nobodi dey du bad tins or nor dey fear God, jos laik Esau wey sel en rite as first born, bikos of fud.
58012017	Una no haw e trai to get-am bak leta, bot e nor fit, ivun doh e beg and krai giv en papa.
58012018	Una don rish Mount Sinai, wer God for tok to Izrel pipol. For der, fire burn, daknes dey der and storm and
58012019	trumpet kon dey mak nois. Izrel pipol hear God vois, so dem beg am mak E stop,
58012020	bikos dem nor fit bear en komand wey sey, "Mak una kil eni anima wey tosh di mountin."
58012021	Wetin hapun dey mak pesin fear, so Mosis kon sey, "I dey fear and dey shake."
58012022	Insted, una don kom Mount Zion; di tawn wer God dey stay; di Jerusalem for hevun wer tazon angels dey. Una don enta di assembli,
58012023	di place wer all di first born gada and dis na di pipol wey God rite dia name for hevun. Una don kom mit God wey go joj evribodi and na-im dey mak pipol pafet.
58012024	Una don kom mit Jisos, di pesin wey God yuz tak start di new kovenant wit en pipol and una don kom mit di blood wey dem spray and dis blood dey tok beta wod wey pas Abel own.
58012025	Mak sure sey una dey obey di Pesin wey dey tok to una! Bikos if Izrel pipol, wey nor gri hear dia oga Mosis wod for eart nor eskape, haw wi go fit eskape, if wi nor gri hear di Pesin wey dey tok to us from hevun?
58012026	For dat taim, en vois dey shake di eart, bot naw, E don promis sey, "Nor bi onli dis eart I go shake, bot I go shake di hevuns tu."
58012027	Dis min sey di tins for eart go shake komot and na onli di tins wey God nor won shake, go rimain.
58012028	Since wi don risiv di kindom wey dem nor fit skata, mak wi tank and woship God wit respet and fear. Mak wi gi-am di kaind woship wey go mak bele swit am.
58012029	Bikos awa God na big and strong fire wey dey distroi tins.
58013001	Mak una dey luv ish oda laik Kristen brodas and sistas.
58013002	Mak una always dey welkom strenja for una haus, bikos laik dis, som pipol don welkom angel enta dia haus and dem nor no.
58013003	Mak una rimemba doz wey dey prizin, laik sey unasef dey der wit dem and mak una rimemba doz wey dey sofa, laik sey una dey sofa laik dem.
58013004	Mak evribodi respet marage: una must mak sure sey una nor slip wit hu nor bi una husban or wife, bikos God go joj pipol wey dey slip wit hu dem nor mari and pipol wey don mari, wey dey slip wit oda pipol.
58013005	Mak una nor luv moni and mak wetin una get rish una, bikos God sey, "I nor go eva liv or abandon yu."
58013006	So mak wi get maind wey go mak us fit sey, "Na God bi my helpa, so wi nor go fear. Wetin humanbin go fit du us?"
58013007	Mak una rimemba una lidas wey tish una God wod; mak una tink abaut di kaind life wey dem dey liv, den mak una folo dia fate.
58013008	Jisos Kraist na di same yestiday, today and foreva, e nor dey shange!
58013009	Mak una nor let difren-difren prishin wey una nor no turn una head. Una spiritual pawa dey kom from God grace, nor bi from fud wey dem sakrifais, bikos di sakrifais nor fit help pipol wey dey du-am.
58013010	Wi get alta wer di wokas for di tabanakol nor fit chop from.
58013011	Di High Prist dey kari anima blood enta di Holi Place as ofrin for sins, bot di anima bodi, na outsaid di camp dem for dey burn am.
58013012	Diafor, Jisos tak en own blood mak sakrifais, so dat en pipol go dey holi. So, Jisos Kraist kon sofa outsaid di camp tu.
58013013	Wi must go mit am for outsaid di camp kon share di shame wit am.
58013014	Bikos for here, wi nor get eni tawn wey go last, bot wi dey wait di tawn wey go kom.
58013015	Tru Kraist, mak wi kontinu to dey giv God praiz as awa sakrifais. So, mak wetin dey kom out from awa mout bi, "Na Jisos, bi Oga."
58013016	Mak una nor forget to du gud and to share wetin una get wit ish oda, bikos doz kaind sakrifais, dey mak bele swit God.
58013017	Mak una obey una lidas and du evritin wey dem tok, bikos na dem dey kare for una soul and dem go ansa God wen E ask dem haw dem du dia wok. Mak una let dem du-am wit hapines, nor bi wit komplain, bikos una nor go get eni beta tin from am.
58013018	Mak una pray for us, bikos wi dey sure sey awa maind klin and wi won liv awa life for di koret way.
58013019	I beg, mak una pray wel-wel, so dat dem go fri mi and I go fit kom mit una soon.
58013020	God wey get peace, di Pesin wey yuz di evalastin kovenant blood bring awa Oga Jisos Kraist kom bak from deat; awa Oga wey dey luk di ship,
58013021	mak E giv una evritin wey una nid to du wetin E wont. Enitin wey gud for en eye, mak E du-am insaid us tru Jisos Kraist. Mak all glori bi Jisos Kraist own foreva and eva. Amen!
58013022	My brodas and sistas, I dey beg una, mak una get patient and listin to di advise wey dey dis my leta, bikos wetin I rite, nor long.
58013023	Mak una no sey dem don riliz awa broda Timoti from prizin. If e kwik kom, e go folo mi kom si una.
58013024	Mak una grit all una lidas and all God pipol. God pipol for Itali dey grit una.
58013025	Mak God grace dey wit all of una.
59001001	Mi James, wey bi God and Jisos Kraist savant, dey grit una wey bi di twef tribes wey dey for evriwer for di wold.
59001002	My brodas and sistas, mak una dey hapi wen una dey face temtashon,
59001003	bikos una no sey, if una win di temtashon, una patient go strong.
59001004	And mak una let patient du en wok, so dat una go dey pafet and komplit, den una go gain evritin.
59001005	Bot if enibodi nid wisdom, mak e ask God wey dey giv am to evribodi. E nor go sey, "No," bot E go giv yu.
59001006	Di pesin wey dey ask, must get fate and mak en maind nor shake, bikos enibodi wey en maind dey shake, bi laik riva wey strong briz dey blow up and dan.
59001007	Mak dat pesin nor tink sey e go risiv enitin from God,
59001008	bikos e get doubol maind and e nor dey stabol for enitin wey e dey du.
59001009	Eni biliva wey poor, mak e hapi, bikos God don lift am up.
59001010	Bot pesin wey get moni, mak e nor proud, bikos e go soon perish laik flawa wey dey for bush.
59001011	As sun dey dry grass and flawa and dia beauti dey die foreva, na so rish pesin go dry, as e dey porshu and luv moni.
59001012	Di pesin wey fit bear wen problem kom mit am, mak e hapi, bikos e don show sey en fate strong and e go get di krawn wey get life, wey God don promis sey E go giv pipol wey luv am.
59001013	Mak nobodi tok wen temtashon kom mit am sey, "God dey test mi," bikos nor-tin fit tempt God and God ensef, nor dey tempt enibodi.
59001014	Bot temtashon dey kom mit pesin wey get bad tins for maind.
59001015	Wen di bad tins wey e won du, don mature, e go mak am sin and wen sin don grow wel-wel, e go kause deat.
59001016	My brodas and sistas, mak nor-tin disiv una,
59001017	bikos evri beta and pafet gift dey kom from God. E dey kom dan from di Papa wey kreate lite and E nor dey shange.
59001018	As God wont am, E kon born us wit di tru mesage, so dat wi go bi first among all wetin E kreate.
59001019	My brodas and sistas, mak una undastand dis tins: Mak una dey listin wel-wel and nor dey kwik tok or ves.
59001020	Humanbin vesnashon nor dey mak pipol liv di life wey God wont.
59001021	So mak una rimov una hand from evri dirti and wiked tins kon put una bodi dan to asept God wod wey dem don plant insaid una, bikos e get pawa to save una soul.
59001022	Mak una nor dey disiv unasef as una dey hear God wod, bot mak sure sey una dey du wetin en wod tok.
59001023	Pesin wey hear God wod and e nor dey du wetin e tok, bi laik pesin wey dey luk en face for mirror.
59001024	Wen di pesin luk ensef finish kon komot go out, e go kwik-kwik forget haw en face bi.
59001025	Bot di pesin wey dey luk God pafet law wey dey fri pipol, dey du wetin di wod tok and e nor dey listin and forget, God go bless am for evritin wey e dey du.
59001026	If enibodi tink sey en dey folo wetin wi dey tish and e nor fit kontrol en mout, dat pesin dey disiv ensef and en religion nor min enitin.
59001027	Bot beta religion wey nor get stain for God eye, naim bi dis: to kare for shildren wey nor get papa and mama and wimen wey dey sofa, bikos dia husban don die. So, mak una kip unasef, so dat dis wold nor go stain una.
59002001	My brodas and sistas, since una get fate for awa Oga Jisos Kraist, mak una nor dey du parsha.
59002002	If pesin wear gold ring and fine klot enta una shosh and poor pesin wit dirti klot enta tu
59002003	and una respet di won wey wear fine klot, kon tel am, "Sidan for beta place," bot una tel di poor pesin, "Stand der," or "Sidan for groun":
59002004	Dat min sey una dey du parsha and kondem pipol from una maind.
59002005	My brodas and sistas, mak una listin! God nor shuz poor pipol for dis wold sey, mak dem rish for fate and inherit di kindom wey E promis sey E go giv doz wey luv am?
59002006	Bot una nor dey respet poor pipol! Nor bi rish pipol dey opres and drag una go kourt?
59002007	Or dem nor dey tok bad abaut Jisos name wey una biliv?
59002008	Bot if una du wetin dem rite for God wod, "Mak yu luv yor nebor as yu luv yorsef," una don du gud bi dat.
59002009	Bot if una du parsha, una dey komit sin and di law don kondem una as pipol wey nor dey du wetin dey di law.
59002010	Di pesin wey dey du evritin wey dey di law and e break won, don break all of dem bi dat.
59002011	Bikos di same God wey sey, "Nor slip wit hu yu nor mari," naim stil sey, "Nor kil enibodi." If yu nor slip wit hu yu nor mari, bot yu kil pesin, yu don break di law bi dat.
59002012	Mak una tok and du laik pipol wey dem go joj wit di law wey go fri pipol.
59002013	Jojment nor get mesi for enibodi wey nor dey mesi for odas, bikos mesi beta pas jojment.
59002014	My brodas and sistas, wetin dey gud if pesin sey e get fate, bot e nor dey du enitin? Dat kaind fate go fit save am?
59002015	If won broda or sista nor get klot to wear or fud to chop
59002016	and won of una tel am, "Mak peace dey wit yu; mak kold nor kash yu and mak yu go chop beleful, bot yu nor gi-am wetin di bodi wont, na wish kiand gud bi dat?"
59002017	Na so fate bi tu, if yor fate nor dey produce beta result, e go die and dey yuzles.
59002018	If enibodi sey,"I get fate and yu get wok." I go sey, "Mak yu show mi yor fate wey nor get wok and I go show yu my fate tru my wok."
59002019	Yu biliv sey na onli won gud God dey. Dimons biliv so tu and fear dey kash dem wel-wel.
59002020	Foolish man! Yu wont mak I show yu sey fate wey nor get wok dey yuzles?
59002021	Wen awa papa Abraham put en pikin Izik for di alta, wetin e du dey gud for God eye?
59002022	Yu nor si sey en fate and wok dey togeda and na en wok mak en fate pafet?

59002024	So, pesin wok dey mak am gud tu, nor bi onli en fate.
59002025	Nor bi so e bi for Rahab, wey bi ashawo, wen e welkom di mesenjas, kon show dem anoda road wey dem go pas run?
59002026	Bodi wey nor get spirit don die, na so tu, fate wey nor get wok, don die.
59003001	My brodas and sistas, evribodi nor go fit bi tisha, bikos yu no sey wi wey dey tish, na awa jojment go big pas,
59003002	bikos wi dey mak meni mistak. If pesin nor dey mak mistak for wetin e dey tok, dat min sey e dey pafet and e go fit kontrol en bodi.
59003003	If wi tie rope for horse mout mak e for obey us, dat min sey wi dey kontrol en bodi.
59003004	Luk ship for wota: E big wel-wel and na strong briz dey fit push am, bot na won smol wheel di pilot dey yuz tak kontrol am.
59003005	Na so di tongue bi tu: naim smol pas for di bodi, bot di tins wey e fit du big wel-wel. Mak una tink haw smol fire fit burn big fores rish groun.
59003006	Di tongue na fire! Na der bad tins ful pas for pesin bodi. E dey spoil di hol bodi and kause fire for pesin life and dis kaind fire dey kom from hell.
59003007	Humanbin dey fit kontrol bird, anima wey dey krip for groun and anima wey dey stay for wota.
59003008	Bot nobodi don eva fit kontrol en tongue wel. Di tongue na bad tin wey nor dey stay won place, bikos e get poison wey fit kil pesin.
59003009	Na di tongue wi tak dey praiz awa papa and Oga Jisos Kraist and naim wi stil dey yuz tak kos pipol wey God kreate laik ensef.
59003010	My brodas and sistas, na di same tongue wi dey yuz tak praiz and kos pipol. Bot e nor sopoz bi laik dat.
59003011	Spring wey dey kom out from groun, nor dey bring out fresh and bita wota from di same place, abi e dey du so?
59003012	My brodas and sistas, fig tri go fit bear olive, abi vine fit bear fig? So tu, spring wey dey bring out salt wota, nor go fit bring fresh wota at-all.
59003013	Hu get sense among una? Di way di pesin dey bihav go show di gentolnes wey wisdom dey bring.
59003014	Bot if jelosi and selfishnes dey en maind, mak e nor boast and lai against di trut.
59003015	Dat kaind wisdom nor kom from God, bot e kom from dis eart wey wiked wel-wel.

59003017	Bot God wisdom dey pure; e get peace; dey gentol; dey asept pipol and gud frut and mesi ful am; e nor dey du wayo or pritend.

59004001	Wetin dey mak una kworel and fite? Nor bi di tins wey dey hungri una to du?
59004002	Yu wont somtin, bot yu nor get-am; yu dey kil, dey wont wetin oda pipol get and yu nor dey fit get-am; so yu go kon dey kworel and fite. Yu nor get, bikos yu nor ask God mak E giv yu.
59004003	Wen yu ask for somtin, yu nor risiv am, bikos yu nor ask wel and yu won tak am du wetin yu laik.
59004004	Una wey dey du bad tins for dis wold, una nor no sey to bi dis wold frend, min sey una bi God enimi? So enibodi wey gri sey en and dis wold na frend, don mak ensef God enimi.
59004005	Abi yu tink sey God nor min wetin E tok wen E sey, "Di Spirit wey I put insaid una dey jelos wel-wel"?
59004006	Bot E giv us plenti grace. Na dis mak God wod sey, "God dey against pesin wey dey kari bodi up, bot E dey giv grace to pipol wey dey put dia bodi dan."

59004009	Mak una krai and mak sorrow dey una heart, den una go show sey una nor dey hapi.
59004010	If una put una bodi dan for God, E go kari una go up.
59004011	My brodas and sistas, mak una nor tok bad abaut ish oda. Enibodi wey tok bad or joj en broda or sista for Kraist, e dey tok bad abaut di law and e dey joj di law. Bot if una joj di law, naim bi sey una nor dey obey di law, bot una don bikom di law joj bi dat.
59004012	Na onli won Pesin giv di law and na-im bi joj. Na-im dey save and distroi. Yu wey dey joj yor nebor, na hu yu ivun tink sey yu bi?
59004013	Luk, yu wey dey sey, "Today or tumoro, wi go-go dis or dat tawn go stay der for won year and du biznes, kon get gain."
59004014	Bot yu nor no tumoro. Wetin yor life bi laik? Yu bi laik smoke wey dey kom out from fire. Pipol go si-am, den smol taim e go vanish.
59004015	Insted, yu sopoz to sey, "If God wont, wi go dey alaif and wi go du dis or dat tin."

59005001	Yu wey get moni, mak yu listin! Krai mak dem hear yor vois, bikos of di bad tins wey go hapun to yu.

60005001	Mi wey bi una felow elda, wey si haw Kraist sofa and go share for God glori wey go soon kom, dey beg di eldas among una sey:
60005002	Mak una kare for di ship wey God giv una hol, jos as shepad dey kare for dia ship. Mak e nor bi laik sey dem fos una du-am, bot na as God wont am. Una nor dey du-am bikos of moni, bot na bikos una won du-am.
60005003	And mak una nor dey opres God pipol wey dey unda una, insted mak una bi ezampol to dem.
