60005005	For di same way, mak una wey young put bodi dan for di eldas. Mak una nor dey kari bodi up for ish oda, bikos God dey opoz proud pipol, bot E dey favor doz wey dey humbol.
60005006	Mak una put una bodi for groun bikos of God and wen di rite taim rish, E go kari una up.

60005009	Mak una nor gi-am shanse, bot mak una fate strong, bikos una no sey na di same tin una brodas and sistas for evriwer for dis wold, dey sofa.

61002015	Since dem komot from di rite way, dem don miss road, bikos dem dey folo Balaam, Beor pikin, wey luv bad tins!
61002016	As God dey koret Balaam for en sin (donkey wey nor sopoz tok kon tok to di profet, so dat e go stop di bad tins wey e dey du).

62004018	Dis kaind luv nor get fear, bikos beta luv dey driv fear komot from pesin heart. If wi dey fear bikos wi nor wont mak God ponish us, dat show sey wi neva rili no haw en luv bi.

62004020	If sombodi sey, "I luv God" and e hate en Kristen broda, e dey lai, bikos pesin wey nor luv en Kristen broda wey e dey si, haw e wont tak luv God wey e nor dey si?
62004021	God don komand us sey: "If enibodi luv mi, mak e luv en broda and sista for Kraist tu."
62005001	Enibodi wey biliv sey na Jisos bi Kraist, don bi God pikin and enibodi wey luv di Papa, luv di pikin wey E born.
62005002	Wi go no sey wi luv God shildren, wen wi luv God and obey en komandment.
62005003	To luv God, na to kip en komandment and en komandment nor dey hard.
62005004	Enibodi wey bi God pikin, don win di wold and na awa fate bi di pawa wey win di wold.
62005005	Pesin wey biliv sey Jisos Kraist na God Pikin, don win di wold.
62005006	Na Jisos Kraist kom dis wold wit wota and blood. Nor bi onli wit wota, bot na wit di wota and di blood. And God Spirit bear witnes sey dis na tru, bikos na God Spirit bi di trut.
62005007	Wi get tiri witnes to show sey wetin wi dey tok, na tru and dem bi:
62005008	God Spirit, di wota and di blood and dis tiri witnes dey tok di same tin.
62005009	If wi gri sey wetin humanbin tok na tru, den wetin God tok abaut en pikin, naim big pas.
62005010	(Di pesin wey biliv God Pikin, go no insaid ensef sey, dis tin na tru, bot pesin wey nor biliv God, dey sey God dey lai, bikos e nor biliv wetin God tok abaut en Pikin).
62005011	Dis na wetin God tok: God don giv us life wey nor dey end and dis life dey insaid en Pikin.
62005012	Enibodi wey get di Pikin, get di life wey nor go end, bot doz wey nor no God Pikin, go die.
62005013	I don rite all dis tins giv una wey biliv God Pikin, so dat una go no sey una get life wey nor go end.
62005014	Na dis tins dey mak awa maind strong enitaim wey wi kom mit God: bikos if wi ask am for enitin wey dey gud for en eye, E go giv us.
62005015	And if wi no sey E dey hear us, den wi biliv sey wi go get di tins wey wi ask from am.
62005016	If enibodi si en broda or sista for Kraist dey komit sin wey nor go kil-am, mak e ask God and God go giv life to dat pesin. E get di kaind sin wey dey kause deat and I nor sey mak una pray mak God forgiv di pesin wey dey komit dat sin.
62005017	Evritin wey nor gud for God eye, na sin, bot e get di sins wey nor dey kause deat.
62005018	Wi no sey enibodi wey bi God pikin, nor dey laik to sin, bot God dey kip en pikin, so dat devol nor go fit tosh am.
62005019	Wi no sey wi bi God shildren and dis wold wey wi dey so, na wiked pipol dey rule am.
62005020	Wi no sey God Pikin don kom and e don giv us sense to no di trut abaut God. And wi dey insaid en Pikin, Jisos Kraist. Na-im bi di ril God and na-im bi di life wey nor go end.
62005021	So my shildren, mak una mak sure sey una nor get enitin to du wit oda gods.

63001006	(Na wetin luv min bi dis: mak wi dey du wetin God wont.) Na di komandment bi dis and jos as wi hear am from di biginin; na so wi sopoz to folo am.

65001001	Dis leta na from Jude, Jisos Kraist savant and James broda. To di pipol wey God don kol, wey Papa God luv don wrap laik klot for Jisos Kraist bodi.
65001002	Mak mesi, peace and luv dey wit una!
65001003	My frends, ivun doh e don dey hungri mi since to rite giv una abaut di salvashon wey wi dey share togeda, naw e strong wel-wel for my maind to rite, so dat una maind go dey strong. So una go fit stand fite for wetin wi biliv; di tins wey God don giv en pipol and nor-tin go fit shange am.
65001004	Som pipol don hide join una and God don mark dem for distroshon. So I won tel una abaut dis tins sey, dis pipol nor dey fear God. Dem don dey yuz God grace as eskuze to dey du bad-bad tins. Dis pipol nor gri asept Kraist as dia Masta and Oga.
65001005	So I won rimaind una ivun doh una don alredi no dis tins. Afta God don first save Izrel pipol from Egypt, e kon distroi doz wey nor biliv am.
65001006	And I stil dey rimaind una abaut di angels wey nor stay for wer God put dem, bot kon komot for wer dem sopoz dey. God don chain dem tie for daknes ontil wen E go joj di wold.
65001007	Mak una yuz Sodom and Gomora and di tawns wey dey near dem, as exampol. God ponish dem wit fire wey nor dey end, bikos both men and wimen dey slip wit ish oda enihaw, dem ivun dey slip wit animas and dem dey du oda wiked tins wey dey dia maind.
65001008	Laik dis tu, dis men wey sey dem dey dream, dey liv bad life, dem nor dey obey God autoriti and dem ivun dey kos angels wey get glori.
65001009	Bot wen Michael, di big angel dey kworel wit devol bikos of Mosis bodi, e nor kos am, bot insted, e sey, "Na God go joj yu!"
65001010	Bot dis pipol nor undastand wetin dem dey tok and dis na wetin dem sopoz to undastand witout sey pesin tish dem. As animas nor dey tink bifor dem du tins, na so dis pipol dey bihav.
65001011	Kos dey dia head! Bikos dem dey bihav laik Kain and bikos of long-trot, dem dey du di mistak wey Balaam du. So dem go must die laik Kora, wey disobey God.
65001012	Wen dis pipol dey folo una chop di feloship fud wey God don bless, dem bi laik shuku-shuku for una bodi. Dem bi laik shepad wey nor dey shame, wey kare for onli ensef. Dem bi laik kloud wey jos dey blow, bot rain nor dey fal. Dem bi laik tri wey nor get fruts and God don root dem komot from groun.
65001013	Dem bi laik wave for sea wey dey foam kom out. Dem bi laik star wey nor dey stay won place and God don kip di place wey deep pas for daknes, dey wait dem.

65001016	Dis pipol dey komplain waka and dey faind fault. Dem dey go eni wer wey dia bodi kari dem go and dem dey boast. Dem dey tok wetin pipol laik to hear, so dat odas go praiz dem.
65001017	Bot my frends wey I luv, mak una rimemba wetin awa Oga Jisos apostols tel una.
65001018	Dem sey, "For di taim wen dis wold won end, som pipol go dey laff una and di tins wey God hate wey dey hungri dem to du, naim go dey push dem."

66004004	Twenti-for oda thrones dey roun di first throne and twenti-for eldas sidan put for di thrones. Dem wear white klot and gold krawn dey dia head.
66004005	Lite dey shine kom out from di throne and thunda dey mak nois from am tu. For di throne front, sevun tosh wey get fire dey burn for der. Dis na God sevun spirit.
66004006	Di throne front dey shine laik mirror and e bi laik kristal. For senta and aroun di throne, for kreatures wey get eye ful bodi, dey for der tu.
66004007	Di first won bi laik lion, di sekon won bi laik melu, di ted won get humanbin face and di fort won bi laik eagle.
66004008	Ish for di for kreatures get sis feda and eye ful di fedas. Dem nor dey eva res for nite or day and dem dey always sey: “Holi! Holi! Holi! Na-im bi di God wey dey mighti. Di Pesin wey dey since, wey dey naw and wey go soon kom.”
66004009	Weneva di for kreatures dey tank, praiz and onor di Pesin wey sidan for di throne wey dey alaif foreva and eva,

66004011	"Awa Oga and God! Yu dey wordi to risiv glori, onor and pawa, bikos na yu kreate evritin as yu wont."
66005001	Den I si sey di Pesin wey sidan for di throne, hol won book for en rite hand. Dem rite somtin put for di front and bak kon lock-am wit sevun keys.
66005002	Den I si won strong angel dey shaut wit loud vois sey: "Na hu dey holi rish to break di keys and opun dis book?"
66005003	Bot nobodi for hevun, eart or unda eart fit opun di book or luk insaid.
66005004	So I start to krai, bikos nobodi dey holi rish to opun di book or luk insaid.
66005005	Den won of di eldas kon tel mi, "Mak yu nor krai again! Luk, di lion for Juda tribe, wey kom from David famili, don win. So e go opun di book and break di sevun keys.
66005006	Den I si won Lamb wey bi laik sey dem don kil-am, bot e stand for di throne senta wit di for kreatures and di twenti-for eldas. E get sevun horns and sevun eyes wey bi God sevun spirit, wey E send enta di eart.
66005007	Den e waka go kolet di book from di Pesin wey sidan for di throne.

66005010	Yu don shuz dem as kings and prists wey go serv God and dem go rule for di eart.’’

66005013	Den I hear evritin wey God kreate for hevun, eart, unda eart, sea and evritin wey dey insaid dem dey sing sey: "Mak praiz, onor, glori and pawa to rule, bi di Pesin wey sidan for di throne and di Lamb own, foreva and eva!"
66005014	And di for kreatures kon sey, "Amen!" Den di eldas fal face groun kon start to woship God.
66006001	As I dey luk, di Lamb kon opun won for di sevun keys and I hear won for di for kreatures dey shaut laik thunda sey, "Mak yu kom!"
66006002	So I luk kon si won white horse dey kom! Di pesin wey dey ride am hol bow and e wear krawn for en head. E go fite and win meni war and na champion e bi.
66006003	Wen di Lamb opun di sekon key, I kon hear di sekon kreature dey sey, "Mak yu kom!"
66006004	Den anoda red horse kom out. Dem giv di pesin wey dey ride am, big sword and pawa to tak rimov peace from dis eart. So pipol kon dey fite and kil ish oda for evriwer.
66006005	Den wen di Lamb opun di ted won, I hear di ted kreature dey sey, "Mak yu kom!" So I luk and I si won blak horse dey kom! Di pesin wey dey ride am hol rula for en hand.
66006006	Den I hear won vois among di for kreatures dey sey, "Dem dey sel sis pound for barley and won bread for onli won penni and mak yu nor spoil di olive oil and wine."
66006007	Wen di Lamb opun di fort key, I hear di fort kreature dey sey, "Mak yu kom!"
66006008	So I luk kon si won horse wey en color bi laik grin wey don dey fade! Di pesin wey dey ride am, na Deat dem dey kol am and en frend na di Grave. Wen dem divide di eart into for, dem giv di tu of dem pawa ova won part, so dat dem go kil pipol wit dia sword, wit honga, diziz and wit wiked animas.
66006009	Wen di Lamb opun di fift key, pipol wey dem don kil bikos of God wod and wetin dem dey tok abaut Kraist, I si dia soul for unda di alta.
66006010	Dem dey krai wit loud vois sey, "Oga wey get pawa, haw long e go tak bifor yu go joj doz wey dey liv for dis eart? Mak yu ponish dem, bikos na dem kil us!"
66006011	Den dem giv ish of dem long white klot kon sey, mak una res smol ontil di oda savants and una brodas for Kraist wey wiked pipol go kil, don komplit.
66006012	Den di Lamb opun di sist key and big eartquake kon hapun. Di sun kon dak laik blak klot and di moon kon dey red laik blood.
66006013	Di stars for skai fal kom groun laik di way fig tri frut wey ripe, dey fal wen strong briz dey blow.
66006014	Di skai kon dey fold laik paper and evri mountin and island move komot from wer dem dey bifor.

66006017	Bikos di day to ponish dem, don kom and nobodi go sovaiv am.
66007001	Den, I si for angels stand for di for kona for di eart and dem hol di for briz, so dat e nor go blow for di eart, di sea or for eni tri.

66007007	12,000 from Simeon tribe, 12,000 from Levi tribe, 12,000 from Isakar tribe,
66007008	12,000 from Zebulun tribe, 12,000 from Josef tribe and 12,000 from Benjamin tribe.

66007010	dey shaut sey, "Awa God wey sidan for di throne and di Lamb, na yu get pawa to save pipol!"

66007015	"Dis na why dem stand for God throne front kon dey serv am for en Tempol, both for nite and day taim.

66008001	Wen di Lamb opun di sevunt key, evriwer for hevun kon kwayet for laik tati minutes.

66008008	Den di sekon angel blow en trumpet and dem trow mountins wey fire dey, enta di sea. If dem divide di sea into tiri, won part kon turn to blood.

66008012	Den di fort angel blow en trumpet and wen dem divide di sun, moon and stars into tiri, dem fal for won part and di part kon dak. So if dem divide day and nite into tiri, won part for di day nor get sun again and won part for di nite, moon and star nor kon dey shine again.
66008013	Den I luk and I hear won eagle dey shaut as e dey flai for skai, "E go bad wel-wel! E go bad wel-wel! E go bad wel-wel for pipol wey dey dis eart, bikos of wetin go hapun wen di last tiri angels go blow dia trumpets."
66009001	Den di fift angel blow en trumpet and I si won star wey fal from hevun kom eart and dem giv am di key wey e go yuz tak opun di pit.

66009008	Dia hair bi laik wimen hair and dia tit bi laik lion own.

66009020	Bot di pipol wey dis tins nor kil, nor stil gri turn kom mit God wey go save dem. Dem kontinu to serv dimon and juju wey dem mak wit gold, silva, bronze, stone and wud. Dis juju nor dey si, hear or waka.
66009021	And insted of dem to turn kom mit God, dem stil dey kil pipol; du majik; dey slip wit hu nor bi dia husban or wife and stil dey tif.
66010001	Den I si anoda angel wey get pawa dey kom dan from hevun insaid kloud and rainbow dey on-top en head. En face dey shine laik sun and en leg bi laik big fire.

66011010	Sinas go dey hapi bikos of dem and dem go dey giv gift to ish-oda to celebrate di tu profet deat, bikos di profets trobol dem wel-wel.
66011011	Afta di tiri and haf days, God go breat life enta dia bodi and dem go wak-up! Fear go kash all doz wey dey luk dem.
66011012	Den won loud vois from hevun go tel di tu profet, "Mak una kom up!" And dem go-go hevun insaid kloud as dia enemis go dey luk dem.
66011013	For dat same taim, beta eartquake go hapun and if dem divide di tawn into ten, won part go distroi finish. Sevun tazon pipol go die for di eartquake and evri oda pesin go fear kon bigin tank God wey dey hevun.
66011014	Di sekon deat don pas, bot si, di ted won go soon kom.

66011016	Di twenti-for eldas wey sidan for di throne bifor God, go fal face groun kon woship God.
66011017	And dem go sey, "Awa Oga God wey dey mighti, wi dey tank yu. Di won wey dey since and wey go always dey, bikos naw, yu don show yor pawa kon start to rule.
66011018	"Di nashons dey ves, bot di taim wey yu go ponish dem, don rish. And na naw yu go joj doz wey don die kon riwod yor savants, di profets, doz wey dey gud and evribodi wey dey fear yor name, both smol and big. Dis na di taim to distroi doz wey dey kause wahala for di eart."
66011019	Den for hevun, God Tempol kon opun and en kovenant ark dey insaid di tempol. Thunda kon dey mak nois and spark, den strong eartquake hapun and big-big ice-blok kon dey fal.
66012001	Den won big sign kon apier for hevun: I si won wuman wey tak sun tie en bodi laik klot, di moon dey unda en leg and won krawn wit twef stars, dey for en head.

66013001	Den I si won beast dey kom out from di sea. E get ten horns, sevun head and ten krawns dey en horns. For en head, name wey dey kos God, naim dem rite put.
66013002	Di beast wey I si, bi laik leopard, bot en leg bi laik bear leg and en mout bi laik lion own. Di dragon kon gi-am pawa, en throne and strong autoriti to rule.

66014001	Den I si di Lamb stand on-top Mount Zion wit 144,000 pipol. Dem rite en name wit en Papa name for dia forehead.

66022010	Den e tel mi, "Nor klose di wods wey dey dis book, bikos di taim don near.
66022011	"Mak di pesin wey dey du bad, kontinu to dey du bad and doz wey get dirti life must kontinu to liv laik dat. Di pesin wey dey du wetin gud for God eye, mak e kontinu to du-am and di wons wey dey holi, must kontinu to dey holi.”
66022012	“(Si! I go soon kom and my riwod dey wit mi. I go pay evribodi akordin to wetin dem don du!
66022013	"Na mi bi di Alfa and Omega, di first and di last, di startin and di endin!)
66022014	"God don bless doz wey wosh dia klot klin, so dem go get autoriti to chop from di tri wey dey giv life and dem go fit pas di gate enta di tawn.
66022015	"Pipol wey dey du laik dogs, doz wey dey du majik and kil odas; doz wey dey serv juju and dey laik to lai, all of dem nor go enta di tawn.
66022016	"Mi, wey bi Kraist, I don send my angel mak e kom tel di pipol for di shosh di trut abaut dis tins. I kom from David famili and na mi bi di brite Star wey dey shine for mornin!"
66022017	Di Spirit and di Bride sey, "Kom!" Mak di pesin wey hear sey, "Kom!" And enibodi wey wota dey hungri, mak e kom; and di pesin wey wont di wota wey dey giv life, mak e drink from am fri of charge.
66022018	I dey warn evribodi wey dey read di profesi wey dem rite for dis book: If enibodi add join wetin dey dis book, di wahala wey dey dis book, God go add am join en life.
66022019	And if enibodi rimov eni wod from dis profesi book, wetin sopoz bi en own for di tri wey dey giv life and for di holi tawn wey dem diskribe for dis book, God go tak am from am.
66022020	Di Pesin wey dey tok dis tins, no sey dis tins na tru. Jisos Kraist sey "Tru-tru, I go soon kom!" Amen! Oga Jisos, mak yu kom!
66022021	Mak Oga Jisos Kraist grace dey wit all of una. Amen
